### [1] [Dirac branch-cut modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28127)
*Bofeng Zhu,Chengzhi Ma,Qiang Wang,Gui-Geng Liu,Xiuhai Zhang,Qi Jie Wang,Baile Zhang,Y. D. Chong*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文揭示了狄拉克场（Dirac field）中束缚态的第三种机制：复狄拉克质量场（complex Dirac mass field）的相位不连续性（phase discontinuities）能够产生沿分支割线（branch-cut）传播的狄拉克分支割线（DBC）模式，其横向约束长度与能量无关，为光子/声学超材料（photonic/acoustic metamaterials）提供了新的波导设计原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，狄拉克场中的束缚态主要归因于两种机制：实狄拉克质量场变号产生的Jackiw-Rebbi态，以及复狄拉克质量场相位奇点（phase singularities）产生的Jackiw-Rossi零模。本文旨在探索是否存在第三种不同的束缚机制。

Method: 通过理论推导证明了相位不连续性（如复分支函数的割线）能够产生沿割线传播的束缚模式，称为狄拉克分支割线（DBC）模式。这些模式遵循有效的一维相对论性狄拉克方程（effective one-dimensional relativistic Dirac equation），其约化质量由跨越割线的相位差决定。同时，利用声学超材料（acoustic metamaterials）进行了实验验证。

Result: 理论推导表明DBC模式具有相对论性色散关系（relativistic dispersion）和与能量无关的横向约束长度，这与Jackiw-Rebbi态、Jackiw-Rossi零模或传统边界模式不同。实验成功实现了DBC模式，验证了其相对论性色散、稳健的横向约束长度以及沿自由形式路径传播的能力。

Conclusion: 复狄拉克质量场中的相位不连续性构成了波导模式的通用设计原理，为光子学和声学超材料提供了新的应用可能性。DBC模式展示了不同于现有束缚机制的特性，特别是其能量无关的横向约束特性。

Abstract: Bound states arising in Dirac fields are usually attributed to two kinds of features: domain walls where a real Dirac mass field changes sign, which host Jackiw-Rebbi states, and phase singularities in a complex Dirac mass field, which host Jackiw-Rossi zero modes. We show that phase discontinuities, such as branch-cuts of complex branch functions, supply a third distinct binding mechanism. We derive the existence of guided modes that propagate along the cut, called Dirac branch-cut (DBC) modes, which obey an effective one-dimensional relativistic Dirac equation with a reduced mass determined by the phase difference across the cut. When the mass field has fixed magnitude, the DBC modes' transverse confinement lengths are energy-independent, unlike Jackiw-Rebbi and Jackiw-Rossi states or conventional boundary modes. Using acoustic metamaterials, we realize DBC modes experimentally, and verify their relativistic dispersion, robust transverse confinement length, and ability to propagate along freeform paths. These results show that phase discontinuities in a complex Dirac mass field constitute a versatile design principle for guided modes, with interesting application possibilities for photonic and acoustic metamaterials.

</details>


### [2] [The role of focused laser plasmonics in shaping SERS spectra of molecules on nanostructured surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28140)
*Fran Nekvapil,Cosmin Farcău*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了表面增强拉曼散射（SERS）光谱对激光焦点相对于固体纳米结构基底轴向位置的依赖性，发现信号强度呈洛伦兹轴向分布且峰值位于样品表面上空，不同谱带强度比随焦点位置变化，这为基于谱带强度比的定量分析提供了重要启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表面增强拉曼散射（SERS）光谱对激光焦点相对于固体纳米结构基底精确轴向位置的依赖性在文献中极少受到关注。本研究旨在探究这种依赖性是否真实存在且具有物理意义。

Method: 通过垂直（Z轴）扫描改变激光焦点与平面SERS基底之间的距离，测量SERS信号变化。同时采用有限差分时域（Finite-Difference Time-Domain, FDTD）模拟来解释观察到的现象。

Result: SERS信号强度呈现洛伦兹轴向分布，峰值始终位于物理样品表面之上。不同光谱区域（SERS谱带和背景）的相对强度沿Z轴非单调、非均匀变化，表明谱带强度比具有焦点依赖性。FDTD模拟将此归因于聚焦和散焦光束与纳米结构金属表面相互作用产生的等离子体近场响应。

Conclusion: 这些发现揭示了固体基底SERS测量中一个先前被忽视的光谱失真来源，对基于谱带强度比的定量分析（quantitative assays）的设计和解释具有直接意义。

Abstract: The dependence of surface-enhanced Raman scattering (SERS) spectra on the precise axial position of the laser focus relative to a solid nanostructured substrate has received little to no attention in the literature. Here we show this dependence is both real and physically meaningful. Through vertical (Z-axis) scans varying the distance between the laser focus and a planar SERS substrate, we find that the SERS signal intensity follows a Lorentzian axial profile that peaks consistently above the physical sample surface. More significantly, the relative intensities of different spectral regions, i.e. SERS bands and background, vary non-monotonically and non-uniformly along the Z axis, meaning that band intensity ratios are focus-dependent. Finite-Difference Time-Domain (FDTD) simulations attribute these effects to plasmonic near-field responses specific to the focused and defocused beam interacting with the nanostructured metal surface. These findings reveal a previously overlooked source of spectral distortion in solid-substrate SERS measurements, with direct implications for the design and interpretation of quantitative assays based on band intensity ratios.

</details>

### [3] [From Hole Theory to Quantum Field Theory: Relativistic Fermions and the Role of Ettore Majorana (1933-1937)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28538)
*Francesco Vissani*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 该论文追溯了1933-1937年间相对论性自旋-1/2粒子理论从空穴理论（Hole theory）到现代量子场论（quantum field theory）框架的演变过程，特别强调了埃托雷·马约拉纳（Ettore Majorana）1937年工作的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在重构相对论性费米子（fermionic）场论发展的关键阶段，通过考察多位作者在形式体系和物理概念上的进展，揭示从空穴理论到现代量子场论框架的转变过程。

Method: 采用历史研究方法，全面追溯费米子场论的发展历程：从1920年代的基础工作开始，聚焦1930年代的研究成果，并以沃尔夫冈·泡利（Wolfgang Pauli）1941年的综合论述作为终点。

Result: 研究表明马约拉纳1937年的量子化程序（quantisation procedure）和对反对易费米子量子场（anti-commuting fermionic quantum fields）的论证，不仅是一个技术变体，而是对负能量解（negative energy solutions）概念的明确拒绝。

Conclusion: 马约拉纳的工作具有概念清晰性和教育价值，其影响延续至今，塑造了后续的理论传统，标志着从空穴理论到现代量子场论框架的决定性转变。

Abstract: Between 1933 and 1937, the treatment of relativistic spin-1/2 particles, initially rooted in Hole theory, evolved into the modern framework of quantum field theory. This paper reconstructs the crucial stages of that transition by examining the formal and physical progress of the numerous authors who shaped the field's modern formalism. This historical study traces the development of fermionic field theory in full, beginning with the foundational work of the 1920s, focussing on the results of the 1930s, and concluding with the influential synthesis of Wolfgang Pauli in 1941, the content of which has shaped the subsequent tradition. Within this framework, particular emphasis is given to Ettore Majorana's 1937 quantisation procedure and argument for anti-commuting fermionic quantum fields. This study demonstrates that Majorana's work was not merely a technical variant, but the definitive rejection of the concept of negative energy solutions, whose conceptual clarity and educational value remain vital today.

</details>

# math.FA [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Weak supermajorization between symplectic spectra of positive definite matrix and its pinching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27634)
*Temjensangba,Hemant Kumar Mishra*

Main category: math.FA

TL;DR: 该论文证明了实正定矩阵的辛特征值（symplectic eigenvalues）满足弱次主化（weak submajorization）关系，并观察到一个有趣的弱超主化（weak supermajorization）不等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究实正定矩阵辛特征值（symplectic eigenvalues）的排序性质，特别是块对角矩阵与原始矩阵辛特征值之间的主化（majorization）关系。

Method: 采用矩阵分析和辛几何方法，通过构造性证明展示辛特征值满足的弱次主化（weak submajorization）关系，并利用矩阵不等式技术推导弱超主化（weak supermajorization）关系。

Result: 证明了对于实正定矩阵$A$，其块对角部分$E \oplus G$的辛特征值向量$d(E \oplus G)$弱次主化于$A$的辛特征值向量$d(A)$，即$d(E \oplus G) \prec^w d(A)$。同时发现了一个有趣的弱超主化关系。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了实正定矩阵辛特征值的重要排序不等式，揭示了块对角化操作对辛特征值分布的影响，为辛几何和矩阵分析领域提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: Let $A = \begin{bmatrix} E & F \\ F^T & G \end{bmatrix}$ be a $2n \times 2n$ real positive definite matrix, where $E, F,$ and $G$ are $n \times n$ blocks. It is shown that
  $\  d(E \oplus G) \prec^w d(A)$.
  Here $d(A)$ denotes the $n$-vector consisting of the symplectic eigenvalues of $A$ arranged in the non-decreasing order. We also observe the following weak supermajorization relation, which is interesting on its own:
 $ λ\left( \left(\mathscr{C}(G)^{1/2} \mathscr{C}(E) \mathscr{C}(G)^{1/2}\right)^{1/2} \right) \prec^w λ\left( \left(G^{1/2} E G^{1/2} \right)^{1/2} \right)$.
  Here $λ\left( \left( G^{1/2}E G^{1/2} \right)^{1/2} \right)$ denotes the $n$-vector with entries given by the eigenvalues of $\left( G^{1/2}E G^{1/2} \right)^{1/2}$ in the non-decreasing order.

</details>


<div id='hep-ph'></div>

# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [5] [Universal Geometric Scaling in Cosmic Ray Spallation: Evidence of a Dynamical Causal Horizon from AMS-02](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26824)
*Yi Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种宏观几何框架来解释宇宙线次级粒子通量比在高刚度下的能量无关平台现象，认为超相对论溅射产生的有效昂鲁温度（Unruh temperature）约5.6-5.8 MeV，与核液气相变极限一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统运动学模型预测复杂的能量依赖演化，但AMS-02测量显示在高刚度（R > 30 GV）下，次级粒子通量比（Li/B、Be/B、Li/Be）严格收敛到能量无关的平台。这一异常现象需要新的理论框架来解释。

Method: 采用宏观几何框架，基于伍兹-萨克森势（Woods-Saxon potential）和π介子交换进行半微观估计，提出超相对论溅射（ultra-relativistic spallation）会断裂残余强相互作用通量管，在残余核上产生极端减速，从而动态生成具有有效昂鲁温度（Unruh temperature）的因果视界。

Result: 理论估计的有效昂鲁温度约为5.6-5.8 MeV，使用Be/B比作为绝对校准通道提取的渐近尺度为6.08 MeV，与理论估计和核液气相变极限（nuclear liquid-gas phase transition limit）一致。对锂比值的盲测显示普遍零斜率收敛。

Conclusion: 在高能条件下，恒定的几何热浴（geometric thermal bath）有效地取代了复杂的微观运动学，为宇宙线次级粒子通量比的高刚度平台现象提供了令人信服的物理解释。

Abstract: The interpretation of high-precision cosmic ray spectra is fundamentally bottlenecked by uncertainties in fragmentation cross-sections. Traditional kinematic models, driven by phase-space expansions, typically predict complex, energy-dependent evolutions. However, AMS-02 measurements reveal that at high rigidities ($R > 30$~GV), secondary-to-secondary flux ratios (Li/B, Be/B, and Li/Be) strictly converge to energy-independent plateaus. To understand this anomaly, we explore a macroscopic geometric framework. The ultra-relativistic spallation of a target nucleus snaps residual strong-interaction flux tubes, inducing an extreme deceleration on the remnant. Using a semi-microscopic estimation based on the Woods-Saxon potential and pion exchange, we suggest this dynamically generates a causal horizon with an effective Unruh temperature $T_U \approx 5.6-5.8$~MeV. Utilizing the Be/B ratio as an absolute calibration channel, we extract an asymptotic scale of $6.08$~MeV, remarkably consistent with our theoretical estimation and the established nuclear liquid-gas phase transition limit. Subsequent blind tests on Lithium ratios demonstrate a universal zero-slope convergence, providing compelling evidence that a constant geometric thermal bath effectively supersedes complex microscopic kinematics at high energies.

</details>


### [6] [The Physics and Prospects of Super-Tau Charm Factories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26879)
*Alexey A. Petrov,Yangheng Zheng*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 超级τ-粲工厂（Super tau-charm factories）是新型高亮度电子-正电子对撞机，运行质心能量范围为2-7 GeV，能够产生前所未有的数据样本，为精确检验标准模型和探索新物理提供独特机会。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在评估超级τ-粲工厂的物理前景，该设施运行在2-7 GeV质心能量范围，覆盖τ轻子、开粲强子、粲偶素态、超子和轻强子等阈值区域，为粒子物理研究提供独特平台。

Method: 通过综述分析（review）方法，系统考察超级τ-粲工厂的物理潜力，重点关注精确粲物理测量、介子和重子的CP破坏、τ轻子性质与稀有衰变，以及非微扰QCD现象如强子化、谱学和类时形状因子。

Result: 超级τ-粲工厂凭借其高亮度、阈值运动学和量子相干产生机制，能够提供前所未有的数据样本，在精确物理前沿占据重要地位，与现有及规划中的实验设施形成互补。

Conclusion: 超级τ-粲工厂将粒子物理的精确前沿（precision frontier）置于前沿地位，通过其独特能力在标准模型检验和新物理搜索方面发挥关键作用，同时面临实验技术和互补性方面的挑战。

Abstract: The proposed Super tau-charm factories are a powerful new class of high-luminosity electron-positron colliders operating in the center-of-mass energy range between 2 and 7 GeV, a region that spans thresholds for tau leptons, open-charm hadrons, charmonium and charmonium-like states, hyperons, and light hadrons. With unprecedented data samples, threshold kinematics, and quantum-coherent production, these facilities offer unique opportunities to advance precision tests of the Standard Model and to search for physics beyond it. In this review, we examine the physics prospects of the Super Tau-Charm Facility, focusing on precision charm measurements, CP violation in mesons and baryons, tau lepton properties and rare decays, and nonperturbative QCD phenomena such as hadronization, spectroscopy, and time-like form factors. We also discuss the experimental landscape, technological challenges, and complementarity with existing and planned facilities. Together, these capabilities position super tau-charm factories at the forefront of the precision frontier in particle physics.

</details>


### [7] [Vorticity-induced modifications of chemical freeze-out in heavy-ion collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27267)
*Nandita Padhan,Kshitish Kumar Pradhan,Arghya Chatterjee,Raghunath Sahoo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了整体旋转（global rotation）对超相对论重离子碰撞中化学冻出（chemical freeze-out）参数的影响。基于强子共振气体（HRG）模型，作者发现旋转会导致化学冻出曲线在T-μ_B相图中向低温方向系统性地偏移，并首次系统性地分析了电荷和奇异数化学势的旋转依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究整体旋转对超相对论重离子碰撞中化学冻出参数的影响。重离子碰撞中产生的夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）可能携带显著的角动量，因此理解旋转效应对于准确描述碰撞系统的热力学性质至关重要。

Method: 研究采用强子共振气体（hadron resonance gas, HRG）模型框架，将常用的冻出判据（包括固定每粒子能量和标度化熵密度）扩展至包含旋转效应。通过这一方法，系统分析了旋转对化学冻出参数的影响。

Result: 研究发现旋转导致化学冻出曲线在T-μ_B相图中向低温方向系统性地偏移。首次在HRG框架内系统研究了电荷和奇异数化学势的旋转依赖性。实验可观测量的分析表明，强子产额比对旋转表现出显著敏感性，而传统的累积量比值受旋转影响相对较小。

Conclusion: 研究表明强子产额比可能为估算重离子碰撞中产生的旋转效应幅度提供更合适的可观测指标。这一发现对于理解旋转夸克-胶子等离子体的热力学性质具有重要意义，并为实验数据分析提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We investigate the influence of global rotation on the chemical freeze-out parameters in ultra-relativistic heavy-ion collisions. Within the framework of the hadron resonance gas (HRG) model, the freeze-out parameters are determined using commonly employed freeze-out criteria, namely the fixed energy per particle and the scaled entropy density, extended here to include rotational effects. We find that the presence of rotation leads to a systematic shift of the chemical freeze-out curve toward lower temperatures in the $T\text{--}μ_B$ phase diagram. The behavior of the electric charge and strangeness chemical potentials in the presence of rotation is also analyzed, providing the first systematic study of their rotational dependence within the HRG framework. Furthermore, we examine the impact of rotation on experimentally relevant observables, including hadron yield ratios and susceptibility ratios of conserved charges. Our results show that while particle yield ratios exhibit noticeable sensitivity to rotation, the conventional cumulant ratios remain comparatively less affected. This indicates that hadronic yield ratios may provide a more suitable observable for estimating the magnitude of rotational effects generated in heavy-ion collisions.

</details>


### [8] [Isolation of photon-nuclear interaction backgrounds in the search for the chiral magnetic effect in relativistic heavy-ion collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27473)
*Jing Gu,Jinhui Chen,Jie Zhao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究评估了相对论性重离子碰撞中相干光子-核相互作用对精确测量手征磁效应（CME）的影响，旨在区分真实CME信号与背景贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手征磁效应（chiral magnetic effect, CME）可能关联于CP破坏，对理解宇宙物质-反物质不对称性至关重要。过去二十年的实验努力致力于寻找CME证据，但背景贡献可能模拟CME信号，需要进一步研究潜在背景源。

Method: 研究估计了相干光子-核相互作用（coherent photon-nuclear interactions）的贡献，这些相互作用由超相对论性重离子碰撞中产生的强电磁场驱动。特别关注与强电磁场相关的背景源，分析光子偏振与电场方向对齐的特性。

Result: 相干光子-核相互作用能够产生电荷依赖的相关性（charge-dependent correlations），这些相关性模拟CME信号的关键特征，但源于不同的物理机制，且区别于流诱导的背景（flow-induced backgrounds）。

Conclusion: 研究定量评估了相干光子-核相互作用对CME精确测量的影响，旨在改进真实CME信号与这些背景贡献的分离，为更准确地探测手征磁效应提供理论支持。

Abstract: The chiral magnetic effect (CME) in relativistic heavy-ion collisions originates from a chirality imbalance among quarks within metastable QCD vacuum domains and may be linked to $CP$ violation, which is believed to play a crucial role in the matter-antimatter asymmetry of the universe. Over the past two decades, extensive experimental efforts at RHIC and the LHC have been devoted to the search for evidence of the CME. Recent advances have greatly improved our understanding of background contributions that can mimic CME-like signals. In particular, analyses utilizing techniques designed to suppress flow-related backgrounds indicate that the CME signal at RHIC, if present, is small. To further investigate potential background sources, particularly those associated with strong electromagnetic fields, we estimate the contribution from coherent photon-nuclear interactions. These interactions are driven by intense electromagnetic fields produced in ultrarelativistic heavy-ion collisions, with cross sections that scale with the field strength. Notably, the polarization of the incident photons is aligned with the electric field, which is oriented along the impact parameter direction and perpendicular to the magnetic field. Consequently, such processes can generate charge-dependent correlations that mimic key features of the CME signal, yet originate from different physics mechanisms and are distinct from flow-induced backgrounds. In this study, we quantitatively assess the influence of these coherent photon-nuclear interactions on the precision measurement of the CME, aiming to improve the separation of the genuine CME signal from these background contributions.

</details>


### [9] [Magnetic moments of open bottom--charm molecular pentaquark octets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27657)
*Halil Mutuk,Xian-Wei Kang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究对开放重味五夸克态 $b\bar{c}qqq$ 和 $c\bar{b}qqq$ 的磁矩进行了系统理论计算，发现 $8_{2f}$ 表示中 $\frac{1}{2}^+\otimes 0^-$ 态具有接近普适的磁矩值，而 $8_{1f}$ 表示则呈现广泛分布，揭示了重味夸克对称性破缺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于系统探究开放重味分子五夸克态（open heavy-flavor molecular pentaquarks）的磁矩特性，这些态由重子-介子束缚态构成，旨在为实验观测提供电磁基准以区分内部结构。

Method: 采用分子图像（molecular picture）将五夸克视为重子-介子的S波束缚态，在组分夸克模型（constituent quark model）框架下，系统构建了对称和反对称轻二夸克构型对应的SU(3)$_f$八重态表示 $8_{1f}$ 和 $8_{2f}$ 的完整自旋-味道波函数。

Result: 计算结果显示：$8_{2f}$ 表示中 $\frac{1}{2}^+\otimes 0^-$ 态磁矩接近普适值（$b\bar{c}qqq$ 约 -0.062$\mu_N$，$c\bar{b}qqq$ 约 +0.362$\mu_N$），源于自旋单态轻二夸克抑制了轻夸克贡献；而 $8_{1f}$ 表示则呈现广泛分布且频繁变号，反映了对称轻二夸克的活跃作用。

Conclusion: $b\bar{c}$ 和 $c\bar{b}$ 家族间的显著差异证明了电磁观测量中重味夸克对称性破缺（heavy-quark flavor symmetry breaking），这些预测为未来实验观测的开放重味五夸克提供了详细的电磁基准，可用于区分内部味道结构和自旋构型。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive theoretical investigation of the magnetic moments of open heavy-flavor molecular pentaquarks with quark compositions $b\bar{c}qqq$ and $c\bar{b}qqq$ (where $q=u,d,s$). Employing a molecular picture in which the pentaquarks are treated as S-wave bound states of a heavy baryon and a meson, we systematically construct the complete spin--flavor wavefunctions for the two distinct SU(3)$_f$ octet representations, $8_{1f}$ and $8_{2f}$, arising from symmetric and antisymmetric light-diquark configurations, respectively. Within the framework of the constituent quark model, we calculate the magnetic moments of spin-parity configurations, $J^P = \frac{1}{2}^-(\frac{1}{2}^+\otimes 0^-)$ and $J^P = \frac{1}{2}^-, \frac{3}{2}^-(\frac{1}{2}^+\otimes 1^-)$, for each member of the $b\bar{c}$ and $c\bar{b}$ octets. Our results reveal a striking hierarchy: in the $8_{2f}$ representation, the $\frac{1}{2}^+\otimes 0^-$ states exhibit near-universal magnetic moments ($μ\approx -0.062\,μ_N$ for $b\bar{c}qqq$ and $μ\approx +0.362\,μ_N$ for $c\bar{b}qqq$), as a direct consequence of the spin-singlet light-diquark that suppresses light-quark contributions. In contrast, the $8_{1f}$ representation shows a broad spectrum of values with frequent sign changes, reflecting the active role of the symmetric light-diquark. The clear differences between the $b\bar{c}$ and $c\bar{b}$ families demonstrate explicit heavy-quark flavor symmetry breaking in electromagnetic observables. These predictions provide a detailed set of electromagnetic benchmarks that can serve as discriminants for the internal flavor structure and spin configuration of future experimentally observed open heavy-flavor pentaquarks, offering valuable guidance for ongoing and future searches at facilities such as LHCb and Belle II.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 该方法能够放松对模型参数空间的约束，使得介子创生机制在现有实验限制下仍然可行，特别是针对使用D介子的机制。

Abstract: Mechanisms of Mesogenesis generate the baryon asymmetry and dark matter of the Universe through late-time decays of Standard Model mesons into baryons and dark matter states. Utilizing the CP violation in the meson systems themselves, the resulting baryon asymmetry is directly controlled by collider observables, the CP asymmetry $A_{CP}$, and the branching fraction for the meson decays. Experimental probes of these decays place strong constraints on the amount of $CP$ violation required, placing it well above observed limits in meson mixing. Additionally, strong lower bounds on the proton lifetime seemingly rule out Mesogenesis mechanisms which use $D$ mesons. In this work, we propose to circumvent these constraints by ``morphing'' the mass of the dark sector particles using a late-time phase transition. The change in mass of the final decay products kinematically excludes meson and proton decays, relaxing the constraints on the model parameter space.

### [13] [Global Structure, Non-Invertible PQ Symmetry, and the DFSZ Domain Wall Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26867)
*Gongjun Choi,Sungwoo Hong,Seth Koren*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文重新审视DFSZ轴子模型中的畴壁问题，发现对称群的整体结构（global structure）对畴壁性质起关键作用，并通过非可逆自然性（Non-invertible Naturalness）策略提出通过小瞬子诱导的非可逆对称性破缺解决畴壁问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来研究发现，对称群的整体结构（global structure）包含重要的理论结构并具有显著的现象学意义。基于此，作者重新审视DFSZ轴子模型，该模型因标准模型（Standard Model）的代结构而存在畴壁问题（domain wall problem）。

Method: 作者分析电弱规范群与Peccei-Quinn对称性之间的整体结构$(G_{\text{EW}} \times U(1)_{\text{PQ}})/\mathbb{Z}_2$如何决定畴壁问题的精确性质。在夸克味$Z'$模型中，畴壁稳定性由非可逆手征对称性（non-invertible chiral symmetry）强制实施，该模型具有色群与规范夸克味群之间的额外整体结构$(SU(3)_C \times G_F)/\mathbb{Z}_3$。

Result: 研究显示整体结构在确定畴壁问题的精确性质中起关键作用，这对三次和四次DFSZ模型都有重要影响。非可逆自然性（Non-invertible Naturalness）策略引导出通过小瞬子诱导的非可逆对称性破缺（small-instanton-induced breaking of non-invertible symmetries）解决畴壁问题的紫外（UV）理论。作者还勾勒了轴子畴壁湮灭可能产生的引力波信号。

Abstract: In recent years it has become increasingly clear that the previously overlooked ``global structure'' of symmetry groups can encode significant theoretical structure and, more importantly, have substantial phenomenological implications. With this in mind we re-examine the DFSZ axion, which suffers from a domain wall problem due to the Standard Model generation structure. We show that global structure $(G_{\text{EW}} \times U(1)_{\text{PQ}})/\mathbb{Z}_2$ acting between the Peccei-Quinn symmetry and the electroweak gauge group plays a crucial role in determining the precise nature of the domain wall problem, which has important implications in both cubic and quartic DFSZ. We then demonstrate that the stability of the domain walls is enforced by a non-invertible chiral symmetry in quark flavor $Z'$ models which have additional global structure $(SU(3)_C \times G_F)/\mathbb{Z}_3$ acting between the color and the gauged quark flavor groups. The strategy of Non-invertible Naturalness then leads us to UV theories that resolve the domain wall problem through small-instanton-induced breaking of non-invertible symmetries. Finally, we sketch potential gravitational wave signatures arising from the annihilation of axion domain walls. Our work illustrates the importance of considerations of global structure in realistic models of particle physics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: HF-NRevo框架扩展了重味碎裂研究的唯象范围，为研究类夸克偶素态和探测质子内禀粲夸克含量开辟了新途径。该方案在高亮度大型强子对撞机（HL-LHC）和未来对撞机设施中拓宽了QCD研究的边界，并可能为探索新物理提供潜在窗口。

Abstract: We report on recent developments of the Heavy-Flavor Non-Relativistic evolution (HF-NRevo) scheme, a framework designed to describe heavy-hadron formation through leading-power fragmentation at moderate and large transverse momentum. The approach combines short-distance inputs obtained from next-to-leading-order NRQCD calculations with collinear scale evolution in a variable-flavor-number scheme, ensuring a consistent treatment of heavy-flavor thresholds and partonic hierarchies. Within this setup we have constructed the NRFF1.0 family of fragmentation functions for $S$-wave heavy quarkonia in their leading NRQCD Fock states. We discuss prospective applications of the HF-NRevo framework in the heavy-ion environment, where it can provide a perturbative baseline for investigating medium-induced modifications of heavy-flavor fragmentation. Its explicit treatment of partonic channels and heavy-flavor thresholds makes it particularly suitable for exploring jet-quenching sensitivity, energy-loss mechanisms, and the emergence of medium-modified fragmentation patterns in the quark-gluon plasma. The HF-NRevo scheme has also been extended to the exotic sector through the TQ4Q1.x and newly released TQ4Q2.0 fragmentation sets, which describe the formation of fully heavy tetraquarks in multiple quantum configurations. These developments open a novel pathway to study quarkoniumlike states and to probe the intrinsic charm content of the proton in forward hadron-collision environments. Altogether, this program broadens the phenomenological reach of heavy-flavor fragmentation studies at the HL-LHC and future collider facilities, opening access to previously unexplored aspects of QCD and potential portals to New Physics.

We identify a particularly interesting regime in which energy can be transferred into sub-luminal plasma modes ($ω< k$) with an efficiency greater than that of super-luminal modes ($ω> k$). Our results highlight a variety of less conventional ways in which axions (and other light degrees of freedom that mix with electromagnetism, such as dark photons or gravitons) can interact in extreme astrophysical environments.

### [16] [Bag Parameters for Heavy Meson Lifetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28516)
*Matthew Black,Robert V. Harlander,Jonas T. Kohnen,Fabian Lange,Antonio Rago,Andrea Shindler,Oliver Witzel*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究首次利用梯度流（gradient flow）结合短流时展开（short flow-time expansion）作为重整化方案，在格点QCD（lattice-QCD）框架下计算了描述重介子寿命比的ΔQ=0四夸克矩阵元，并获得了完整的误差预算。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重介子寿命比的理论预测需要精确计算ΔQ=0四夸克算符的矩阵元，但此类算符在重整化过程中存在算符混合（operator mixing）问题，传统格点QCD方法难以获得完整误差预算。

Method: 采用梯度流重整化方案，在六个RBC/UKQCD 2+1味（flavor）畴壁费米子（domain-wall fermion）系综上进行计算。通过多尺度匹配程序（multi-scale matching procedure）结合重整化群跑动（renormalization-group running），利用短流时展开系数至次次领头阶（NNLO）匹配到MS-bar方案。

Result: 在SU(3)F对称点获得了描述τ(D_s)/τ(D^0)寿命比的相关算符参数：B_1^MS-bar(3 GeV)=1.0524(97), B_2^MS-bar(3 GeV)=0.9621(70), ε_1^MS-bar(3 GeV)=-0.2275(76), ε_2^MS-bar(3 GeV)=-0.0005(8)。这是首次包含完整误差预算的ΔQ=0四夸克算符格点QCD确定。

Conclusion: 该方法为更高精度的重介子寿命预测及类似存在重整化算符混合的物理量计算开辟了新路径，首次实现了包含完整误差预算的ΔQ=0四夸克算符格点QCD确定。

Abstract: We calculate the dimension-six $ΔQ=0$ four-quark matrix elements describing heavy-meson lifetime ratios using the gradient flow with its short flow-time expansion as a renormalization procedure. On six RBC/UKQCD 2+1-flavor domain-wall fermion ensembles, we determine flowed bag parameters for physical charm and strange quarks and match to the $\overline{\text{MS}}$ scheme with perturbative short flow-time expansion coefficients through next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO). A multi-scale matching procedure using renormalization-group running improves the extrapolation to zero flow time. For the operators relevant to $τ(D_s)/τ(D^0)$ at the SU(3)$_{\rm F}$ symmetric point, we obtain $B_1^{\overline{\text{MS}}}(3\,{\rm GeV})=1.0524(97)$,$B_2^{\overline{\text{MS}}}(3\,{\rm GeV})=0.9621(70)$, $ε_1^{\overline{\text{MS}}}(3\,{\rm GeV})=-0.2275(76)$, and $ε_2^{\overline{\text{MS}}}(3\,{\rm GeV})=-0.0005(8)$ using a specific choice of evanescent operators. This is the first lattice-QCD determination of $ΔQ=0$ four-quark operators with a full error budget. It opens the path towards higher-precision predictions of heavy-meson lifetimes and similar quantities exhibiting operator mixing under renormalization.

</details>


### [17] [Axion EFT in the BMHV Scheme: Flavor Currents, Evanescent Operators and Ward Identities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26880)
*Deepanshu Bisht,Sabyasachi Chakraborty,Atanu Samanta*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了BMHV方案中的轴子有效场论，重点研究了费米子五维算符的重整化及相关手征流。通过推导裸和重整化的Ward恒等式，验证了至两圈阶的有效性，并阐明了瞬逝算符在恢复四维Ward恒等式中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在系统分析Breitenlohner-Maison-`t Hooft-Veltman (BMHV)方案中的轴子有效场论（axion effective field theory），重点关注费米子五维算符（fermionic dimension-five operators）的重整化及相关手征流（chiral flavor currents）。研究动机源于在d≠4维度中γ₅的非反对易性导致瞬逝算符（evanescent operators）出现，从而破坏朴素Ward恒等式。

Method: 采用BMHV方案框架，推导了手征流的裸和重整化Ward恒等式（bare and renormalized Ward identities），明确识别了运动方程（equation-of-motion）和瞬逝算符贡献。通过图计算（diagrammatic calculations）验证了这些恒等式至两圈阶O(α_s²)的有效性，包括极点项和有限项。

Result: 研究结果表明瞬逝算符如何混合到物理算符中，并确定了恢复四维Ward恒等式所需的有限重整化（finite renormalization），从而恢复了轴流重整化（axial current renormalization）和反常（anomaly）的预期结构。验证了这些恒等式在两圈阶的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文结果为轴子有效场论中的多圈计算提供了一个一致且透明的框架，并强调了瞬逝算符在维持方案一致性（scheme consistency）中的关键作用。该研究为BMHV方案中的高阶计算建立了系统方法。

Abstract: We present a systematic analysis of axion effective field theory within the Breitenlohner-Maison-`t Hooft-Veltman (BMHV) scheme, focusing on the renormalization of fermionic dimension-five operators and the associated chiral flavor currents. In this framework, the non-anticommuting nature of $γ_5$ in $d \neq 4$ dimensions leads to violations of naive Ward identities through the emergence of evanescent operators. We derive the bare and renormalized Ward identities for chiral currents, explicitly identifying the equation-of-motion and evanescent operator contributions. Using diagrammatic calculations, we verify the validity of these identities up to two-loop order $\mathcal{O}(α_s^2)$, including both pole and finite terms. We demonstrate how evanescent operators mix into physical operators and determine the finite renormalization required to restore four-dimensional Ward identities, recovering the expected structure of axial current renormalization and the anomaly. Our results provide a consistent and transparent framework for multi-loop computations in axion EFT and highlight the essential role of evanescent operators in maintaining scheme consistency.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于精确计算$e^+ e^- \to π^+ π^- γ$过程的辐射修正，以量化味工厂（flavour factories）辐射返回实验中描述π介子-光子相互作用的模型不确定性。这扩展了先前对$e^+ e^- \to π^+ π^-$能量扫描过程的研究。

Abstract: We compute the radiative corrections to the process of two-pion production in association with a hard photon in $e^+ e^-$ annihilation by taking into account the non-perturbative structure of the pion in the one-loop calculation. For this purpose, we adopt the generalised vector meson dominance model to insert the pion form factor in loop integrals for the treatment of final-state radiation and initial-final state interference at next-to-leading order. We compare our predictions with the results of the naive factorised scalar QED approach for experimentally relevant observables in the measurement of the $e^+ e^- \to π^+ π^- γ$ process. The computation extends previous results obtained for the energy scan process $e^+ e^- \to π^+ π^-$ and can be used to quantify the uncertainty due to the model describing the pion-photon interaction in radiative return experiments at flavour factories.

### [19] [Density screening effects in the NJL model: Chiral condensate, speed of sound, and the Critical End Point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26924)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子色动力学相图是高能物理的核心课题，其中临界终点的寻找是FAIR和NICA重离子实验的主要目标。目前高密度区域的一级相变缺乏直接实验证据，需要理论模型进行探索。

Method: 采用Nambu-Jona-Lasinio模型，通过引入温度与化学势相关的有效耦合常数$G(T,μ)$来包含介质屏蔽效应。应用一致的正则化方案和Sommerfeld展开，在能隙方程中纳入低温和高密度修正。

Result: 数值分析显示屏蔽效应会改变临界终点的可能位置，并修正手征相变的性质。研究还关注了手征凝聚、动力学夸克质量和声速的行为变化。

Abstract: The phase diagram of Quantum Chromodynamics (QCD) remains a central topic in high-energy physics. At high temperature and low baryochemical potential, the chiral transition is experimentally observed and theoretically explored to be a smooth crossover, while at high densities, a first-order phase transition is theoretically expected in lack of direct experimental evidence. The search for the Critical End Point (CEP), where both regimes meet, is one of the main objectives of heavy-ion experiments at FAIR and NICA. In this work, we explore the QCD phase diagram structure using the Nambu--Jona-Lasinio (NJL) model, incorporating medium screening effects through an effective coupling $G(T,μ)$ for $μ\gg T\sim 0$. We apply a consistent regularization scheme and Sommerfeld expansion to include low thermal and large density corrections in the gap equation. Our numerical analysis focuses on the behavior of the chiral condensate, the dynamical quark mass, and the speed of sound. We find that screening effects shift the posible position of the CEP and modify the nature of the chiral transition. These findings provide theoretical support for ongoing experimental searches and may have implications for the physics of compact stars.

### [20] [Late-time attractors in relativistic spin hydrodynamics in Gubser flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27182)
*Gen-Hui Li,Xiang Ren,Dong-Lin Wang,Shi Pu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了Gubser流中最小因果自旋流体动力学的自旋密度晚期渐近解和吸引子结构，发现当系统特征长度远大于固有时时，自旋密度可表现为类似传统热力学变量的慢衰减流体动力学模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索最小因果自旋流体动力学（minimal causal spin hydrodynamics）在Gubser流中的晚期渐近行为，特别是自旋密度的吸引子结构和衰减特性，以理解自旋作为流体动力学模式的演化规律。

Method: 方法包括推导自旋密度的微分方程，获得其晚期渐近解，识别数值解中的吸引子（attractors）和排斥子（repellers），并将这些解映射回平坦闵可夫斯基空间（flat Minkowski space）。

Result: 结果显示存在自旋密度呈现幂律衰减的参数区域，当系统特征长度远大于固有时时，多个自旋密度分量可衰减得与传统相对论流体动力学中的热力学变量一样缓慢，此时自旋密度表现为受流动晚期标度律支配的流体动力学模式。

Conclusion: 结论表明在特定条件下，自旋密度可展现出类似传统流体动力学变量的慢衰减行为，这为理解自旋作为流体动力学模式在晚期演化中的标度特性提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We investigate the late-time asymptotic solutions and attractor structure of the spin density in minimal causal spin hydrodynamics in Gubser flow. After deriving the differential equation governing the spin density, we obtain its late-time asymptotic solutions and identify both attractors and repellers in the corresponding numerical solutions. We then map these solutions back to flat Minkowski space and find parameter regions where the spin density exhibits a power-law decay. We further show that, when the characteristic length scale of the system is much larger than the proper time, several components of the spin density can decay as slowly as conventional thermodynamic variables in relativistic hydrodynamics. In this regime, the spin density behaves as a hydrodynamic mode governed by the late-time scaling laws of the flow.

### [21] [On the predictivity of axion dark matter in the presence of Peccei-Quinn breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28098)
*Michael Zantedeschi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 研究表明，暴胀后量子色动力学（QCD）轴子（axion）在特定条件下可能不是暗物质的预测性候选者，当小的显式Peccei-Quinn对称性破缺在QCD相变前变得动力学相关时，轴子弦-壁网络会提前湮灭，遗迹丰度不再仅由QCD动力学决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探讨暴胀后量子色动力学（QCD）轴子作为暗物质候选者的预测性限制。动机源于考虑小的显式Peccei-Quinn对称性破缺在QCD相变前变得动力学相关的情况，这可能会改变轴子遗迹丰度的计算框架。

Method: 研究方法基于分析显式Peccei-Quinn对称性破缺引入的质量标度$μ$对早期动力学的影响。由于QCD对轴子质量的贡献在高温下受到热抑制，$μ$可以控制早期时间动力学，从而影响轴子弦-壁网络（axion string-wall network）的湮灭时间。

Result: 结果显示，在这种条件下，轴子弦-壁网络会更早湮灭，遗迹丰度不再主要由QCD动力学单独决定，而是同时依赖于轴子衰变常数$f_a$和质量标度$μ$。这种效应与QCD轴子暗物质相关的参数空间重叠，并可能完全跨越该空间。

Conclusion: 结论表明，暴胀后QCD轴子不一定能作为暗物质的预测性候选者，当小的显式Peccei-Quinn对称性破缺在QCD相变前变得动力学相关时，轴子遗迹丰度的计算需要考虑额外的参数$μ$，这扩展了传统QCD轴子暗物质模型的参数空间。

Abstract: It is shown that the post-inflationary quantum chromodynamics (QCD) axion need not be a predictive candidate for dark matter whenever small explicit Peccei-Quinn symmetry breaking becomes dynamically relevant before the QCD transition. Although strongly constrained by the strong CP bound, such breaking remains phenomenologically viable and introduces a mass scale $μ$ that can control the early-time dynamics, as the QCD contribution to the axion mass is thermally suppressed at high temperatures. In this case, the axion string-wall network annihilates earlier, and the relic abundance is no longer primarily set by QCD dynamics alone, but instead depends on $μ$, in addition to $f_a$, the axion decay constant. This effect overlaps with the parameter space relevant for QCD axion dark matter and, depending on ultraviolet parameters and initial conditions, can extend across it entirely.

Result: 研究结果推导出了两个平行金属板之间的相互作用能和力的具体表达式。这些表达式描述了在介子场构成的真空中，当金属板非常接近时量子真空涨落产生的效应。

### [23] [Removing the Cosmological Bound on the Axion Scale via Confinement During Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28620)
*Gia Dvali,Sophia Fitz,Lucy Komisel*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在SU(5)大统一理论框架下，通过高能标禁闭实现轴子的早期弛豫，研究暴胀宇宙学中的强QCD时期。该机制消除了轴子衰变常数的宇宙学上限，使其可作为任意大衰变常数的暗物质候选者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究轴子（axion）在暴胀宇宙学中的早期弛豫机制，旨在消除传统轴子模型中衰变常数（decay constant）的宇宙学上限。通过SU(5)大统一理论框架下的高能标禁闭，为轴子提供早期势能并稀释其能量密度。

Method: 在SU(5)大统一理论中实现早期强QCD相，考虑两种机制：1）暴胀子与规范场的直接耦合；2）暴胀时期SU(5)对称性恢复。该方法适用于所有已知不可见轴子实现方案，包括Peccei-Quinn（PQ）型（DFSZ和KSVZ）以及基于QCD规范冗余的两形式规范轴子表述。

Result: 该机制成功消除了轴子衰变常数的宇宙学上限，即使在暴胀期间PQ标量期望值为零时，轴子仍作为良好定义的自由度存在。对于DFSZ情况，该相位由普通夸克凝聚组成，相当于早期宇宙版本的η'介子。

Conclusion: 在所有考虑的场景中，现今的轴子可作为任意大衰变常数下的可行暗物质候选者。该机制通过SU(5)大统一理论中的高能标禁闭实现轴子早期弛豫，为轴子暗物质模型提供了新的宇宙学可行性。

Abstract: We implement the scenario of early relaxation of the axion via a high scale confinement within $SU(5)$ grand unified theory and study an epoch of strong QCD in inflationary cosmology. We consider scenarios in which, during inflation, the $SU(5)$ is either entirely or partially in the confining phase. This generates an early potential for the axion and dilutes its energy density removing any cosmological upper bound on the decay constant. We show that a phase of strong QCD can be realized by at least two mechanisms: 1) A direct coupling between the inflaton and the gauge fields and/or 2) by restoration of the $SU(5)$ symmetry during the inflationary epoch. In the latter case, strong coupling is already achieved via the RG running of the $SU(5)$ gauge coupling. We show that the mechanism works for all known realizations of the invisible axion idea: Peccei-Quinn (PQ) type formulations in which the anomalous global symmetry is realized via additional scalars (DFSZ) or heavy fermions (KSVZ) as well as the two-form gauge axion formulation based entirely on the QCD gauge redundancy without any anomalous global symmetry. Even if the expectation value of the PQ scalar vanishes during inflation, the axion is a well defined degree of freedom represented by the phase of the fermion 't Hooft determinant. For the DFSZ case, this phase is composed out of a condensate of the ordinary quarks, amounting to an early universe version of the $η'$-meson. In all considered scenarios, the present day axion can be a viable dark matter candidate for an arbitrarily large value of the decay constant.

### [24] [Ergodicity breaking in matrix-product-state effective Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26870)
*Andrew Hallam,Jared Jeyaretnam,Zlatko Papić*

TL;DR: 本文证明密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）可作为研究大系统量子热化（quantum thermalization）及其破缺的通用谱探测工具，超越了精确对角化（exact diagonalization）的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体系统中热化及其破缺由中谱本征态（mid-spectrum eigenstates）决定，但这些态通常只能通过精确对角化在小系统中获得，限制了研究规模。

Method: 利用密度矩阵重整化群有效哈密顿量，该对象通常用于变分近似基态，但本文证明其编码了远离平衡动力学的详细信息。在随机场XXZ自旋链（random-field XXZ spin chain）中分析该有效哈密顿量的谱特性。

Result: 有效哈密顿量的谱成功捕获了从热化到多体局域（many-body localized）区域的转变，包括对遍历气泡（ergodic bubbles）的空间分辨探测。该方法还能捕获与量子多体疤痕（quantum many-body scars）相关的弱遍历破缺（weak ergodicity breaking）。

Conclusion: 密度矩阵重整化群有效哈密顿量被确立为研究大系统中量子热化及其破缺的通用谱探测工具，突破了精确对角化的系统尺寸限制。

Abstract: Thermalization and its breakdown in interacting quantum many-body systems are governed by mid-spectrum eigenstates, which are typically accessible only in small system sizes amenable to exact diagonalization. Here we demonstrate that the density-matrix renormalization group (DMRG) effective Hamiltonian, an object routinely used to variationally approximate ground states, encodes detailed information about the dynamics far from equilibrium. In the random-field XXZ spin chain, the spectrum of the effective Hamiltonian is shown to capture the transition from thermal to many-body localized regimes, including spatially resolved probes of ergodic bubbles. Furthermore, the same approach also captures weak ergodicity breaking associated with quantum many-body scars. Our results establish the DMRG effective Hamiltonian as a versatile spectral probe of quantum thermalization and its breakdown in large systems beyond exact diagonalization.

### [25] [Reflections on time-reversal in the Symmetry Topological Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26884)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间反演对称性作为反幺正算符，不适用于基于幺正对称性的通用分析。虽然对称拓扑场论（SymTFT）方法为物相分类提供了统一框架，但未能自然地包含反幺正对称性，因此需要扩展该框架以涵盖此类对称性。

Method: 采用对称性富化的SymTFT方法，首先构建与内部幺正对称性相关的标准SymTFT，然后通过背景时间反演对称性进行富化。详细分析该富化SymTFT的拓扑边界条件，并探讨线算符与非局域弦序参数的关系。

Result: 通过分析富化SymTFT的拓扑边界条件，能够表征保持富化对称性的(1+1)维有能隙相。研究发现，在晶格上，只有当端点算符为厄米算符时，正确的端点电荷才与时间反演电荷一致。

Conclusion: 该方法成功将时间反演对称性纳入SymTFT框架，为理解反幺正对称性在物相分类中的作用提供了系统途径，并揭示了弦序参数在反幺正情况下的微妙性质。

Abstract: Symmetry under time-reversal appears in the microscopic description of many physical systems. In a quantum mechanical setting it acts as an anti-unitary operator, so does not fall under general analyses based on unitary symmetries. In classifying zero temperature phases of matter in (1+1)d lattice models, the role of anti-unitary symmetries is, however, well-understood. In recent years, the Symmetry Topological Field Theory (SymTFT) approach to this classification has given a general framework to understand symmetries as topological defects, but does not naturally include anti-unitary symmetries. Following recent proposals in the literature, we adopt a symmetry-enriched SymTFT for a theory with both internal and time-reversal symmetry. In particular, we take a standard SymTFT associated with an internal unitary symmetry that is then enriched by a background time-reversal symmetry. A detailed analysis of the topological boundary conditions of this enriched SymTFT allows us to characterize the corresponding (1+1)d gapped phases that preserve the enriching symmetry (i.e. those that do not spontaneously break this symmetry in the ground state). Line operators in the SymTFT approach are related to non-local string-order parameters (with charged end-point operators) for SPT phases. These are subtle in the anti-unitary case and we explore them both on the lattice and in the continuum. We include an analysis of unitary string order parameters that reveal the Klein bottle SPT invariant. On the lattice, we show that the correct end-point charge coincides with the time-reversal-charge only when the end-point operator is hermitian.

</details>


### [26] [Nonequilibrium from Equilibrium: Chiral Current-Carrying States in the Spin-1 Babujian-Takhtajan Chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26897)
*Bahar Jafari-Zadeh,Chenan Wei,Hrachya M. Babujian,Tigran A. Sedrakyan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了自旋-1 Babujian-Takhtajan链受其第三守恒荷Q₃形变的情况。研究发现Q₃是无量纲能量流，其局域密度是"修饰的"标量手征性算符而非裸手征性。形变哈密顿量H_α=H+αQ₃提供了一个局域、精确可解的流偏置，导致在临界值α_c=J/(8π)处发生量子相变，从无手征性的临界相转变为同时携带电流和手征性的无能隙手征相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索自旋-1 Babujian-Takhtajan链受其第三守恒荷Q₃形变后的物理性质。特别关注Q₃作为能量流的物理意义，以及形变哈密顿量如何通过重新排序本征态而选择性地使高能电流携带态成为倾斜问题的基态。

Method: 研究方法包括推导第三守恒荷Q₃并证明其作为无量纲能量流的性质。使用热力学贝特拟设（thermodynamic Bethe ansatz）进行解析计算，并通过密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）数值模拟进行验证。分析形变哈密顿量H_α=H+αQ₃的相变行为。

Result: 研究发现量子相变发生在临界值α_c=J/(8π)。当α<α_c时，基态保持未形变的Babujian-Takhtajan相，其低能有效场论由k=2的SU(2) Wess-Zumino-Witten（WZW）模型描述，中心荷c=3/2且⟨Q₃⟩=0。当α>α_c时，系统进入无能隙手征电流携带相，同样具有c=3/2的中心荷。自由能在临界点附近以(α-α_c)²的形式开始变化，而能量流则线性开启。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了自旋-1 Babujian-Takhtajan链受Q₃形变后出现的量子相变现象。形变后的系统在临界值α_c处从无手征性的临界相转变为同时携带电流和手征性的无能隙手征相。最直接的实验实现途径包括光学晶格中的复合自旋-1玻色子，以及基于囚禁离子或超导电路的可编程qutrit模拟器。

Abstract: We study the spin-$1$ Babujian-Takhtajan chain deformed by its third conserved charge $Q_3$. We derive $Q_3$ and show that it is a dimensionless energy current and that its local density is a dressed scalar-chirality operator rather than bare chirality alone, as is the case for the spin-$1/2$ Heisenberg chain. The deformation $H_α=H+αQ_3$ therefore provides a local, exactly solvable current bias: it leaves the eigenstates of the original Hamiltonian unchanged, but reorders them so that selected high-energy current-carrying states become ground states of the tilted problem. Using the thermodynamic Bethe ansatz and confirming the analytical calculations with DMRG, we find a quantum phase transition at $α_c={J}/(8π)$. For $α<α_c$, the ground-state remains the undeformed Babujian-Takhtajan phase whose low-energy effective field theory is described by the $SU(2)$ Wess-Zumino-Witten (WZW) model at level $k=2$ representing a critical phase characterized by a central charge $c=3/2$ and $\langle Q_3\rangle=0$. For $α>α_c$, a finite rapidity interval forms, and the system enters a gapless chiral current-carrying sector described by a $c=3/2$ CFT. Near the threshold, the free energy starts quadratically as a function of $α-α_c$, while the energy current turn on linearly. The scalar chirality turns on at the same threshold, showing that the postcritical sector is simultaneously current-carrying and chiral. The most immediate experimental routes are composite spin-1 bosons in optical lattices, and programmable qutrit simulators based on trapped ions or superconducting circuits.

The ability to tune the normal state resistivity of La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ films to display non-Fermi liquid behavior under such a modest hydrostatic pressure range - only 6 - 8 % of that typically applied via diamond anvil cell (DAC) in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ single crystals to achieve comparable effects - is both noteworthy and unexpected. ### [28] [Exact $\mathbb{Z}_2$ electromagnetic duality of $\mathbb{Z}_2$ toric code is non-Clifford](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28230)
*Ryohei Kobayashi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文证明二维$\mathbb{Z}_2$环面码（toric code）的电磁对偶性（electromagnetic duality）若为内部$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性，则不能由Clifford电路实现，必须是非Clifford电路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维$\mathbb{Z}_2$环面码（toric code）具有交换电性和磁性准粒子的全局对称性，即电磁对偶性（electromagnetic duality）。已知实现方式包括晶格平移对称性、由Clifford电路生成的精确$\mathbb{Z}_4$对称性，以及由非Clifford电路生成的精确$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性。

Method: 通过严格证明方法，针对具有粗粒度平移不变性（coarse translation invariance）的对称性，其中平移量为$l$个晶格单位，且$l$为一般奇数的情况进行分析。

Result: 证明Clifford电磁对偶性不能实现精确的内部$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性。因此，精确的内部$\mathbb{Z}_2$电磁对偶性必须是非Clifford的，而一般内部Clifford实现必然具有$\mathbb{Z}_{2^m}$代数结构，其中$m\ge 2$。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明精确电磁对偶性与电路的Clifford层级（Clifford hierarchy）之间存在意想不到的联系。

Abstract: The 2D $\mathbb{Z}_2$ toric code admits a global symmetry exchanging electric and magnetic quasiparticles, known as electromagnetic duality. Known realizations include lattice translation symmetry, an exact $\mathbb{Z}_4$ symmetry generated by a Clifford circuit, and an exact $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry generated by a non-Clifford circuit. We show that a Clifford electromagnetic duality cannot realize an exact internal $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry. This is proved rigorously for symmetries with coarse translation invariance by $l$ lattice units for generic odd $l$. Therefore an exact internal $\mathbb{Z}_2$ electromagnetic duality must be non-Clifford, whereas generic internal Clifford realization necessarily has $\mathbb{Z}_{2^m}$ algebra with $m\ge 2$. Our result suggests an unexpected connection between exact electromagnetic duality and Clifford hierarchy of circuits.

### [29] [Categorical Time-Reversal Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28720)
*Rui Wen,Sakura Schafer-Nameki*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文将反幺正对称性（如时间反演对称性）纳入范畴对称性分类框架，提出Galois实融合范畴作为反幺正对称性的正确范畴模型，并基于此分类具有反线性对称性的有能隙相。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于范畴对称性（categorical symmetries）的相分类研究主要局限于具有复域上幺正（高阶）范畴对称性的相。本文旨在将时间反演对称性等反幺正对称性（anti-unitary symmetries）纳入该框架，扩展相分类的范畴方法。

Method: 引入实域上的融合范畴（fusion categories over ℝ）作为描述反幺正对称性的物理结构，特别定义了一类Galois实融合范畴（Galois-real fusion categories）。通过模块范畴（module categories）分类具有反线性对称性的有能隙相，并发展对称性拓扑场论（SymTFT）框架。

Result: 建立了Galois实融合范畴作为反幺正对称性的正确范畴模型，提供了包括群论范畴（group-theoretical categories）和实Tambara-Yamagami融合范畴在内的具体实例。证明了通过规范子群（gauging subgroups）产生的反线性对称性对偶性，并展示了Morita等价的反线性对称性源于同一ℤ₂ᵀ-富化SymTFT的不同边界。

Conclusion: Galois实融合范畴为包含反幺正对称性的相提供了系统的范畴描述框架。该工作将范畴对称性方法扩展到实域，建立了反线性对称性的分类理论，并通过SymTFT框架统一了不同对称性描述。

Abstract: The classification of phases using categorical symmetries has greatly expanded the landscape of gapped and gapless phases. So far, however, these developments have largely been restricted to phases with unitary (higher-)categorical symmetries over $\mathbb{C}$. In this work, we incorporate anti-unitary symmetries, such as time-reversal symmetry $\mathbb{Z}_2^T$, and show that the relevant physical structures are naturally described by fusion categories over $\mathbb{R}$. A class of real fusion categories, which we call Galois-real fusion categories, provides the correct categorical model for anti-unitary symmetries. A simple example is the time-reversal symmetry $\mathbb{Z}_2^T$ itself. We discuss the basic structures of real fusion categories and present a range of examples, including the group-theoretical categories $(G^T)^ω$ and $\mathsf{Rep}(G^T)$ associated to anti-linear groups $G^T$, as well as non-invertible time-reversal symmetries described by a real analogue of Tambara--Yamagami fusion categories. We then classify gapped phases enriched with anti-linear symmetries in terms of module categories over Galois-real fusion categories. We furthermore apply the categorical formulation to prove dualities (i.e. gauge or Morita equivalences) of anti-linear symmetries generated by gauging subgroups. Complementing this, we also develop a Symmetry Topological Field Theory (SymTFT) framework, in which Galois-real fusion categories arise as boundary conditions of a $\mathbb{Z}_2^T$-enriched SymTFT. Morita equivalent anti-linear symmetries are shown to arise as different boundaries of the same $\mathbb{Z}_2^T$-enriched SymTFT.

Abstract: Correlated electron systems with topological flat bands show great promise in exploring exotic quantum phenomena. However, such crystalline materials remain rare. Here we report the discovery of a novel material, Cs$_3$V$_9$Te$_{13}$, which unexpectedly exhibits magnetism and significant electron correlations. ### [32] [Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless Quantum Supercriticality in XXZ Heisenberg Spin Chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27789)
*Haoshun Chen,Enze Lv,Ning Xi,Fei Ye,Wei Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究表明，在量子伊辛模型中，对称性破缺的纵向场可以诱导从量子临界点发出的量子超临界区域。本研究旨在探索量子超临界现象是否也存在于自旋-1/2 XXZ模型中，包括伊辛型和BKT型超临界性。

Result: 发现BKT量子临界点具有量子超临界交叉标度 $T \propto h^{2/3}$ 和Grüneisen比标度 $Γ_h \propto T^{-3/2}$，这些标度与伊辛超临界标度不同。然而，BKT和伊辛情况的奇异Grüneisen比标度函数 $φ_Γ(x)$ 都可以用相同的表达式 $φ_Γ(x) \approx x/(1+x^2)$ 近似描述。

In this paper, we show that the QSR also emerges in the spin-1/2 XXZ model, in both the form of Ising and Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless (BKT) supercriticality. Using ground-state and finite-temperature tensor-network methods, we investigate quantum supercritical phenomena near a BKT QCP. We reveal a quantum supercritical crossover scaling $T \propto h^{2/3}$ and a Grüneisen ratio scaling $Γ_h \propto T^{-3/2}$ for the BKT QCP, which differ from the corresponding Ising supercritical scalings. Nevertheless, we find that the scaling function $φ_Γ(x)$ of the singular Grüneisen ratio for both BKT and Ising cases can be approximately described by the same expression $φ_Γ(x) \approx x/(1+x^2)$. Our work extends the study of quantum supercritical phenomena from the Ising to the XXZ Heisenberg model, thereby revealing the presence of BKT quantum supercriticality and broadening the scope of quantum supercritical physics.

</details>


### [33] [Competing interlayer charge order and quantum monopole reorganisation in bilayer kagome spin ice via quantum annealing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27826)
*Kumar Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究利用D-Wave Advantage2量子退火器的双层架构实现了首个可编程双层kagome自旋冰系统，发现了层间耦合驱动的从铁电到反铁电交错电荷序的尖锐相变，并建立了量子自旋冰实验的方法学标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受挫磁体中的磁单极子（magnetic monopoles）是典型的分数化准粒子，但目前缺乏能同时调控其禁闭（confinement）并保持冰规则（ice-rule）物理的实验平台。该研究旨在填补这一空白。

Abstract: Magnetic monopoles in frustrated magnets are paradigmatic fractionalised quasiparticles, yet no experimental platform simultaneously tunes their confinement and preserves ice-rule physics. Here we exploit the native bilayer architecture of a D-Wave Advantage2 quantum annealer to realise the first programmable two-plane kagome spin ice, spanning $1{,}536$ logical spins across a $4\times13\times14$ grid of system size, interlayer coupling, and quantum drive. We find that interlayer exchange drives a sharp transition from ferroelectric to antiferroelectric staggered charge order, an Ice-II phase with no classical or single-layer analogue, with a critical onset at $(J_{\perp}/J_1)^{*} \approx 0.044$ that is stable across five decades of annealing time. Restricting the charge structure factor to ice-rule plaquettes reveals an order-of-magnitude enhancement over conventional all-plaquette estimators, demonstrating that quantum-selected charge order is invisible to defect-diluted probes and establishing a methodological standard for future quantum spin ice experiments. The quantum renormalisation of the monopole chemical potential sets a concrete engineering target for the transmon circuit-QED kagome ice required to enter the monopole deconfinement regime. Three falsifiable predictions follow for existing Ni$_{81}$Fe$_{19}$ nanowire bilayer architectures: a critical interlayer separation, an elevated monopole activation temperature, and an order-of-magnitude enhancement of the Ice-II signal in published X-ray datasets, all testable without new fabrication.

By implementing a direct one-to-one mapping between lattice spins and physical qubits, together with engineered extended couplings, we realize effective dipolar interactions on frustrated lattices comprising more than 400 vertices. Tuning transverse-field fluctuations enables us to probe the real-time dynamics of Dirac-string defects and interacting monopole plasmas. We observe super-diffusive monopole transport, with scaling exponents intermediate between classical diffusion and ballistic motion, indicating dynamics beyond classical stochastic relaxation and consistent with coherent propagation within an emergent gauge manifold. These results establish programmable quantum spin ice as a scalable platform for investigating fractionalized excitations and emergent gauge dynamics in engineered quantum matter.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The layered honeycomb magnet $α$-RuCl$_3$ has attracted intense scrutiny as a prime candidate for realizing the Kitaev quantum spin liquid, yet a consensus on its microscopic Hamiltonian remains elusive due to the material's extreme sensitivity to structural details. Here, we report a comprehensive reexamination of the low-temperature crystallographic and magnetic structures of high-quality $α$-RuCl$_3$ single crystals using unpolarized and polarized neutron diffraction. We confirm a sharp, first-order structural phase transition to the rhombohedral $R\bar{3}$ space group with a pronounced thermal hysteresis. Crucially, using both spherical and longitudinal neutron polarization analysis, we determine the 3D orientation of the ordered magnetic moment without the ambiguity typically arising from domain distributions. We find that the Ru$^{3+}$ magnetic moments in the zigzag phase are tilted by $15.7^\circ$ out of the hexagonal plane and, remarkably, exhibit an additional in-plane twist of $-13.8^\circ$. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激子凝聚（exciton condensation）具有宏观尺度上的均匀相位相干性，但相位因子具有空间依赖性的更奇特量子现象尚未被探索。激子凝聚体能否自发形成具有空间调制相位分布的状态仍是一个开放性问题。

Method: 研究在扭转半导体双层结构（twisted semiconductor bilayers）中探索新型激子密度波，利用这些系统中固有的动力学阻挫（kinetic frustration）来稳定具有非平凡相位模式的激子凝聚体。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了激子凝聚体相位自由度在定义新型关联态中的关键作用，并计算了这些非常规凝聚体中杂质诱导的特征态，为实验探测提供了明确的识别特征。

Abstract: Exciton condensation, characterized by uniform phase coherence across macroscopic length scales, has enabled the discovery of a variety of excitonic states, greatly enriching our understanding of correlated many-body physics. More exotic quantum phenomena are anticipated when the phase factor develops spatial dependence. However, whether excitonic condensates with spatially modulated phase profiles can emerge spontaneously remains an open question. In this work, we uncover novel forms of excitonic density waves featuring nontrivial phase patterns in twisted semiconductor bilayers. Remarkably, we show that kinetic frustration inherent to these systems stabilizes excitonic condensates arranged into a vortex-antivortex lattice. This represents a class of correlated states previously unknown in two-dimensional semiconductors, wherein the phase degrees of freedom of exciton condensates play a defining role. Such states spontaneously break both time-reversal and inversion symmetries, leading to non-reciprocal exciton transport, an effect we term the excitonic diode effect. Furthermore, we compute and identify characteristic impurity-induced states in these unconventional condensates, providing distinct signatures for their experimental detection.

### [37] [Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid and charge-density wave in a quasi-one-dimensional material](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28186)
*Jing Li,Guo-Wei Yang,Bai-Zhuo Li,Yi Liu,Si-Qi Wu,Ji-Yong Liu,Jin-Ke Bao,Xiaoxian Yan,Hua-Xun Li,Jia-Xin Li,Jia-Lu Wang,Yun-Lei Sun,Yi-Ming Lu,Jia-Yi Lu,Yi-Qiang Lin,Hui Xing,Chao Cao,Hao Jiang,Yang Liu,Guang-Han Cao,Hai-Qing Lin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究报道了一种新型准一维材料Cs$_{1-δ}$Cr$_3$S$_3$，首次在一维电子系统中实现了电荷密度波（CDW）态与Tomonaga-Luttinger液体（TLL）态这两种对立量子相的共存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在一维电子系统中，费米液体态通常会因电子相互作用而转变为Tomonaga-Luttinger液体（TLL），或因Peierls不稳定性而转变为绝缘性的电荷密度波（CDW）相。这两种现象通常相互排斥，在真实材料中难以共存。

Method: 研究通过电输运测量和角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）验证TLL行为，观察到温度、偏压和电子能量的幂律标度关系。同时通过结构分析和光学测量证实CDW态的存在，并结合能带结构计算揭示其电子结构特征。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了Cs$_{1-δ}$Cr$_3$S$_3$作为罕见的材料平台，其中对立的费米液体不稳定性可以共存并交织，为一维系统中涌现量子现象的研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: In one-dimensional (1D) electron systems, the Fermi liquid state breaks down due either to electron interactions, which results in a Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid (TLL) state, or to Peierls instability, which leads to an insulating charge-density-wave (CDW) phase. In general, these two phenomena are mutually exclusive, and their coexistence remains elusive in real materials. Here, we report the discovery of a new quasi-1D material, Cs$_{1-δ}$Cr$_3$S$_3$, which unexpectedly exhibits coexistence of the antithetical CDW and TLL states. The CDW state is evidenced by the intra-unit-cell dimerization, and the opening of an optical band gap of $\sim$250 meV. Meanwhile, TLL behaviour is unambiguously demonstrated by the measurements of electrical transport and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, which reveal a power-law scaling with temperature, bias voltage and electron energy. Band structure calculations reveal isolated, linearly dispersive, 1D bands around the Fermi level. For the dimerized CDW phase, the 1D Fermi-surface sheets located at the boundary of the Brillouin zone are gapped from intra-unit-cell bond symmetry breaking. Experimentally, subtle Cs vacancies shift the Fermi level into the linearly dispersive valence band, enabling the observation of TLL behaviour without interrupting the CDW order. This work establishes Cs$_{1-δ}$Cr$_3$S$_3$ as a rare material platform in which the antagonistic Fermi-liquid instabilities coexist and intertwine, opening new avenues for studying emergent quantum phenomena in 1D systems.

### [38] [Superradiant Charge Density Waves in a Driven Cavity-Matter Hybrid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28432)
*Luka Skolc,Sambuddha Chattopadhyay,Filip Marijanović,Qitong Li,Jonathan Keeling,Benjamin L. Lev,Eugene Demler*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出将掺杂、驱动的过渡金属二硫化物耦合到光学腔的平台。利用纳米光栅产生大面内光学动量的电场，使腔光子通过激子-极化子过程（exciton-polaron processes）高效耦合到电子密度涨落。采用线性稳定性分析（linear-stability analysis）确定超辐射有序的阈值并绘制驱动相图。

Result: 研究表明，将光栅周期调谐至匹配增强的电子密度涨落（如维格纳结晶附近的涨落）可显著降低所需的泵浦强度。确定了超辐射有序的阈值并绘制了驱动相图。

Conclusion: 该工作为量子材料中实现腔控电子序（cavity-controlled electronic order）建立了一条新途径，通过纳米光栅解决了光学波长与电子尺度不匹配的问题。

Abstract: Optical cavities enable strong, long-range, light-matter interactions that can drive collective ordering phenomena, such as superradiant self-organization in ultracold atomic gases. Extending these ideas to solid-state electron systems could enable continuous-wave optical control of electronic order, but is impeded by the mismatch between optical wavelengths and electronic length scales. Here, we propose a platform for realizing superradiant charge density waves (sCDWs) in doped, driven transition-metal dichalcogenides coupled to an optical cavity. A nanoscale grating generates electric fields at large in-plane optical momenta, allowing cavity photons to couple efficiently to electronic density fluctuations through exciton-polaron processes. Using a linear-stability analysis, we determine the threshold for superradiant ordering and map out the driven phase diagram. We show that tuning the grating periodicity to match the enhanced electronic density fluctuations - such as those near Wigner crystallization - substantially lowers the required pump intensity. Our results establish a novel route toward cavity-controlled electronic order in quantum materials.

### [39] [High Sensitivity Methodologies to Detect Radio Band Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26848)
*Wei Hong,Peng He,Tong-Jie Zhang,Shi-Yu Li,Pei Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨引力波（GWs）通过Gertsenshtein-Zeldovich效应在脉冲星磁层中转化为电磁信号的可能性，评估FAST和SKA2-MID望远镜对两类引力波源（瞬态事件和随机背景）的探测能力，并提出多种观测方法提升探测灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究聚焦于两颗特定脉冲星（PSR J1856-3754和PSR J0720-3125），采用数值模拟评估FAST和SKA2-MID望远镜的探测能力。提出了四种观测方法以降低甚高频引力波的可探测能量密度极限，其中"多脉冲星多望远镜"（MPMT）方法因允许交叉验证和排除虚假候选而表现最佳。

Result: 在3 GHz频率下近6000小时观测和5σ探测阈值的假设下，瞬态事件的最小可探测特征应变（characteristic strain）预计为hc≈10⁻²³，随机背景为hc≈10⁻³³。在积分时间和转换效率的乐观假设下，射电波段搜索可能接近测试代表性甚高频引力波场景所需的灵敏度。

Conclusion: 脉冲星磁层中的引力波-电磁转换可能对银河系内某些重复快速射电暴（fast radio bursts）的起源具有相关性。射电波段搜索有望达到探测甚高频引力波所需的灵敏度水平，为引力波探测开辟新途径。

Abstract: Gravitational waves (GWs) can resonate with magnetic fields through the Gertsenshtein-Zeldovich effect, producing electromagnetic signals at the same frequency. In pulsar magnetospheres, this conversion may yield a faint radio-band signal that could be detected. In this work, we focus on two specific pulsars, PSR J1856-3754 and PSR J0720-3125, and use numerical simulations to evaluate how well the FAST and SKA2-MID telescopes could detect such signals. We consider transient events, including primordial-black-hole-like mergers, as well as stochastic backgrounds, including primordial GWs. To improve detection sensitivity, we propose four observational methods to lower the detectable energy-density limit of very high-frequency (VHF) GWs; the "Multiple Pulsars with Multiple Telescopes" (MPMT) method performs best because it allows cross-validation and rejection of false candidates. Under the assumption of nearly 6000 hours of observation at 3 GHz and a $5σ$ detection threshold, the minimum detectable characteristic strain is projected to be $h_c \approx 10^{-23}$ for transient events and $h_c \approx 10^{-33}$ for stochastic backgrounds. Under optimistic assumptions on integration time and conversion efficiency, these projections suggest that radio-band searches may approach the sensitivity needed to begin testing representative VHF GW scenarios. More broadly, this conversion in pulsar magnetospheres could be relevant to the origin of some repeating fast radio bursts in the our galaxy.

### [40] [Dynamical tidal response of neutron stars as a probe of dense-matter properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26886)

Motivation: 动力学潮汐形变在双中子星系统晚期旋近阶段发射的引力波中起关键作用，研究旨在系统探索相对论性（动力学和耗散性）潮汐形变如何依赖于中子星内部结构，以理解状态方程对潮汐效应的影响。

Method: 使用两类解析状态方程模型：第一类是基于核物理可观测量参数化的核子模型，包括对称能系数和饱和性质；第二类是夸克物质的玩具模型——MIT袋模型（MIT bag model）。为模拟潮汐耗散，自洽地包含了弱相互作用驱动的体粘性效应贡献，同时考虑了核子和夸克物质状态方程。

Result: 耗散性潮汐对频率和温度敏感，但其幅度（由弱相互作用驱动的体粘性效应预测）在当前研究的状态方程模型中太小，无法被当前或未来观测检测到。然而，保守性动力学潮汐响应函数强烈依赖于对称能斜率和高阶系数。

Conclusion: 引力波观测可通过其对保守性动力学潮汐的影响，用于探测对称能的高阶系数，这为通过引力波数据约束核物质状态方程提供了新途径。

Abstract: Dynamical tidal deformations play a crucial role in the gravitational waves emitted by binary neutron star systems during their late inspiral. In this work, we systematically explore how relativistic (dynamical and dissipative) tidal deformations depend on the internal structure of a neutron star using two analytic classes of equations of state. The first class is a nucleonic model that is parameterized by nuclear physics observables, such as the symmetry energy coefficients and saturation properties. The second class is a toy model of quark matter, the MIT bag model. To model tidal dissipation, we self-consistently include contributions from weak-interaction-driven bulk-viscous effects while considering both the nucleonic and the quark-matter equations of state. The dissipative tide is sensitive to frequency and temperature, but its magnitude, as predicted by weak-interaction-driven bulk-viscous effects, is too small (within the equation-of-state models studied here) to be detectable by current or future observations. However, we find that the (conservative) dynamical tidal response function depends strongly on the slope of the symmetry energy and on higher-order coefficients of the symmetry energy; this implies that gravitational-wave observations could be used to probe higher-order coefficients of the symmetry energy through their effect on the (conservative) dynamical tide.

</details>


### [41] [Covariant Hamiltonian quantization of teleparallel equivalents to general relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26961)
*David Chester,Vipul Pandey*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文构建了一种协变哈密顿量（covariant Hamiltonian）表述，将场强（field strengths）作为速度场，避免了广义相对论（general relativity）中哈密顿量约束导致的"冻结形式主义（frozen formalism）"，为探索非微扰量子引力（nonperturbative quantum gravity）提供了新框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统正则广义相对论（canonical general relativity）和惠勒-德威特方程（Wheeler-DeWitt equation）存在哈密顿量约束导致的"冻结形式主义"问题，而超曲面形变（hypersurface deformations）则产生重叶规范变换（refoliation gauge transformations）。需要构建新的理论框架来避免这些问题。

Method: 采用场强作为速度场构建协变哈密顿量表述，推广了德东德-韦伊力学（De Donder-Weyl mechanics）。结合广义多辛几何（generalized multisymplectic geometry）与协变相空间方法（covariant phase space methods），引入了无优先时间坐标的朝永-施温格型方程（Tomonaga-Schwinger-type equation）。

Result: 由于远平行等效广义相对论（teleparallel equivalents to general relativity）在场强中是二次的，场强哈密顿量密度（field-strength Hamiltonian densities）是非奇异的，避免了来自勒让德简并（Legendre degeneracy）的主要约束。提出了使用重整化超曲面形变生成元（renormalized hypersurface deformation generators）的点分裂正则化（point-splitting regularization）作为超曲面依赖演化的候选方案。

Conclusion: 虽然紫外发散（ultraviolet divergences）、算符域问题（operator domain issues）和反常自由性（anomaly freedom）仍是未解决问题，但该框架为探索经典上等价于广义相对论的非微扰量子引力提供了新途径。

Abstract: A covariant Hamiltonian formulation generalizing De Donder-Weyl mechanics is constructed with field strengths as velocity fields. Since the teleparallel equivalents to general relativity are quadratic in field strengths, the field-strength Hamiltonian densities are non-singular and avoid primary constraints specifically from Legendre degeneracy. In contrast, canonical general relativity and the Wheeler-DeWitt equation have a frozen formalism due to Hamiltonian constraints, while hypersurface deformations give refoliation gauge transformations. We introduce a Tomonaga-Schwinger-type equation without a preferred time coordinate by combining the generalized multisymplectic geometry with covariant phase space methods. Point-splitting regularization with renormalized hypersurface deformation generators is proposed as a candidate for hypersurface-dependent evolution. While ultraviolet divergences, operator domain issues, and anomaly freedom are still open problems, we provide a new framework for exploring nonperturbative quantum gravity that is classically equivalent to general relativity.

In order to eliminate possible coordinate artifacts, the study is formulated in terms of the relative motion between two test particles. The results show that the relative kinetic energy variation exhibits a quartic dependence on the wave amplitude in the regime of low initial velocities. The coefficient of this scaling is found to depend on the multipolar structure of the wave, reflecting the spatial gradients associated with higher polarization modes. It is further shown that the energy memory effect is determined by the integrated tidal field, linking the permanent change in the relative kinetic energy to the history of the spacetime curvature carried by the wave.13

Abstract: We consider static, spherically symmetric solutions of 5D general relativity with magnetic fields governed by nonlinear electrodynamics (NED) with the Lagrangian $L(F)$, $F = F_{AB} F^{AB}$, and show that generic solutions describe either 5D black holes (also called black strings due to a circular extra dimension) or so-called mirror stars (also called topological stars) with perfectly reflecting boundary surfaces. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在线性化量子引力框架下，从粒子在引力场中的拉格朗日量出发，利用外尔引力电磁（Weyl gravitoelectromagnetism）形式体系，推导与引力抗磁耦合相关的相互作用哈密顿量。

Abstract: In the framework of linearized quantum gravity, we investigate the quantum gravitational interaction induced by the gravitodiamagnetic coupling of two massive objects to vacuum fluctuations of the gravitational field. Starting from the Lagrangian of a particle in a gravitational field and employing the formalism of Weyl gravitoelectromagnetism, we derive the interaction Hamiltonian associated with gravitodiamagnetic coupling. Unlike the linear couplings that arise in gravitoelectric and gravitomagnetic interactions, the gravitodiamagnetic coupling depends quadratically on the gravitomagnetic field. Based on this Hamiltonian, we show that, for a spherically symmetric gravitational hydrogen-like system in its ground state, the induced quadrupole moment has the opposite sign to the applied gravitomagnetic field, which is the defining signature of gravitodiamagnetism. Using leading-order perturbation theory, we further obtain an explicit expression for the resulting interaction potential, which is attractive and scales as $r^{-11}$ at all separations, where $r$ denotes the distance between the two objects.

### [47] [Bohmian singularity resolution and quantum relaxation in Bianchi type-I quantum cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27229)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigate cosmological singularity resolution and relaxation dynamics within the Bohmian mechanics via the plane-symmetric Bianchi type-I minisuperspace model in the Wheeler-DeWitt framework of quantum cosmology by constructing wave functions as Gaussian and Lorentzian wavepackets. Our analyses of the corresponding Bohmian trajectories reveal that Gaussian superposition predominantly yields classical singular solutions, with only a low fraction of small-amplitude cyclic trajectories. On the other hand, the Lorentzian wavepacket, characterized by the power-law momentum tail, generates stronger quantum potential barrier and a substantially rich velocity field, producing a significant fraction of non-singular bounce trajectories over extended volume ranges. We further examine quantum relaxation by evolving non-equilibrium distributions under the corresponding guidance dynamics. The Gaussian superposition exhibits laminar flow leading to boundary accumulation and incomplete relaxation, with non-monotonic decay of the $H$-function followed by saturation. In contrast, the Lorentzian wavepacket induces more complex trajectories, yielding monotonic decay of the $H$-function and better, though still incomplete, approach to Born-rule equilibrium. These results demonstrate that the inherent structure of the wave packet governs both singularity resolution and quantum relaxation through the nature of the Bohmian velocity field.

### [48] [The point-particle-limit effective-source approach for computing gravitational self-force in the Lorenz gauge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27284)
*Chao Zhang,Yungui Gong,Xuchen Lu,Wenting Zhou*

Main category: gr-qc

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统有效源方法（traditional effective-source method）受限于复杂的解析表达式和固有的平滑性限制，导致计算成本高昂且实现复杂。这些局限性阻碍了相关研究的进展，需要新的方法来解决这些问题。

Method: 提出点粒子极限有效源方法，通过解析地将有效源尺寸取为零，将问题转化为粒子位置处由局域奇异场（local singular field）控制的推迟度规场（retarded metric field）的明确定义跳跃条件。该方法自然与间断伽辽金方案（discontinuous Galerkin scheme）配对，利用其处理解间断性的内在能力来精确实施跳跃条件。

Result: 将传统和点粒子极限有效源方法应用于计算史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）周围圆形轨道上点粒子的洛伦兹规范（Lorenz gauge）时域引力度规扰动（time-domain gravitational metric perturbation）和引力自作用力（gravitational self-force）。数值结果比较显示点粒子极限有效源方法具有显著优势。

Conclusion: 点粒子极限有效源方法的正确性和效率得到验证，为计算一般测地线轨道（generic geodesic orbits）或长时间自洽轨道演化（long-time self-consistent orbital evolution）建立了数值基础。

Abstract: The traditional effective-source method is hampered by complex analytical expressions and the inherent smoothness limit, which incur high computational costs and complicate implementation. To overcome these limitations, we introduce the point-particle-limit effective source method, which analytically takes the size of the effective source to zero, thereby transforming the problem into a well-defined jump condition of retarded metric field at the particle position governed by the local singular field. This formulation naturally pairs with a discontinuous Galerkin scheme, whose inherent capacity for accommodating solution discontinuities enables highly accurate enforcement of the jump conditions. We apply both the traditional and point-particle-limit effective source method to calculate the time-domain gravitational metric perturbation and gravitational self-force in the Lorenz gauge on a point particle in a circular orbit around a Schwarzschild black hole. The comparison of numerical results shows the excellent advantage of the point-particle-limit effective source method, which validates the correctness and efficiency of the point-particle-limit effective source method and thereby establishes a numerical foundation for computing generic geodesic orbits or long-time self-consistent orbital evolution.

### [49] [Quantizing the exterior region of a Schwarzschild-AdS black hole leads to a resolution of the information paradox on a quantum level](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27339)
*Claus Gerhardt*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过量子引力模型对Schwarzschild-AdS黑洞外部区域进行量子化，解决了量子层面的信息悖论问题。通过内外区域量子化的一致性选择，建立了希尔伯特空间和哈密顿量的幺正等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解决黑洞量子化中的信息悖论问题。具体动机源于在黑洞外部区域量子化过程中，多重度参数$m_i$的选择缺乏明确指导，而内部区域的量子化则提供了自然的选择依据。

Method: 采用量子引力模型对Schwarzschild-AdS黑洞外部区域进行量子化。通过求解双曲方程得到时间本征函数$w_i$和空间本征分布$v_{ij}$的乘积解，其中本征值具有多重度$m_i$。关键方法是将内部区域量子化中通过最大化值选择的$m_i$参数应用于外部区域。

Result: 由于内外区域的时间哈密顿量相同，本征值也相同，这种一致性选择定义了相应希尔伯特空间和哈密顿量之间的幺正等价性。这一结果直接表明在量子层面上不存在信息悖论。

Conclusion: 通过将内部区域量子化中确定的参数选择逻辑应用于外部区域，建立了内外量子描述的幺正等价性，从而在量子引力框架下解决了黑洞信息悖论问题。

Abstract: We quantize the exterior region of a Schwarzschild-AdS black hole using our model of quantum gravity. The resulting hyperbolic equation is solved by products of temporal eigenfunctions $w_i$, the eigenvalues of which all have multiplicity one, and spatial eigendistributions $v_{ij}$ having the same eigenvalues but with multiplicities $1\le m_i$, where the $m_i$ could in principle be arbitrarily large. Regarding only the exterior region, there was no guidance how to determine the values of the $m_i$. However, considering also the quantization of the interior region, where the same question did not arise since the $m_i$ could be chosen by maximizing the value, it seemed logical to choose the same values, too, in the exterior case. Since the eigenvalues in the interior are the same because the temporal Hamiltonian is the same in both cases, this choice defined a unitary equivalence between the respective Hilbert spaces and the respective Hamiltonians. Hence, there is no information paradox on a quantum level.

</details>


### [50] [Continuous Sensitivity Analysis for $δN$ Formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27366)
*S. Mohammad Ahmadi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种系统方法，将连续灵敏度分析（Continuous Sensitivity Analysis）应用于梯度修正的δN形式体系，简化了包含梯度相互作用的宇宙学可观测量计算，并在Starobinsky模型中得到了包含全梯度修正的功率谱解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准δN形式体系依赖于分离宇宙假设（separate universe assumption），忽略了重要的空间梯度相互作用。虽然已有工作通过有效源项将梯度相互作用纳入背景动力学，但实际计算仍然技术挑战性很大，因为宇宙学可观测量需要评估总e-折叠数对初始条件的敏感性。

Method: 本文开发了一种系统方法，将连续灵敏度分析（Continuous Sensitivity Analysis）应用于梯度修正的δN形式体系。该方法通过求解场雅可比矩阵（field Jacobian）和海森矩阵（Hessian）的耦合一阶微分方程组，获得所需的相空间导数。

Result: 该方法显著简化了δN形式体系的解析和数值评估。在Starobinsky模型的显式演示中，得到了包含全梯度修正的k-依赖功率谱解析表达式，并获得了准确捕捉梯度源贡献的等边非高斯性参数f_NL^eq的解析估计。

Conclusion: 所开发的连续灵敏度分析方法为梯度修正的δN形式体系提供了系统简化方案，使包含梯度相互作用的宇宙学可观测量计算更加可行，特别是在具有急剧转变的暴胀模型中。

Abstract: The $δN$ formalism provides a powerful non-perturbative framework for following the evolution of primordial curvature perturbations on super-horizon scales. However, its standard implementation relies on the separate universe assumption, which neglects significant spatial gradient interactions. Recent work has addressed this limitation by incorporating gradient interactions directly into the background dynamics through an effective source term in the Klein--Gordon equation, thereby extending the applicability of the $δN$ framework beyond the separate universe approximation. Despite this conceptual progress, practical calculations within the $δN$ formalism remain technically challenging, as cosmological observables require evaluating the sensitivity of the total number of $e$-folds to initial conditions, a task that becomes even more involved once gradient contributions are included. In this work, we develop a systematic method to simplify these calculations by applying Continuous Sensitivity Analysis to the gradient-corrected $δN$ framework. In this approach, the required phase-space derivatives are obtained by solving a set of coupled first-order differential equations for the field Jacobian and Hessian, which significantly streamlines both analytical and numerical evaluations of $δN$ formalism. As an explicit demonstration, we apply the method to the Starobinsky model, which features a sharp transition into an ultra-slow-roll phase. Within this setup, we derive analytical expressions for the $k$-dependent power spectrum including full gradient corrections, and obtain an analytical estimate of the equilateral non-Gaussianity parameter $f_{\rm NL}^{\rm eq}$ that accurately captures the gradient-sourced contributions.

</details>
