Abstract: Kagome materials provide a powerful platform for exploring how flat electronic bands promote symmetry-breaking quantum states, yet studies have so far focused mainly on kagome-derived $d$-electron flat bands. In this paper, we introduce CeRu$_{3}$Si$_{2}$, a kagome superconductor in which our first-principles calculations show the coexistence of Ru $d$-orbital kagome flat bands and heavy-fermion flat bands derived from Ce$^{4+}$ $4f$-states. Theoretical calculations further highlight the correlated nature of these charge-order states. Deep within the charge-ordered state, magnetoresistance emerges below 80 K and strengthens further below 30 K. Zero-field muon spin-rotation measurements show no time-reversal symmetry (TRS) breaking in the normal state, in contrast to LaRu$_{3}$Si$_{2}$ and YRu$_{3}$Si$_{2}$. However, an applied magnetic field induces weak magnetism. Furthermore, we identify that CeRu$_{3}$Si$_{2}$ is the first 132-type kagome compound to host nodal superconductivity together with spontaneous internal magnetic fields, providing clear evidence for intrinsic TRS breaking in the superconducting state. These results establish CeRu$_{3}$Si$_{2}$ as a unique platform where intertwined kagome $d$- and heavy fermion $f$-electron flat bands generate a rich hierarchy of electronic orders.

Abstract: Understanding the phase diagram of kagome superconductors from a microscopic perspective is crucial for clarifying the interplay between charge order and superconductivity. Ti-doped CsV$_{3}$Sb$_{5}$ exhibits a nonmonotonic temperature-doping phase diagram in which both $T_{\rm c}$ and the charge-order temperature initially decrease with doping, followed by a crossover from long-range to short-range charge order and a subsequent increase in $T_{\rm c}$. Here, we report a muon spin rotation ($μ$SR) study of Ti-doped CsV$_{3}$Sb$_{5}$ at two representative compositions: underdoped (Ti$_{0.05}$-CVS) and optimally doped (Ti$_{0.22}$-CVS). In the superconducting state, both samples exhibit anisotropic nodeless pairing with low superfluid density. Hydrostatic pressure substantially enhances both $T_{\rm c}$ and the superfluid density (by $\sim$2.5), revealing a linear correlation between them and pointing to unconventional pairing. Above $\sim$1 GPa, a crossover from anisotropic to isotropic nodeless pairing is observed. Despite the different nature of charge order in the two doping regimes, the superconducting responses are remarkably similar, suggesting that the competition between superconductivity and charge order occurs on a local scale, largely independent of the long-range coherence of the charge-ordered state.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用同步辐射X射线衍射（synchrotron radiation x-ray diffraction）分析结构稳定性，通过热容（heat capacity）测量确定超导类型，并利用电阻率（electrical resistivity）测量在高达2.5 GPa压力下研究超导临界温度的变化。

Conclusion: 压力对AuxPd1-xTe2的超导性质影响有限，超导特性基本保持不变。通过比较金掺杂与未掺杂PdTe2的实验结果，讨论了Tc的成分依赖性，为理解这一材料体系的超导机制提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Transition metal ditellurides with the CdI2-type structure are materials with intriguing superconducting and electronic properties as demonstrated by PdTe2. Gold substituted PdTe2, AuxPd1-xTe2, adopts the CdI2-type structure for a Pd content larger than 43 at.% at room temperature, and in this range enhanced superconductivity with a critical temperature (Tc) above 4 K has been reported (Kudo et al., PRB 93, 140505, 2016). Here we present the effect of pressure on the structural and superconducting properties of AuxPd1-xTe2 for x=0.15, 0.25 and 0.35 with Tc =2.7, 4.1, and 4.6 K at 1 atm, respectively. Synchrotron radiation x-ray diffraction shows that the CdI2-type structure remains stable up to 8 GPa for all three compositions and that they have almost the same volume compressibility. Heat capacity measurements show that Au substituted PdTe2 exhibits type-II superconductivity, that evolves from weak-coupling BCS for x = 0.15 to strong-coupling for x = 0.25 and 0.35. Electrical resistivity measurements up to a pressure of 2.5 GPa show that Tc(P) for x = 0.25 and 0.35 passes through a shallow maximum of 4.2 and 4.7 K at P ~ 0.3 and 0.7 GPa, respectively, compared to the monotonic decrease for x = 0.15. Furthermore, the pressure variation of the superconducting H - T phase diagram at each composition indicates that the superconducting properties remain essentially unchanged with pressure. The composition dependence of $T_{\rm c}$ is discussed by comparing the experimental results of AuxPd1-xTe2 to those of undoped PdTe2.

### [104] [Pumping of spin supercurrent in unitary triplet superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27945)
*Ping Li,Tao Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在三重态超导体（triplet superconductors）中产生自旋超电流（spin supercurrents）的通用原理，通过类比电荷传输中的安德烈夫反射（Andreev reflection）机制，并假设自旋守恒（spin conservation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超导体中，安德烈夫反射机制能够高效地将正常金属注入的电流转换为超电流（supercurrent），从而保持电荷守恒。本文旨在将这一电荷传输原理推广到自旋自由度，为三重态超导体中的自旋超电流生成提供通用框架。

Method: 基于自旋守恒假设，类比电荷传输中的安德烈夫反射机制，提出生成自旋超电流的通用原理。具体实现方案涉及利用邻近磁性纳米结构（proximity magnetic nanostructure）的磁化动力学 ${\bf M}(t)$，在幺正三重态超导体（unitary triplet superconductors）中高效产生自旋超电流。

Result: 研究发现了一个与三重态超导序参量（triplet superconducting order parameter）成正比的自旋力矩（spin torque），在自旋守恒情景下可将粒子自旋转换为库珀对（Cooper pairs）的自旋。该自旋泵浦（spin pumping）效率不受传统电子自旋泵浦中 $d{\bf M}/dt\times {\bf M}$ 项的限制，这源于涌现的粒子-空穴对称性（emergent particle-hole symmetry）。

Conclusion: 这一通用原理为在许多非常规超导体（unconventional superconductors）中产生和操控无耗散自旋电流（dissipationless spin currents）提供了一种高效方法，超越了传统的电子自旋泵浦机制。

Abstract: One efficient mechanism for generating a charge supercurrent is Andreev reflection, in which the electric current injected from a normal metal into a conventional superconductor is converted into a supercurrent, thereby preserving charge conservation. We here propose a general principle for generating spin supercurrents in triplet superconductors by analogy with such charge transport, i.e., assuming spin conservation. We find a spin torque that is proportional to the triplet superconducting order parameter and, in the spin-conservation scenario, converts the particle spin to that of Cooper pairs. Based on this general principle, we propose an implementation to efficiently generate a spin supercurrent in unitary triplet superconductors, even though Cooper pairs carry no spin polarization at equilibrium, by the magnetization dynamics ${\bf M}(t)$ of a proximity magnetic nanostructure. The efficiency of this spin pumping is not solely limited to the $d{\bf M}/dt\times {\bf M}$ due to the emergent particle-hole symmetry, thereby going beyond the conventional spin pumping of electrons. This general principle provides an efficient approach to generating and manipulating dissipationless spin currents in many unconventional superconductors.

### [105] [Bogoliubov flat bands in twisted layered materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28490)
*Keiji Yada,Yuri Fukaya,Yukio Tanaka*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在扭曲层状d波超导体中，通过调控扭曲角度在Bogoliubov准粒子谱中实现平带（flat bands）的新机制，为超导扭曲电子学（superconducting twistronics）建立了新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平带（flat bands）在凝聚态物理中因其为实现强关联和拓扑量子相提供了肥沃平台而备受关注，但以往研究主要集中于正常态电子结构中的平带。本研究旨在探索超导态中Bogoliubov准粒子谱的平带形成机制。

Method: 通过分析扭曲层状d波超导体（twisted layered d-wave superconductors），研究其Bogoliubov准粒子谱中平带的出现条件。采用低能有效哈密顿量（low-energy effective Hamiltonian）分析，并利用单层系统的贝里联络（Berry connection）作为平带形成的明确判据。

Result: 当超导序参量（superconducting order parameter）在面内C₂旋转下为奇函数时，可以在旋转轴附近设计出Bogoliubov平带（Bogoliubov flat bands）。扭曲角度（twist angle）成为设计无能隙平带超导体（gapless flat-band superconductors）的有效调控参数。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了超导扭曲电子学（superconducting twistronics）的新范式，其中扭曲角度作为设计无能隙平带超导体的强大调控参数，为探索新型超导量子相提供了新途径。

Abstract: Flat bands have attracted considerable interest in condensed matter physics because they provide a fertile platform for realizing strongly correlated and topological quantum phases. To date, however, most studies have focused on flat bands in normal-state electronic structures, such as those found in graphene and transition metal dichalcogenides. In this work, we investigate the emergence of flat bands in the superconducting Bogoliubov quasiparticle spectrum of twisted layered $d$-wave superconductors. We show that when the superconducting order parameter is odd under the in-plane $\mathrm{C}_2$ rotation, Bogoliubov flat bands can be engineered in the vicinity of the rotation axis. By analyzing a low-energy effective Hamiltonian, we demonstrate that the Berry connection of single layer system provides a clear criterion for the formation of the Bogoliubov flat bands. Our results establish a new paradigm of superconducting twistronics, in which the twist angle acts as a powerful tuning parameter for designing gapless flat-band superconductors.

### [106] [Pattern of the Tc(p) dependence with huge "anomaly 1/8" - in new property observed in La2-xBaxCuO4 and YBa2Cu3O6+delta at room temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28641)
*A. V. Fetisov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究发现铜酸盐高温超导体（HTSC）在室温水合过程中，其重量变化与低温超导转变温度Tc(p)的浓度依赖性表现出几乎完全相同的模式，包括"1/8异常"特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜酸盐高温超导体（cuprate HTSCs）的Tc(p)关系呈现穹顶状分布，在p=0.16处达到最大值，并在p=1/8附近出现下降（"1/8异常"），这与CuO2平面中的电荷和自旋有序相关。研究旨在探索这些低温特征在室温条件下的表现。

Method: 通过研究La2-xBaxCuO4和YBa2Cu3O6+δ在室温（RT）及高频磁场影响下的水合过程（hydration process），测量HTSC样品在水合初始阶段的异常重量变化。

Result: 对于两种研究的化合物，重量变化对浓度p的依赖性几乎完全复制了相应Tc(p)依赖关系的模式，包括"1/8异常"。这表明HTSC系统的特征低温特性在室温条件下也有明显表现。

Conclusion: 在室温条件下观察到与低温超导特性相关的特征模式，这一发现对于HTSC理论的进一步发展具有重要意义，为理解高温超导机制提供了新的实验视角。

Abstract: Cuprate HTSCs exhibit a dome-shaped dependence of the superconducting transition temperature on the charge carrier concentration, Tc(p), with a maximum at p = 0.16. Near the composition p = 1/8, a dip in Tc is observed (the "1/8 anomaly"), which is associated with charge and spin ordering in the CuO2 planes. By investigating the hydration process of La2-xBaxCuO4 and YBa2Cu3O6+delta conducted at room temperature (RT) and under the influence of a high-frequency magnetic field, we have discovered unusual weight changes in HTSC samples during the initial stage of hydration. For both studied compounds, the dependence of weight changes on the concentration p was found to almost exactly replicate the patterns of the corresponding Tc(p) dependencies, including the "1/8 anomaly". Such a manifestation of characteristic low-temperature features of HTSC systems at RT is intriguing. The results of this experimental work will be useful for the further development of HTSC theories.

</details>

### [107] [Operator Norm Bounds for Multi-leg Matrix Tensors and Applications to Random Matrix Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27659)
*Benoît Collins,Wangjun Yuan*

Main category: math.OA

TL;DR: 本文研究了算子范数约束下矩阵张量部分迹（partial traces）的极值问题，建立了基于彩色有向图的图形形式体系，推导出精确的极值界，并将其应用于多矩阵随机矩阵理论，扩展了渐近自由（asymptotic freeness）概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究算子范数约束下矩阵张量部分迹的极值问题。这类多线性量在随机矩阵理论和量子信息中具有重要意义，但缺乏系统的分析框架。

Method: 作者开发了全面的图形形式体系（graphical formalism），使用彩色有向图编码多腿部分迹、部分置换（partial permutations）及其矩。通过该框架分析关联图中所有可能内部顶点配对下的最大有向环数。

Result: 证明了部分迹 $(\mathrm{Tr}_{σ_1} \otimes \ldots \otimes \mathrm{Tr}_{σ_k})(A_1, \ldots, A_m)$ 在 $\|A_i\| \le 1$ 约束下的最大值精确等于 $N^{M(σ_1,\ldots,σ_k)}$，其中 $N$ 为维度，$M$ 表示关联图中最大有向环数。进一步推导了部分置换生成矩阵的算子范数估计。

Conclusion: 该图形框架为多矩阵随机矩阵理论提供了强大的组合工具。通过分析 Ginibre 系综模型，将渐近自由概念扩展到矩阵系数代数，严格分离了非交叉配对（non-crossing pairings）与交叉配对（crossing pairings）的渐近行为。

Abstract: We investigate the extremal values of partial traces of matrix tensors under operator norm constraints. To evaluate these multi-linear quantities, we develop a comprehensive graphical formalism that encodes multi-leg partial traces, partial permutations, and their moments using colored directed graphs. With this graphical framework, we establish optimal, sharp bounds for the partial trace $(\mathrm{Tr}_{σ_1} \otimes \ldots \otimes \mathrm{Tr}_{σ_k})(A_1, \ldots, A_m)$ over matrices bounded by $\|A_i\| \le 1$. Specifically, we prove that this maximum evaluates exactly to $N^{M(σ_1,\ldots,σ_k)}$, where $N$ is the dimension and $M$ represents the maximal number of directed cycles in the associated graph across all possible internal vertex pairings. We further derive explicit operator norm estimates for matrices generated by partial traces of partial permutations. Finally, we apply these combinatorial bounds to multi-matrix random matrix theory. By examining models involving Ginibre ensembles, we extend concepts of asymptotic freeness to matrix coefficient algebras, establishing operator norm estimates that rigorously separate the asymptotic behavior of non-crossing and crossing pairings.

</details>

### [108] [Heavy-Meson Bag Parameters using Gradient Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28517)
*Matthew Black,Robert V. Harlander,Jonas T. Kohnen,Fabian Lange,Antonio Rago,Andrea Shindler,Oliver Witzel*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该论文提出将梯度流（gradient flow）与短流时展开（short flow-time expansion）相结合作为四夸克算符矩阵元的重整化方法，应用于中性重介子混合（ΔQ=2）和重介子寿命（ΔQ=0）相关的袋参数计算，并在格点QCD中实现了高精度结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发一种有效的重整化程序来处理四夸克算符矩阵元，这些算符对于理解中性重介子混合和重介子寿命至关重要。传统方法面临幂次发散混合的挑战，需要新的计算框架。

Method: 采用梯度流与短流时展开（GF+SFTX）相结合的重整化方法，使用六个RBC/UKQCD 2+1味畴壁费米子系综进行计算。实施多尺度匹配策略和重整化群改进的流时演化，并利用微扰SFTX系数进行MS-bar方案匹配，达到QCD中的次次领头阶精度。

Result: 对于虚构的中性D_s介子，获得ΔQ=2的MS-bar袋参数B₁(3 GeV)=0.7673(123)，与现有D⁰混合短距离计算结果一致。对于ΔQ=0寿命比算符基，得到MS-bar结果：B₁(3 GeV)=1.0524(97)、B₂(3 GeV)=0.9621(71)、ε₁(3 GeV)=-0.2275(76)、ε₂(3 GeV)=-0.0005(8)。

Conclusion: GF+SFTX方法能够精确确定六维四夸克算符，为未来格点计算建立了框架。该方法将幂次发散混合的挑战转移到连续理论中，并通过SFTX处理，适用于更复杂的算符基计算。

Abstract: We demonstrate the use of the gradient flow combined with the short flow-time expansion (GF+SFTX) as a renormalization procedure for four-quark operator matrix elements and associated bag parameters relevant to neutral heavy-meson mixing ($ΔQ=2$) and heavy-meson lifetimes ($ΔQ=0$). Using six RBC/UKQCD 2+1-flavor domain-wall fermion ensembles, we calculate for a charm-strange system with physical quark masses flowed bag parameters and match them to the $\overline{\text{MS}}$ scheme using perturbative SFTX coefficients up to next-to-next-to-leading order in QCD. We employ a multi-scale matching strategy and a renormalization-group improved flow-time evolution which allows for a reliable estimate of systematic uncertainties. For a fictitious neutral $D_s$ meson, we obtain the $ΔQ=2$ $\overline{\text{MS}}$ bag parameter ${\cal B}^{\overline{\text{MS}}}_1(3\,{\rm GeV})=0.7673(123)$, consistent with existing short-distance $D^0$ mixing determinations. For the $ΔQ=0$ lifetime-ratio operator basis, we find the $\overline{\text{MS}}$ results $B^{\overline{\text{MS}}}_1(3\,{\rm GeV})=1.0524(97)$, $B^{\overline{\text{MS}}}_2(3\,{\rm GeV})=0.9621(71)$, $ε^{\overline{\text{MS}}}_1(3\,{\rm GeV})=-0.2275(76)$, and $ε^{\overline{\text{MS}}}_2(3\,{\rm GeV})=-0.0005(8)$. We provide conversion formulae to re-express these results for an arbitrary choice of evanescent operators. These results demonstrate that GF+SFTX can deliver precise determinations of dimension-six four-quark operators and establish a framework for future lattice computations including more complex operator bases, where the challenge of power-divergent mixing is shifted to the continuum and handled in the SFTX.

</details>

*Anosh Joseph,David Schaich*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究通过晶格模拟（lattice simulation）研究三维最大超对称杨-米尔斯理论（maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory）的非微扰相图，发现空间解禁闭转变温度与全息对偶（holographic duality）的低温大N预测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索三维最大超对称杨-米尔斯理论的非微扰相图（nonperturbative phase diagram），特别是空间解禁闭转变（spatial deconfinement transition）。该转变在全息对偶中对应于对偶引力理论中局域化与均匀化黑膜（localized and homogeneous black branes）之间的转变。

Method: 采用保留部分超对称代数（supersymmetry algebra）的晶格表述（lattice formulation），在有限晶格间距下进行研究。使用SU(8)规范群，晶格尺寸为$N_L^2 \times N_T$，其中$N_T = 8$、$10$和$12$，纵横比$α= N_L/N_T \leq 3$。

Result: 获得的转变温度与全息对偶的低温大N预测$T_c \propto α^3$一致。这一结果为该设定下的规范-引力对应（gauge-gravity correspondence）提供了进一步证据。

Conclusion: 研究通过晶格模拟验证了三维最大超对称杨-米尔斯理论的空间解禁闭转变温度符合全息对偶的预测，为规范-引力对应关系提供了数值支持证据。

Abstract: We present new results from our lattice investigations of maximally supersymmetric Yang--Mills theory in three dimensions, focusing on its nonperturbative phase diagram. Using a lattice formulation that preserves part of the supersymmetry algebra at finite lattice spacing, we study the spatial deconfinement transition, which holography relates to the transition between localized and homogeneous black branes in the dual gravity theory. Our analysis employs $N_L^2 \times N_T$ lattices with $N = 8$ colors in the SU($N$) gauge group, considering $N_T = 8$, $10$ and $12$, in each case with aspect ratios $α= N_L/N_T \leq 3$. The resulting transition temperatures are consistent with the holographic low-temperature, large-$N$ prediction $T_c \propto α^3$, providing further evidence for the gauge--gravity correspondence in this setting.

### [110] [Applying the Worldvolume Hybrid Monte Carlo method to lattice gauge theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28629)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数值符号问题（numerical sign problem）是计算物理中的核心挑战之一。现有方法如Lefschetz-thimble方法存在固有的遍历性问题（ergodicity issues），需要更可靠且计算高效的算法来解决这些问题。

Method: 本文扩展了世界体积混合蒙特卡洛（Worldvolume Hybrid Monte Carlo, WV-HMC）方法，将其应用于群流形（group manifolds）。该方法为格点规范理论（lattice gauge theories）提供了严格的数学框架，避免了传统方法的遍历性问题。

Result: WV-HMC方法被成功扩展至群流形，为格点规范理论的计算提供了可靠且计算高效的算法框架。这一扩展使得该方法能够应用于更广泛的物理系统，同时保持其避免数值符号问题和遍历性问题的优势。

Conclusion: 扩展至群流形的WV-HMC方法为格点规范理论提供了严格的数学框架，解决了数值符号问题和传统方法的遍历性问题，是计算物理中一个有前景的可靠算法。

Abstract: The numerical sign problem remains one of the central challenges in computational physics. The Worldvolume Hybrid Monte Carlo (WV-HMC) method has recently been proposed as a reliable and computationally efficient algorithm that crucially avoids the ergodicity issues inherent in Lefschetz-thimble approaches. In these proceedings, after outlining the key ideas behind WV-HMC, we present its extension to group manifolds. This provides a rigorous framework for applying WV-HMC to lattice gauge theories.

### [111] [Deep brain microelectrode signal: $q$-statistical approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27322)
*Ana Luiza Souza Tavares,Henrique Santos Lima,Artur Pedro Martins Neto,Bruno Duarte Gomes,Constantino Tsallis*

Main category: physics.med-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析帕金森病患者深部脑刺激手术中获得的微电极记录，发现所有记录的振幅统计均服从q-高斯分布（q>1），且q和β参数满足单一函数约束q=3-1.85β^{-0.33}，表明基底节-丘脑-皮层环路存在近临界动力学特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在表征帕金森病患者深部脑刺激手术中获得的微电极记录（MERs）的振幅统计特性，特别关注丘脑底核（STN）内外记录的差异，以探索基底节-丘脑-皮层环路的动力学特征。

Method: 研究分析了46名帕金森病患者的184个微电极记录，其中STN内外记录数量平衡。使用基于非可加熵泛函的q-高斯分布对每个记录的概率密度进行定量描述，并在超统计框架下分析参数关系。

Result: 所有记录的振幅统计均服从q-高斯分布（q>1），反映持久的长程时间相关性。q和β参数在所有184个记录中满足单一函数约束q=3-1.85β^{-0.33}（R≈-0.91），这是近临界动力学的定量标志。q值在STN边界无显著差异，而逆宽度参数β显示适度系统性差异。

Conclusion: q>1本身不足以区分健康与病理状态，但紧密的q(β)耦合关系构成了帕金森病皮质-基底节-丘脑-皮层环路的候选近临界性特征，这一特征先前已在无标度网络增长和材料断裂声学前兆中被识别。

Abstract: We characterize the amplitude statistics of intraoperative microelectrode recordings (MERs) obtained during deep brain stimulation (DBS) surgery in 46 patients with Parkinson's disease, using 184 recordings equally balanced between inside and outside the subthalamic nucleus (STN). The probability density of every recording is quantitatively well described by a $q$-Gaussian (grounded on a nonadditive entropic functional), $ρ(x) \propto [1 + β(q-1) x^2]^{-1/(q-1)}$, with $q > 1$ in all cases, reflecting persistent long-range temporal correlations inconsistent with Gaussian dynamics. Within the superstatistics framework, the slowly fluctuating local variance visible in the raw MER signals is a physical mechanism that directly generates the $q > 1$ form. Beyond individual fits, $q$ and $β$ collapse across all 184 recordings onto the single functional constraint $q = 3 - 1.85\,β^{-0.33}$ ($R \approx -0.91$), a reduction to one effective degree of freedom that is the quantitative hallmark of near-critical dynamics, previously identified in scale-free network growth and in acoustic precursors of material fracture. The index $q$ is statistically indistinguishable across the STN boundary ($\langle\bar{q}_\text{out}/\bar{q}_\text{in} \rangle = 1.03$), while the inverse-widthparameter shows a modest systematic difference ($\langle\barβ_\text{out}/\barβ_\text{in} \rangle = 1.18$). Since $q > 1$ is expected for any brain structure exhibiting long-range correlations, healthy or pathological, it is the tight $q(β)$ coupling, not $q > 1$ per se, that constitutes the candidate near-criticality signature of the parkinsonian cortico-basal-ganglia-thalamocortical loop.

### [112] [Moiré and frustration physics of dipolar supersolids under periodic confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27983)
*Ze-Hong Guo,Kai Gan,and Qizhong Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值求解扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程，分析了二维偶极超固态（dipolar supersolid）在外部周期性约束下的基态相图。重点研究了三角形、蜂窝形和方形光学晶格（optical lattices）对自发超固态序的影响，揭示了软自组织晶格与刚性外势竞争产生的莫尔超结构（moiré superstructures）和重构态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索周期性约束下偶极超固态的基态相行为，特别是自组织软晶格与刚性外势之间的竞争如何产生新颖的物理现象。该研究将这种系统作为探索莫尔物理（moiré physics）的非传统途径。

Method: 研究方法采用数值求解扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程（extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation），分析二维偶极超固态在三角形、蜂窝形和方形光学晶格约束下的行为。研究参数包括晶格深度V₀和本征液滴间距与外部晶格周期的可公度比（commensurability ratio）。

Result: 研究结果表明，在三角形和蜂窝形约束下，软自组织超固态晶格与刚性外势的竞争可在弱至中等晶格深度区域产生长波长莫尔超结构，并出现环状团簇（ring-like clusters）和条纹段构型（stripe-segment configurations）等重构态序列。方形晶格则因C₆本征序与C₄几何结构间的对称性失配（symmetry mismatch），导致受挫诱导的各向异性态（frustration-induced anisotropic states）和对称性降低的团簇排列。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，周期性约束下的偶极超固态为探索莫尔物理提供了非传统途径，其中莫尔超结构源于自组织软晶格与外部强加刚性晶格之间的竞争。该研究建立了不同晶格几何对超固态相行为影响的系统分类框架。

Abstract: We study the ground-state phases of a two-dimensional dipolar supersolid subjected to external periodic confinement by numerically solving the extended Gross--Pitaevskii equation. Focusing on a regime in which the unconfined system forms an intrinsic triangular droplet crystal, we consider triangular, honeycomb, and square optical lattices and classify them into isostructural and heterostructural settings relative to the spontaneous supersolid order. We map out the stationary states as functions of the lattice depth $V_0$ and the commensurability ratio between the intrinsic droplet spacing and the external lattice period. For triangular and honeycomb confinements, the competition between the soft self-organized supersolid lattice and the rigid external potential can generate long-wavelength moiré superstructures in the weak- to intermediate-lattice regime, together with a sequence of reconstructed states including ring-like clusters and stripe-segment configurations. By contrast, the square lattice introduces strong symmetry mismatch between the intrinsic $C_6$ order and the imposed $C_4$ geometry, leading to frustration-induced anisotropic states and symmetry-reduced cluster arrangements. Our results establish dipolar supersolids under periodic confinement as an unconventional route to exploring moiré physics, where moiré superstructures arise from the competition between a self-organized soft lattice and an externally imposed rigid one.

### [114] [Simulating cavity QED with spin-orbit coupled Bose-Einstein condensates revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28368)
*Muhammad S. Hasan,Karol Gietka*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究评估了自旋轨道耦合玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（spin-orbit coupled Bose-Einstein condensates）模拟腔量子电动力学（cavity quantum electrodynamics）现象的潜力与局限，发现其能准确模拟单原子与量子化场耦合的物理（量子拉比模型），但无法再现迪克模型（Dicke model）的集体效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合成平台模拟腔量子电动力学为探索无真实光子的光-物质相互作用提供了新途径，同时可将腔基技术移植到其他系统。自旋轨道耦合玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体作为可控平台，其内部自由度与运动自由度耦合，可模拟腔量子电动力学的某些方面。

Method: 研究批判性评估了自旋轨道耦合玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体模拟腔量子电动力学现象的程度，重点关注压缩（squeezing）和纠缠生成（entanglement generation）效应。

Result: 研究表明，自旋轨道耦合玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体能忠实再现单原子与量子化场耦合的物理，实现量子拉比模型（quantum Rabi model）的类似物，但本质上无法捕捉迪克模型特有的集体效应，如腔介导的多体纠缠（cavity-mediated many-body entanglement）。

Conclusion: 结果阐明了自旋轨道耦合玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体作为腔量子电动力学模拟器的潜力与根本局限性，为未来在无光子、高度可调平台中生成和控制物质的非经典态提供了指导。

Abstract: Simulating cavity quantum electrodynamics in synthetic platforms offers a promising route to exploring light-matter interactions without real photons, while enabling the transfer of cavity-based techniques to other systems. Among such platforms, Bose-Einstein condensates with synthetic spin-orbit coupling provide a controllable setting where internal and motional degrees of freedom become coupled, mimicking aspects of cavity quantum electrodynamics. In this work, we critically assess the extent to which spin-orbit coupled Bose-Einstein condensates can emulate cavity quantum electrodynamics phenomena, with a focus on squeezing and entanglement generation. We show that spin-orbit coupled Bose-Einstein condensates can faithfully reproduce the physics of a single atom coupled to a quantized field, realizing an analogue of the quantum Rabi model but inherently fail to capture genuine collective effects characteristic of the Dicke model, such as cavity-mediated many-body entanglement. Our results clarify both the potential and the fundamental limitations of spin-orbit coupled Bose-Einstein condensates as analogue quantum simulators of cavity quantum electrodynamics, offering guidance for future strategies to generate and control non-classical states of matter in photon-free, highly tunable platforms.

</details>


### [115] [Emergence of a molecular quantum liquid in one dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28635)
*Rajashri Parida,Biswajit Paul,Harish S. Adsule,Diptiman Sen,Tapan Mishra,Adhip Agarwala*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 研究一维硬核玻色子（或自由无自旋费米海）在仅作用于二点子群上的最近邻吸引Hubbard型相互作用下的相行为。系统在大吸引相互作用下形成二聚体分子流体，但在中等吸引势时出现相分离区域，其中系统处于吸收态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究强相互作用一维系统中分子形成的物理机制，特别关注仅作用于二点子群的最近邻吸引相互作用如何影响硬核玻色子（或自由无自旋费米海）的相行为。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group）研究和有效低能哈密顿量（effective low-energy Hamiltonians）分析，分离量子过程以揭示分子形成的物理机制。

Result: 系统在大吸引相互作用下稳定形成二聚体分子流体，其复合分子具有有效弱跳跃尺度和由虚量子涨落主导的排斥相互作用。在中等吸引势时，系统实现相分离区域，其中系统处于吸收态，这是由于二聚体之间出现的吸引相互作用导致局部电荷密度波（charge-density wave）池，粒子有效聚集于局部半填充状态。

Conclusion: 分子超流体在添加未配对原子时会自发电荷有序化，反映了系统对孤立原子存在的极端敏感性。研究揭示了强相互作用一维系统中分子形成的量子过程物理机制。

Abstract: We investigate the fate of a one-dimensional lattice superfluid formed by hard-core bosons, aka `atoms' (alternatively, a free spinless Fermi sea) subjected to nearest-neighbor attractive Hubbard-like interactions only in subgroups of two sites. The system, as expected, stabilizes a fluid of dimerized molecules at large attractive interactions. However, the composite molecules have an effective meek hopping scale and dominant repulsive interactions solely due to virtual quantum fluctuations. Interestingly, at an intermediate attractive potential, the system realizes a phase-separated region where the system is in an absorbing state. We show that this phase-separated region is due to an emergent attractive interaction between the dimers which leads to a local charge-density wave puddle where particles effectively cluster with local half-filling. Moreover the molecular superfluid gets spontaneously charge-ordered in the addition of an unpaired atom, reflecting the extreme sensitivity of the system to the existence of lone atoms. Using density-matrix renormalization group studies and effective low-energy Hamiltonians, we isolate the quantum processes to uncover the physics behind molecule formation in a strongly interacting one-dimensional system.

### [116] [Anomalous phonon dispersion near yielding in athermal crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26825)
*Fumiaki Nakai,Michio Otsuki,Kuniyasu Saitoh,Hiroaki Katsuragi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有序非热固体（ordered athermal solids）在屈服点附近的振动特性尚未得到充分理解，需要揭示其屈服机制的本质特征。

Method: 通过分析剪切晶体（sheared crystal）的振动模式，研究波数空间（wave number space）中的低频区域形成机制，并解析推导相关的标度律（scaling laws）。

Result: 屈服由方向性扩展的多模软化（directionally extended multimode softening）主导，形成十字形低频区域；沿软化方向声学色散从ω∼k变为ω∼k²；振动态密度从德拜标度（Debye scaling）过渡到非德拜标度（non-Debye scaling），并伴随发散的长度尺度（diverging length scale）。

Conclusion: 有序非热固体的屈服机制本质上是方向性扩展的多模软化过程，这一发现通过解析推导的标度律得到了理论验证，深化了对固体屈服行为的理解。

Abstract: Vibrational properties of ordered athermal solids near yielding remain poorly understood. We show that yielding in a sheared crystal is governed not by a single localized instability but by directionally extended multimode softening that forms a cross-shaped low-frequency region in wave number space. Near yielding, the acoustic dispersion $ω\sim k$ is replaced by $ω\sim k^2$ along the soft direction, and the vibrational density of states crosses over from Debye to non-Debye scaling, with a diverging length scale. We analytically derive these scaling laws.

### [117] [Bubble-induced versus thermodynamic voltage losses during pressurized alkaline water electrolysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26855)
*Hannes Rox,Feng Liang,Robert Baumann,Mateusz M. Marzec,Krystian Sokołowski,Xuegeng Yang,Andrés F. Lasagni,Roel van de Krol,Kerstin Eckert*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了压力对水电解（water electrolysis）中气泡行为及效率的影响，发现高压下气泡尺寸减小可降低气泡诱导的电压损失，从而补偿热力学电压损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为实现可再生能源驱动的经济性氢能生产，需要深入理解气泡对水电解效率的影响。高压电解可降低机械压缩成本，因此需研究绝对压力对电化学性能和气泡尺寸的作用机制。

Method: 采用直接激光写入（Direct Laser Writing）技术制备不同尺寸的柱状图案镍电极，在1-6 bar压力范围内研究气泡尺寸变化。通过测量不同电流密度下的阴极电位，分析压力对电压损失的影响。

Result: 气泡尺寸随压力增加而减小，且柱状结构尺寸增大时气泡在所有压力下均变大。在-25 mA/cm²电流密度下，阴极电位随压力增加符合能斯特方程（Nernst equation）预测的热力学电压损失（约23 mV）。令人意外的是，在100 mA/cm²高电流密度下，过电位降低达约60 mV。

Conclusion: 压力增加导致气泡尺寸减小，从而最小化气泡引起的电压损失，补偿了热力学电压损失。应用白金汉π定理（Buckingham Π-theorem）可推导无量纲数来表征气泡诱导与热力学电压损失的比例关系。

Abstract: Understanding how bubbles influence the efficiency of water electrolysis is crucial to achieve economically competitive hydrogen, generated by renewable energy sources, such as wind and solar power. Water electrolysis is typically performed at high pressures to reduce the cost of energy-intensive mechanical compression of the produced H2. Thus, a better understanding of how the absolute pressure affects electrochemical performance and bubble size is necessary. In general, bubble sizes decrease as the pressure increases. Using different-sized pillar-patterned Ni electrodes generated by Direct Laser Writing, the detached bubble sizes can be modified even at elevated pressures. As the pillar size increases, the bubbles become larger at all pressures investigated from 1 to 6 bar. At a current density of -25 mA/cm2, the cathodic potential increases with pressure according to the thermodynamic voltage losses given by the Nernst equation (~ 23 mV at p = 6 bar). Surprisingly, increasing the current density to 100 mA/cm2 leads to a reduction of the overpotential by up to ~ 60 mV. Reduced bubble sizes at increased pressures minimize the losses caused by the bubbles, thereby compensating for the thermodynamic voltage penalty. Applying the Buckingham Π-theorem enables the derivation of dimensionless numbers to characterize the ratio of bubble-induced and thermodynamic voltage losses

</details>

*Pengju Wu,Jie Du,Liang Yao,Hang Li,Xiaodong Zhou,Tao Zhu,Wenhong Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles investigation）系统研究了25种Co基全赫斯勒合金Co2YZ（Y = V, Cr, Mn, Fe, Co; Z = Al, Ga, Si, Ge, Sn）。通过筛选识别出具有大磁致伸缩的化合物，并探索了两种工程化调控策略：费米能级调控和自旋轨道耦合增强。

Conclusion: 本研究不仅识别了新型磁致伸缩应用候选材料，还建立了清晰的物理基础设计原则，为加速发现新型功能磁性材料提供了指导。研究揭示了磁致伸缩性能与材料组成之间的可预测关系，为材料设计提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The pursuit of high-performance, rare-earth-free magnetostrictive materials is crucial for advancing technologies in sensing, actuation, and microelectromechanical systems. Heusler alloys represent a promising, yet underexplored, class of materials for this purpose. In this work, we perform a systematic first-principles investigation of the magnetostrictive properties of 25 Co-based full Heusler alloys, Co$_2$YZ (Y = V, Cr, Mn, Fe, Co; Z = Al, Ga, Si, Ge, Sn). Our screening identifies 10 compounds with large predicted magnetostriction ($|λ_{001}| > 100$~ppm), highlighted by Co$_3$Si with a giant value of -966~ppm. Furthermore, we demonstrate two effective strategies for engineering magnetostriction: (i) tuning the Fermi level, which enhances the magnetostriction of Co$_3$Sn to -905~ppm via Sb doping, and (ii) amplifying the spin-orbit coupling, which boosts the magnetostriction of Co$_2$CrGa to a colossal -1008~ppm through Re substitution. Our analysis reveals a general predictive rule, uncovering a linear relationship between the magnetostriction and the choice of the Y-site transition metal. This work not only identifies novel candidates for magnetostrictive applications but also establishes clear, physically-grounded design principles to accelerate the discovery of new functional magnetic materials.

### [119] [Electrostatic Effects of Self Trapped Holes in Gallium Oxide Devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26958)
*Nathan Wriedt,Joe McGlone,Davide Orlandini,Siddharth Rajan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和理论分析，揭示了氧化镓（gallium oxide）器件中光生自陷空穴（self-trapped holes）通过福勒-诺德海姆隧穿（Fowler-Nordheim tunneling）机制影响器件静电特性和电流传导的物理机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氧化镓作为超宽禁带半导体（ultra-wide bandgap semiconductor）在功率电子和紫外-C（UV-C）光电子领域具有优异性能，但其在光照下的行为机制尚不明确。研究旨在探究光生自陷空穴如何影响氧化镓器件的静电特性和电流传导。

Method: 采用具有半透明镍阳极的垂直肖特基光电二极管（vertical Schottky photodiode），在暗态和带隙以上光照条件下进行电容-电压（capacitance-voltage）、电流-电压（current-voltage）以及温度依赖的I-V测量。通过应用福勒-诺德海姆隧穿理论分析光电流增益（photocurrent gain）。

Result: 传统镜像力势垒降低模型（image-force barrier-lowering models）需要不切实际的高界面电场，表明存在替代机制。福勒-诺德海姆隧穿理论成功解释了测量的光电流和光电容结果，获得了物理上合理的电场值，并量化了自陷空穴的二维浓度（two-dimensional concentration）。

Conclusion: 光照诱导的电荷显著改变器件静电特性。理解这种基于隧穿的光电流增益机制对于设计用于UV-C探测器和功率电子的氧化镓器件至关重要。

Abstract: Gallium oxide is an ultra-wide bandgap semiconductor with exceptional properties for power electronics and UV-C optoelectronics, but its behavior under illumination remains poorly understood. In this work, we investigate how optically generated self-trapped holes influence electrostatics and current conduction in gallium oxide devices. Using a vertical Schottky photodiode with a semi-transparent Ni anode, we performed capacitance-voltage, current-voltage, and temperature-dependent I-V measurements under dark and above-bandgap illumination. Analysis of photocurrent gain reveals that conventional image-force barrier-lowering models require unrealistically high interfacial electric fields, suggesting the presence of an alternative mechanism. By applying Fowler-Nordheim tunneling theory, we reconcile measured photocurrents and photo-capacitance results with physically plausible fields and quantify the two-dimensional concentration of self-trapped holes. Our findings demonstrate that illumination-induced charge significantly alters device electrostatics. Understanding this tunneling-based photocurrent gain mechanism is critical for designing gallium oxide devices for UV-C detectors and power electronics.

### [120] [Heterointerface-Engineered Electrochemically Exfoliated MoS2/WS2 2D-Layered Nanocomposite for Efficient Visible-Light Photocatalytic Degradation of Sorafenib](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26960)
*I. Agnes Felicia Roy,Kuo Yuan Hwa,Aravindan Santhan,Slava V Rotkin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过电化学剥离法制备了MoS2/WS2异质结构纳米复合材料，用于可见光催化降解抗癌药物索拉非尼，在2小时内实现了约92%的降解效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水体中药污染物日益增多引发环境担忧，特别是索拉非尼（sorafenib）等持久性抗癌药物难以通过常规方法有效去除，需要开发高效降解技术。

Method: 采用电化学剥离法（electrochemical exfoliation method）制备超薄MoS2/WS2二维/二维层状纳米复合材料，通过场发射扫描电子显微镜（FE-SEM）、原子力显微镜（AFM）、拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）和紫外-可见光谱（UV-visible spectroscopy）进行结构表征。

Result: MoS2/WS2异质结构复合材料表现出显著增强的光催化性能，在可见光照射下2小时内实现约92%的索拉非尼降解，远优于纯MoS2和WS2纳米片。

Conclusion: 电化学剥离的MoS2/WS2异质结构复合材料可作为有效催化平台去除持久性药物污染物，其优异性能源于界面形成的Type-II能带排列（Type-II band alignment）促进电荷分离和抑制电子-空穴复合。

Abstract: The increasing prevalence of pharmaceutical contaminants within the aquatic environment has generated considerable environmental concerns, especially regarding persistent anticancer medications like the kinase inhibitor sorafenib (SRF), which are inadequately eliminated by standard degradation methods. A heterointerface-engineered MoS2/WS2, 2D/2D layered nanocomposite was fabricated using an electrochemical exfoliation method to facilitate effective visible-light-driven photocatalytic degradation of SRF. The electrochemical exfoliation method yielded ultrathin 9.62-layer thickness MoS2/WS2 nanosheets with numerous exposed edge sites and an increased specific surface area, facilitating the development of well-interconnected van der Waals heterointerfaces. Comprehensive structural and morphological examinations utilizing field emission scanning electron microscopy (FE-SEM), atomic force microscopy (AFM), Raman spectroscopy, and UV-visible spectroscopy validated the effective synthesis of few-layer nanosheets and their heterostructure interfaces. In contrast to the pure MoS2 and WS2 nanosheets, the MoS2/WS2 heterostructure composite demonstrated significantly enhanced photocatalytic efficacy, attaining roughly 92 % degradation of SRF within 2h under visible-light exposure. The enhanced catalytic efficiency is mainly due to the establishment of a Type-II band alignment at the MoS2/WS2 interface, facilitating effective charge separation and directional charge transfer while inhibiting electron-hole recombination. The robust interfacial interaction among the transition metal dichalcogenide layers accelerates visible-light absorption and the production of reactive oxygen species. This study illustrates that electrochemically exfoliated MoS2/WS2 heterostructure composites serve as a viable catalytic platform for the successful removal of persistent pharmaceutical pollutants.

</details>


### [121] [Channeling-in channeling-out revisited: selected area electron channeling and electron backscatter diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27082)
*T. Ben Britton,M. Haroon Qaiser,Ruth M. Birch*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过结合选区电子通道花样（SA-ECP）与电子背散射衍射（EBSD）技术，直接探测了通道效应（channeling-in）对EBSD信号的显著影响，揭示了常规分析中常被简化的动力学效应的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扫描电子显微镜结合电子背散射衍射（EBSD）和电子通道技术能提供丰富的晶体学衬度，但在定量分析中，通道效应（channeling-in和channeling-out）的相互影响常被简化或忽略。本研究旨在直接探究通道效应对EBSD信号的具体影响。

Method: 采用选区电子通道花样（SA-ECP）技术，从单晶硅片上获取数据，同时在每个入射束方向记录EBSD花样。通过比较基于Hough变换的质量指标（花样质量、带衬度、带斜率）、花样匹配互相关系数以及基于傅里叶变换的信噪比，分析通道效应的影响。

Result: 所有分析指标均显示出强烈的晶体学调制，这些调制遵循底层ECP结构，在原始和背景校正后的花样中均可见。类似的广角通道特征也出现在常规低倍EBSD图中，表明通道效应在常规映射条件下同样相关，而不仅限于专门的ECP实验。

Conclusion: 通道效应能显著影响基于质量的EBSD数据解释，对花样模糊分析、高分辨率应变映射以及依赖衍射花样细微变化的统计或机器学习方法均有影响。提出的SA-ECP与EBSD结合策略为可视化并控制SEM中的通道效应耦合提供了实用框架，为设计实验和探测器配置提供了新途径。

Abstract: Scanning electron microscopy combined with electron backscatter diffraction (EBSD) and electron channeling provides rich crystallographic contrast, but the mutual influence of channeling-in and channeling-out is often simplified or neglected in quantitative analyses. In this work, we use selected-area electron channeling patterns (SA-ECPs) acquired from a single-crystal silicon wafer while recording an EBSD pattern at every incident beam direction, thereby directly probing how channeling-in affects the EBSD signal. We show that common Hough-based quality metrics (pattern quality, band contrast, and band slope), pattern-matching cross-correlation coefficients, and Fourier-based signal-to-noise ratios all exhibit strong crystallographic modulations that follow the underlying ECP, in both raw and background-corrected patterns. Similar wide-angle channeling features are also visible in conventional, low-magnification EBSD maps, indicating that channeling-in effects are relevant under routine mapping conditions and not only in specialized ECP experiments. These observations highlight that channeling-in can significantly bias quality-based interpretation of EBSD data, with consequences for methods such as pattern blurring analysis, high-resolution strain mapping, and emerging statistical or machine-learning approaches that rely on subtle variations in diffraction patterns. The combined SA-ECP and EBSD strategy presented here offers a practical framework to visualize and potentially control channeling-in/channeling-out coupling in the SEM, suggesting new routes to design experiments and detector configurations that either mitigate or intentionally exploit these dynamical effects.

</details>


### [122] [The switching of bipolar and unipolar magnetostriction in polycrystalline ZnO film](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27246)
*Suman Guchhait,Saumen Chaudhuri,A. K. Das*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究报道了室温下多晶ZnO薄膜的磁致伸缩特性，通过自主研发的光学悬臂梁磁强计（CBM）装置，测量了面内磁场旋转0-90度时的磁致伸缩行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索多晶ZnO薄膜在面内磁场旋转条件下的磁致伸缩特性，为微纳电子器件中的传感器和执行器应用提供材料基础。

Method: 采用自主研发的光学悬臂梁磁强计（optical cantilever beam magnetometer, CBM）装置，在室温下测量多晶ZnO薄膜在面内磁场旋转0-90度时的磁致伸缩响应。

Result: 研究发现薄膜表现出双极（拉伸和压缩）和单极（拉伸/压缩）磁致伸缩特性，且随着面内磁场旋转角度变化，观察到双极和单极磁致伸缩的切换行为。

Conclusion: 磁致伸缩的切换行为归因于材料的晶体各向异性，双极和单极磁致伸缩特性的出现使ZnO薄膜成为适用于微纳电子器件中传感器和执行器制造的理想候选材料。

Abstract: We report the investigation of magnetostrictive property of polycrystalline ZnO film at room temperature on rotating a magnetic field in the plane of the film from 0 deg to 90 deg by an indigenously developed optical cantilever beam magnetometer (CBM) setup. In this study, the film exhibits bipolar (tensile & compressive) and unipolar (tensile/compressive) nature of magnetostriction with the angle of rotation of in-plane magnetic field. Moreover, we observe switching behavior of bipolar and unipolar magnetostriction as the applied field is rotated in the plane of the film. The switching of magnetostriction is attributed to the crystal anisotropy of the material. The appearance of bipolar and unipolar magnetostriction has made the ZnO film a suitable candidate for the fabrication of sensors as well as actuators applicable in micro and nano-electronic devices.

### [123] [Designing dislocation-driven polar vortex networks in twisted perovskites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27272)

Abstract: Twisting two atomic layers produces a geometric moire pattern, but bonding-induced interfacial reconstruction fundamentally transforms this into an ordered dislocation network - a distinction obscured in weakly-bonded van der Waals systems. Although in-plane topological vortex nanostructures arising from twisting-induced lateral strain modulation have been linked to periodic moire patterns in freestanding perovskite layers and 2D bilayers, their coupling to the interfacial dislocation network in twisted layers remains unresolved. Here we demonstrate that twisting freestanding SrTiO3 layers undergo interfacial reconstruction into a network of screw dislocations, accompanied by the emergence of in-plane topological vortices. Unlike in previous reports, these vortices are associated with the periodicity of the dislocation network rather than with geometric moire patterns. Four-dimensional scanning transmission electron microscopy (4D-STEM) reveals long-range ordered vortex-antivortex arrays with nearly continuous polarisation rotation. A machine-learning interatomic potential, trained on first-principles calculations, together with phase-field modelling, confirms that competing strains within the dislocation network stabilize polar vortex-antivortex pairs and drive the emergence of an electronic superlattice with a well-defined periodicity. Our results establish twist-controlled dislocation networks as a new and versatile route to designing local polar and electronic structures in oxide materials.

### [124] [Low-scaling \textit{GW} calculation of quasi-particle energies within numerical atomic orbital framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27292)
*Min-Ye Zhang,Peize Lin,Rong Shi,Xinguo Ren*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于数值原子轨道（NAO）基组框架的低标度空间-时间GW算法，通过局部分辨恒等式（LRI）技术将极化函数和自能计算复杂度从传统O(N⁴)降低到O(N²)或更好，实现了大尺度系统的GW计算效率提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GW近似下的多体微扰理论是描述真实材料电子能带结构的常用方法，但其高计算成本阻碍了在大尺度系统中的应用。传统实现中的极化函数和GW自能计算具有O(N⁴)的标度，限制了该方法的应用范围。

Method: 提出了基于数值原子轨道（numerical atomic orbital, NAO）基组框架的空间-时间算法，通过在实空间中计算极化函数和自能，利用局部分辨恒等式（localized resolution of identity, LRI）技术构建低标度算法。该算法在LibRPA库中实现并与FHI-aims代码包接口。

Result: 基准计算表明，低标度实现产生的准粒子能量与FHI-aims中先前实现的传统O(N⁴) k空间形式非常一致。对于研究系统，观察到的整体标度相对于规范方法显著降低，且在少于100个原子的系统中即显示出优势。

Conclusion: 基于NAO的LRI增强空间-时间GW算法成功将极化函数和自能计算复杂度从O(N⁴)降低到O(N²)或更好，为GW方法在大尺度系统中的应用提供了高效计算框架。

Abstract: The many-body perturbation theory within the $GW$ approximation is a widely used method for describing the electronic band structures in real materials. Its application to large-scale systems is, however, impeded by its high computational cost. The rate-limiting steps in a typical $GW$ implementation are the evaluation of the polarization function under the random phase approximation (RPA) and the evaluation of the $GW$ self-energy, both of which have a canonical $O(N^4)$ scaling with $N$ being the system size. The conventional space-time algorithm within the plane-wave basis sets reduces the scaling from $O(N^4)$ to $O(N^3)$, albeit with a large prefactor and increased memory cost. Here, we present a space-time algorithm within the numerical atomic orbital (NAO) basis-set framework, for which the evaluation of the polarization function and self-energy is formally reduced to $O(N^2)$ or better with respect to system size. This is achieved by computing these quantities in real space, where low-scaling algorithms can be formulated by leveraging the localized resolution of identity (LRI) technique. The resulting NAO-based, LRI-enhanced space-time $GW$ algorithm has been implemented in the LibRPA library interfaced with the FHI-aims code package. Benchmark calculations for crystalline solids show that the low-scaling implementation yields quasi-particle energies in close agreement with the conventional $O(N^4)$ k-space formalism previously implemented in FHI-aims. For the systems studied here, the observed overall scaling is substantially reduced relative to the canonical approach, and the low-scaling implementation becomes advantageous already for systems containing fewer than 100 atoms.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在GaAs(001)衬底上生长单晶FeCo薄膜，通过改变Co浓度（x）进行合金化。使用自旋轨道铁磁共振（spin orbit ferromagnetic resonance）技术测量朗德g因子（Lande g factor）、吉尔伯特阻尼（Gilbert damping, α）和界面自旋轨道场（interfacial spin orbit fields）。

Here, we demonstrate that the interfacial spin orbit interaction (SOI) in single crystalline FeCo thin films grown on GaAs(001) can be continuously tuned via alloying. Using spin orbit ferromagnetic resonance, we find that the Lande g factor, the Gilbert damping (alpha), and the interfacial spin orbit fields exhibit a common nonmonotonic dependence on Co concentration. Furthermore, we observe linear scaling between alpha and (g-2)^2, establishing a direct correlation between interfacial SOI and magnetic relaxation. These results identify alloying as an effective knob to engineer interfacial SOI and damping in single crystalline ferromagnet semiconductor heterostructures.

The framework is implemented within an explicit finite-element solver, where the constitutive update reduces to inexpensive operator evaluations rather than repeated MD solves. Memory effects are represented through learned internal states, and transfer learning across temperature enables the surrogate to capture thermally dependent viscoelastic behavior. The method is assessed using polyurea through cyclic loading, Taylor impact, and plate impact simulations and compared with an experimentally calibrated viscoelastic polyurea model and a Johnson-Cook model. *Gen Fukuzawa,Yebin Lee,Teruyasu Mizoguchi*

TL;DR: 该研究通过第一性原理计算发现，37°转角（Sigma 37结构）的双层石墨烯（tBLG）能够同时实现最优的锂离子嵌入能（-2.39 eV）和最低的扩散势垒（0.14 eV），解决了传统堆叠构型中稳定性与扩散速率的权衡问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 控制离子传输是先进能源存储的核心挑战。传统双层石墨烯堆叠构型面临固有权衡：AA堆叠提供稳定的锂嵌入但扩散势垒高，而AB堆叠扩散快但嵌入稳定性差。转角双层石墨烯（tBLG）有望克服这一限制，但不同转角下的系统理解仍然有限。

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（first-principles density functional theory）研究tBLG中的锂嵌入，通过势能面（potential energy surface, PES）映射评估多个转角下的嵌入能和扩散势垒。使用平滑原子位置重叠（Smooth Overlap of Atomic Positions, SOAP）描述符分析PES特征。

Result: Sigma 37结构（9.43°转角）在所有测试结构中同时实现了最有利的嵌入能（-2.39 eV）和最低的扩散势垒（0.14 eV）。SOAP分析表明PES由局部原子环境决定，基于有限结构训练的模型能够高精度预测未测试构型的PES。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了通过转角工程调控二维层状材料中离子传输的系统框架。PES的可转移性使得无需大量第一性原理计算即可高效筛选，为设计高性能离子传输材料提供了新途径。

Abstract: Controlling ion transport is a fundamental challenge for advanced energy storage. Bilayer graphene offers a unique platform for modulating ion diffusion via twist-angle-dependent moire superlattices, yet conventional stacking configurations face an inherent trade-off: AA stacking provides stable Li intercalation but high diffusion barriers, while AB stacking enables fast diffusion but poor intercalation stability. Twisted bilayer graphene (tBLG) offers potential to overcome this limitation, yet systematic understanding across different twist angles remains limited. Here, we investigate Li intercalation in tBLG using first-principles density functional theory, evaluating intercalation energies and diffusion barriers across multiple twist angles through potential energy surface (PES) mapping. The Sigma 37 structure (9.43 degrees) simultaneously achieves the most favorable intercalation energy (-2.39 eV) and the lowest diffusion barrier (0.14 eV) among all structures examined, resolving the conventional stacking trade-off. Furthermore, using the Smooth Overlap of Atomic Positions (SOAP) descriptor, we demonstrate that the PES is governed by local atomic environments and that a model trained on limited structures predicts the PES of untested configurations with high accuracy. This transferability enables efficient screening without exhaustive first-principles calculations, establishing a systematic framework for twist-angle engineering of ion transport in two-dimensional layered materials.

</details>


### [132] [The rise of unconventional magnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27505)

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该综述论文系统探讨了非常规磁性（unconventional magnetism）在动量空间中的三个关键方面：自旋织构（spin textures）、量子几何（quantum geometry）和涌现准粒子（emergent quasiparticles），并展望了其与铁电性、超导性和莫尔工程（moiré engineering）的耦合前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非常规磁性代表了凝聚态物理的范式转变，它有效结合了反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）的高速、高密度优势和铁磁体（ferromagnets）的易读写能力。自旋空间群理论（spin space group theory）的发展为解耦磁几何与相对论性自旋轨道耦合提供了系统方法，推动了具有补偿磁化和时间反演奇性（time-reversal-odd）响应的非常规磁体的探索。

Method: 论文采用对称性分析（symmetry analysis）视角，阐明时间反演奇性物理响应的机制，包括非相对论性自旋分裂（non-relativistic spin splitting）、反常和非线性霍尔效应（anomalous and nonlinear Hall effects），以及奇异的电子和磁子拓扑相（electronic and magnonic topological phases）。

Result: 综述涵盖了非常规磁性在动量空间的三个关键方面：自旋织构、量子几何和涌现准粒子。通过对称性驱动的见解，揭示了这些系统如何产生独特的时间反演奇性响应，为开发新型功能材料提供了理论基础。

Conclusion: 该综述展望了将非常规磁性分别与铁电性（ferroelectricity）、超导性（superconductivity）和莫尔工程耦合的前景。通过利用对称性驱动的见解，强调了非常规磁体在开发下一代高速、高能效自旋电子器件（spintronic devices）中的功能潜力。

Abstract: Unconventional magnetism represents a paradigm shift in condensed matter physics, effectively bridging the fast, high-density advantages of antiferromagnets with the facile read-write capability of ferromagnets. Recent developments in spin space group theory have established a systematic methodology to decouple magnetic geometry from relativistic spin-orbit coupling, driving the exploration of unconventional magnets that exhibit compensated magnetization with time-reversal-odd responses. Here, we review unconventional magnetism across three pivotal facets in momentum space: spin textures, quantum geometry, and emergent quasiparticles. From the perspective of symmetry analysis, we elucidate the mechanisms underlying time-reversal-odd physical responses, including non-relativistic spin splitting, anomalous and nonlinear Hall effects, and exotic electronic and magnonic topological phases. Finally, we provide a forward-looking perspective on coupling unconventional magnetism with ferroelectricity, superconductivity, and moiré engineering. By exploiting symmetry-driven insights, this review highlights the functional potential of unconventional magnets in developing next-generation, high-speed, and energy-efficient spintronic devices.

Method: SPT利用光谱能量振荡与空间散射路径之间的傅里叶对偶性，通过将光谱分解为频域，有效隔离了实验数据中固有的去稳定化噪声中的稳健结构配位信号。该方法在大规模多样化原子环境库上进行训练。

Here, we present the Spectral Pattern Translator (SPT), a physics-informed deep learning framework that establishes a robust bridge between large-scale theoretical datasets and experimental reality. Our strategy exploits the Fourier duality between spectral energy oscillations and spatial scattering paths to overcome the "simulation-to-experiment" gap. By decomposing spectra into frequency domains, SPT effectively isolates robust structural coordination signals from the destabilizing noise inherent in experimental data. Trained on a massive library of diverse atomic environments, this approach achieves state-of-the-art accuracy in resolving continuous phase transitions in battery cathodes and deciphering local order in amorphous materials. With millisecond-scale latency, SPT removes the primary computational barrier to autonomous materials discovery, establishing a robust, noise-resilient engine for closed-loop robotic chemistry.

### [138] [The Shape of Chocolate: A Topological Perspective on Food Microstructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27854)
*Matteo Rucco*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过拓扑数据分析（TDA）框架表征可可脂在巧克力调温过程中的分子自组织行为，发现最佳调温晶型（Form V）具有独特的拓扑特征，可作为工业巧克力调温的非侵入性质量指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过拓扑数据分析（Topological Data Analysis, TDA）表征可可脂（cocoa butter）在黑暗巧克力调温过程中的分子自组织行为，为工业巧克力调温过程开发非侵入性质量指标。

Method: 采用物理启发的粒子模拟对N=100个甘油三酯分子在15-60°C全温度范围内进行建模，覆盖可可脂所有六种晶型（Forms I-VI）以及熔融和过热状态。在每个温度点构建Vietoris-Rips过滤，计算持续同调群H0、H1和H2，并通过持续熵（persistent entropy）E = -∑ p_i log₂(p_i)分析持续图。

Result: Form V（最佳调温晶型，29.5-34°C）表现出独特的拓扑特征：H0持续熵局部最小值（E0 = 5.74 ± 0.04 bits）、第一贝蒂数（Betti number）β₁显著降低（1562 ± 35）以及H2熵全局最小值（E2 = 12.29 ± 0.25 bits），反映了层间片层空腔的相干性。基于Rucco（2026）的定理1和推论1，持续熵能在相变诱导宏观尺度拓扑质量变化时区分有序和无序相。

Conclusion: 拓扑数据分析（TDA）指标可作为工业巧克力调温过程的非侵入性质量指标，持续熵能够有效区分可可脂在不同温度状态下的有序和无序相，为巧克力制造过程的质量控制提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We present a computational framework for characterizing the molecular self-organization of cocoa butter (Theobroma cacao) during dark chocolate tempering through the lens of Topological Data Analysis (TDA). A physics-inspired particle simulation models N=100 triglyceride molecules across the full temperature range 15--60 degrees C, spanning all six crystalline polymorphs of cocoa butter (Forms I--VI) as well as the melt and superheating regimes. At each temperature tick, we construct a Vietoris-Rips filtration and compute the persistent homology groups H0 (connected components), H1 (independent cycles), and H2 (3D voids). The resulting persistence diagrams are analyzed via persistent entropy E = -sum_i p_i log2(p_i), where p_i = l_i / sum_j l_j and l_i = death_i - birth_i denotes feature lifetime; essential classes are assigned death = m+1 (m = eps_max) following the standard persistent entropy convention (Rucco 2026, arXiv:2602.09058). Our results demonstrate that Form V (the optimal tempering polymorph, 29.5--34 degrees C) is characterized by a distinctive topological signature: a local minimum in the H0 persistent entropy (E0 = 5.74 +/- 0.04 bits), a pronounced depression in the first Betti number beta_1 (1562 +/- 35), and a global minimum in the H2 entropy (E2 = 12.29 +/- 0.25 bits) reflecting coherent inter-bilayer lamellar cavities. Via Theorem 1 and Corollary 1 of Rucco (2026), persistent entropy is proven to separate the ordered and disordered phases by an asymptotically non-vanishing gap whenever a phase transition induces the creation or destruction of topological mass at macroscopic scales -- a condition we verify empirically across all eight cocoa butter regimes. These findings suggest that TDA-based metrics could serve as non-invasive quality indicators for industrial chocolate tempering processes.

### [139] [Shining light on short-range atomic ordering in semiconductors alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27876)
*Anis Attiaoui,Shunda Chen,Joseph C. Woicik,J. Zach Lentz,Liliane M. Vogl,Jarod E. Meyer,Kunal Mukherjee,Andrew Minor,Tianshu Li,Paul C. McIntyre*

This work indicates that control of SRO can be an important design degree of freedom, along with factors such as average composition and strain, for band engineering, and suggests the potential for atomistic determination and tuning of SRO in other semiconductor alloy systems.

Abstract: We present a detailed analysis of the universal relationship between grain boundary (GB) free energy and GB self-diffusion coefficient derived by Borisov et al. (1964). Here, we re-derive the Borisov equation from ground up, identifying its underlying assumptions, correcting some errors and inconsistencies, and extending the original model to the case of impurity diffusion and diffusion by the interstitialcy and interstitial-dumbbell mechanisms. By contrast, the realization of intrinsic single-phase materials with coexisting ferromagnetism and ferroelectricity remains a longstanding challenge in the field. CuIn0.2V0.8P2S6 develops ferromagnetic ordering with the Curie temperature (TC) of 14.6 K, as evidenced by pronounced magnetic hysteresis and a relatively large remanent magnetization. Notably, the appearance of a magnetodielectric response below TC is consistent with the anticipated interplay between the ferromagnetic and ferroelectric orders. These results highlight a promising route toward single-phase van der Waals multiferroics with coexisting ferroic orders.

### [143] [Localization-driven exchange contrast in diffusion exchange spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27907)
*Teddy X Cai,Nathan H Williamson,Peter J Basser*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 扩散交换谱（DEXSY）在无真实交换的单一反射边界系统中也能产生类似交换的信号对比，这源于边缘增强效应导致的表观交换率，可能造成对真实屏障渗透过程的误判。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散交换谱（diffusion exchange spectroscopy, DEXSY）通常用于探测不同受限域之间的交换过程，但现有分析假设高斯扩散和一阶交换动力学。研究发现其他情况也可能产生类似信号对比，导致潜在的错误解释。

Method: 采用数值方法求解离散时空中的Bloch-Torrey方程，使用矩阵算子生成信号。研究在扩展场梯度和相同编码条件下的DEXSY信号，特别关注具有反射边界且无弛豫的一维隔室系统。

Result: 在定位化（localization）区域，即使在这个最小系统中也能从DEXSY信号提取出表观一阶交换速率常数k。测量得到的k近似正比于D/L²，通常k ≈ π²D/L²，这与拉普拉斯基的第一个非零特征值相关。

Conclusion: DEXSY及相关方法如滤波交换谱（filter exchange spectroscopy, FEXSY）可能对真实屏障渗透过程不具备特异性，因为定位化驱动的交换效应也能产生类似信号对比。

Abstract: Diffusion exchange spectroscopy (DEXSY) is a method to probe exchange between domains of varying confinement. Analyses of DEXSY signals typically assume Gaussian diffusion within distinct compartments and first-order exchange kinetics between them. Other situations can yield DEXSY signal contrast with respect to mixing time, however, leading to potentially erroneous interpretation. Here, we demonstrate that a one-dimensional compartment with reflecting boundaries and without relaxation can by itself produce such contrast in certain experimental regimes. The origin of this contrast is the diffusive mixing of spin isochromats initially near versus far from either boundary, as the former can be relatively coherent in an effect known as edge enhancement or signal localization. We consider DEXSY signals in the case of extended field gradients and identical encodings. Signals were generated via a numerical approach that solves the Bloch-Torrey equation in discrete space and time using matrix operators. We find that in the localization regime, an apparent first-order rate constant of exchange, $k$, can be extracted from DEXSY signals even in this minimal system. The measured $k$ is approximately proportional to $D/L^2$, where $D$ is the diffusivity and $L$ is the domain size. Typically, $k \approx π^2 D/L^2$. We attribute this localization-driven exchange to the relaxation of spatial magnetization modes with mixing time, noting that $π^2 D/L^2$ is the first non-zero eigenvalue of the Laplacian basis. These results demonstrate that DEXSY and related methods such as filter exchange spectroscopy (FEXSY) may not be specific to genuine barrier permeation.

Abstract: Chiral phonons are mirror-symmetric vibrations that correspond to twisting and rotational motions of atoms. In chiral biomolecules, they correspond to low-energy terahertz (THz)-range vibrations of the molecular segments involving dozens of atoms whose energies are sensitive to the chirality of the molecules and local atomic geometries. Here we present spectral signatures of chiral phonons in circularly polarized low-frequency Raman and Raman optical activity (ROA) spectra from crystals of several amino acids in different enantiomeric forms. Along with complementary THz circular dichroism (TCD) measurements, our ROA data reveal two sets of bisignate peaks in valine, alanine, tyrosine and proline between 1 and 4.5 THz that are more intense than the ROA peaks in the fingerprint region. Density functional theory (DFT) calculations on L-alanine attribute these modes to twisting and shearing molecular motions. The strong agreement between the ROA and TCD data demonstrates the power of these complementary vibrational spectroscopy techniques to identify chiral phonons in biomolecules, and offers new insights into their vibrational properties and interactions with circularly polarized light.

Motivation: 研究旨在探究金刚石氮空位（NV）色心作为固态光学制冷材料的潜力，特别关注反斯托克斯（anti-Stokes）光学冷却机制在实际系统中的表现和限制因素。

Result: 实验发现低于零声子线（ZPL）的激发会驱动带负电NV-和中性NV0之间的电荷态转换，从而抑制NV-介导的冷却通道。模拟预测了反斯托克斯冷却的自限制行为，并明确了维持净冷却的激发条件。

Conclusion: 研究确定电荷态转换是基于缺陷的光学制冷的关键瓶颈，每个NV中心的估算冷却功率在微观尺度上与半导体量子点和稀土光学制冷器相当。

Abstract: Anti-Stokes optical cooling in diamond nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers is experimentally and numerically investigated. Photoluminescence-excitation spectroscopy reveals pronounced phonon-assisted anti-Stokes emission under excitation below the zero-phonon line (ZPL). However, the below-ZPL excitation drives photoinduced charge-state conversion between negatively-charged NV- and neutral NV0, thereby suppressing the NV- mediated cooling channel. Time-resolved photoluminescence (PL) measurements reveal an increase in the effective PL lifetime with excitation density, reflecting an increasing NV0 contribution. By fitting nanosecond and millisecond PL dynamics with a minimal rate-equation model, we extract effective optical pumping and charge-conversion rates, which enables us to quantitatively simulate the cooling performance. The simulations predict a self-limiting behavior of anti-Stokes cooling and clarify the excitation conditions under which net cooling can be sustained within this effective model. The estimated cooling power per NV center is comparable, on a microscopic basis, to values discussed for semiconductor quantum dots and rare-earth optical coolers. These results identify charge-state conversion as a key bottleneck for defect-based optical refrigeration.

### [148] [Fractional Modeling of Thermoelastic Fracture Behavior in a Cracked PZT-4 Strip under Transient Thermal Loading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28025)

Abstract: This paper investigates the thermoelastic fracture response of a transversely isotropic piezoelectric strip containing a vertical insulated crack under transient thermal shock loading and pre-existing stress fields. The analysis is conducted within the framework of generalized fractional heat conduction using the Ezzat model, which incorporates thermal relaxation and memory-dependent effects. The problem is formulated as a mixed boundary value problem governed by fractional thermoelastic equations. The Laplace transform technique is employed to obtain temperature and coupled fields in the transform domain. The resulting system of singular integral equations is solved using the Lobatto-Chebyshev collocation method to determine the displacement discontinuity and the associated thermal stress intensity factors at the crack tips. The transient response in the time domain is recovered through numerical inversion of the Laplace transform using the Stehfest algorithm. Numerical results for PZT-4 are presented to examine the influence of fractional order, thermal relaxation time, pre-existing stresses, and geometric parameters on temperature distribution, thermoelastic stress fields, and stress intensity factors. The results demonstrate significant deviations from classical Fourier predictions, revealing wave-like thermal behavior and inherent memory effects associated with fractional heat conduction. The present formulation establishes a unified framework for the analysis of thermoelastic fracture in piezoelectric ceramics and provides insights into the design and reliability of smart structures operating under severe thermal conditions.

### [149] [Unconventional views on orbitronics supported by experimental results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28075)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用Ni/(Pt)Ti/Au异质结构，通过铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance）和热梯度（thermal gradients）产生角动量，测量产生的电荷电流，并分析其与Ti层厚度的关系。

Result: 观测到的电荷电流在Ti厚度达到60纳米时仍保持独立，这与轨道在Ti中的传输理论不符。电流大小取决于Ti的两个界面，表明在局域轨道-自旋相互转换前后存在自旋介导的传输（spin-mediated transport）。

Conclusion: 实验结果不支持轨道电流的长程传输模型，而是支持轨道极化与轨道-自旋转换的局域特性，以及自旋介导的传输机制，这对轨道电子学的基本假设提出了重要修正。

Abstract: Emerging orbitronics assumes long-range orbital current transport, analogous to spin currents. However, recent theory and experiments challenge this view, showing rather local characters for orbital polarization and orbit-spin conversions. We study angular momentum generated by ferromagnetic resonance and thermal gradients in Ni/(Pt)Ti/Au heterostructures. The observed charge current produced is independent of Ti thickness up to 60 nm, incompatible with orbital transport in Ti. Instead, its magnitude depends on both Ti interfaces, evidencing spin-mediated transport in between after and before local orbit-spin interconversions.

Method: 采用截面洛伦兹透射电子显微镜（cross-sectional Lorentz transmission electron microscopy）和电子全息技术（electron holography）研究Fe₃GeTe₂（FGT）/石墨/FGT异质结构，重建层内和层间的局部磁场分布。

Abstract: Magnetic van der Waals (vdW) materials are promising for memory and logic applications because of their highly tunable magnetic properties and compatibility with vdW heterostructure devices. However, in conventional plan-view measurements, coupling between magnetic textures in stacked layers is difficult to resolve because the magnetic signal is integrated over the sample thickness. Here, these interactions are quantified in Fe$_3$GeTe$_2$ (FGT)/graphite/FGT heterostructures using cross-sectional Lorentz transmission electron microscopy and electron holography, enabling reconstruction of the local magnetic field within and between the layers. Domain alignment weakens with increasing FGT separation, yielding a dipolar coupling length scale of $λ= 34 \pm 4$ nm for the cross-sectional geometry studied here, corresponding to the average separation at which domain misalignment first emerges. This length scale coincides with an approximately 50\% reduction in the interlayer magnetic field relative to bulk FGT. Surface effects result in canting of the magnetic moments away from the easy axis up to $\sim$100 nm from a surface. Finally, the domain walls are narrow ($\sim$9 nm), while micromagnetic simulations reproduce the observed textures without invoking Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction. These results quantify the internal and stray fields in stacked vdW magnets and guide the design of devices that require controllable coupling between magnetic textures.

In this work, we demonstrate the epitaxial growth of hematite thin films on y- and z-cut lithium niobate (LiNbO$_3$) substrates using pulsed laser deposition (PLD). LiNbO$_3$ as piezoelectric substrate is of particular interest as it enables the efficient excitation of surface acoustic waves (SAWs) with interdigital transducers. The different substrate cuts allow for different orientations of the Néel vector. Films grown on y-cut LiNbO3 are single-crystalline and single-phase, while those deposited on z-cut LiNbO$_3$ exhibit two distinct in-plane (ip) domains rotated 60° relative to each other. *Duc-Duy Tran,Cedric Mannequin,Fabrice Donatini,Masahiro Sasaki,Etienne Gheeraert*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在开发一种无需掩模、无损伤的纳米加工路线，用于金刚石半导体和其他化学惰性材料。传统方法需要光刻或等离子体处理，而本方法直接在扫描电镜（SEM）环境中实现高精度图案化。

Method: 通过综合分析扫描电镜环境中的电子-气体、电子-金刚石以及气体-表面相互作用，研究揭示了刻蚀过程主要由低能二次电子（secondary electrons）驱动。这些二次电子促使气体解离并生成自由基，随后含氧和氮的自由基在金刚石表面发生化学吸附，形成挥发性含碳物种并在持续电子辐照下脱附。

Result: 该工艺展现出两种不同的机制：由气体通量控制的分子限制机制和由电流密度控制的电子限制机制。实现了高达212 nm的刻蚀深度和低至200 nm的横向分辨率。观察到时间依赖的各向异性，其中(100)表面转变为(111)晶面形态，提高了刻蚀产额。

Conclusion: 这些结果确立了气体环境中电子束诱导刻蚀（EBIE）的通用二次电子驱动机制，为金刚石半导体和其他化学惰性材料提供了一种无需掩模、无损伤的纳米加工途径。

Abstract: We report a direct, maskless electron beam-induced etching (EBIE) process for diamond in air, enabling high-precision patterning without lithography or plasma processing. Through a comprehensive analysis of electron-gas, electron-diamond, and gas-surface interactions in the SEM environment, we demonstrate that etching is predominantly governed by low-energy secondary electrons, which drive gas dissociation and radical generation. The resulting oxygen- and nitrogen-based radicals chemisorb on the diamond surface, form volatile carbon-containing species, and desorb under continued electron irradiation, enabling controlled material removal. The process exhibits two distinct regimes: a molecule-limited regime governed by gas flux and an electron-limited regime controlled by current density. Etch depths up to 212 nm and lateral resolution down to 200 nm are achieved. Time-dependent anisotropy is observed, with (100) surfaces transitioning to (111)-faceted morphologies, enhancing etch yield. These results establish a general secondary electron-driven mechanism for EBIE in gas environments, providing a maskless, damage-free nanofabrication route for diamond semiconductor and other chemically inert materials.

### [154] [Intrinsically ultralow thermal conductivity in all-inorganic superatomic bulk crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28267)
*Mingzhang Yang,Yuxi Wang,Jun Deng,Tianping Ying,Qinghua Zhang,Nianjie Liang,Xiaobing Liu,Bai Song,Jian-gang Guo,Xiaolong Chen*

TL;DR: 该研究成功生长了高质量超原子（superatomic）单晶Re6Se8Te7和Re6Te15，发现它们具有极低的热导率（κ），在室温下分别为0.32和0.53 W m⁻¹ K⁻¹，属于全无机块体晶体中报道的最低值之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超原子化合物（superatomic compounds）由通过弱化学键交织的原子簇组成，表现出大的非谐性振动，是超低热导率材料的理想候选。然而，由于复杂的化学成分和化学键，生长块体超原子单晶具有挑战性，对其本征热性质的研究也很缺乏。

Method: 研究生长了高质量的Re6Se8Te7和Re6Te15超原子单晶，这两种材料均为窄带隙半导体，在外加物理压力下会转变为金属。通过测量热导率、分析格吕乃森参数（Grüneisen parameter）和平均声速，并使用经典德拜-卡拉韦模型（Debye-Callaway model）描述热导率的温度依赖性。

Result: 室温下Re6Se8Te7和Re6Te15的热导率分别为0.32和0.53 W m⁻¹ K⁻¹，属于全无机块体晶体中报道的最低值。这主要归因于大的格吕乃森参数（1.93）和低的平均声速（<1482 m/s）。玻色峰（boson peak）的出现验证了无序声子输运的存在，且350 K以上热导率值接近玻璃态扩散模型推导的上限。

Conclusion: 超原子化合物因其极低的热导率和独特的结构特性，成为寻找超低热导率材料和能量管理材料的有前景的体系。软Te7网络弱嵌入刚性Re6Se8（Re6Te8）准立方簇的结构设计是实现低热导率的关键。

Abstract: Superatomic compounds, composed of atomic clusters interwoven by weak chemical bonds exhibit large anharmonicity vibrations, are excellent candidates for ultralow thermal conductivity (\k{appa}) materials. However, growing bulk superatomic single crystals is challenging due to complex chemical composition and chemical bonds, and studies on their intrinsic thermal property are scarce. Here, we grew high-quality superatomic single crystals of Re6Se8Te7 and Re6Te15, both of which are narrow band gap semiconductors that change into metals under external physical pressure. At room-temperature, the \k{appa} are 0.32 W m-1 K-1 and 0.53 W m-1 K-1 in Re6Se8Te7 and Re6Te15, respectively, ranking among the lowest value reported in all-inorganic bulk crystals. It is mainly attributed to the large Grüneisen parameter (1.93) and low average sound speed (< 1482 m/s), which are due to soft Te7 nets weakly embedded among the rigid Re6Se8 (Re6Te8) quasi-cubic clusters. The appearance of boson peak, i. e., hump of C(T)/T3, verifies the existence of disordered phonon transports. Besides, the temperature dependence of \k{appa} can be described by classic Debye-Callaway model. Notably, above 350 K, the \k{appa} values of Re6Se8Te7 and Re6Te15 are remarkably close to the upper limit derived from glassy-like diffusion model. This finding sets the superatomic compounds as a promising family for searching ultralow-\k{appa} and energy management materials.

</details>


### [155] [Quantitative Analysis of Light Induced Ion Segregation in Mixed-Halide Perovskites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28289)
*Petr Machovec,Lukáš Horák,Milan Dopita,Neda Neykova,Lucie Landová,Jakub Holovský,Václav Holý*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合卤化物钙钛矿（mixed-halide perovskites, MHPs）通过化学计量变化可实现良好的带隙可调性，这对制造多结太阳能电池至关重要。然而，光照下MHP中的卤化物离子会发生分离，形成富I和富Br区域，从而降低潜在太阳能电池的效率。

Method: 研究引入了一种详细调查MHP在光照期间和之后卤化物离子分布的方法。通过计算卤化物分离产生的应变场，利用获得的原子局部位移计算X射线漫散射（x-ray diffuse scattering）。通过拟合在FA0.83Cs0.17Pb(I0.6Br0.4)3多晶薄膜上测量的实验数据，确定了光照MHP中Br⁻和I⁻离子的分布。

Result: 确定了光照下混合卤化物钙钛矿中Br⁻和I⁻离子的分布，并追踪了暗态下分离过程的后续弛豫。观察到在光照期间，在略微富I的体积内形成了高度富Br的区域。

Conclusion: 该方法成功表征了混合卤化物钙钛矿中卤化物离子的动态分布行为，揭示了光照诱导的卤化物分离机制及其弛豫过程，为理解MHP材料的光稳定性问题提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Mixed-halide perovskites (MHPs) offer good band gap tunability by stoichiometry changes, which is an essential property for the creation of multijunction solar cells. However, under illumination, halide ions in MHP segregate and create I- and Br-rich regions, which decreases the efficiency of potential solar cells. In this work, a method for a detailed investigation of the distribution of halide ions within the MHP during and after illumination is introduced. Calculations of the strain field created by the halide segregation were performed, and the obtained local displacement of atoms was used to calculate the x-ray diffuse scattering. By fitting the experimental data measured on the thin polycrystalline layer of FA0.83Cs0.17Pb(I0.6Br0.4)3 the distribution of Br- and I- ions within an illuminated MHP was determined and the subsequent relaxation process of the segregation in the dark was tracked. Creation of highly Br-rich regions within slightly I-rich volume during the illumination was observed.

### [156] [Work-Function-Resolved Imaging of Relaxation Oscillations and Chemical Spillover in CO Oxidation over Platinum Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28354)
*Karel Vařeka,Michal Potoček,Adam Očkovič,Tomáš Šikola,Zhu-Jun Wang,Petr Bábor,Miroslav Kolíbal*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究结合操作扫描电子显微镜与频率调制开尔文探针力显微镜，首次实现了铂表面CO氧化反应前沿的工作函数分辨成像，揭示了化学波传播的局部电子机制与时空不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铂表面CO氧化反应中的化学波表现出复杂的时空自振荡现象，但在操作条件下驱动其传播的局部电子机制仍不清楚。需要发展原位表征技术来揭示反应前沿的物理本质。

Method: 研究结合操作扫描电子显微镜（operando scanning electron microscopy）与频率调制开尔文探针力显微镜（frequency-modulated Kelvin probe force microscopy, FM-KPFM），同时映射二次电子对比度和局部工作函数变化。利用KPFM尖端作为局部传感器，首次实现了反应前沿的工作函数分辨成像。

Result: 研究明确区分了CO覆盖态和氧覆盖态，发现化学波的溢流过程（spillover process）具有显著的时间不对称性和空间异质性过渡阈值。KPFM识别出氧覆盖的快速开始，随后逐渐扩散松弛回CO覆盖态，即使在低压力（10^-2 Pa）下也表现出弛豫型振荡（relaxation-type oscillations）。

Conclusion: 相关反应-扩散模拟重现了这种波形态，证实高分辨率工作函数信号为工作催化剂表面的内部结构和动力学异质性提供了独特见解。该方法为理解表面反应机制提供了新的实验途径。

Abstract: Chemical waves of CO oxidation on platinum surfaces exhibit complex spatio-temporal self-oscillations, yet the local electronic mechanisms driving their propagation remain poorly understood under operando conditions. In this work, we combine operando scanning electron microscopy with frequency-modulated Kelvin probe force microscopy (FM-KPFM) to simultaneously map secondary electron contrast and local work-function variations during CO oxidation on Pt. By utilizing the KPFM tip as a localized sensor, we provide the first work-function-resolved imaging of reaction fronts, enabling an unambiguous physical assignment of CO- and oxygen-covered states. Our results demonstrate that the spillover process of chemical wave-the transition and expansion of adsorbate phases-is characterized by a pronounced temporal asymmetry and spatial heterogeneity transition thresholds. KPFM identifies a rapid onset of oxygen coverage followed by a gradual, diffuse relaxation back to the CO-covered state, indicative of relaxation-type oscillations even at low pressures (10^-2 Pa). Correlative reaction-diffusion simulations reproduce this wave morphology, confirming that the high-resolution work-function signal provides unique insights into the internal structure and kinetic heterogeneity of the working catalyst surface.

### [157] [Incipient magnetic instability in RuO$_2$ with random phase approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28355)
*Diana Csontosová,Kyo-Hoon Ahn,Jan Kuneš*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过哈特里-福克近似（Hartree-Fock approximation）和随机相位近似（random phase approximation）分析RuO₂的不稳定性，使用三轨道哈伯德模型（three-orbital Hubbard model）发现自旋磁化率（spin susceptibility）是主导响应通道，并识别出交变磁序（altermagnetic order）为低温下的主要不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究RuO₂中磁不稳定性的起源，特别关注交变磁体（altermagnets）与反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）之间的定性差异，以理解该材料系统的磁有序行为。

Method: 采用无自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的三轨道哈伯德模型（three-orbital Hubbard model），结合哈特里-福克近似（Hartree-Fock approximation）和随机相位近似（random phase approximation），分析静态磁化率（static susceptibility）的本征值和本征向量。

Result: 在非磁性相中，自旋磁化率（spin susceptibility）是主导响应通道；在无自旋轨道耦合的化学计量系统中，低温下出现共格交变磁序（commensurate altermagnetic order），而高温或有限空穴掺杂（hole doping）时则出现非共格波矢（incommensurate wave vectors）。

Conclusion: 通过分析交错韦斯场（staggered Weiss field）引起的能带分裂，阐明了磁不稳定性的起源，并讨论了交变磁体（altermagnets）与反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）之间的定性差异。

Abstract: We study the instability in RuO$_2$ using the Hartree-Fock approximation followed by the random phase approximation. We employ a three-orbital Hubbard model without spin-orbit coupling. An analysis of the eigenvalues and eigenvectors of the static susceptibility in the non-magnetic phase for various local interaction parameters $U$, $J_H$, and hole doping $n$ shows that the spin susceptibility is the dominant response channel. In the stoichiometric system without spin-orbit coupling, commensurate altermagnetic order is identified as the leading instability at sufficiently low temperatures, whereas at higher temperatures or finite hole doping, incommensurate wave vectors emerge. To elucidate the origin of the magnetic instability, we analyze the band spitting by the staggered Weiss field and discuss the qualitative difference between altermagnets and antiferromagnets.
