### [158] [Role of spatiotemporal nonuniformities in laser-induced magnetization precession damping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28364)
*P. I. Gerevenkov,Ia. A. Filatov,L. A. Shelukhin,P. A. Dvortsova,A. M. Kalashnikova*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了铁磁体中激光诱导磁化进动测量中阻尼时间异常减少的现象并非材料本征特性，而是由非均匀激发区域内局域磁化进动干涉所致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁磁体中激光诱导磁化进动测量常在磁场诱导的二阶自旋取向转变（field-induced second-order spin-orientation transition）附近观察到阻尼时间异常减少，这一行为无法用线性化的Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert方程描述，需要探究其物理起源。

Method: 通过结合泵浦-探测实验（pump-probe experiments）、考虑泵浦和探测光斑有限尺寸的解析建模，以及微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulations），系统研究了非均匀激发区域内的磁化动力学。

Result: 研究表明标准宏自旋方法（standard macrospin approach）无法捕捉观测到的动力学行为。激发区域内磁参数的非均匀弛豫（inhomogeneous relaxation）会扭曲测量的进动包络，而偶极场（dipole fields）则在其频率中产生时间非单调项。

Conclusion: 该异常现象并非材料特性，而是源于非均匀激发区域内局域磁化进动的干涉效应，强调了临界场附近激发局域性（excitation locality）的关键作用。

Abstract: Laser-induced magnetization precession measurements in ferromagnets often reveal an anomalous decrease in the damping time near a field-induced second-order spin-orientation transition, a behavior that cannot be described by the linearized Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation. Here we demonstrate that this anomaly is not a material property but results from interference of precessing local magnetizations within the inhomogeneously excited region. By combining pump-probe experiments, analytical modeling that accounts for the finite sizes of the pump and probe spots, and micromagnetic simulations, we show that the standard macrospin approach fails to capture the observed dynamics. The inhomogeneous relaxation of magnetic parameters within the excitation area distorts the measured precession envelope, while dipole fields give rise to a temporally non-monotonic term in its frequency. Our results highlight the critical role of excitation locality in a vicinity of critical fields.

</details>


### [159] [Stable Asymmetric Magnetization Reversal in Epitaxial Co(001)/CoO(001) Bilayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28424)
*Maik Gaerner,Judith Bünte,Finn Peters,Inga Ennen,Hermann Tetzlaff,Johannes Fiedler,Tomasz Blachowicz,Luana Caron,Andreas Hütten,Andrea Ehrmann,Martin Wortmann*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过分子束外延（MBE）制备了外延fcc-Co(001)/CoO(001)薄膜，系统研究了交换偏置（EB）体系中磁滞回线的不对称性及其与训练循环和偏置大小的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁磁/反铁磁（FM/AFM）双层体系中的交换偏置（exchange bias）现象在通过反铁磁奈尔温度场冷却后会导致磁滞回线偏移，有时伴随上升与下降分支的不对称性。以往研究多集中于多晶体系，本研究旨在探究外延单晶体系中的不对称磁化反转特性。

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）在MgO(001)衬底上生长外延fcc-Co(001)/CoO(001)薄膜，通过纵向和横向磁光克尔效应（magneto-optic Kerr effect）在室温下测量不同磁场方向与易磁化轴夹角时的磁化反转过程，并在低于阻塞温度（blocking temperature）场冷却后观察不对称磁化反转。

Result: 研究发现，不同外磁场与易磁化轴夹角会导致通过稳定中间态的磁化反转过程不同。低于阻塞温度场冷却后观察到显著的不对称磁化反转，且与多晶双层体系不同，该不对称性在多次训练循环（training cycles）后保持恒定，其大小与交换偏置（EB）幅度直接相关。

Conclusion: 外延fcc-Co(001)/CoO(001)薄膜中的不对称磁化反转行为与多晶体系存在本质差异，其不对称性的稳定性及其与交换偏置大小的直接关联为理解交换偏置机制提供了新的实验依据。

Abstract: The exchange bias (EB) in ferromagnetic/antiferromagnetic (FM/AFM) bilayer systems causes a shift of the magnetic hysteresis curve after field cooling through the Néel temperature of the AFM. In some cases, this shift is accompanied by an asymmetry between ascending and descending branches. In the past, this asymmetric magnetization reversal has been studied in different bilayer systems, including polycrystalline Co/CoO thin films. Here we investigate the asymmetric magnetization reversal in an epitaxial fcc-Co(001)/CoO(001) thin film grown on MgO(001) by molecular beam epitaxy at varying temperatures up to room temperature after field cooling along the easy and the hard axes. Room temperature measurements of the longitudinal and transverse magneto-optic Kerr effect show different magnetization reversal processes via stable intermediate states for different angles between external magnetic field and magnetic easy axes. Once the sample is cooled below the blocking temperature, a pronounced asymmetric magnetization reversal can be observed. We show that in contrast to polycrystalline bilayers, the loop asymmetry stays constant after multiple training cycles and that the magnitude of the asymmetry is directly correlated with the magnitude of the EB.

</details>


### [160] [Oxygen as a dual function regulator in MoS2 CVD synthesis: enhancing precursor evaporation while modulating reaction kinetics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28461)
*Keerthana S Kumar,Abhijit Gogoi,Madhavan DK Nampoothiri,Bhavesh Kumar Acharya,Manvi Verma,Ananth Govind Rajan,Akshay Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了氧辅助化学气相沉积（O-CVD）中氧的双重作用机制，通过优化硫氧比（S:O2）实现了大面积高质量单层MoS2的可控制备。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二硫化钼（MoS2）作为二维过渡金属硫族化合物（TMD），在光电子和量子技术应用中前景广阔，但面临可扩展合成和缺陷工程的挑战。氧辅助化学气相沉积（O-CVD）虽显示出潜力，但其作用机制尚不明确。

Method: 采用氧剂量实验、密度泛函理论（DFT）计算、计算流体动力学（CFD）模拟和从头算分子动力学（AIMD）模拟相结合的方法。通过实验调控氧的流量间隔、流速和流动时间，并与CFD模拟关联分析。

Result: 研究发现氧在O-CVD中具有双重作用：AIMD显示氧促进MoO3升华并增强Mo3O9供应；DFT表明硫氧化物因其体积大于纯S2而限制反应性MoS6中间体形成。通过优化成核期MoO3舟和基底处的低硫氧比（S:O2）与生长期基底处的高S:O2，可获得大面积高质量单层MoS2。

Conclusion: 研究提出了MoS2合成的动力学相图，使可控氧剂量可作为可扩展、缺陷控制单层MoS2合成的调节参数，为高质量二维材料制备提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Molybdenum disulfide (MoS2) is a promising 2D transition metal dichalcogenide (TMD) for optoelectronics and quantum technology applications, but faces challenges in scalable synthesis and defect engineering. Oxygen-assisted chemical vapor deposition (O-CVD), which introduces in-situ oxygen during growth, shows excellent potential in resolving both issues at once. Although co-flowing oxygen shows improvement in growth, the underlying mechanistic role of oxygen remains unclear. In this work, a combination of oxygen dosing experiments, density functional theory (DFT) calculations, computational fluid dynamics (CFD) simulations, and ab initio molecular dynamics (AIMD) simulations, uncover the dual role of oxygen in O-CVD. Firstly, AIMD reveals that oxygen increases MoO3 sublimation and enhances Mo3O9 supply. Concomitantly, DFT reveals that sulphur oxides, due to their bulkier nature than pure S2, limit the formation of reactive MoS6 intermediates. Subsequently, by experimentally varying the oxygen flow-interval, flow-rate, and flow-time, and correlating them with CFD simulations, we decouple oxygen's roles in source-poisoning prevention (i.e. MoO3 evaporation) and growth regulation. We find that maintaining a low sulphur-to-oxygen (S:O2) ratio at the MoO3 boat and substrate during nucleation, and a high S:O2 ratio at the substrate during growth is the key to obtaining large-area high-quality monolayer MoS2, confirmed by our optical measurements. Based on our understanding, we present a kinetic phase diagram for MoS2 synthesis, which will enable controlled oxygen dosing as a tuning parameter for scalable, defect-controlled monolayer MoS2 synthesis.

</details>


### [161] [Pentagonal PdTe2 Monolayer for Sustainable Solar-driven Hydrogen Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28726)
*Narender Kumar,Shambhu Bhandari,Dario Alfè,Nacir Tit,Ravindra Pandey*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究证明五边形PdTe2单层是一种高度可调的二维光催化剂，具有1.75 eV带隙和高空穴迁移率。通过应变工程（特别是+2%和+3%拉伸应变）可实现自发水分解，在pH=7条件下获得20.40%的太阳能-氢转化效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索五边形PdTe2单层作为高效可调二维光催化剂的潜力，特别关注通过机械应变工程优化其水分解性能，以实现可持续的太阳能驱动制氢。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算，结合HSE06泛函，分析拉伸应变（特别是+2%和+3%）对材料电子结构和催化性能的影响。通过计算吉布斯自由能（Gibbs free energy, ΔG）途径和光学吸收特性，评估氢析出反应（hydrogen evolution reaction, HER）和氧析出反应（oxygen evolution reaction, OER）的过电位。

Result: 在+3%拉伸应变下，价带顶和导带底跨越水氧化还原电位（H+/H2和O2/H2O），实现自发水分解。优化后的过电位为ηHER = 0.70 V和ηOER = 0.72 V（pH=7）。低空穴有效质量促进快速电荷提取，减少复合。太阳能-氢转化效率达到20.40%，优于多种已报道的二维催化剂。

Conclusion: 五边形PdTe2单层通过应变工程展现出卓越的光催化水分解性能，特别是在+3%拉伸应变下获得优化的催化活性和20.40%的太阳能-氢转化效率，使其成为可持续太阳能驱动制氢的优异候选材料。

Abstract: This investigation demonstrates that the pentagonal PdTe2 (penta-PdTe2) monolayer is a highly tunable two-dimensional (2D) photocatalyst, characterized by the bandgap of 1.75 eV and high hole mobility. Using density functional theory calculations with the HSE06 functional, we show that tensile strain engineering (particularly at +2% and +3%) is essential for enabling spontaneous water splitting. At these strain values, the valence-band maximum and conduction-band maximum straddle the water redox potentials (H+/H2 and O2/H2O) in both acidic (pH=0) and neutral (pH=7) conditions. The monolayer's low hole effective mass facilitates rapid charge extraction, mitigating recombination and driving the oxygen evolution reaction (OER) more effectively than many hexagonal and pentagonal counterparts. The Gibbs free energy (ΔG) pathways indicate that overpotentials for the hydrogen evolution reaction (HER) and OER are highly sensitive to mechanical deformation, specifically biaxial strain, through which +3% tensile strain, yielding an optimized balance of overpotentials of ηHER = 0.70 V and ηOER = 0.72 V at pH=7. Finally, integrating optical absorption with thermodynamic driving forces results in a Solar-to-Hydrogen (STH) efficiency of 20.40% at pH 7. This exceeds the performance of several previously reported 2D catalysts, positioning penta-PdTe2 as a superior candidate for sustainable, solar-driven hydrogen production.

</details>

### [162] [Exploring Late-Time Cosmic Acceleration in VCDM Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27178)
*Sai Swagat Mishra,Soumya Kanta Bhoi,P. K. Sahoo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本研究通过约束一个能有效再现类VCDM行为的极小修正引力理论，检验其宇宙学意义。该模型在完整数据集组合（CC+RSD+DESI DR2+Union3）的统计比较中优于ΛCDM，表明此类理论可作为标准宇宙学范式的有力替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索极小修正引力理论（minimally modified gravity theory）的宇宙学意义，该理论能有效再现类VCDM（VCDM-like）行为。研究动机源于寻找标准ΛCDM宇宙学范式的竞争性替代方案。

Method: 采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）框架约束模型参数，结合CC、RSD、DESI BAO DR2和Union3数据集。同时考察背景和扰动层面的可观测量，包括哈勃参数（Hubble parameter）、减速参数（deceleration parameter）、有效状态方程（effective equation of state）、距离模数（distance modulus）以及通过fσ₈(z)可观测量分析宇宙结构的增长率（growth rate）。

Result: 模型成功再现了观测到的膨胀历史（expansion history），在z≃0.3附近展现出哈勃演化的平滑过渡（smooth transition），且宇宙学参数行为一致。在完整数据集组合（CC+RSD+DESI DR2+Union3）的统计比较中，该模型表现优于ΛCDM。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，具有类VCDM动力学的极小修正引力理论可作为标准宇宙学范式（standard cosmological paradigm）的一致且具有竞争力的替代方案。这些发现凸显了此类理论在解释宇宙观测数据方面的潜力。

Abstract: In this work, we have considered a minimally modified gravity theory that effectively reproduces VCDM-like behavior to investigate its cosmological implications. The model parameters are constrained using a combination of CC, RSD, DESI BAO DR2, and Union3 datasets. The model parameters are constrained using an MCMC framework, ensuring a robust estimation of credible intervals. We examine both background and perturbation-level observables, analyzing the Hubble parameter, deceleration parameter, effective equation of state, distance modulus, and the growth rate of cosmic structures through the \(fσ_8(z)\) observable. Our results show that the model successfully reproduces the observed expansion history, featuring a smooth transition in the Hubble evolution around \(z \simeq 0.3\), and consistent behaviour of cosmological parameters. The model outperforms \(Λ\)CDM in the statistical comparisons for the full dataset combination (CC+RSD+DESI DR2+Union3). These results highlight the potential of minimally modified gravity theories with VCDM-like dynamics as consistent and competitive alternatives to the standard cosmological paradigm.

</details>


### [163] [Model-independent test of the cosmic distance duality relation with recent observational data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27616)
*Xing Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究采用两种模型无关方法检验宇宙距离对偶关系（CDDR），利用超新星、重子声学振荡、宇宙计时器和伽马射线暴等观测数据，结果支持CDDR在1σ置信水平内成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在检验宇宙距离对偶关系（cosmic distance duality relation, CDDR）的有效性，该关系是标准宇宙学模型的基本假设之一。通过模型无关方法进行检验，可以避免特定宇宙学模型的先验假设影响。

Method: 采用两种模型无关方法：方法I基于PAge参数化（PAge parametrization），该方法以宇宙年龄表征膨胀历史；方法II使用高斯过程（Gaussian process）对超新星光度距离进行非参数重构。两种方法均结合Ia型超新星（SN）、重子声学振荡（BAO）、宇宙计时器和伽马射线暴（GRB）观测数据，包括最新的PantheonPlus和DES Dovekie超新星样本以及DESI DR2 BAO数据。

Result: 研究结果支持宇宙距离对偶关系在1σ置信水平内成立。不同数据组合的分析表明该结论具有稳健性，尽管伽马射线暴数据延伸至更高红移，但其约束能力显著弱于其他低红移探针。PantheonPlus和DES Dovekie样本得到一致结果，两种方法的结果相互一致。

Conclusion: 基于两种模型无关方法的分析均未发现宇宙距离对偶关系违反的证据，支持该基本宇宙学关系的有效性。研究展示了不同观测探针在检验基础物理关系中的作用和局限性。

Abstract: We test the cosmic distance duality relation (CDDR) using two model-independent methods. Method I is based on the PAge parametrization, which characterizes the expansion history in terms of the cosmic age. Parametrizations of possible CDDR violations are constrained using observational data from Type Ia supernovae (SN), baryon acoustic oscillations (BAO), cosmic chronometers, and gamma-ray bursts (GRB), including the latest PantheonPlus and DES Dovekie SN samples and DESI DR2 BAO data. The results support the validity of the CDDR within $1σ$. Different combinations of data sets are further explored to assess the impact of various probes and calibration choices, demonstrating the robustness of this conclusion. Although GRB data extend to higher redshifts, their constraining power is significantly weaker than that of the other low-redshift probes. The PantheonPlus and DES Dovekie samples yield consistent results. Method II uses a non-parametric Gaussian process reconstruction of the luminosity distance from SN data, combined with BAO measurements to construct the observed CDDR violation and constrain its parametrizations. The results are consistent with those from Method I, and we find no evidence for a violation of the CDDR.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [164] [Updates on the DEAP-3600 experiment and steps towards the ARGO experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27372)
*Susnata Seth*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: DEAP-3600是目前全球最大的单相液氩暗物质探测器，已为氩核上的WIMP-核子自旋无关散射截面设定了最严格的排除限，并正在开发下一代300吨液氩探测器ARGO以提升暗物质探测灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗物质（dark matter）探测是粒子物理和宇宙学的核心课题之一。DEAP-3600作为最大的单相液氩探测器，旨在通过提高探测灵敏度和降低本底来寻找弱相互作用大质量粒子（WIMP）等暗物质候选者。

Method: 采用位于SNOLAB地下2公里处的3.3吨液氩靶，利用优异的脉冲形状甄别（pulse-shape discrimination）技术抑制低能β衰变本底，并结合精确的位置重建（position reconstruction）技术。通过硬件升级减少残余α本底，并开展模拟研究评估放射性中子本底及其抑制策略。

Result: DEAP-3600为质量高于30 GeV/c²的WIMP-核子自旋无关散射截面在氩核上设定了最严格的排除限，并对超重、多重散射暗物质候选者提供了领先的灵敏度。作为全球氩暗物质合作组（GADMC）的一部分，下一代ARGO探测器正在开发中，其300吨的液氩质量将显著提升对稀有暗物质相互作用的探测能力。

Conclusion: DEAP-3600在暗物质探测领域取得了重要进展，通过技术改进和本底抑制提升了探测灵敏度。下一代ARGO探测器的开发将进一步推动暗物质探测能力，而相关的本底研究和抑制策略将为探测器设计提供关键输入。

Abstract: The DEAP-3600 experiment, with an approximately 3.3 tonne liquid argon (LAr) target, is currently the world's largest single-phase LAr dark matter detector. It is located 2 km underground at SNOLAB, Canada, one of the most radiopure underground laboratories. With excellent pulse-shape discrimination against low-energy beta decays and precise position reconstruction, DEAP-3600 has set the most stringent WIMP-nucleon spin-independent cross-section exclusion limits for masses above 30 GeV/c$^{2}$ on argon and provided leading sensitivity to superheavy, multi-scattering dark matter candidate. Here we report the recent advances in understanding LAr properties and position reconstruction techniques using DEAP-3600 data along with hardware upgrades to mitigate residual challenging $α$-backgrounds for WIMP search. As a part of Global Argon Dark Matter Collaboration (GADMC), the next-generation ARGO detector, featuring a 300-tonne fiducial LAr mass, is under development to significantly enhance sensitivity to rare dark matter interactions. Simulation-based studies of radiogenic neutron backgrounds and their mitigation strategies provide essential input to this design and will be described here.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: LHCb实验测量了B介子衰变中的CP不对称性，发现B⁰→Ds⁻D⁺的CP不对称性接近零，而Bₛ⁰→Ds⁺D⁻的CP不对称性为0.103±0.053±0.010，两者均与CP对称性一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在测量B介子衰变中的电荷宇称（CP）不对称性，特别是对B⁰→Ds⁻D⁺和Bₛ⁰→Ds⁺D⁻衰变过程进行精确测量。这些测量对于检验标准模型中的CP破坏机制具有重要意义。

Method: 利用LHCb实验收集的质子-质子对撞数据，对应积分亮度为9fb⁻¹。通过分析B⁰和Bₛ⁰介子的衰变产物，测量其CP不对称性参数A_CP，并分别给出统计和系统不确定性。

Result: 测量结果显示：A_CP(B⁰→Ds⁻D⁺)=0.0009±0.0053±0.0040，A_CP(Bₛ⁰→Ds⁺D⁻)=0.103±0.053±0.010。这是首次对Bₛ⁰衰变中该不对称性的测量，也是迄今为止对B⁰衰变最精确的测量。

Conclusion: 两个测量结果均与CP对称性一致，表明在这些特定的B介子衰变通道中未发现显著的CP破坏效应。这些结果为标准模型的CP破坏机制提供了重要的实验约束。

Abstract: Measurements of the combined CP asymmetries in $\kern 0.18em\overline{\kern -0.18em B}^0 \to D_s^- D^+$ and $\kern 0.18em\overline{\kern -0.18em B}_s^0 \to D_s^+ D^-$ decays are made using proton-proton collision data collected by the LHCb experiment, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 9fb$^{-1}$. The measurements are found to be \begin{aligned} A_{CP}(\kern 0.18em\overline{\kern -0.18em B}^0 \to D_s^- D^+) &= 0.0009 \pm 0.0053 \pm 0.0040, \\ A_{CP}(\kern 0.18em\overline{\kern -0.18em B}_s^0 \to D_s^+ D^-) &= 0.103\phantom{0} \pm 0.053\phantom{0} \pm 0.010, \end{aligned} where the first and second uncertainties are statistical and systematic, respectively. This is the first measurement of this asymmetry in $\kern 0.18em\overline{\kern -0.18em B}_s^0$ decays, and the most precise measurement to date for $\kern 0.18em\overline{\kern -0.18em B}^0$ decays. Both measurements are found to be consistent with CP symmetry.

</details>

Zhao,Y. P. Zhao,Y. X. Zhao,Z. G. Zhao,A. Zhemchugov,B. Zheng,B. M. Zheng,J. P. Zheng,W. J. Zheng,W. Q. Zheng,X. R. Zheng,Y. H. Zheng,B. Zhong,C. Zhong,H. Zhou,J. Q. Zhou,S. Zhou,X. Zhou,X. K. Zhou,X. R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,J. H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: BESIII实验首次观测到Λc⁺→nπ⁺η衰变，统计显著性达9.5σ，测量了分支比并设定了中间过程的上限，采用基于Transformer的深度学习架构进行信号背景分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在首次观测Λc⁺重子到nπ⁺η末态的衰变过程，测量其分支比（branching fraction），并探索可能的中间共振态a₀(980)⁺的产生机制。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上采集的6.1 fb⁻¹数据，质心能量范围为√s=4.600-4.843 GeV。采用基于Transformer架构的深度学习方法来区分信号与强子背景（hadronic backgrounds），并进行系统误差量化。

Result: 首次观测到Λc⁺→nπ⁺η衰变，统计显著性为9.5σ。分支比比值为ℬ(Λc⁺→nπ⁺η)/ℬ(Λc⁺→Λπ⁺η)=0.155±0.031(stat.)±0.012(syst.)，绝对分支比为(2.94±0.59(stat.)±0.23(syst.)±0.13(ref.))×10⁻³。对中间过程Λc⁺→na₀(980)⁺设定了90%置信水平上限8.4×10⁻⁴。

Conclusion: 该研究首次观测并精确测量了Λc⁺→nπ⁺η衰变过程，为理解粲重子（charm baryon）衰变机制提供了重要实验数据，同时展示了深度学习技术在粒子物理数据分析中的有效应用。

Abstract: By analysing 6.1 ${\rm fb}^{-1}$ of data collected at center-of-mass energies between $\sqrt{s}=4.600$ and 4.843 $\rm GeV$ with the BESIII detector at the BEPCII collider, we observe the decay $Λ_c^+\to nπ^+η$ for the first time with a statistical significance of $9.5σ$. The ratio of branching fractions $\mathcal{B}(Λ_c^+\to nπ^+η)/\mathcal{B}(Λ_c^+\to Λπ^+η)$ is measured to be $0.155\pm0.031_{\rm stat.}\pm0.012_{\rm syst.}$ Taking the world average of $\mathcal{B}(Λ_c^+\to Λπ^+η)$ as reference, the absolute branching fraction is calculated to be $\mathcal{B}(Λ_c^+\to nπ^+η)=(2.94\pm0.59_{\rm stat.}\pm0.23_{\rm syst.}\pm0.13_{\rm ref.})\times10^{-3}$. The intermediate process $Λ_c^+\to na_0(980)^+$ is also searched for in the $π^+η$ invariant mass spectrum. Since no significant signal is found, the upper limit on $\mathcal{B}(Λ_c^+\to na_0(980)^+)\times\mathcal{B}(a_0(980)^+\toπ^+η)$ is set to $8.4\times10^{-4}$ at 90\% confidence level. A sophisticated deep learning approach using a Transformer-based architecture is employed to distinguish signals from prevalent hadronic backgrounds, complemented by thorough validation and systematic uncertainty quantification.

</details>

Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 首次观测到双粲重子Ξ_{cc}^+，通过其衰变到Λ_c^+ K^- π^+末态，统计显著性超过7个标准差，这是LHCb Run 3探测器首次发现的新粒子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在首次观测双粲重子（doubly charmed baryon）Ξ_{cc}^+，这是粒子物理学中寻找已久的重要强子态，对理解量子色动力学（QCD）和重子结构具有重要意义。

Method: 利用LHCb Run 3探测器在2024年收集的质子-质子（proton-proton）对撞数据，质心能量为13.6 TeV，总积分亮度为6.9 fb^{-1}，通过分析Ξ_{cc}^+衰变到Λ_c^+ K^- π^+的末态进行观测。

Result: 首次观测到Ξ_{cc}^+，统计显著性超过7σ；测得质量为3619.97 ± 0.83(统计) ± 0.26(系统) ^{+1.90}_{-1.30}(寿命) MeV/c^2；确定Ξ_{cc}^+与Ξ_{cc}^{++}的质量差为-1.77 ± 0.84 ± 0.15 ^{+1.90}_{-1.30} MeV/c^2。

Conclusion: 这是首次使用LHCb Run 3探测器观测到的新粒子，成功发现了双粲重子Ξ_{cc}^+，为强子谱学和量子色动力学研究提供了重要实验证据。

Abstract: The first observation of the doubly charmed baryon $\itΞ_{cc}^+$ is reported through its decay to the $\itΛ_c^+ K^-π^+$ final state, with a statistical significance exceeding seven standard deviations. The observation is made using proton-proton collision data collected in 2024 with the LHCb Run 3 detector at a center-of-mass energy of 13.6 TeV, corresponding to a total integrated luminosity of $6.9\,\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$. The $\itΞ_{cc}^+$ mass is measured to be $3619.97 \pm 0.83 \pm 0.26 \,^{+1.90}_{-1.30}\,\mathrm{MeV}/c^2$, where the first uncertainty is statistical, the second is systematic, and the third is due to the unknown $\itΞ_{cc}^+$ lifetime, which is assumed to lie in the range 15-160 fs with a baseline value of 45 fs. The difference between the masses of the $\itΞ_{cc}^+$ and $\itΞ_{cc}^{++}$ baryons is determined to be $-1.77 \pm 0.84 \pm 0.15 \,^{+1.90}_{-1.30}\,\mathrm{MeV}/c^2$. This is the first observation of a new particle made with the LHCb Run 3 detector.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验采用缺失质量技术（missing mass technique）：当湮灭过程产生一个可见光子和一个暗光子时，电磁量能器（electromagnetic calorimeter）记录可见光子。通过已知束流能量重建暗光子质量，实现对暗光子的探测。

Result: 本文重点介绍了PADME数据分析技术、背景成分分析以及背景抑制程序。这些方法为从实验数据中提取暗光子信号提供了系统框架。

Conclusion: PADME实验通过正电子湮灭过程和缺失质量技术，为探测连接可见与隐藏扇区的暗光子提供了系统的实验方案和分析框架。

PADME explores the process of annihilation of beam positrons with the electrons in a fixed target, employing the missing mass technique: in case the annihilation results in the associate production of one visible and one Dark photon, the first can be registered by the experiment's electromagnetic calorimeter and the Dark Photon mass can be reconstructed knowing the beam energy. This paper presents the analysis techniques that are being employed for the PADME data, as well as the background composition and rejection procedure.

### [169] [Inclusive jet cross section in $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 200$ and $510$ GeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28695)
*The STAR Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文报告了在RHIC的STAR探测器上测量的质子-质子碰撞中双微分喷注（jet）横截面，作为喷注横向动量（p_T）和赝快度（η）的函数，质心能量为√s = 200和510 GeV。这些数据用于约束质子中的胶子部分子分布函数（PDF），并与次次领头阶（NNLO）微扰量子色动力学（pQCD）计算进行比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在RHIC的质子-质子碰撞中，喷注产生主要由胶子-胶子（gg）和夸克-胶子（qg）部分子过程主导，这为直接探测质子中的胶子部分子分布函数（PDF）提供了与深度非弹性散射互补的方法。特别是在x_T区域（0.07-0.5和0.03-0.31），胶子PDF在TeV能级的质子-质子（pp）或质子-反质子（p\bar{p}）对撞机数据中约束较差。

Method: 使用STAR探测器研究质子-质子碰撞，测量双微分包容喷注横截面作为喷注横向动量（p_T）和赝快度（η）的函数。通过应用离轴锥方法（off-axis cone method）对喷注p_T进行底层事件贡献的校正。在中间赝快度区域（|η| < 0.9）进行测量。

Result: 获得了在质心能量√s = 200和510 GeV下的双微分包容喷注横截面数据。在中间赝快度区域，运动学覆盖范围扩展到x_T = 0.07-0.5（200 GeV）和x_T = 0.03-0.31（510 GeV）。这些包容喷注横截面与使用多个最新PDF集作为输入的次次领头阶（NNLO）微扰量子色动力学（pQCD）计算进行了比较。

Conclusion: 这些结果将进一步约束胶子部分子分布函数（PDF），帮助调校蒙特卡洛生成器（Monte Carlo generators），并为研究夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）提供关键参考数据。测量数据与理论计算的比较有助于验证和改进对质子内部结构的理解。

Abstract: Jets are collimated clusters of particles formed by the hadronization of partons following a hard interaction. In proton-proton ($pp$) collisions at the Relativistic Heavy Ion Collider (RHIC), jet production is dominated by $gg$ and $qg$ partonic processes, allowing us to directly probe the gluon parton distribution function (PDF) in the proton in a way complementary to deep inelastic scattering. In this paper, we report the double-differential inclusive-jet cross sections as a function of jet transverse momentum, $p_{\rm T}$, and pseudorapidity, $η$, at center-of-mass energies $\sqrt{s} = 200$ and $510$~GeV, from $pp$ collisions studied with the STAR detector. The jet $p_{\rm T}$ is corrected for underlying event contributions by applying an off-axis cone method. At mid-pseudorapidity, $|η| < 0.9$, the kinematic coverage of our data extends to $0.07 < x_{\rm T} \text{ (}= 2p_{\rm T}{} / \sqrt{s} \text{)} < 0.5$ and $0.03 < x_{\rm T} < 0.31$ at $\sqrt{s} = 200$~and 510 GeV, respectively, where the gluon PDF is poorly constrained by the TeV-scale $pp$~($p\bar{p}$) colliders. The inclusive jet cross sections are compared to the next-to-next-to-leading order perturbative quantum chromodynamics calculations using several recent PDF sets as inputs. These results will further constrain the gluon PDF, help tune Monte Carlo generators, and provide critical reference data needed to study the quark-gluon plasma.

### [170] [The Structure of Scientific Socialism: Quantum Emergence, Frustration, and the Non-Dual Dialectic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27649)
*Sindhunil Barman Roy*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典马克思主义及其革命代数建立在19世纪牛顿唯物主义的本体论约束内——一个离散、可预测的台球式相互作用世界。然而，20世纪物理学从托马斯·库恩的范式转换到菲尔·安德森的涌现哲学，已经瓦解了这种机械世界观的基础。

Method: 通过将现代凝聚态物理（condensed matter physics）与非二元吠檀多哲学（Advaita Vedanta）相结合，并透过自旋玻璃（Spin-Glasses）和莫特绝缘体（Mott Insulators）的视角考察几何阻挫（Geometric Frustration）与竞争相互作用（Competing Interactions）概念。

Result: 论证社会停滞与综合是普遍意识场（universal consciousness field）的涌现特性而非机械必然性，并探索这种量子信息辩证法如何解决个体与集体之间的本质张力。

Conclusion: 这种量子信息辩证法呼应了薛定谔和海森堡关于现实基本统一的直觉，为科学社会主义提供了基于现代物理学和哲学的新理论框架。

Abstract: Classical Marxism and the algebra of revolution were formulated within the ontological constraints of 19th-century Newtonian materialism-a world of discrete, predictable, billiard-ball interactions. However, the 20th-century transitions in physics, from Thomas Kuhn's paradigm shifts to Phil Anderson's philosophy of emergence, have dismantled the reductionist foundations of this mechanical worldview. This paper proposes a New Manifesto for Scientific Socialism by synthesizing modern condensed matter physics with the non-dual philosophy of Advaita Vedanta. By examining the concepts of Geometric Frustration and Competing Interactions through the lens of Spin-Glasses and Mott Insulators, we argue that social stasis and synthesis are emergent properties of a universal consciousness field rather than mechanical inevitabilities. We further explore how this quantum-informed dialectic resolves the essential tension between the individual and the collective, echoing the intuitions of Schrodinger and Heisenberg regarding the foundational unity of reality.

### [171] [Enumeration of general planar hypermaps with an alternating boundary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28571)
*Valentin Baillard,Ariane Carrance,Bertrand Eynard*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文扩展了平面超图（planar hypermaps）的枚举研究，针对具有交替边界（alternating boundary）的情况，通过新的策略获得了一般情况下的代数方程，并应用于伊辛四角化（Ising quadrangulations）获得显式有理参数化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在扩展Bouttier和第二作者先前工作中引入的具有交替边界的平面超图的枚举研究。先前研究仅针对m-星座（m-constellations）情况获得了显式有理参数化，需要开发新策略处理更一般情况。

Method: 本文开发了一种新策略，通过经典的多对一对应关系（many-to-one correspondence）获得一般情况下的代数方程，包括由伊辛模型（Ising model）装饰的映射。策略的关键步骤是同时消除两个催化变量（catalytic variables），并将此策略应用于伊辛四角化情况。

Result: 在伊辛四角化（Ising quadrangulations）情况下获得了显式有理参数化（explicit rational parametrization）。研究结果显示，星座情况下的一些显著性质在一般情况下不再成立。

Conclusion: 本文成功扩展了具有交替边界的平面超图的枚举研究，开发了处理一般情况的新策略，并在伊辛四角化情况下获得了显式有理参数化，揭示了星座情况与一般情况的差异。

Abstract: In this paper, we extend the enumerative study of planar hypermaps with an alternating boundary introduced in an earlier work of Bouttier and the second author. In that article, an explicit rational parametrization was obtained for the associated generating function in the case of m-constellations, using a variant of the kernel method. We develop here a new strategy to obtain an algebraic equation in the general case, which includes maps decorated by the Ising model, through a classical many-to-one correspondence. One of the main steps of our strategy is the simultaneous elimination of two catalytic variables. We then apply this strategy to the case of Ising quadrangulations, where we obtain an explicit rational parametrization. As a consequence, we show that some notable properties of the constellations case are no longer satisfied in general.

### [172] [Fractional epidemics from quantum loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26708)
*Jose Jesus Bernal-Alvarado,David Delepine*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过非平衡量子场论模型，首次从第一性原理推导出时空分数阶流行病动力学，揭示了异常传播机制下有效再生数（Reff）从标量转变为谱色散关系的本质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典流行病学隔室模型基于充分混合的局部相互作用近似，无法捕捉真实世界疫情中观察到的重尾爆发动力学和长程空间相关性。虽然分数阶微积分常被用于建模这些异常行为，但分数阶算符的引入通常是现象学的。

Method: 采用非平衡量子场论模型，通过Doi-Peliti形式主义将随机传染过程映射到规范介导的场论。超越静态平均场近似，计算完整的动力学单圈真空极化，证明积分掉动态涨落的宿主真空会产生异常的动量和频率标度。

Result: 推导出耦合的时空分数阶积分-微分方程，其中非线性传播顶点由抛物型Riesz势和Riemann-Liouville时间导数控制。在异常区域（α<2），局部Debye屏蔽被修正，促进了Lévy飞行超级传播和时间雪崩。有效再生数（Reff）不再是标量，转变为严格受紫外空间截断限制的谱色散关系。

Conclusion: 分数阶时空流行病动力学可以从第一性原理自然且严格地推导出来，这为理解异常传播机制提供了理论基础，并揭示了有效再生数在异常传播机制下的本质转变。

Abstract: Classical compartmental models of epidemiology rely on well-mixed, local interaction approximations that fail to capture the heavy-tailed burst dynamics and long-range spatial correlations observed in real-world outbreaks. While fractional calculus is frequently employed to model these anomalous behaviors, fractional operators are introduced phenomenologically. In this work, we demonstrate that fractional space-time epidemic dynamics emerge naturally and rigorously from first principles using a non-equilibrium quantum field theory model. By mapping the stochastic contagion process to a gauge-mediated field theory via the Doi-Peliti formalism, we go beyond the static mean-field approximation to compute the full dynamical one-loop vacuum polarization. We prove that integrating out a dynamically fluctuating host vacuum generates anomalous momentum and frequency scaling. Transitioning back to coordinate space, this derives a coupled space-time fractional integro-differential equations, where the non-linear transmission vertex is governed by parabolic Riesz potentials and Riemann-Liouville time derivatives. We show that in the anomalous regime ($α< 2$), local Debye screening is modified, facilitating Lévy flight super-spreading and temporal avalanches. Consequently, the effective reproductive number ($R_{eff}$) ceases to be a scalar, transforming into a spectral dispersion relation bounded strictly by the ultraviolet spatial cutoff.

### [173] [Topologically quantized macroscopic attractor states in hydrated DNA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26847)
*Mariusz Pietruszka*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 驱动耗散系统在环境条件下通常表现出由涨落和弛豫塑造的连续响应，离散宏观态仅在特定动力学约束下出现。本研究旨在探索在环境条件下经典系统中宏观量子化的涌现机制。

Method: 研究采用准二维水合DNA样品在磁激发下的实验系统，测量横向极化电压Vxy的时间序列。通过统计分析和贝叶斯模型选择（Bayesian model selection）方法，识别多态共存的特征。

Result: Vxy电压表现出电报式切换（telegraph switching）行为，在明确定义的能级间随机转换。统计分析显示双峰分布，贝叶斯模型选择强烈支持多态共存。这些观测可在相位场框架（phase-field framework）中得到一致解释，其中集体U(1)极化相组织成整数标记的缠绕扇区（winding sectors）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，宏观量子化可在环境条件下的经典系统中涌现，这是由相位拓扑约束的耗散动力学（dissipative dynamics）所导致。离散电压水平反映了驱动系统的拓扑不同吸引子（topologically distinct attractors），相滑移事件（phase-slip events）介导了态间转换。

Abstract: Driven dissipative systems at ambient conditions typically exhibit continuous responses shaped by fluctuations and relaxation, with discrete macroscopic states arising only under specific dynamical constraints. Here, we report the emergence of discrete attractor states in a quasi-two-dimensional hydrated DNA sample under magnetic excitation. The transverse polarization voltage Vxy displays telegraph switching between well-defined levels, indicating stochastic transitions between metastable macroscopic states. Statistical analysis of the voltage time series reveals bimodal distributions and strong Bayesian model selection in favor of multiple coexisting states. These observations can be consistently interpreted within a phase-field framework in which a collective U(1) polarization phase organizes into integer-labeled winding sectors, with transitions mediated by phase-slip events. This framework gives rise to discrete voltage levels reflecting topologically distinct attractors of the driven system. The results suggest that macroscopic quantization can emerge in a classical system at ambient conditions as a consequence of dissipative dynamics constrained by phase topology.

### [174] [Information Theoretic Signatures of Localization and Mobility Edges in Quasiperiodic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27175)
*Arpita Goswami*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究基于Tsallis熵（Tsallis entropy）的信息论框架，分析一维准周期晶格模型中的局域化转变和迁移率边现象。通过引入熵梯度敏感性（entropy-gradient susceptibility）作为可调探针，能够清晰区分全局局域化转变与迁移率边物理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于开发一种基于信息论的方法来探测准周期系统中的局域化转变和迁移率边现象。传统方法在区分全局转变与迁移率边共存状态方面存在局限，需要更灵敏的探测工具。

Method: 采用Tsallis熵作为单粒子本征态的连续归一化泛函，其中熵指数q可调，能够增强局域峰（q>1）或扩展分量（q<1）的贡献。基于此框架，引入熵梯度敏感性，定义为Tsallis熵随能量的变化率，用于探测谱中本征态结构的变化。

Result: 在Aubry-Andre模型中，所有本征态经历均匀转变，熵平滑变化，敏感性呈现宽交叉。而在具有迁移率边的系统中，包括准周期调制的Su-Schrieffer-Heeger链和广义Aubry-Andre模型，局域态与扩展态共存导致尖锐谱变化，产生显著且与系统尺寸无关的峰。定性行为在熵参数q的广泛范围内持续存在。

Conclusion: 研究建立了一种信息论方法，利用Tsallis熵的连续q依赖性构建基于导数的谱异质性度量，为迁移率边现象提供了与传统状态分辨测量互补且物理透明的诊断工具。

Abstract: We investigate localization transitions and mobility edge phenomena in one-dimensional quasiperiodic lattice models using an information theoretic framework based on the Tsallis entropy of single particle eigenstates.We employ the Tsallis entropy as a continuous, normalized functional of wavefunction amplitudes, where the entropic index $q$ provides a tunable sensitivity to different regions of the probability distribution, enhancing the contribution of localized peaks ($q>1$) or extended components ($q<1$). Building on this framework, we introduce an entropy-gradient susceptibility defined from the energy dependence of the Tsallis entropy, which probes variations in eigenstate structure across the spectrum. We show that this quantity clearly distinguishes global localization transitions from mobility edge physics. In the Aubry Andre model, where all eigenstates undergo a uniform transition, the entropy varies smoothly, resulting in a broad crossover in the susceptibility. In contrast, in systems hosting mobility edges, including a quasiperiodically modulated Su Schrieffer Heeger chain and the generalized Aubry Andre model, the coexistence of localized and extended states produces sharp spectral variations, leading to a pronounced and system size independent peak. The qualitative behavior persists over a broad range of the entropic parameter $q$, with systematic variations reflecting its role as a tunable probe of spectral structure. Our results establish an information theoretic approach that leverages the continuous $q$ dependence of Tsallis entropy to construct a derivative based measure of spectral heterogeneity, providing a complementary and physically transparent diagnostic of mobility edge phenomena beyond conventional state resolved measures.

### [175] [Trinity of Varentropy: Finiteness, Fluctuations, and Stability in Power-Law Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27997)
*Hiroki Suyari*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于重整化熵（renormalized entropy）的幂律分布热力学框架，通过变熵（Varentropy）概念解释了非线性参数q的物理起源，建立了q与热库热容C的关系|q-1|≃1/C。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 幂律分布在复杂系统中广泛存在，但建立其热力学一致性仍是一个理论挑战。本文旨在解决幂律统计的热力学基础问题，特别是针对强关联系统。

Method: 基于组合q-阶乘（combinatorial q-factorial）的渐近标度推导出重整化熵s_{2-q}，通过变熵概念解释非线性参数q的物理起源，并将宏观变分原理与微观超统计框架统一。

Result: 重整化熵为强关联系统提供了稳定的热力学极限，保持有限值（O(N^0)）。建立了参数q与热库热容量C的关系：|q-1|≃1/C，表明幂律统计为有限系统提供了热力学描述。

Conclusion: 幂律统计提供了有限系统的热力学描述，当热库具有有限热容量时，需要超越标准玻尔兹曼-吉布斯极限（C→∞）的推广。该框架为复杂系统中的幂律分布建立了热力学一致性基础。

Abstract: Power-law distributions are widely observed in complex systems, yet establishing their thermodynamic consistency remains a theoretical challenge. In this paper, we present a thermodynamic framework for power-law statistics based on the \textit{renormalized entropy} $s_{2-q}$. Derived from the asymptotic scaling of the combinatorial $q$-factorial, this quantity yields a stable thermodynamic limit, remaining finite ($O(N^0)$) for systems with strong correlations. Furthermore, we clarify the physical origin of the nonlinearity parameter $q$ through the concept of \textit{Varentropy} (Variance of Entropy). By unifying the macroscopic variational principle with the microscopic Superstatistics framework, we derive the relation $|q-1| \simeq 1/C$, where $C$ is the heat capacity of the reservoir. This result suggests that power-law statistics provides a thermodynamic description of finite systems, where the finite heat capacity of the heat bath necessitates a generalization beyond the standard Boltzmann-Gibbs limit ($C \to \infty$).

### [176] [Continuum Free-Energy Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27239)
*Trey Li*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在建立一种新的计算范式——连续自由能计算（continuum free-energy computing），将计算问题编码为可编程自由能泛函，利用物理系统的本征弛豫动力学进行求解。

Method: 方法基于非本征朗道理论（nonintrinsic Landau theory），通过空间控制局部相偏置（local phase bias）实现离子图案化FeRh的物理实现，利用反铁磁-铁磁界面运动（antiferromagnetic-ferromagnetic interface motion）作为弛豫机制。

Result: 研究识别了离子图案化FeRh作为该计算范式的可行物理实现，并确定了两个代表性任务类别、一个最小操作协议（minimal operating protocol）以及主要物理约束。

Conclusion: 该工作提出了连续自由能计算这一新计算范式，展示了其在离子图案化FeRh系统中的物理实现潜力，为基于弛豫动力学的计算提供了理论框架和具体实现方案。

Abstract: Building on nonintrinsic Landau theory, we introduce continuum free-energy computing as a new computing paradigm in which problem instances are encoded in programmable free-energy functionals and solved by intrinsic relaxational dynamics. We identify ion-patterned FeRh as a plausible physical realization through spatial control of the local phase bias, with antiferromagnetic-ferromagnetic interface motion providing the relaxational mechanism. We further identify two representative task classes, a minimal operating protocol, and the main physical constraints.

### [177] [Emergent Competition Between Dynamical Channels in Nonequilibrium Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27256)
*R. A. Dumer,M. Godoy,J. F. F. Mendes*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无拒绝连续时间动力学蒙特卡洛框架，用于研究由多个并发动力学机制支配的随机系统。通过研究结合保守Katz-Lebowitz-Spohn交换和非保守Glauber单自旋翻转的驱动反铁磁Ising模型，发现这些动力学的共存显著重塑了非平衡相图，稳定了原本会被驱动场破坏的反铁磁序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入无拒绝连续时间动力学蒙特卡洛（kinetic Monte Carlo）框架，其中每个动力学通道的相对活性通过其跃迁速率从瞬时构型自洽地涌现。以结合保守Katz-Lebowitz-Spohn交换和非保守Glauber单自旋翻转的驱动反铁磁Ising模型作为示例系统。

Result: 动力学共存显著重塑了温度-场平面上的非平衡相图，在原本驱动场会破坏反铁磁序的区域稳定了反铁磁序。在近零温极限下，相边界遵循幂律标度T∼|E-Ec|，指数接近1；在中等温度下，相变属于二维Ising普适类；在低温下，相变保持连续，序参量指数趋近于零。

Conclusion: 允许竞争动力学通道与系统协同演化能够从根本上改变其临界性质，揭示单一动力学描述中隐藏的集体行为，为理解多机制非平衡系统的相变行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: We introduce a rejection-free continuous-time kinetic Monte Carlo framework to study stochastic systems governed by multiple concurrent dynamical mechanisms. In this approach, the relative activity of each dynamical channel emerges self-consistently from the instantaneous configuration through its transition rates. As an illustration, we investigate a driven antiferromagnetic Ising model on a square lattice combining conservative Katz-Lebowitz-Spohn exchanges and nonconserving Glauber single-spin flips. We show that the coexistence of these dynamics qualitatively reshapes the nonequilibrium phase diagram in the temperature-field plane, stabilizing antiferromagnetic order in regions where the driving field would otherwise destroy it. Near the zero-temperature limit, the phase boundary follows a power-law scaling $T\sim|E-E_c|$ with an exponent close to unity. At intermediate temperatures, the transition belongs to the two-dimensional Ising universality class, while at low temperatures it remains continuous, with the order-parameter exponent approaching zero. Our results demonstrate that allowing competing dynamical channels to coevolve with the system can fundamentally alter its critical properties, revealing collective behavior hidden in single-dynamics descriptions.

### [178] [Geometric Foundations of Stochastic and Quantum Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28292)
*David V. Svintradze*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种随机动力学的几何表述，其中噪声、扩散、路径概率、涨落定理和熵产生都源于演化流形的内在几何结构，而非外部强加的随机性。该理论建立了曲率-噪声对应关系，并将经典随机行为、热力学不可逆性和量子跃迁振幅统一于移动流形框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在从几何角度重新理解随机动力学，探索噪声、扩散和熵产生等随机现象是否可以从确定性几何演化中自然涌现，而非依赖于外部随机性假设。这为解决经典随机行为与量子动力学之间的明显区别提供了几何框架。

Method: 基于移动流形理论，建立了曲率-噪声对应关系：涨落由逆曲率张量控制，熵产生由曲率形变控制。在移动超曲面上推导了不变连续性定律，得到几何福克-普朗克方程，曲率-速度耦合产生了决定路径权重的二次Onsager-Machlup泛函。

Result: 熵泛函满足曲率驱动的单调性定律，为热力学第二定律提供了几何推导。在二维情况下，曲率不变量简化为高斯曲率并编码拓扑信息，拓扑转变产生离散的熵跳跃。当环境空间具有闵可夫斯基度规时，产生耗散热权重的曲率-动能二次形式也产生振荡相位权重，控制熵演化的拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子获得薛定谔型结构。

Conclusion: 该理论表明随机行为、热力学不可逆性和量子跃迁振幅在移动流形框架中得到了统一。几何不仅容纳随机性，随机行为更是确定性几何演化的结果。该理论预测了曲率控制的各向异性扩散、拓扑变化事件中的熵跳跃，以及经典随机权重和量子振幅由同一曲率-动能作用产生的几何热-量子交叉。

Abstract: We develop a geometric formulation of stochastic dynamics in which noise, diffusion, path probabilities, fluctuation theorems, and entropy production arise from the intrinsic geometry of an evolving manifold rather than from externally imposed randomness. Within the theory of moving manifolds, we establish a curvature-noise correspondence: fluctuations are governed by the inverse curvature tensor, while entropy production is controlled by curvature deformation. The invariant continuity law on a moving hypersurface yields a geometric Fokker-Planck equation, and curvature-velocity coupling generates a quadratic Onsager-Machlup functional determining path weights. The resulting entropy functional satisfies a curvature-driven monotonicity law, providing a geometric derivation of the Second Law. In two dimensions, the curvature invariant reduces to Gaussian curvature and encodes topology, so topological transitions produce discrete entropy jumps. When the ambient space carries a Minkowskian signature, the same curvature-kinetic quadratic form that generates dissipative thermal weights produces oscillatory phase weights, and the Laplace-Beltrami operator governing entropy evolution acquires a Schrödinger-type structure. This provides a geometric resolution of the apparent distinction between classical stochastic behaviour and quantum dynamics. These results show that stochastic behaviour, thermodynamic irreversibility, and quantum transition amplitudes are unified within the moving manifold framework. Geometry does not merely accommodate stochasticity; stochastic behaviour arises as a consequence of deterministic geometric evolution. The theory predicts curvature-controlled anisotropic diffusion, entropy jumps at topology-changing events, and a geometric thermal-quantum crossover in which classical stochastic weights and quantum amplitudes are generated by the same curvature-kinetic action.

</details>


### [179] [Microscopic Pathways to Helix Formation: Packing Stabilization and Sticky Interactions in Chiral Polymer Condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27485)
*Biman Bagchi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究阐明了螺旋构象并非聚合物塌缩的普适结果，而是需要特定物理机制。通过识别两种无需生化特异性的最小化途径，解释了螺旋结构如何从各向同性吸引的半柔性聚合物中稳定形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于弯曲弹性和各向同性内聚力的最小化理论无法解释螺旋构象的形成，因为这类描述缺乏选择扭转、螺距或周期性堆积的机制。研究旨在阐明螺旋结构稳定所需的物理条件，解释为何螺旋在聚合物塌缩中非普适存在。

Method: 识别了两种物理上不同的最小化途径：途径(A)基于几何和空间位阻效应，结合管状堆积（厚度）约束与通用吸引力；途径(B)基于能量和匹配性，通过单体间周期性"粘附点"（sticker）吸引力实现相互作用间距与链几何的匹配。两种途径均推导了解析关系式。

Result: 途径(A)选择具有有限半径和螺距的理想螺旋堆积，左右手螺旋保持自由能完全简并，因此手性（chirality）可在无显式手性相互作用下自发出现。途径(B)通过匹配性稳定螺旋态，使沿主链的重复接触成为可能，与经典的Gibbs-DiMarzio和Zimm-Bragg机制自然连接。

Conclusion: 该框架解释了为何螺旋在聚合物塌缩中非普适存在，识别了稳定螺旋所需的物理要素，并为螺旋和手性凝聚态（condensates）何时出现提供了可检验的预测。解析关系式以持久长度（persistence length）$L_p$、相互作用强度和链长$N$表示。

Abstract: Helices are not generic outcomes of polymer collapse. Collapsed conformations of semiflexible polymers with isotropic attractions typically form globules, toroids, or rod-like structures, as seen in simulations and described by coarse-grained necklace and surface-tension models. Helical conformations, in contrast, are generally absent in minimal theories based solely on bending elasticity and isotropic cohesion, since such descriptions lack any mechanism to select torsion, pitch, or periodic packing. Here we identify two minimal and physically distinct routes by which helices can become stable without invoking biochemical specificity. Route (A) is geometric and steric: combining a tube-like packing (thickness) constraint with generic attractions selects an ideal helical packing with finite radius and pitch. Left- and right-handed helices remain exactly degenerate in free energy, so chirality emerges spontaneously even without explicit chiral interactions. Route (B) is energetic and commensurate: periodic "sticker" attractions between monomers separated by a fixed contour distance $m$ enforce a registry between interaction spacing and chain geometry. This commensurability stabilizes helical states by enabling repeated contacts along the backbone, naturally connecting to classical Gibbs-DiMarzio and Zimm-Bragg mechanisms. For both routes, we derive analytical relations for helix radius and pitch, curvature and bending energy, contact-distance constraints, and crossover conditions to toroidal and rod-like morphologies, expressed in terms of persistence length $L_p$, interaction strength, and chain length $N$. This framework explains why helices are non-generic in polymer collapse, identifies the physical ingredients required for their stabilization, and provides testable predictions for when helical and chiral condensates should emerge.

Abstract: Fluctuations in parameters that are typically treated as fixed play a crucial role in the behavior of complex systems. However, to date, we lack a general non-equilibrium thermodynamic treatment of such a complex system. In this Letter, to address this problem, we develop a framework in which fluctuating interactions between units of nonlinear network systems are modeled as uncorrelated colored noise (i.e., annealed disorder) with a correlation time. This approach enables us to quantify how the entropy production rate (EPR) depends on both the characteristic time-scale and the strength of the disorder. Using dynamical mean field theory, we derive an exact expression for EPR at any transient time that is validated by simulations of the full non-linear dynamics. At stationarity, a relation between EPR and autocorrelation is established and then used to analytically study the particular case of linear systems.

### [181] [Conditional KPZ reduction in a one-dimensional model of bosonic dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27887)
*Rin Takada*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨波状暗物质（wave-like dark matter）的一维Gross-Pitaevskii-Poisson模型中，何种粗粒化变量可与Kardar-Parisi-Zhang（KPZ）固定点进行有意义的比较。研究发现相关场不是原始微观相位，而是来自声波扇区（sound sector）的分支解析粗粒化相位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用一维Gross-Pitaevskii-Poisson玩具模型，分析自引力作用下玻色场的动力学。通过构建来自声波扇区的分支解析粗粒化相位（branch-resolved coarse-grained phase），在Jeans尺度以上和微观截断以下的窗口内，将自引力视为局部声动力学的弱变形。

Conclusion: 该研究未确立自引力玻色暗物质的KPZ普适性，但识别了适当的比较场和受控区域，在此区域内可以提出精确的固定点测试。研究结果为后续检验KPZ固定点提供了理论基础和具体框架。

Abstract: Wave-like dark matter described by a high-occupancy self-gravitating bosonic field provides a microscopic setting in which both amplitude and phase are dynamical. We study a one-dimensional Gross--Pitaevskii--Poisson toy model and ask which coarse-grained variable, if any, can be meaningfully compared with the 1+1-dimensional Kardar--Parisi--Zhang (KPZ) fixed point. We show that the relevant field is not the raw microscopic phase but a branch-resolved coarse-grained phase built from the sound sector. Above the Jeans scale and below the microscopic cutoff, self-gravity acts as a weak deformation of local sound dynamics. In this window the exact linear modes admit a local sound form, and a weakly nonlinear projection yields a nonvanishing same-chirality Burgers self-coupling. Under one-branch dominance together with a local Markov closure, the dominant branch reduces conditionally to a KPZ-type equation. We also formulate a dictionary from microscopic initial data to the canonical curved, flat, and stationary KPZ benchmarks. Our results do not establish KPZ universality for self-gravitating bosonic dark matter, but they identify the proper comparison field and the controlled regime in which an exact fixed-point test can be posed.

### [182] [Scaling of Long-Range Loop-Erased Random Walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27992)
*Tianning Xiao,Xianzhi Pan,Zhijie Fan,Youjin Deng*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过蒙特卡洛模拟研究了长程环路擦除随机游走（LR-LERW）的标度性质，其中基础随机游走具有幂律步长分布。研究发现d_N指数随σ连续变化，在临界维度上下呈现不同标度行为，并观察到对数修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究长程环路擦除随机游走（long-range loop-erased random walks, LR-LERW）的标度性质，其中基础随机游走具有类似Lévy飞行的幂律步长分布。该研究旨在理解长程相互作用如何影响环路擦除过程的临界行为。

Method: 采用广泛的蒙特卡洛模拟（extensive Monte Carlo simulations），测量环路擦除步数N与空间范围R之间的标度关系N ∼ R^{d_N}。在不同空间维度（d = 1, 2, 3）以及d=4和5的边际点σ=2处，计算几何指数d_N随σ的变化。

Result: 观察到d_N随σ增加从长程（LR）到短程（SR）行为的连续交叉。在上临界维度d<d_c=4以下，当σ<d/2时环路擦除渐近无关，d_N=σ符合Lévy飞行标度；当d/2<σ<2时环路擦除相关，d_N连续变化趋向SR-LERW值。在σ=d/2或σ=2的边际点观察到清晰的对数修正。

Conclusion: 研究结果提供了LR-LERW跨维度的d_N(σ)系统数值确定，支持σ_*=2作为长程与短程临界行为边界的普遍性，该边界已在多种统计模型中得到证实。在上临界维度及以上，σ=2时的标度行为N ∼ R^2/ln R与相应Lévy飞行一致。

Abstract: We study the scaling properties of long-range loop-erased random walks (LR-LERW), where the underlying random walker performs Lévy-flight-like jumps with a power-law step-length distribution $P(\mathbf{r})\sim |\mathbf{r}|^{-(d+σ)}$. Using extensive Monte Carlo simulations, we measure the scaling relation $N \sim R^{d_N}$ between the loop-erased step number $N$ and the spatial extent $R$, and determine the geometric exponent $d_N$ for various values of $σ$ in spatial dimensions $d = 1, 2,$ and $3$, as well as at the marginal point $σ= 2$ in $d=4$ and $5$. We observe a continuous crossover from long-range (LR) to short-range (SR) behavior as $σ$ increases. Below the upper critical dimension $d<d_c=4$, for $σ< d/2$, loop erasure is asymptotically irrelevant and $d_N=σ$, consistent with Lévy-flight scaling. For $d/2 < σ< 2$, loop erasure becomes relevant and $d_N$ varies continuously toward the SR-LERW value. At the marginal points with $σ=d/2$ or $σ=2$, clear logarithmic corrections are observed. At and above the upper critical dimension, $d \geq 4$, the scaling at $σ=2$ is found to be $N \sim R^2/\ln R$, consistent with that of the corresponding Lévy flight. Our results provide a systematic numerical determination of $d_N(σ)$ for the LR-LERW across dimensions, and are consistent with $σ_* = 2$ as the boundary between LR and SR critical behaviors recently established in a broad variety of statistical models.

</details>


### [183] [Ergotropic rearrangement of phase space density](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28388)
*Michele Campisi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提供了经典系统遍历性（ergotropy，即可用能量）的通用表达式，突破了先前对相空间密度连续且无平台区域的限制。通过将遍历性问题转化为函数重排问题，引入了"遍历性重排"概念，并应用于热力学极限下的经典遍历性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前经典系统遍历性的显式表达式仅适用于相空间密度连续且无平台区域的情况，这限制了其应用范围。本研究旨在提供适用于更一般情况的遍历性通用表达式。

Method: 将遍历性问题转化为函数重排问题，从而推导出通用表达式。该方法引入了"遍历性重排"概念，该概念推广了测度论中的"对称递减重排"。

Result: 获得了适用于任意相空间密度的经典遍历性通用表达式。在热力学极限下，发现任何形式为$ρ=f(H_0)$的密度都是渐近被动的，其中$H_0$是系统哈密顿量，$f$是任意函数。

Conclusion: 通过函数重排方法成功推导出经典遍历性的通用表达式，突破了先前限制。在热力学极限下，形式为$ρ=f(H_0)$的密度表现出渐近被动特性，这为经典系统能量提取能力的研究提供了新见解。

Abstract: The explicit expression of ergotropy (a.k.a. available energy) of a classical system is known for the case when the system phase space density is continuous and with no plateaus. Here we provide the general expression of ergotropy that applies without those limitations. It easily follows upon casting the ergotropy problem as a function rearrangement problem. This leads to the notion of "ergotropic rearangement" which generalises that of "symmetric decreasing rearrangement" (an advanced topic of measure theory). We apply it to investigate the fate of classical ergotropy in the thermodynamic limit, and find that any density of the form $ρ=f(H_0)$ is asymptotically passive, where $H_0$ is the system Hamiltonian and $f$ a generic function.

</details>

### [184] [A classification of irreducible unitary modules over $\mathfrak{u}(p,q|n)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28094)
*Mark D. Gould,Artem Pulemotov,Jorgen Rasmussen,Yang Zhang*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 该论文对一般线性李超代数（general linear Lie superalgebra）$\mathfrak{gl}_{p+q|n}$的非紧实形式$\mathfrak{u}(p,q|n)$的所有不可约最高权酉模（irreducible highest-weight unitary modules）进行了完全分类，并给出了最高权的显式充要条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于对一般线性李超代数$\mathfrak{gl}_{p+q|n}$的非紧实形式$\mathfrak{u}(p,q|n)$的不可约最高权酉模进行系统分类。这类分类问题在李超代数表示理论中具有重要意义，特别是在理解酉表示的结构和性质方面。

Method: 研究方法结合了$\mathfrak{gl}_{p+q|n}$的Howe对偶性（Howe duality）与最大紧子代数（maximal compact subalgebra）的二次不变量（quadratic invariant）。通过这一组合方法，建立了对最高权的显式充要条件。

Result: 主要结果是对$\mathfrak{u}(p,q|n)$的所有不可约最高权酉模进行了完全分类，并给出了最高权的显式充要条件。此外，通过对偶性分类了$\mathfrak{u}(p,q|n)$的所有不可约最低权酉模，并通过李超代数同构分类了$\mathfrak{u}(n|q,p)$的所有不可约酉模。

Conclusion: 该研究成功完成了对$\mathfrak{u}(p,q|n)$不可约最高权酉模的完全分类，并利用对偶性和同构关系将结果推广到相关代数结构，为李超代数表示理论提供了重要的分类结果。

Abstract: We classify all irreducible highest-weight unitary modules over the non-compact real form $\mathfrak{u}(p,q|n)$ of the general linear Lie superalgebra $\mathfrak{gl}_{p+q|n}$. The classification is given by explicit necessary and sufficient conditions on the highest weights. Our approach combines the Howe duality for $\mathfrak{gl}_{p+q|n}$ with a quadratic invariant of the maximal compact subalgebra. As consequences, we classify all irreducible lowest-weight unitary modules over $\mathfrak{u}(p,q|n)$ via duality, and all irreducible unitary modules over $\mathfrak{u}(n|q,p)$ via an isomorphism of Lie superalgebras.

</details>

### [185] [Semiautomatic dimensional screening of plastic scintillator cubes using image analysis and robotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26732)
*Tatsuya Kikawa,Mao Tani,Atsuko K. Ichikawa,Tsunayuki Matsubara,Tsuyoshi Nakaya,Tomohisa Ogawa*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文开发了一套用于1 cm³塑料闪烁体立方体尺寸筛选的半自动系统，该系统通过旋转平台、高分辨率相机和图像分析软件实现尺寸、表面突起和光纤孔位置的测量，并引入6轴机械臂实现立方体的自动分类，为未来大型粒子物理探测器提供可扩展的精确质量控制方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型粒子物理探测器通常包含数百万个重复组件，因此精确高效的质量控制至关重要。本研究旨在开发一套用于1 cm³塑料闪烁体立方体（plastic scintillator cubes）的尺寸筛选系统，这些立方体可能用于未来的中微子探测器（neutrino detectors）。

Method: 系统采用电机驱动旋转平台（motorized rotating stage）、六台高分辨率相机和图像分析软件，测量立方体尺寸、表面突起以及用于光学读出的波长位移光纤（wavelength-shifting fibers）的孔位置。基于这些测量结果，每个立方体被自动分类为合格或缺陷品。为在保持方向的同时将立方体按孔位置分为48组，引入了6轴机械臂（6-axis robotic arm）。

Result: 构建并验证了原型系统，实现了10 μm的测量精度，与人工筛选的一致性超过80%。完整系统的剔除率（rejection rate）达到3.1%，表明系统能够有效识别缺陷组件。

Conclusion: 该方法为未来大型粒子物理探测器提供了可扩展（scalable）、精确且高效的质量控制方案，有助于确保大规模探测器组件的质量一致性。

Abstract: Large-scale particle physics detectors often contain millions of repeated components, making precise and efficient quality control essential. We have developed a semiautomatic system for dimensional screening of 1 cm$^3$ plastic scintillator cubes for their potential use in future neutrino detectors. The system employs a motorized rotating stage, six high-resolution cameras, and image analysis software to measure cube size, surface protrusions, and the positions of holes for wavelength-shifting fibers used in optical readout. Based on these measurements, each cube is automatically classified as either acceptable or defective. We constructed and validated a prototype system, achieving a measurement precision of 10 $μ$m and over 80% consistency with manual screening. To enable classification of cubes into 48 groups based on hole positions while preserving their orientation, we introduced a 6-axis robotic arm. The completed system achieved a rejection rate of 3.1%. Our approach contributes to scalable, precise, and efficient quality control for future large-scale particle physics detectors.

</details>

*D. S. Akerib,A. K. Al Musalhi,F. Alder,B. J. Almquist,C. S. Amarasinghe,A. Ames,T. J. Anderson,N. Angelides,H. M. Araújo,J. E. Armstrong,M. Arthurs,A. Baker,S. Balashov,J. Bang,J. W. Bargemann,E. E. Murphy,H. N. Nelson,F. Neves,A. Nguyen,C. L. O'Brien,F. H. O'Shea,I. Olcina,K. C. Oliver-Mallory,J. Orpwood,K. Y. Oyulmaz,K. J. Palladino,N. J. Pannifer,S. J. Patton,B. Penning,G. Pereira,E. Perry,T. Pershing,A. Piepke,S. S. Poudel,Y. Qie,J. Reichenbacher,C. A. Rhyne,G. R. C. Rischbieter,E. Ritchey,H. S. Riyat,R. Rosero,N. J. Rowe,T. Rushton,D. Rynders,S. Saltão,D. Santone,A. B. M. R. Sazzad,R. W. Schnee,G. Sehr,B. Shafer,S. Shaw,W. Sherman,K. Shi,T. Shutt,C. Silva,G. Sinev,J. Siniscalco,A. M. Slivar,A. M. Softley-Brown,V. N. Solovov,P. Sorensen,J. Soria,T. J. Sumner,A. Swain,M. Szydagis,D. R. Tiedt,D. R. Tovey,J. Tranter,M. Trask,K. Trengove,M. Tripathi,A. Usón,A. C. Vaitkus,O. Valentino,V. Velan,A. Wang,J. J. Wang,Y. Wang,L. Weeldreyer,T. J. Whitis,K. Wild,M. Williams,J. Winnicki,L. Wolf,F. L. H. Wolfs,S. Woodford,D. Woodward,C. J. Wright,Q. Xia,J. Xu,Y. Xu,M. Yeh,D. Yeum,J. Young,W. Zha,H. Zhang,T. Zhang,Y. Zhou*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: LUX-ZEPLIN (LZ)实验通过脉冲形状甄别（PSD）和电荷-光信号比（charge-to-light）的双因子甄别（TFD）方法，显著提高了暗物质探测中电子反冲（ER）背景的抑制能力，将ER泄漏率降低至15%，特定背景过程可降至5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗物质直接探测的主要挑战在于区分弱相互作用大质量粒子（WIMPs）信号与背景事件。LZ实验需要改进电子反冲（ER）背景的抑制方法，脉冲形状甄别（PSD）为液氙探测器提供了额外的背景抑制手段。

Method: 开发了分析框架以重建单个光子的探测时间，精确表征闪烁脉冲形状。优化了光子时序即时分数甄别器，并将脉冲形状甄别（PSD）与电荷-光信号比（charge-to-light）方法结合，形成双因子甄别（TFD）技术。

Result: 脉冲形状甄别（PSD）实现了低至15%的ER泄漏率，对于特定背景过程如$^{124}$Xe双电子俘获，泄漏率进一步降至约5%。双因子甄别（TFD）将大闪烁脉冲对应的假阳性率降低最多两倍。

Conclusion: 脉冲形状甄别（PSD）和双因子甄别（TFD）方法在LZ实验的WS2024运行数据中得到应用，显著提升了暗物质探测的背景抑制性能，为弱相互作用大质量粒子（WIMPs）搜索提供了更有效的甄别工具。

Abstract: The LUX-ZEPLIN (LZ) experiment is a direct-detection dark matter experiment, optimized to search for weakly interacting massive particles (WIMPs) through WIMP-nucleon interactions. The main challenge in dark matter detection is differentiating between WIMP signals and background events. In LZ, the ratio of ionization to scintillation signals (charge-to-light) is the primary method for rejecting electronic recoil (ER) background. Pulse shape discrimination (PSD) offers a method for additional ER backgrounds rejection in liquid xenon detectors. In this paper, the discrimination power of PSD with the LZ experiment is discussed. To precisely characterize the scintillation pulse shape, an analysis framework is developed to reconstruct the detection time of individual photons. Using LZ calibration data, the photon-timing prompt fraction discriminator is optimized and achieves ER leakage as low as $15\%$. For specific background processes such as $^{124}$Xe double electron capture, the leakage is reduced further to about $5\%$. PSD is combined with charge-to-light to form two-factor discrimination (TFD). The optimized TFD performance is compared with the performance of the charge-to-light method, with the corresponding false positive rate reduced by up to a factor of two for large scintillation pulses. Finally, PSD and TFD are applied to data from LZ's WS2024 run and their performance is summarized.

### [187] [Xenon Signal Denoising via Supervised, Semi-Supervised, and Unsupervised Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27005)
*Grant Kendrick Parker,Jason Brodsky,Indra Chakraborty*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种基于机器学习的去噪算法，用于提升单相液氙时间投影室在无中微子双贝塔衰变探测中的能量分辨率。监督、无监督和半监督模型均能显著去除模拟测量中的噪声，同时保留信号信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在改进单相液氙时间投影室（single-phase liquid xenon time projection chamber）在无中微子双贝塔衰变（neutrinoless double beta decay）探测中的能量分辨率。传统算法存在局限性，需要探索机器学习方法以提升探测灵敏度。

Method: 研究开发了基于机器学习的去噪算法，包括监督学习（supervised）、无监督学习（unsupervised）和半监督学习（semi-supervised）三种模型。这些模型应用于模拟测量数据的噪声去除，同时确保信号信息的完整性。

Result: 监督模型实现了<1%的能量分辨率，半监督模型达到约1%的能量分辨率，而无监督模型的性能约为1.5%。所有模型均能显著去除噪声并保留信号，证明机器学习去噪相比传统算法具有优势。

Conclusion: 研究表明，即使实验人员缺乏完美的先验信号知识，机器学习去噪仍能显著提升能量分辨率。这些模型为实现下一代无中微子双贝塔衰变搜索的灵敏度提供了现实可行的技术路径。

Abstract: This study presents a denoising algorithm trained using machine learning to improve the energy resolution of a single-phase liquid xenon time projection chamber for neutrinoless double beta decay detection. Supervised, unsupervised, and semi-supervised models are demonstrated to significantly remove noise from simulated measurements while preserving signal information. The supervised model achieves an energy resolution of $<1\%$, while the semi-supervised models achieve energy resolutions of $\sim 1\%$, and the unsupervised model performance is $\sim 1.5\%$. This work is evidence that machine learning denoising can improve energy resolution compared to traditional algorithms, even when experimentalists lack perfect a priori knowledge of the signals. Such models provide a realistic path toward next-generation sensitivity in $0νββ$ searches.

</details>


### [188] [Construction and characterization of a muon trigger detector for the PSI muEDM experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27483)
*Guan Ming Wong,Tianqi Hu,Samip Basnet,Chavdar Dutsov,Siew Yan Hoh,David Höhl,Xingyun Huang,Timothy David Hume,Alexander Johannes Jäger,Kim Siang Khaw,Meng Lyu,Ljiljana Morvaj,Jun Kai Ng,Angela Papa,Diego Alejandro Sanz Becerra,Philipp Schmidt-Wellenburg,Yusuke Takeuchi,Yonghao Zeng*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文介绍了为瑞士PSI研究所μ子电偶极矩（muEDM）实验开发的μ子触发探测器（MTD）的升级设计、建造和束流测试结果。该探测器通过门探测器与活动孔径探测器的反符合触发机制，实现了对可存储μ子的精确识别，为将μ子EDM测量灵敏度提高三个数量级提供了关键技术支撑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: μ子电偶极矩（muEDM）实验旨在将μ子EDM测量的灵敏度比当前BNL Muon g-2实验建立的极限提高三个数量级以上。精确识别进入存储螺线管入口的可存储μ子至关重要，因为MTD需要快速触发脉冲磁踢器，将μ子限制在螺线管中心区域的弱聚焦磁场中。

Method: MTD包含两个子系统：由四个硅光电倍增管（SiPMs）读出的0.1mm厚塑料闪烁体"门探测器"，以及由六个SiPMs读出的5mm厚CNC加工塑料闪烁体"活动孔径探测器"。通过接受度研究优化了活动孔径探测器的几何结构，以最大化存储效率和本底否决效率。集成快速电子学在反符合条件下产生LVTTL触发信号——在门探测器中检测到μ子但在孔径中未检测到——确保选择性触发可存储μ子事件。

Result: 在PSI πE1束流线上使用22.5 MeV/c μ子进行了缩比条件下的测试，以表征探测器响应和触发性能。开发了包含详细光学光子传输和SiPM响应建模的Geant4模拟，与测量的事件拓扑结构再现了约97%的一致性。这些结果验证了探测器设计，并证明了MTD已准备好部署在完整的muEDM第一阶段装置中。

Conclusion: MTD的升级设计、建造和束流测试结果验证了其性能满足muEDM实验要求。探测器系统通过优化的几何设计和反符合触发机制，实现了对可存储μ子的精确识别，为将μ子EDM测量灵敏度提高三个数量级提供了可靠的技术基础。

Abstract: We present the upgraded design, construction, and beam test results for the Muon Trigger Detector (MTD) developed for the muon Electric Dipole Moment (muEDM) experiment at the Paul Scherrer Institute (PSI) in Switzerland. This experiment aims to improve the sensitivity of the muon EDM measurement by more than three orders of magnitude beyond the current limit established by the BNL Muon $g-2$ experiment. Precise identification of storable incoming muons at the entrance of the storage solenoid is essential, as the MTD must rapidly trigger a pulsed magnetic kicker to confine muons in the central region of the solenoid, where a weakly focusing magnetic field is maintained. The MTD comprises two subsystems: a \SI{0.1}{mm}-thick plastic scintillator ``gate detector'' read out by four silicon photomultipliers (SiPMs), and a \SI{5}{mm}-thick CNC-machined plastic scintillator ``active aperture detector'' read out by six SiPMs. The geometry of the active aperture detector was optimized through acceptance studies to maximize both storage efficiency and background veto efficiency. Integrated fast electronics generate an LVTTL trigger signal under an anti-coincidence condition -- a muon detected in the gate but not in the aperture -- ensuring selective triggering of storable muon events for the EDM measurement. The system was tested at the PSI $π$E1 beamline using \SI{22.5}{MeV/\textit{c}} muons under scaled-down conditions to characterize detector response and trigger performance. A Geant4 simulation incorporating detailed optical photon transport and SiPM response modeling was developed and reproduces the measured event topologies with ${\sim}97\%$ agreement. These results validate the detector design and demonstrate the MTD's readiness for deployment in the full muEDM Phase-1 setup.

</details>


### [189] [Precision timing detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27566)
*Martina Malberti,Xiaohu Sun*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文综述了高能物理实验中精密时间测量技术的最新进展，重点介绍了用于未来对撞机（如HL-LHC）的粒子识别和堆积抑制的关键探测器技术，并探讨了该领域的未来发展方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精密时间测量在高能物理实验中至关重要，特别是在未来对撞机（如高亮度大型强子对撞机HL-LHC）的挑战性条件下，用于粒子识别（particle identification）和堆积（pileup）抑制。随着对撞机环境日益复杂，需要先进的定时测量技术来满足实验需求。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，首先介绍对撞机实验中精密时间测量的动机、定时测量的物理原理以及影响探测器时间分辨率（time resolution）的关键因素。随后系统调研了近年来发展的关键探测器技术，包括硅光电倍增管（SiPMs）读取的闪烁体、低增益雪崩二极管（LGADs）、多间隙电阻板室（MRPCs）等。

Result: 综述展示了多种精密时间测量技术的进展，并以当前对撞机实验中的探测器为例，讨论了精密时间测量在大规模系统中的集成应用。同时探讨了该领域的新兴技术和未来发展方向。

Conclusion: 精密时间测量技术在高能物理实验中持续发展，新兴技术有望对下一代高能物理实验产生重要影响。该综述为未来对撞机实验中的定时探测器技术发展提供了全面的技术评估和方向指引。

Abstract: Precision timing has played a critical role in high-energy physics experiments, particularly for particle identification and the suppression of pileup under the challenging conditions expected at future colliders like the High-Luminosity Large Hadron Collider (HL-LHC). Over the past decades, significant advancements in timing measurement technologies have been made to meet the demands of increasingly complex collider environments. After introducing the motivation for precision timing in collider experiments, the underlying physical principles of timing measurements and the most important factors influencing the time resolution of a detector, this review presents a survey of key detector technologies developed in recent years, including scintillators read out by silicon photo-multipliers (SiPMs), low-gain avalanche diodes (LGADs), multi-gap resistive plate chambers (MRPCs). The integration of precision timing into large-scale systems is discussed with examples from detectors at current collider experiments. Finally, we explore emerging technologies and future directions in the field, highlighting their potential impact on the next generation of high-energy physics experiments.

### [190] [Suppression of $^{14}\mathrm{C}$ photon hits in large liquid scintillator detectors via spatiotemporal deep learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27727)
*Junle Li,Zhaoxiang Wu,Guanda Gong,Zhaohan Li,Wuming Luo,Jiahui Wei,Wenxing Fang,Hehe Fan*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出三种模型用于标记液体闪烁体探测器中$^{14}$C光子击中，以抑制其对能量分辨率的影响，在模拟数据中实现了25%-48%的$^{14}$C召回率，同时保持$e^+$误识别率低于1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 液体闪烁体探测器（liquid scintillator detectors）因其低能量阈值和高能量分辨率而广泛应用于中微子实验。尽管$^{14}$C在液体闪烁体中丰度极低，但其β衰变产生的光子会污染信号，降低能量分辨率。

Method: 本文提出三种模型在$^{14}$C堆积的$e^+$事件中标记$^{14}$C光子击中：一个门控时空图神经网络（gated spatiotemporal graph neural network）和两个基于Transformer的模型，分别采用标量和矢量电荷编码。

Result: 在动能低于5 MeV的模拟数据集中，每个事件包含一个$^{14}$C和一个$e^+$，模型实现了25%-48%的$^{14}$C召回率，同时保持$e^+$到$^{14}$C的误识别率低于1%。这显著改善了$e^+$和$^{14}$C光子击中在时空上强烈重叠事件的总电荷分辨率。

Conclusion: 所提出的模型能有效抑制$^{14}$C对能量分辨率的影响，特别是在$e^+$和$^{14}$C光子击中时空重叠严重的情况下，通过标记$^{14}$C光子击中实现了能量分辨率的显著提升。

Abstract: Liquid scintillator detectors are widely used in neutrino experiments due to their low energy threshold and high energy resolution. Despite the tiny abundance of $^{14}$C in LS, the photons induced by the $β$ decay of the $^{14}$C isotope inevitably contaminate the signal, degrading the energy resolution. In this work, we propose three models to tag $^{14}$C photon hits in $e^+$ events with $^{14}$C pile-up, thereby suppressing its impact on the energy resolution at the hit level: a gated spatiotemporal graph neural network and two Transformer-based models with scalar and vector charge encoding. For a simulation dataset in which each event contains one $^{14}$C and one $e^+$ with kinetic energy below 5 MeV, the models achieve $^{14}$C recall rates of 25%-48% while maintaining $e^+$ to $^{14}$C misidentification below 1%, leading to a large improvement in the resolution of total charge for events where $e^+$ and $^{14}$C photon hits strongly overlap in space and time.

</details>

*M. Cappelli,A. Wallach,H. Abele,G. Angloher,B. Arnold,M. Atzori Corona,A. Bento,E. Bossio,F. Buchsteiner,J. Burkhart,F. Cappella,N. Casali,R. Cerulli,A. Cruciani,G. Method: 研究提出了两种互补方法：第一种通过映射器件在广泛工作点范围内的信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio），识别数据采集时具有最大灵敏度的最优配置；第二种利用探测器的双读出（double readout）特性，通过二维最优滤波器分析（two-dimensional optimum filter analysis）结合不同通道信息，有效降低能量阈值。

Result: 同时应用两种技术，使用基于CaWO4的探测器获得了2.94±0.05（统计误差）eV的基线分辨率（baseline resolution），为NUCLEUS实验首次运行提供了有前景的结果。

Conclusion: 在NUCLEUS实验背景下开发和测试的这两种互补方法，成功提升了由跃迁边缘传感器（transition-edge sensors）读出的低温探测器的灵敏度，为实现稀有事件搜索的最佳探测性能提供了有效技术路径。

Abstract: Phonon-mediated cryogenic calorimeters find application in rare event searches due to their intrinsically low energy threshold. Achieving the best sensitivity for this kind of detectors is crucial for signal identification, leading to various optimization techniques. In this work, we present two complementary methods to increase the sensitivity of cryogenic detectors read out by transition-edge sensors, developed and tested in the context of the NUCLEUS experiment. The first procedure maps the signal-to-noise ratio of the device across a wide range of operating points, to identify the configuration with maximal sensitivity to be used during data taking. The second method exploits the double readout of the detector, combining the information on different channels with a two-dimensional optimum filter analysis that effectively lowers the energy threshold. With both techniques at the same time, we obtained a baseline resolution of 2.94 $\pm$ 0.05 (stat) eV using a CaWO4 based detector, achieving a promising result in view of the first run of NUCLEUS at the experimental site.

### [192] [Process Development and First Cryogenic Operation of Compact Germanium Ring-Contact HPGe Prototypes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28505)
*Kunming Dong,Shasika Panamaldeniya,Dongming Mei*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文报道了首个锗环接触（GeRC）工艺验证原型的制造与低温测试，为LEGEND-1000等稀有事件实验所需的高性能高纯锗探测器开发了非平面电极几何结构的可行性工艺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀有事件实验如LEGEND-1000需要具有优异能量分辨率、低电子噪声和可扩展低本底封装的高纯锗（HPGe）探测器。锗环接触（GeRC）概念通过凹陷的环槽电极几何结构来满足这一需求，旨在在更大晶体中保持点接触式的低电容信号形成，但其可靠制造此前尚未得到验证。

Method: 开发了优化的制造流程，包括核心钻孔、槽切割、非平面抛光、共形非晶锗（a-Ge）封装、铝图案化和GeRC特异性低温安装。使用两个独立的溅射系统测试薄膜序列在不同沉积环境下的可操作性，并在77K下对两个紧凑型n型GeRC原型进行低温操作测试。

Result: 两个器件在77K下均能稳定偏置，基于脉冲器的电容代理测量显示耗尽起始电压约为340V，与静电建模一致，并能从²⁴¹Am和¹³⁷Cs产生可识别的全能峰。这为几何特异性GeRC开发建立了原理验证工艺和读出基准。

Conclusion: 虽然这些结果尚未构成可部署的大质量GeRC技术，但为下一步工作奠定了基础：在环槽拓扑结构上集成共形锂漆沉积和受控扩散工艺，以形成稳健的锂扩散外接触。

The germanium ring-contact (GeRC) concept addresses this need through a recessed ring-and-groove electrode geometry intended to preserve point-contact-like low-capacitance signal formation in larger crystals. However, reliable GeRC fabrication has remained unproven because the non-planar groove geometry complicates machining, surface recovery, conformal passivation, and especially the eventual formation of a robust lithium-diffused outer contact.
  We report the fabrication and first cryogenic operation of two compact n-type GeRC process-validation prototypes produced from in-house HPGe crystals at the University of South Dakota. An optimized workflow was developed for core drilling, groove cutting, non-planar polishing, conformal amorphous-germanium (a-Ge) encapsulation, Al patterning, and GeRC-specific cryogenic mounting. Two independent sputtering systems were used to test whether the thin-film sequence remains operable across substantially different deposition environments. At 77~K, both devices biased stably, showed an inferred depletion onset near 340~V from a pulser-based capacitance proxy consistent with electrostatic modeling, and produced identifiable full-energy peaks from $^{241}\mathrm{Am}$ and $^{137}\mathrm{Cs}$. These results establish a proof-of-principle process and readout baseline for geometry-specific GeRC development. They do not yet constitute a deployment-ready large-mass GeRC technology, but they define the foundation for the next step: integrating conformal lithium-paint deposition and controlled diffusion on the ring-and-groove topology.

### [193] [Multi-GPU fast Fourier transforms in MATLAB (for large-scale phase-field crystal simulations)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26818)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了基于MATLAB的框架，实现二维和三维快速傅里叶变换（fast Fourier transforms）在多GPU上的并行计算，采用两种互补的多GPU策略来克服单GPU内存限制并加速谱求解器（spectral solvers）。

Result: 该数值框架实现了显著的加速效果：标准PFC模拟获得约6倍加速，多物理扩展（multiphysics extensions）获得高达60倍加速，相比运行在数百个核心上的纯CPU实现。

Conclusion: 该多GPU快速傅里叶变换框架有效解决了相场晶体模型大规模模拟中的计算瓶颈，为高精度数值模拟提供了高效的计算工具。

Abstract: We present a MATLAB-based framework for two- and three-dimensional fast Fourier transforms on multiple GPUs for large-scale numerical simulations using the pseudo-spectral Fourier method. The software implements two complementary multi-GPU strategies that overcome single-GPU memory limitations and accelerate spectral solvers. This approach is motivated by and applied to phase-field crystal (PFC) models, which are governed by tenth-order partial differential equations, require fine spatial resolution, and are typically formulated in periodic domains. Our resulting numerical framework achieves significant speedups, approximately sixfold for standard PFC simulations and up to sixtyfold for multiphysics extensions, compared to a purely CPU-based implementation running on hundreds of cores.

### [194] [Chemical tuning of electronic and transport properties of the Bi-Se-Te family of topological insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26918)
*Maxwell Doyle,Benjamin Schrunk,D. L. Schlagel,Thomas A. Lagrasso,Adam Kaminski*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 利用激光角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）研究Bi₂(Se₁₋ₓTeₓ)₃拓扑绝缘体中Te含量增加对电子性质的影响，发现Te含量增加会降低化学势，减少体带态密度，导致电阻率从金属性转变为半导体性温度依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究化学替代（chemical substitution）如何改变Bi₂(Se₁₋ₓTeₓ)₃（BiSeTe）系列拓扑绝缘体的电子性质，特别是通过调节Te含量来调控材料的电子结构和输运特性。

Method: 采用激光基角分辨光电子能谱（Angle-Resolved Photoemission Spectroscopy, ARPES）技术，系统研究不同Te含量（x值）的Bi₂(Se₁₋ₓTeₓ)₃样品，分析其电子结构和能带变化。

Result: Te含量增加会降低化学势（chemical potential），导致狄拉克点（Dirac point）结合能降低，体带（bulk band）态密度减少；电阻率温度依赖性从金属性转变为半导体性，最高Te浓度样品在最低温度下电阻率趋于饱和。

Conclusion: 最高Te浓度样品中电阻率平台的出现表明金属性拓扑表面态（metallic topological surface states）主导电导，这为研究其输运性质提供了可能性，展示了通过化学替代调控拓扑绝缘体电子性质的可行性。

Abstract: We use laser-based Angle-Resolved Photoemission Spectroscopy (ARPES) to study how chemical substitution modifies the electronic properties of the Bi2(Se{1-x}Tex)3 (BiSeTe) family of topological insulators. We find that increasing the Te content lowers the chemical potential, leading to a decrease in the binding energy of the Dirac point and a reduction in the density of states originating from the bulk band. This reduction leads to a transition from metallic to semiconducting temperature dependence of the resistivity. For the highest Te concentration, the resistivity nearly saturates at the lowest temperatures. The presence of this plateau indicates that metallic topological surface states dominate the conductance, opening the possibility of studying their transport properties.

</details>


### [195] [Bistable Fourth Sound Resonance in Superfluid $^3$He-B due to Gap Suppression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27131)
*Alexander J. Shook,Daksh Malhotra,Aymar Muhikira,John P. Davis*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该研究开发了纳米流体谐振器，在高度受限的几何结构中激发第四声（fourth sound）声学模式，观察到超流速度临界行为，并与金兹堡-朗道（Ginzburg-Landau）模型预测进行比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超流氦-3（superfluid $^3$He）在高度受限几何结构中的独特性质尚未充分探索，其中表面效应对热力学和流体力学性质起主导作用。研究旨在通过纳米流体器件连接流体力学测量与表面能隙抑制（surface gap suppression）和表面束缚态（surface-bound states）的理论预测。

Method: 开发了纳米流体谐振器（nanofluidic resonators），在薄通道（750-1800 nm）中激发第四声声学模式，该受限尺度仅比超流相干长度（superfluid coherence length）大1-2个数量级。建立了器件模型，将共振振幅校准为超流速度（superfluid velocity）。

Result: 施加足够大的驱动力时，观察到共振的非线性软化（non-linear softening），解释为超流能隙（superfluid gap）的流动抑制。校准后的超流速度在特定速度下表现出临界行为（critical behavior），其中一个临界速度对应于平行于流动的能隙分量被抑制为零。

Conclusion: 校准速度与金兹堡-朗道模型（Ginzburg-Landau model）预测基本一致。该测量代表了将纳米流体器件的流体力学测量与表面能隙抑制和表面束缚态理论预测相联系的持续努力。

Abstract: Superfluidity in $^3$He exhibits many unique properties that are of interest to modern condensed matter research, including multiple superfluid phase transitions, topological defects, and exotic classes of excitations like Majorana and Weyl fermions. Many of the most interesting theoretical proposals, which remain underexplored, are realized in highly confined geometries, where surface effects play a dominant role in the thermodynamic and hydrodynamic properties. We have developed nanofluidic resonators capable of exciting a fourth-sound acoustic mode in thin channels with a highly confined dimension ($750-1800$ nm) that is only $1-2$ orders of magnitude larger than the superfluid coherence length. When a sufficiently large drive force is applied, we observe a non-linear softening of the resonance that we interpret as due to the flow suppression of the superfluid gap. We have developed a model of the device that allows the resonance amplitude to be calibrated into a superfluid velocity, which exhibits critical behavior at particular velocities. We identify one of the observed critical velocities as being the velocity at which the gap component parallel to the flow is suppressed to zero. We compare the calibrated velocity to the prediction of a Ginzburg-Landau model, and find reasonable agreement. This measurement represents an ongoing effort to link the hydrodynamic measurements of these nanofluidic devices to theoretical predictions regarding surface gap suppression and surface-bound states.

</details>


### [196] [Direct and inverse photoemission spectra from the screened multichannel Dyson equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27329)
*Pina Romaniello,J. Arjan Berger*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文提出了屏蔽多通道戴森方程（screened multichannel Dyson equation），用于从第一性原理模拟直接和逆光电子能谱，相比标准方法能更准确地描述硅等离子体激元卫星峰的位置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标准多通道戴森方程（standard multichannel Dyson equation）和GW等标准多体方法在描述光电子能谱时存在局限性，特别是对硅等离子体激元卫星峰（plasmon satellite）的结合能估计过高，需要改进电子间相互作用的屏蔽处理。

Method: 提出了屏蔽多通道戴森方程，该方法通过正确包含所有粒子-粒子（particle-particle）和电子-空穴（electron-hole）相互作用因其他电子存在而产生的屏蔽效应，改进了标准多通道戴森方程。

Result: 以体硅（bulk silicon）为例，屏蔽多通道戴森方程能够捕捉直接和逆光电子能谱的主要特征，特别是能准确描述硅等离子体激元卫星峰的位置，而GW、标准多通道戴森方程和二阶玻恩近似（second-Born approximation）都严重高估了该卫星峰的结合能。

Conclusion: 正确屏蔽所有粒子-粒子和电子-空穴相互作用对于准确描述光电子能谱至关重要，屏蔽多通道戴森方程为此提供了有效解决方案，相比现有多体方法在描述等离子体激元卫星峰方面具有显著优势。

Abstract: We present the screened multichannel Dyson equation for the simulation of both direct and inverse photoemission spectra from first principles. The screened multichannel Dyson equation improves upon the standard multichannel Dyson equation by correctly including the screening of all particle-particle and electron-hole interactions due to the presence of the other electrons. Using the example of bulk silicon, we demonstrate that the screened multichannel Dyson equation can capture the main features of the direct and inverse photoemission spectra. In particular, it captures the correct position of the silicon plasmon satellite, unlike standard many-body approaches such as $GW$, which strongly overestimates the binding energy of this satellite. Finally, we show that also the standard multichannel Dyson equation and the second-Born approximation strongly overestimate the binding energy of the plasmon satellite, thus demonstrating the importance of properly screening all particle-particle and electron-hole interactions.

### [197] [Characterizing the Linearity of Magnonic Devices for Radio-Frequency Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27470)
*Robert Erdelyi,Adam Papp Levente Maucha,Philipp Pirro,Matthias Wagner,Dieter Ferling,Johannes Greil,Markus Becherer,Gyorgy Csaba*
