### [198] [Weakly nonlinear models for hydroelastic water waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27802)
*Diego Alonso-Orán,Rafael Granero-Belinchón,Juliana S. Ziebell*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该研究推导了水弹性波与非线性粘弹性板耦合的简化界面模型，在弱非线性小坡度条件下获得了双向非局部演化方程，并建立了包含板诱导主导色散和耗散效应的单向传播模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立水弹性波与非线性粘弹性板耦合系统的简化界面模型，以更有效地描述界面动力学行为，特别是考虑板材料引起的色散和耗散效应。

Method: 在弱非线性小坡度（weakly nonlinear small-steepness）条件下，推导了双向非局部演化方程（bidirectional nonlocal evolution equations）捕获二次阶界面动力学，并建立了两种单向模型（unidirectional models）描述单向传播。采用双参数正则化（two-parameter regularization）和嵌套不动点（nested fixed points）方法证明双向模型的局部适定性。

Result: 获得了具有双重非线性结构（doubly nonlinear structure）的双向模型，其中一个非线性椭圆算子作用于界面加速度。证明了双向模型对小数据的局部适定性（local well-posedness），以及单向模型对任意数据的局部适定性和小数据的全局适定性（global well-posedness）。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了水弹性波与非线性粘弹性板耦合的简化界面模型，提供了严格的数学分析框架，证明了模型在适当条件下的适定性，为相关物理系统的数值模拟和理论分析奠定了基础。

Abstract: In this work, we derive reduced interface models for hydroelastic water waves coupled to a nonlinear viscoelastic plate. In a weakly nonlinear small-steepness regime we obtain bidirectional nonlocal evolution equations capturing the interface dynamics up to quadratic order, and we also derive two unidirectional models describing one-way propagation while retaining the leading dispersive and dissipative effects induced by the plate. Remarkably, one of the bidirectional model has a doubly nonlinear structure in the sense that there there is a nonlinear elliptic operator acting on the acceleration of the interface. We prove local well-posedness for the bidirectional model for small data via a two-parameter regularization and nested fixed points. For the unidirectional models, we obtain local well-posedness for arbitrary data and global well-posedness for small data.

### [199] [Long-time behaviour of rouleau formation models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28194)
*Eugenia Franco,Bernhard Kepka*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个模拟血液中红细胞缗钱状聚集（rouleaux formation）的双组分凝聚方程（two-component coagulation equation）。对于齐次度为2的乘积核（product kernel），作者刻画了导致凝胶化（gelation）的初始数据，并证明了当凝胶化发生时，解会沿着簇空间（space of cluster）的某个方向局部化（localization），且该方向由初始数据决定。解还沿着局部化方向收敛到自相似解（self-similar solution）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究血液中红细胞缗钱状聚集（rouleaux formation）的数学模型。通过分析双组分凝聚方程（two-component coagulation equation），作者希望理解凝胶化（gelation）现象的发生条件及其动态特性，这对于理解血液流变学（rheology）和病理状态具有重要意义。

Method: 作者采用双组分凝聚方程（two-component coagulation equation）作为数学模型，并考虑齐次度为2的乘积核（product kernel）。通过数学分析的方法，研究该方程的动力学行为，特别是凝胶化（gelation）发生的条件以及解在凝胶化时间附近的渐近行为。

Result: 研究结果表明，对于特定的初始数据，系统会发生凝胶化（gelation）。当凝胶化发生时，解在簇空间（space of cluster）中会沿着由初始数据决定的方向局部化（localization）。此外，解沿着局部化方向收敛到自相似解（self-similar solution）。

Conclusion: 本文成功刻画了双组分凝聚方程（two-component coagulation equation）中导致凝胶化（gelation）的初始数据条件，并揭示了凝胶化过程中解的局部化（localization）行为和自相似收敛（self-similar convergence）特性。这些结果为理解血液中红细胞缗钱状聚集的动力学提供了重要的数学理论基础。

Abstract: In this paper we study a two-component coagulation equation that models the aggregation of rouleaux in blood. We consider product kernels that have homogeneity $2$ and we characterize the initial data that lead to gelation. We prove that, when gelation occurs, the solution to the two-component coagulation equation localizes along a direction of the space of cluster as $ t $ approaches the gelation time $0 < T_* < \infty $. The localization direction is determined by the initial datum. We also prove that the solution converges to a self-similar solution along the direction of localization.

### [200] [A mathematical description of the spin Hall effect of light in inhomogeneous media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28697)
*Sam C. Collingbourne,Marius A. Oancea,Jan Sbierski*

TL;DR: 本文研究了各向同性非均匀介质中麦克斯韦方程的高斯波包解，推导了描述测地线运动主导阶修正的常微分方程组，为光自旋霍尔效应提供了数学证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非均匀介质中光波包传播的修正效应，特别是测地线运动的高阶修正，旨在为光自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect of light）提供严格的数学基础。

Method: 通过分析各向同性非均匀介质中麦克斯韦方程的高斯波包解，推导出一组捕获测地线运动主导阶修正的常微分方程系统，该系统在逆频率的一阶近似下闭合。

Result: 系统包含能量质心、线动量、角动量和四极矩等动力学量，并证明具有相反圆偏振的高斯波包能量质心通常沿不同方向传播，从而为光自旋霍尔效应提供了数学证明。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了描述非均匀介质中光波包传播修正的数学模型，为光自旋霍尔效应提供了严格的数学证明，揭示了偏振依赖的传播方向分离现象。

Abstract: We study Gaussian wave packet solutions for Maxwell's equations in an isotropic, inhomogeneous medium and derive a system of ordinary differential equations that captures the leading-order correction to geodesic motion. The dynamical quantities in this system are the energy centroid, the linear and angular momentum, and the quadrupole moment. Furthermore, the system is closed to first order in the inverse frequency. As an immediate consequence, the energy centroids of Gaussian wave packets with opposite circular polarisations generally propagate in different directions, thereby providing a mathematical proof of the spin Hall effect of light in an inhomogeneous medium.

### [201] [Slow dispersion in Floquet-Dirac Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28715)
*Anthony Bloch,Amir Sagiv,Stefan Steinerberger*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究非自治哈密顿系统（non-autonomous Hamiltonian systems）的色散衰减（dispersive decay）行为，针对一维狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）在时间周期外力作用下，构造了衰减速率不高于t^{-1/10}的系统，并推测任意慢衰减t^{-ε}（ε>0）应可实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非自治系统的色散衰减理论尚不完善，先前研究显示存在时间周期外力作用下的一维狄拉克方程具有异常缓慢的t^{-1/5}衰减速率。预期此类行为非普遍现象，需要特定外力项才能实现。

Method: 提出更一般的构造方法（general ansatz）和系统化程序（systematic procedure），用于构建色散衰减速率不高于t^{-1/10}的方程。限制主要来自代数约束（algebraic limitations）。

Result: 成功构造了衰减速率不高于t^{-1/10}的非自治哈密顿系统，超越了先前t^{-1/5}的结果。代数约束是主要限制因素，但理论上任意慢衰减t^{-ε}（ε>0）应可实现。

Conclusion: 非自治哈密顿系统可实现比先前预期更慢的色散衰减速率，当前限制仅为代数约束，理论上应能实现任意缓慢的衰减行为。

Abstract: We study dispersive decay for non-autonomous Hamiltonian systems. While the general theory for dispersion in such non-autonomous systems is largely open, it was shown \cite{kraisler2025time} that there exists a time-periodically forced one-dimensional Dirac equation with unusually slow dispersive decay rate of $t^{-1/5}$. It is to be expected that such behavior is not generic and requires a very particular forcing term; we provide a more general ansatz and systematic procedure to construct such an equation with a dispersive decay rate no faster than $t^{-1/10}$. Our limitations are purely algebraic and it stands to reason that arbitrarily slow decay, $t^{-\varepsilon}$ for every $\varepsilon > 0$, should be achievable.

### [202] [Data-driven discovery and control of multistable nonlinear systems and hysteresis via structured Neural ODEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27024)
*Ike Griss Salas,Ethan King*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 提出一种最小化结构的神经常微分方程（Neural ODE）架构，通过强制轨迹稳定性为多稳态系统提供可处理的参数化，在短时间训练中高效且能捕捉多个吸引域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多工程物理过程表现出非线性但渐近稳定的动力学，收敛到由控制输入确定的有限平衡点集。从数据中识别此类系统具有挑战性：稳定动力学提供有限激励，模型发现通常非唯一。

Method: 提出最小化结构的神经常微分方程（Neural ODE）架构，通过向量场形式 $F(x,u) = f(x)\,(x - g(x,u))$ 强制轨迹稳定性，其中 $f(x) < 0$ 元素确保收缩性，$g(x,u)$ 确定多吸引子位置。

Result: 在多个非线性基准测试中，所提结构在短时间训练中高效，能捕捉多个吸引域（basins of attraction），并通过隐式平衡映射 $g$ 实现高效的基于梯度的反馈控制。

Conclusion: 该最小化结构的神经常微分方程架构为多稳态系统的数据驱动识别提供了有效的参数化方法，同时确保了动力学稳定性并支持控制应用。

Abstract: Many engineered physical processes exhibit nonlinear but asymptotically stable dynamics that converge to a finite set of equilibria determined by control inputs. Identifying such systems from data is challenging: stable dynamics provide limited excitation and model discovery is often non-unique. We propose a minimally structured Neural Ordinary Differential Equation (NODE) architecture that enforces trajectory stability and provides a tractable parameterization for multistable systems, by learning a vector field in the form $F(x,u) = f(x)\,(x - g(x,u))$, where $f(x) < 0$ elementwise ensures contraction and $g(x,u)$ determines the multi-attractor locations. Across several nonlinear benchmarks, the proposed structure is efficient on short time horizon training, captures multiple basins of attraction, and enables efficient gradient-based feedback control through the implicit equilibrium map $g$.

</details>


### [203] [Structure-Preserving Learning of Nonholonomic Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27580)
*Thomas Beckers,Anthony Bloch,Leonardo Colombo*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种保持结构的高斯过程（GP）框架，用于学习非完整（nonholonomic）系统动力学，通过引入非完整矩阵值核函数确保学习到的向量场在所有输入下都满足非完整约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据驱动建模在机器人学和控制领域日益重要，但标准学习方法通常忽略非完整系统的几何结构。这导致学习到的动力学可能违反非完整约束，产生物理不一致的运动。

Method: 提出了一种结构保持的高斯过程（structure-preserving Gaussian process）框架，核心是引入非完整矩阵值核函数（nonholonomic matrix-valued kernel），将约束分布直接整合到GP先验中。

Result: 证明了所提核函数是半正定的，描述了其相关再生核希尔伯特空间（reproducing kernel Hilbert space）作为容许向量场空间的特征，并证明了所得估计器具有适应约束分布的坐标表示。同时建立了学习模型的一致性。

Conclusion: 在垂直滚动圆盘上的数值仿真验证了所提方法的有效性，表明该框架能够确保学习到的向量场在所有输入下都满足非完整约束。

Abstract: Data-driven modeling is playing an increasing role in robotics and control, yet standard learning methods typically ignore the geometric structure of nonholonomic systems. As a consequence, the learned dynamics may violate the nonholonomic constraints and produce physically inconsistent motions. In this paper, we introduce a structure-preserving Gaussian process (GP) framework for learning nonholonomic dynamics. Our main ingredient is a nonholonomic matrix-valued kernel that incorporates the constraint distribution directly into the GP prior. This construction ensures that the learned vector field satisfies the nonholonomic constraints for all inputs. We show that the proposed kernel is positive semidefinite, characterize its associated reproducing kernel Hilbert space as a space of admissible vector fields, and prove that the resulting estimator admits a coordinate representation adapted to the constraint distribution. We also establish the consistency of the learned model. Numerical simulations on a vertical rolling disk illustrate the effectiveness of the proposed approach.

</details>

Result: 对于新张量结构的费曼积分（Feynman integrals）是红外有限的，研究提供了相关代码作为实现自动化计算的重要步骤。

Abstract: We calculate field theory loop amplitudes by string methods, applied to half-maximal 4-point one-loop graviton amplitudes. Infrared divergences are regulated similarly to soft-collinear effective field theory (SCET): new mass scales are introduced, here by higher-point kinematics. We use an analytically continued single-valued polylogarithm as generating function. The Feynman integrals for the new tensor structures are infrared finite. We provide code as a step towards automation.

### [205] [High energy scattering and null strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26910)
*Arjun Bagchi,Sachin Grover,Sharang Rajesh Iyer,Amartya Saha*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于世界面（worldsheet）对称性的弦散射超高能区内在描述，展示了张力为零的零弦（null string）在诱导真空（induced vacuum）上的散射振幅与通常弦振幅的高能极限一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在构建弦散射超高能区的内在世界面描述。当弦处于极高能量时，基本弦变得无张力（tensionless），在平坦目标时空中，世界面变为零曲面（null surface），从而出现张力为零的零弦。

Method: 方法基于世界面对称性从两个Virasoro代数副本转变为二维共形Carroll代数（或等价的三维BMS代数）。通过仔细遵循张力极限（tensionless limit），构建了零弦在诱导真空上的散射振幅，特别是积分顶点算符（integrated vertex operators）。

Result: 结果显示，从零弦世界面方法构建的散射振幅与通常弦振幅的高能极限一致。零弦模糊了开弦（open string）和闭弦（closed string）的区别，这在振幅层面也有所体现。四点振幅恢复了所有预期区域，包括Gross-Mende区和Regge极限。

Conclusion: 零弦在诱导真空上的散射振幅成功描述了弦散射的高能行为。研究还发现了一类仅在零张力弦中自然出现的顶点算符，这些算符在壳时重现了早期分析，并暗示了超出微扰张性弦的特征。

Abstract: We propose an instrinsic worldsheet description of the ultra-high energy regime of string scattering based on worldsheet symmetries. At very high energies, the fundamental string becomes tensionless and in flat target spacetimes, the worldsheet becomes a null surface. Tensionless null strings thus emerge and the worldsheet symmetries morph from two copies of the Virasoro algebra to the two dimensional (2d) conformal Carroll or equivalently the 3d Bondi-van der Burgh-Metzner-Sachs (BMS) algebra. Tensionless strings have three inequivalent vacua over which they can be constructed, leading to distinct quantum theories. High energy tensile strings naturally connect to null strings built on the so-called induced vacuum.
  Our principle goal in this paper is the construction of scattering amplitudes for null strings in the induced vacuum. We show that these amplitudes, constructed from worldsheet methods of the null string, coincide with the high energy limit of usual string amplitudes. A crucial part of our analysis is the construction of integrated vertex operators. This achieved by relying on lessons from the parent string theory and following the tensionless limit carefully. A striking feature of the null string is the blurring of differences between open and closed strings. We see this at the level of the amplitudes as well. We then focus on four-point amplitudes and recover all expected regimes including the Gross-Mende regime and the Regge limit. We finally comment on a new class of vertex operators which arise naturally only in the zero tension string. This reproduces all our earlier analyses when put onshell but also has hints of signatures beyond the perturbative tensile string.

</details>

Result: 研究发现该模型的微分方程本质上与描述圆形膜（如鼓膜）振动的方程相同，这为研究此类物体的动力学提供了额外的物理联系。

Abstract: The powerful techniques of holographic quantum chromodynamics (QCD) can be employed in the investigation of glueballs -- composite particles made solely of gluons, the strong nuclear force mediators. In particular, the so-called hardwall model yields predictions for the values of the masses of various glueball states, which are related to the solutions of the differential equations of the model. It turns out that those equations are essentially the same as the ones governing the vibrations of a circular membrane like that of a drumhead, which may serve as extra motivation for studying the dynamics of such an object as an undergraduate physics student.

### [207] [The Lee-Yang model and its generalizations through the lens of long-range deformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27031)
*Fanny Eustachon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过微扰方法测试了二维非幺正共形极小模型 $\mathcal{M}(2,2m+1)$ 作为具有复相互作用 $i\varphi^{2m-1}$ 的标量场理论重整化群固定点的猜想。研究发现对于 $m>2$ 的情况，基于极小模型及其Landau-Ginzburg形式论的两种长程构造之间存在不一致性，而 $m=2$ 的长程Lee-Yang模型则与长程Ising模型类似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在测试一个近期猜想：二维非幺正共形极小模型 $\mathcal{M}(2,2m+1)$ 可能作为具有复相互作用 $i\varphi^{2m-1}$ 的标量场理论的重整化群（renormalization group）固定点。这一猜想涉及非幺正（non-unitary）共形场论与特定标量场理论之间的对应关系。

Method: 采用微扰方法（perturbative study）研究两种独立的长程构造（long-range constructions）：一种基于极小模型本身，另一种基于其潜在的Landau-Ginzburg形式论。通过比较这两种构造的对应关系来测试原始猜想。

Result: 对于 $m>2$ 的情况，当试图将基于极小模型和基于Landau-Ginzburg形式论的两种构造联系起来时，发现了不一致性（inconsistencies）。然而，对于 $m=2$ 的特殊情况（即长程Lee-Yang模型），研究显示其与长程Ising模型类似。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，对于 $m>2$ 的情况，原始猜想可能存在局限性，因为两种构造方法无法一致地联系起来。而 $m=2$ 的长程Lee-Yang模型则表现出与已知长程Ising模型相似的性质，支持了该特殊情况下的对应关系。

Abstract: In two dimensions, the non-unitary class of conformal minimal models, $\mathcal{M}(2,2m+1)$, has been recently conjectured to arise as renormalization-group fixed points of scalar field theories with complex $i\varphi^{2m-1}$ interaction, $m\in \mathbb{N}$, $m\ge2$. We test a variation of this conjecture through the perturbative study of two separate long-range constructions based on respectively the minimal model and its potential Landau-Ginzburg formalism. For $m>2$, inconsistencies are found when subsequently relating both constructions. In contrast, the long-range Lee-Yang model, the $m=2$ case, is shown to be analogue to the long-range Ising model.

### [208] [Universality in Relativistic Spinning Particle Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27353)
*Joon-Hwi Kim,Sangmin Lee*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文建立了四维时空中与电磁或引力耦合的大质量自旋粒子模型之间的等价关系，在自旋大小保持的范畴内，证明了四种代表性模型描述相同的物理，并推导了BMT和QMPD方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立不同大质量自旋粒子模型之间的统一框架，特别是在与电磁或引力相互作用时，揭示它们之间的物理等价性，为处理高自旋多极相互作用提供理论基础。

Method: 采用模型无关的方法，在自旋大小保持的范畴内，分析四种代表性模型：矢量振荡器（vector oscillator）、旋量振荡器（spinor oscillator）、球面陀螺（spherical top）和大质量扭量（massive twistor），并推导Bargmann-Michel-Telegdi（BMT）和四极矩Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon（QMPD）方程。

Result: 证明了四种模型在自由和相互作用理论中描述完全相同的物理，建立了相互作用球面陀螺模型的严格构造，特别强调自旋规范不变性，并提供了处理高自旋多极相互作用的通用框架。

Conclusion: 该统一框架不仅建立了不同自旋粒子模型的等价性，还为黑洞物理、守恒荷以及后牛顿或后闵可夫斯基框架的应用提供了理论基础，能够纳入更高自旋多极相互作用。

Abstract: We establish an equivalence between massive spinning particle models in four spacetime dimensions coupled to electromagnetism or gravity, within the spin-magnitude-preserving sector. Four representative models in the literature are shown to describe exactly the same physics in their free and interacting theories: vector oscillator, spinor oscillator, spherical top, and massive twistor. The Bargmann-Michel-Telegdi (BMT) and quadrupolar Mathisson-Papapetrou-Dixon (QMPD) equations are derived in a model-independent fashion. This universal framework allows for incorporating higher spin multipole interactions as well. We establish the rigorous construction of the interacting theory of the spherical top model with emphasis on spin gauge invariance. Applications to black hole physics, conserved charges, and post-Newtonian or post-Minkowskian frameworks are discussed.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将理论置于S^3球面上，分析三维球面曲率对动力学不稳定性和热力学不稳定性起始点的不同影响。通过改变曲率参数，研究等离子体在不同几何条件下的稳定性行为。

Abstract: Homogeneous and isotropic equilibrium states of strongly coupled ${\cal N}=4$ supersymmetric Yang-Mills charged plasma in ${\mathbb R}^3$ with equal chemical potentials for the maximal Abelian subgroup of the $R$-symmetry group become dynamically unstable below some critical temperature. The instabilities arise in the $R$-symmetry charge transport, precisely when the equilibrium state becomes thermodynamically unstable. We study the fate these correlated instabilities when the theory is place on $S^3$. The curvature of the three-sphere affects the onset of the dynamical and the thermodynamic instabilities differently: increasing the curvature at low temperatures can stabilize its transport, but leave the plasma thermodynamically unstable. ### [212] [Emergent strings, holography, and cosmology from four-fermion interactions: a bottom-up derivation of AdS/CFT, dS/CFT, and $w_{1+\infty}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27824)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Bargmann-Wigner方案，分析(1+1)维Gross-Neveu模型中手征凝聚Δ₀=⟨ψ̄ψ⟩与自旋-1配对Δ₁=⟨Φ̄₁Φ₁⟩的竞争关系。该竞争定义了涌现的径向坐标z=m⁻¹(Δ₁/Δ₀²-1)^{1/2}，其局域涨落通过共动导数追踪，在大N物种色散增强下生成AdS₃线元。

Conclusion: 凝聚竞争机制本身就是额外维度，为全息对偶提供了第一性原理推导。该框架可推广至(2+1)维NJL模型得到AdS₄/CFT₃和dS₄/CFT₃实现，并结构识别w_{1+∞} celestial代数；推广至(3+1)维NJL模型得到AdS₅/CFT₄和全息QCD，正确捕获QCD红外物理，包括手征对称性破缺和线性Regge轨迹M_s²=4(s+1)Λ_QCD²。

Using a Bargmann-Wigner scheme, the competition between chiral condensation $Δ_0=\langle\barψψ\rangle$ and spin-1 pairing $Δ_1=\langle\barΦ_1Φ_1\rangle$ defines an emergent radial coordinate $z=m^{-1}(Δ_1/Δ_0^2-1)^{1/2}$; local fluctuations of this ratio, tracked by a comoving derivative, generate the AdS$_3$ line element via the enhanced large-$N$ species dispersion; the condensate competition \emph{is} the extra dimension. From this single mechanism the complete AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$ correspondence emerges: Newton's constant, the Virasoro algebra ($c=2N^2$), D1-branes with open strings, open/closed T-duality, the Hagedorn/BKT transition, and the BTZ black hole whose horizon circumference is quantised in Planck units by individual vortex nucleation events. Analytic continuation $z\to iζ$ across the chiral critical point realises the Strominger dS/CFT conjecture microscopically. Six constraints identify the emergent string as Type IIB on AdS$_3\times S^3\times\mathcal{M}_4$, with emergent worldsheet $\mathcal{N}=(1,1)$ supersymmetry, NS/R spectral flow, and GSO projection. Extension to the $(2+1)$d NJL model yields AdS$_4$/CFT$_3$, a dS$_4$/CFT$_3$ realisation, and a structural identification of the $w_{1+\infty}$ celestial algebra. Abstract: We study modular properties of conformal field theories perturbed by holomorphic fields. The derivation makes use of general properties of torus correlation functions, in particular the Zhu recursion relation. ### [215] [A Twisted Origin for Magnetic Carroll Supersymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28269)

Method: 作者证明相关磁卡罗尔代数并非来自标准相对论超对称代数的简单收缩（naive contraction），而是源于扭曲的相对论父代数。作为具体实现，构建了三维N=2磁卡罗尔代数及其超对称矢量多重态（supersymmetric vector-multiplet）作用量。

Abstract: Magnetic Carrollian theories provide a natural setting for field theories with nontrivial spatial structure in the Carroll limit and are therefore natural candidates for flat-space holographic duals. Embedding such boundary theories into a top-down framework requires a consistent supersymmetric completion and, in particular, an understanding of the relativistic origin of magnetic Carroll supersymmetry. We show that the relevant magnetic Carroll algebra does not arise from a naive contraction of the standard relativistic supersymmetry algebra, but instead descends from a twisted relativistic parent. As an explicit realization, we construct a three-dimensional ${\mathcal{N}}=2$ magnetic Carroll algebra together with a supersymmetric vector-multiplet action. Unlike the electric case, the resulting structure contains one supercharge that squares to spatial momentum, a mixed anticommutator that yields the Hamiltonian, and a nilpotent second supercharge. This provides a physical and relativistic origin for a super-BMS$_4$ structure recently identified by complementary algebraic methods, and strengthens the case for magnetic Carroll theories in flat-space holography and supersymmetric asymptotic symmetries.

### [217] [Physics as Code: From Scans to Theorems with ITP APIs in $SU(5)$ Model Building](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28406)
*Sven Krippendorf,Joseph Tooby-Smith*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于交互式定理证明器（ITP）的形式化方法，用于解决理论物理中有界但组合庞大的模型空间问题。通过将电荷谱、谓词和约化操作形式化为可重用的定义，从已证明的约化定理推导分类，而非依赖临时扫描。在SU(5)案例研究中展示了该方法，实现了对满足特定约束的有界电荷谱的正式验证分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理论物理中常面临对有界但组合庞大的模型空间进行可靠全局陈述的挑战。穷举扫描变得不透明或不切实际，而统计探索本身无法提供定理支持的保证。这促使需要将模型构建问题本身形式化到交互式定理证明器（interactive theorem prover, ITP）中的工作流程。

Method: 开发了一种基于API的方法论，在Lean交互式定理证明器中形式化有界模型构建问题。核心步骤是将相关电荷谱（charge spectra）、谓词（predicates）和约化操作（reduction moves）表示为可重用的ITP定义，然后从已证明的约化定理而非临时扫描推导分类。在PhysLib中实现为可重用基础设施而非一次性验证脚本。

Result: 在电荷谱层面，分类了满足顶夸克汤川耦合（top-quark Yukawa coupling）、避免选定危险算符集并满足最小电荷谱完备性条件的有界谱。主要结果表明，有界搜索空间中的每个此类谱都源于有限数量的最小顶-汤川见证（minimal top-Yukawa witnesses）以及受控完备化和认证闭包步骤。该分类提供了所研究电荷谱设置中完整可行类的正式验证描述。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了交互式定理证明器如何将组合困难的模型构建问题转化为以正确性为先的可重用工作流程。生成的认证分类可作为下游分析的可靠输入，为理论物理模型构建提供了形式化验证的新范式。

Abstract: A recurring challenge in theoretical physics is to make reliable global statements about bounded but combinatorially large model spaces. Exhaustive scans quickly become opaque or impractical, while statistical exploration does not by itself provide theorem-backed guarantees. This motivates workflows in which the model-building problem itself is formalized inside an interactive theorem prover (ITP).
  In this paper we develop an API-based methodology for formalizing such bounded model-building questions inside Lean, an interactive theorem prover. The central step is to represent the relevant charge spectra, predicates, and reduction moves as reusable ITP definitions, and then to derive the classification from proved reduction theorems rather than from an ad hoc scan. We demonstrate the strategy in a concrete $SU(5)$ case study motivated by F-theory model building with additional Abelian symmetries.
  At the charge-spectrum layer, we classify bounded spectra that admit a top-quark Yukawa coupling, avoid a selected set of dangerous operators, and satisfy a minimal charge-spectrum completeness condition. Our main result shows that every such spectrum in the bounded search space arises from finitely many minimal top-Yukawa witnesses together with controlled completions and certified closure steps. This classification represents a formally verified description of the full viable class in the charge-spectrum setting studied here.
  The development is implemented inside PhysLib as reusable infrastructure rather than as a one-off verification script. It provides a proof of principle for how interactive theorem provers can turn combinatorially difficult model-building problems into correctness-first, reusable workflows, and we discuss how the resulting certified classification can serve as reliable input for downstream analyses.

</details>


### [218] [Lecture Notes on Positivity Properties of Scattering Amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28454)
*Prashanth Raman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文综述了完全单调（CM）函数和Stieltjes函数在量子场论中的物理意义与应用，探讨了这些数学性质如何从散射振幅幺正性、解析性等物理原理中产生，并展示了其在S-矩阵约束、数值自举方法和正几何中的重要作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在探讨完全单调（completely monotone, CM）函数和Stieltjes函数这两类满足无限层级正性约束的数学概念在量子场论（quantum field theory, QFT）中的物理意义。这些经典分析概念最近被发现出现在量子场论的基本构建块和可观测量中，包括欧几里得区域的标量费曼积分和$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM中的库仑分支振幅。

Method: 论文采用综述性方法，首先回顾完全单调函数和Stieltjes函数的数学结构，然后系统探讨这些性质的物理和几何起源。分析范围涵盖散射振幅的幺正性（unitarity）和解析性（analyticity）、费曼积分的参数表示结构等多个方面。

Result: 研究揭示了这些函数性质与量子场论基本物理原理之间的深刻联系，包括它们如何从散射振幅的幺正性和解析性中产生。论文还展示了这些数学性质在多个领域的应用，包括对解析S-矩阵的约束、数值自举方法（numerical bootstrap methods）的影响，以及与正几何（positive geometry）的联系。

Conclusion: 完全单调函数和Stieltjes函数在量子场论中具有重要的物理意义，其正性约束与量子场论的基本原理密切相关。这些函数性质与正几何之间存在紧密联系，为理解量子场论的结构提供了新的几何视角，特别是在散射振幅和宇宙学关联子的研究中具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: We review completely monotone (CM) and Stieltjes functions, which are classes of functions obeying an infinite hierarchy of positivity constraints. While these are classical concepts in analysis, such properties have recently been shown to arise in many fundamental building blocks and observables of quantum field theory (QFT), including scalar Feynman integrals in the Euclidean region and Coulomb branch amplitudes in $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM.
  After reviewing their mathematical structure, we discuss the physical and geometric origins of these properties, ranging from unitarity and analyticity in scattering amplitudes to the structure of parametric representations of Feynman integrals. We then survey a number of applications, including constraints on the analytic S-matrix, implications for numerical bootstrap methods, and connections to positive geometry, where we present evidence for a close relation between these functions and geometric volume interpretations.
  These notes are based on an extended series of lectures delivered at the \emph{Positive Geometry in Scattering Amplitudes and Cosmological Correlators} workshop, held at the International Centre for Theoretical Sciences (ICTS), Bengaluru, in February 2025.

### [220] [Which Functions Admit a Positive Geometry? From Branch Cuts to String Amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28543)
*Hyungrok Kim,Jonah Stalknecht*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文将正几何（positive geometry）框架推广到无限线段并集，使典范形式（canonical form）能包含分支割线（branch cuts），并引入伪亏格（pseudogenus）概念分类亚纯函数（meromorphic functions）。研究还展示了开弦和闭弦振幅的d对数（d log）形式具有正几何结构，为四点KLT双拷贝（KLT double copy）提供了完全几何解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 正几何框架通常将物理可观测量编码为运动学空间区域的典范形式，但现有方法主要局限于有理函数。本研究旨在推广该框架以处理更广泛的函数类型，包括具有分支割线的函数，从而扩展正几何在物理振幅描述中的应用范围。

Method: 通过考虑无限线段并集（infinite union of line segments）的推广，研究在正几何的连续极限（continuum limit）中描述具有分支割线的正几何。引入伪亏格概念对亚纯函数进行分类，并约束一维正几何可能产生的函数类型。

Result: 研究表明典范形式可以写为伪亏格为零函数的d对数形式。线段并集编码的谱（spectrum）与弦态塔（stringy tower of states）或具有三个以上紧致方向的Kaluza-Klein塔一致，但前提是几乎所有此类态对散射振幅没有贡献。开弦和闭弦振幅的d对数形式均具有正几何结构。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将正几何框架推广到超越有理函数的范畴，为KLT双拷贝在四点的情形提供了完整的几何解释。伪亏格概念的引入为亚纯函数的分类提供了新工具，扩展了正几何在描述物理振幅方面的应用潜力。

Abstract: Positive geometry provides a geometric framework where physical observables are encoded as canonical forms associated to regions of kinematic space. In this paper we consider a generalisation to an infinite union of line segments, which allows us to capture canonical forms beyond rational functions. In the continuum limit of positive geometries, we show that we can generalise even further and describe positive geometries whose canonical forms contain branch cuts. We will constrain which functions can be obtained as the canonical form of one-dimensional positive geometries. We introduce the notion of the pseudogenus to classify meromorphic functions, and show that canonical forms can be written as the $\mathrm d\log$ of a function with pseudogenus zero. Furthermore, we argue that the spectrum encoded by a union of line segments is consistent with the presence of a stringy tower of states or a Kaluza-Klein tower with three or more compact directions only if nearly all such states do not contribute to the scattering amplitude. In addition, we show how the d log of both open and closed string amplitudes admits a positive geometry. This allows us to give a fully geometric interpretation for the KLT double copy at four points.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解体驱动Floquet共形场论中对称性分辨纠缠熵的演化规律，特别是对称性分辨Rényi熵在不同电荷扇区中如何趋近或偏离均分（equipartition）。

Method: 方法聚焦于二维自由紧致玻色子CFT，分析Virasoro代数中$\mathfrak{sl}^{(k)}(2,\mathbb{R})$子代数的存在如何引入自由参数$k$，从而控制均分的破坏。基于Virasoro代数的一般振子表示，预期该机制可推广至自由玻色子CFT之外。

Result: 结果显示，$\mathfrak{sl}^{(k)}(2,\mathbb{R})$子代数的存在引入了标签$k$作为自由参数，能够控制电荷扇区间的均分破坏。该效应源于低频与高频模式间的显式耦合，且该机制预期在自由玻色子CFT之外仍持续存在。

Conclusion: 结论表明，通过Virasoro代数的子代数结构可以控制对称性分辨熵的均分行为，且该机制具有普适性。最后讨论了非幺正演化下边界态精细对称性分辨熵的实时动力学如何被修改，这可能与后选择弱测量相关联。

Abstract: We study the evolution of symmetry-resolved entanglement entropy in bulk-driven Floquet conformal field theories (CFTs). Focusing on the two-dimensional free compact boson CFT, we analyze how symmetry-resolved Rényi entropies approach or depart from equipartition among charge sectors. We show that the existence of an $\mathfrak{sl}^{(k)}(2,\mathbb{R})$ subalgebra of the Virasoro algebra introduces a free parameter, the label $k$, which allows us to control the breakdown of equipartition. We argue that this effect originates from an explicit coupling between low- and high-frequency modes. Based on a general oscillator representation of the Virasoro algebra, we expect this mechanism to persist beyond the free boson CFT. Finally, we discuss how the real-time dynamics of fine-grained symmetry-resolved entropies of a boundary state are modified under non-unitary evolution, which can be associated with post-selected weak measurements.

*Patrick Copinger,James P. Edwards,Karthik Rajeev*

TL;DR: 本文研究了非零背景电磁场中任意数量光子的散射振幅，使用世界线形式体系构建了主公式，克服了先前恒定背景场研究的限制，并放宽了平面波的零条件假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究更符合物理现实的激光-等离子体色散特性，克服先前在恒定背景场中研究此类振幅的局限性，并放宽平面波研究中常见的零条件假设。

Method: 采用第一量子化世界线形式体系（first-quantised worldline formalism），构建了非零背景场中N光子振幅的主公式。该方法系统地考虑了非零参数$\mathfrak{n}^2$的所有阶次，并将其作为展开参数处理。

Result: 推导了坐标和动量空间传播子（及其LSZ截断振幅）和有效作用量的世界线表示，每个都非微扰地包含了非零背景场。进一步概述了$\mathfrak{n}^{2}$展开的部分重求和，并通过无光子插入的有效作用量中非零恒定交叉场的精确可解特例验证了主公式。

Motivated to account for more physically realistic laser-plasma dispersive properties, our approach overcomes prior work studying such amplitudes in a constant background field and relaxes the familiar null criterion assumed for plane waves.
  Master Formulae for the $N$-photon amplitudes dressed by the non-null background are constructed using the first-quantised worldline formalism, which can systematically account for all orders in the non-null parameter, $\mathfrak{n}^2$, treated here as an expansion parameter. These are derived from worldline representations of the coordinate and momentum space propagators (and their LSZ-truncated amplitudes) and the effective action, each incorporating the non-null background non-perturbatively. We then outline a partial resummation of their expansions in $\mathfrak{n}^{2}$. A special exactly solvable case of non-null constant crossed fields without photon insertion in the effective action is explored to test the Master Formulae that result. The validity of the presented master formulae is further checked against known expressions for the wavefunction and non-linear Compton scattering in a non-null background to lowest order in the non-null parameter.

Abstract: Tight matching with the environment is key to effective robot operation in complex settings. We propose instead using materials available in the environment to functionalize in situ spun webs, reducing payload and uniquely matching the structure to its surroundings. As a demonstration, we transform an optically scattering PVDF fiber web into an optically absorbing, polypyrrole-grafted structure via pyrrole vapour exposure. Two activator-delivery strategies are shown: liquid infusion into a prefabricated web, and activator pre-embedding in the spinning mixture.   <summary>Details</summary>

Here, we introduce a small-scale compact, foldable, and robust soft electromagnetic robot (M-SEMR) with more than nine locomotion modes designed for such a scenario. Featuring a six-spoke elastomer body embedded with liquid metal channels and driven by Laplace forces under a static magnetic field, the M-SEMR is capable of rapid transitions (< 0.35 s) among different locomotion modes. It achieves exceptional agility, including high-speed rolling (818 mm/s, 26 BL/s), omnidirectional crawling, jumping, and swimming. Notably, the robot can fold to reduce its volume by 79%, enabling it to traverse confined spaces. We further validate its navigation capabilities on complex terrains, including discrete obstacles, viscoelastic gelatin surfaces, viscous fluids, and simulated biological tissues. This system offers a versatile strategy for developing high-mobility soft robots for future biomedical applications.

TL;DR: 本研究系统探究了非功能化聚(N-异丙基丙烯酰胺)(pNIPAM)微凝胶的网络拓扑结构（特别是交联剂浓度与分布）如何调控其在盐溶液中的离子敏感性。通过分析八种不同微凝胶架构（从超低交联到核-壳及均质交联变体）在0至100 mM NaCl离子强度下的行为，揭示了网络拓扑与离子强度对微凝胶热响应特性的多维影响。

Method: 研究系统分析了八种不同的微凝胶架构，涵盖从超低交联(ULC)到核-壳(core-corona)及均质交联(HC)变体。通过22个批次的动态光散射实验，分析了关键热响应特性，包括体积相变温度(VPTT)偏移、盐耐受阈值、滞后指数和絮凝动力学（仅在极端盐度1000 mM NaCl和25°C条件下）。

Result: 研究实现了对离子强度、交联剂(MBA)存在与否、空间交联分布以及热力学状态如何在不同温度下决定微凝胶行为的多维分析。实验数据揭示了网络拓扑结构对微凝胶盐敏感性的显著影响。

Conclusion: 最后，研究评估了该实验库对现有理论框架（特别是Flory-Rehner和Flory-Rehner-Donnan模型）的适用性，解决了关于这些模型在描述复杂微凝胶系统中有效性的持续争论。这项工作为理解网络拓扑如何调控微凝胶离子敏感性提供了系统性见解。

Abstract: The utility of non functionalized poly(N-isopropylacrylamide) (pNIPAM) microgels in physiological and environmental applications is strictly dependent on their reversible thermoresponsiveness and stability in saline media. Despite their importance, a unified understanding of how network topology specifically crosslinker concentration and distribution regulates ionic sensitivity remains fragmented in the literature. This work systematically investigates the interplay between network topology and ionic strength (0 to 100 mM NaCl) across eight distinct microgel architectures, ranging from ultra-low crosslinked (ULC) to core-corona and homogeneously crosslinked (HC) variants. Utilizing dynamic light scattering across 22 batches, we analyzed critical thermoresponsive properties, including volume phase transition temperature (VPTT) shifts, salt tolerance thresholds, hysteresis indices, and flocculation kinetics (only at extreme salinity, 1000 mM NaCl and at 25 deg C). This comprehensive investigation enables a multidimensional analysis of how ionic strength, the presence or absence of crosslinkers (MBA), spatial crosslinking distribution, and thermodynamic states dictate microgel behavior across varying temperatures. Finally, we evaluate the applicability of this experimental library to established theoretical frameworks, specifically the Flory Rehner and Flory Rehner Donnan models, addressing ongoing debates regarding their validity in describing complex microgel systems.

### [227] [Interpretable liquid crystal phase classification via two-by-two ordinal patterns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26723)

Abstract: Liquid crystal textures encode rich structural information, yet mapping these images to mesophase identity remains challenging because visually similar patterns can arise from distinct structures. Our approach generalizes to unseen compounds and accurately distinguishes between phase identity and material origin. ### [230] [Characterizing exact dynamics of a trapped active Brownian particle under torque in two and three dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26967)
*Anweshika Pattanayak,Amir Shee,Abhishek Chaudhuri,Debasish Chaudhuri*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一个精确解析框架，用于分析手性活性布朗粒子在谐波势阱中的瞬态动力学。研究获得了所有时间依赖矩的闭式表达式，揭示了二维和三维系统中超峰度（excess kurtosis）的不同演化行为，为受限手性活性动力学提供了实验可观测的特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性（chirality）、自推进（self-propulsion）和空间限制（spatial confinement）的相互作用会产生显著的非平衡涨落，其高阶统计量携带了位置分布动态和形状的信息。研究旨在理解这些因素如何共同塑造瞬态动力学。

Method: 基于福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equation）的拉普拉斯变换解，建立了一个精确的解析框架，用于分析二维和三维谐波势阱中手性活性布朗粒子（chiral active Brownian particle）的瞬态动力学。获得了所有时间依赖矩（time-dependent moments）直至四阶的闭式表达式。

Result: 在二维系统中，超峰度呈现阻尼振荡响应（damped oscillatory response），具有多重重入交叉（re-entrant crossovers），从反映活性偏心环状位置分布的负值演变为表征重尾涨落的正值。在三维系统中，超峰度始终保持负值，表明存在稳健的活性非高斯态（active non-Gaussian state），其特征为扭矩轴与其法向径向张成的二维平面上的半环状至带状位置分布。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，手性、推进、限制以及维度共同塑造了瞬态动力学，同时为受限手性活性动力学提供了实验可观测的特征。该解析框架能够完全表征瞬态和稳态区域内的超峰度演化。

Abstract: The interplay of chirality, self-propulsion, and spatial confinement generates striking non-equilibrium fluctuations whose higher-order statistics carry information about the dynamics and shape of the position distribution. Here, we present an exact analytical framework, based on a Laplace-transform solution of the Fokker-Planck equation, for the transient dynamics of a chiral active Brownian particle in a harmonic trap, in both two and three dimensions. We obtain closed-form expressions for all time-dependent moments up to fourth order, enabling a complete characterization of the excess kurtosis throughout the transient and steady-state regimes. In two dimensions, the excess kurtosis exhibits a damped oscillatory response with multiple re-entrant crossovers, evolving from negative values that reflect active off-centered ring-like position distributions to positive values characteristic of heavy-tailed fluctuations. This damped oscillatory excess kurtosis appears both for free and harmonic confinement, although increasing the trapping stiffness progressively suppresses it, and the positive excess kurtosis eventually vanishes at sufficiently high stiffness. In contrast, in three dimensions, the excess kurtosis remains negative, indicating a robustly active non-Gaussian state characterized by half-ring-like to band-like position distributions in the two-dimensional plane spanned by the torque axis and its normal radial direction. Our results demonstrate how chirality, propulsion, and confinement, together with dimensionality, shape transient dynamics, while providing experimentally accessible signatures of confined chiral active dynamics.

### [232] [Penetration of Rigid Rods, Flexible Rods, and Granular Jets into Low-Density Granular Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27262)
*J. E. Benítez-Zamudio,S. Hidalgo-Caballero,F. Pacheco-Vázquez*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 研究比较了刚性杆、柔性杆和颗粒阵列在二维颗粒床中的垂直穿透动力学。与球形侵入体不同，杆状物会因床层不均匀而偏离垂直方向，最终达到水平构型，其动力学受长度、刚度和惯性矩影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注球形侵入体（spherical intruders）在颗粒材料中的穿透行为，但对杆状物（rods）的穿透动力学了解有限。本研究旨在探索刚性杆、柔性杆和非粘性颗粒阵列在二维颗粒床中的垂直穿透行为，比较三者的动力学差异。

Method: 采用实验方法，在由膨胀聚苯乙烯球（expanded polystyrene spheres）组成的二维颗粒床中进行垂直穿透实验。研究对象包括刚性杆（rigid rods）、柔性杆（flexible rods）和垂直排列的非粘性颗粒阵列（vertical arrays of non-cohesive particles），并通过高速摄像记录穿透过程。同时辅以分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）验证颗粒阵列的行为。

Result: 杆状物会因床层堆积分数（packing fraction）不均匀而迅速偏离垂直方向，在阻力矩作用下旋转并沿曲线轨迹运动，最终达到水平构型。短杆因惯性矩（moment of inertia）较小而偏离更快；长柔性杆会发生屈曲（buckling），而相同尺寸的刚性杆在偏离前穿透更深。颗粒阵列同样会失去垂直性并最终呈水平构型，其穿透深度远小于等效质量的杆，停止机制基于构成颗粒碰撞过程中的垂直-水平动量转移（vertical-to-horizontal momentum transfer）。

Conclusion: 杆状物在颗粒床中的穿透动力学与球形侵入体显著不同，其偏离垂直方向的行为受床层不均匀性、杆的几何尺寸、刚度和惯性矩共同影响。颗粒阵列的穿透行为进一步揭示了动量转移在停止机制中的关键作用。

Abstract: The penetration of projectiles into granular materials has been mainly studied using spherical intruders. Here we explore the dynamics of rods penetrating vertically in a two-dimensional granular bed composed of expanded polystyrene spheres. The experiments were performed using rigid rods, flexible rods and vertical arrays of non-cohesive particles, and the dynamics for the three cases was compared. In contrast to the vertical penetration observed for a single spherical projectile, high speed videos reveal that a rod rapidly deviates from its initial vertical direction due to inhomogeneities of the bed packing fraction. Then, the rod rotates due to the torque induced by the resistance force and follows a curved trajectory until be aligned horizontally at a final depth. A short rod tends to deviate faster than a longer rod due to the smaller moment of inertia. Moreover, long flexible rods always lose their vertical alignment and experience buckling, whereas rigid rods of the same size penetrate deeper before being deviated. On the other hand, experiments and molecular dynamics simulations show that a initially vertical array of grains also loses its verticality and stops adopting a final horizontal configuration. The granular array penetrates considerably less than the rods of equivalent mass, and the stopping mechanism is based on vertical-to-horizontal momentum transfer during a collisional process of the constituting particles.

### [233] [Bonded-particle model for magneto-elastic rods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27279)
*Gabriel Alkuino,Joel T. Clemmer,Christian D. Santangelo,Teng Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种磁弹性杆的键合粒子模型（bonded-particle model），该模型在单一离散元框架内统一了大变形、接触和长程磁相互作用。模型通过LAMMPS实现，并验证了其在扭转失稳、磁化梁偏转和磁滞等基准问题中的准确性，同时展示了与流体求解器耦合的多物理场能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型难以在统一框架内同时处理磁弹性杆的大变形、接触和长程磁相互作用。本文旨在开发一个集成的离散元模型，以克服这些限制并实现多物理场耦合模拟。

Method: 采用键合粒子模型（bonded-particle model）将杆离散为可定向粒子，通过共旋转键（co-rotational bonds）连接，捕捉拉伸、剪切、弯曲和扭转。在粒子层面引入磁耦合，每个粒子携带随其旋转的偶极矩（dipole moment），实现外场驱动和长程偶极-偶极相互作用（dipole-dipole interactions）。模型在LAMMPS中实现，并可通过浸没边界法（immersed boundary method）与格子玻尔兹曼流体求解器（lattice Boltzmann fluid solver）耦合。

Result: 模型在三个基准问题上得到验证：极端扭转下直杆和曲杆的缠绕失稳（writhing instabilities）、均匀和恒定梯度场中磁化梁的大偏转、以及具有偶极-偶极相互作用的螺旋杆的机械磁滞（mechanical hysteresis）。所有案例均与实验、解析和数值参考结果表现出良好一致性。

Conclusion: 所开发的磁弹性杆键合粒子模型成功统一了大变形、接触和长程磁相互作用，验证了其准确性，并展示了与流体求解器耦合的多物理场能力，为复杂磁弹性系统的模拟提供了有效框架。

Abstract: We develop a bonded-particle model for magneto-elastic rods that unifies large deformations, contact, and long-range magnetic interactions within a single discrete-element framework. The rod is discretized into orientable particles connected by co-rotational bonds that capture stretching, shearing, bending, and twisting through a symmetric decomposition of relative displacement and rotation. Magnetic coupling is introduced at the particle level: each particle carries a dipole moment that rotates with it, enabling both external-field actuation and long-range dipole--dipole interactions without modifying the structural formulation. We implement the model in LAMMPS to take advantage of its parallel efficiency, long-range electrostatic solvers, and multiphysics capabilities. We validate the framework against three benchmark problems: writhing instabilities of straight and curved rods under extreme twisting, large deflections of magnetized beams in uniform and constant-gradient fields, and mechanical hysteresis of helical rods with dipole--dipole interactions. To demonstrate multiphysics capability, we couple the model with a lattice Boltzmann fluid solver via the immersed boundary method and simulate filaments in oscillatory channel flow and fluid pumping by magnetically actuated cilia arrays. Across all examples, the model shows good agreement with experimental, analytical, and numerical reference results.

</details>


### [234] [Surfactant reorientation under shear: dynamic surface tension and droplet deformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27285)
*Alexandra J. Hardy,Abdallah Daddi-Moussa-Ider,Elsen Tjhung*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究采用相场模型（phase-field model）研究剪切流（shear flow）下表面活性剂覆盖液滴的变形行为，揭示了表面活性剂极化（polarization）重定向（reorientation）如何动态改变表面张力（surface tension），从而影响受限几何（confined geometries）中液滴的变形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究剪切流中表面活性剂覆盖液滴的变形机制，特别关注表面活性剂浓度（surfactant concentration）和极化（polarization）如何影响界面性质，以及这些微观变化如何宏观地影响液滴在受限环境中的变形行为。

Method: 采用相场模型（phase-field model），该模型明确考虑了表面活性剂浓度及其极化（代表平均分子取向）。研究分为两部分：首先分析平坦界面（flat interface）在切向剪切（tangential shear）下的行为，然后研究弱受限（weakly confined）和强受限（strongly confined）几何中液滴的变形。

Result: 切向剪切导致表面活性剂极化偏离界面法线，降低其降低界面自由能的能力，从而增加有效表面张力（effective surface tension）。在弱受限区域，数值结果在小毛细数（capillary numbers）下恢复线性泰勒标度（linear Taylor scaling），在大毛细数下与修正的Maffettone-Minale唯象模型（phenomenological model）吻合。表面活性剂通过降低有效表面张力增强变形。在强受限区域，壁面效应（wall effects）进一步增加变形，结果可通过包含Shapira-Haber修正来定性描述。

Conclusion: 表面活性剂在流动下的重定向（reorientation）为剪切依赖性表面张力（shear-dependent surface tension）提供了微观机制，并对受限多相流（confined multiphase flows）中液滴变形具有重要影响。

Abstract: We study the deformation of a surfactant-covered droplet under shear flow using a phase-field model that explicitly accounts for both the surfactant concentration and its polarization, representing the average molecular orientation. We first consider a flat interface and show that an imposed tangential shear causes the surfactant polarization to tilt away from the interface normal. This reorientation reduces the ability of surfactants to lower the interfacial free energy, leading to an increase in the effective surface tension and demonstrating that surface tension can be dynamically modified by shear. We then examine droplet deformation under shear in both weakly and strongly confined geometries. In the weak-confinement regime, numerical results recover the linear Taylor scaling at small capillary numbers, while at larger capillary numbers they are accurately described by a modified Maffettone-Minale phenomenological model. The presence of surfactants enhances deformation through a reduction in the effective surface tension. In the strong-confinement regime, wall effects further increase droplet deformation, with results qualitatively captured by including the Shapira-Haber correction. Overall, our findings show that surfactant reorientation under flow provides a microscopic mechanism for shear-dependent surface tension and has significant implications for droplet deformation in confined multiphase flows.

</details>


### [235] [Shear-induced self-diffusivity in dilute suspensions with repulsive interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27396)
*Anu V S Nath,Pijush Patra,Anubhab Roy*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 在稀薄非布朗悬浮液中进行简单剪切时，弱中心排斥力打破粒子间流体动力相互作用的前后对称性，产生不可逆横向位移，导致剪切诱导自扩散。该扩散率具有梯度分量相对于涡度分量的对数增强结构各向异性，且标度律对多种物理机制具有普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在零雷诺数下，稀薄非布朗悬浮液（dilute non-Brownian suspension）中粒子间的成对流体动力相互作用（pairwise hydrodynamic interactions）具有前后对称性，不产生净跨流线位移。需要研究弱中心排斥力如何打破这种对称性并诱导扩散。

Method: 采用弱排斥极限下的匹配渐近展开法（matched asymptotic expansions），推导剪切诱导自扩散率（shear-induced self-diffusivity）梯度分量和涡度分量的闭合形式标度律。通过全数值轨迹积分验证渐近预测，以静电排斥为代表性案例，采用Gouy-Chapman双电层模型。

Result: 梯度分量相对于涡度分量表现出对数增强（logarithmic enhancement），这种结构各向异性对所有单调衰减的排斥势均持续存在。具体相互作用仅通过力剖面加权流体动力迁移函数的积分泛函体现，表明标度律对电双层排斥、空间位阻相互作用等不同物理机制具有普适性。数值验证显示渐近预测与全数值轨迹积分结果在预期范围内高度一致。

Conclusion: 弱中心排斥力打破稀薄非布朗悬浮液中流体动力相互作用的前后对称性，产生剪切诱导自扩散。推导的标度律揭示了扩散率的结构各向异性，且该标度行为对多种短程中心力机制具有普适性，为理解剪切悬浮液中的输运现象提供了理论框架。

Abstract: In a dilute non-Brownian suspension undergoing simple shear, pairwise hydrodynamic interactions are fore-aft symmetric at zero Reynolds number and produce no net cross-streamline displacement. A weak central repulsive force between particles breaks this symmetry, deflecting trajectories and generating irreversible transverse displacements that cumulatively yield a shear-induced self-diffusivity. We derive, via matched asymptotic expansions in the limit of weak repulsion, closed-form scaling laws for the gradient and vorticity components of this diffusivity. The gradient component exhibits a logarithmic enhancement relative to the vorticity component, a structural anisotropy that persists for all monotonically decaying repulsive potentials. The specific interaction enters only through integral functionals of the force profile weighted by hydrodynamic mobility functions, establishing that the scaling is universal across physically distinct mechanisms, such as electrical double-layer repulsion, steric interactions, or any other short-range central force. We validate the asymptotic predictions against full numerical trajectory integration for the representative case of electrostatic repulsion, modelled using the Gouy-Chapman description of the electrical double layer, and find excellent agreement in the expected regime.

</details>


### [236] [The effects of ionic valency and size asymmetry on counterion adsorption](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27444)
*Or Ben Yaakov,Haim Diamant,Rudolf Podgornik,David Andelman*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多价离子溶液中溶剂与离子尺寸不对称性对带电表面附近平衡性质的影响，旨在理解尺寸不对称性如何改变经典泊松-玻尔兹曼理论描述的浓度分布行为。

Method: 针对单一离子物种推导了带电表面处的广义格雷厄姆方程（generalized Grahame equation），并对一般离子-溶剂尺寸比获得了浓度分布随表面距离变化的解析结果。

Result: 弱表面电荷和小离子-溶剂尺寸比时，浓度分布遵循稀溶液条件下的经典泊松-玻尔兹曼方程；高表面电荷和大离子尺寸时，表面附近浓度分布饱和，溶液性质对表面电荷密度和尺寸不对称性呈现独特依赖关系。

Conclusion: 稀溶液与饱和状态之间的转变取决于表面电荷和离子尺寸不对称性；在饱和状态下，含不同价态和尺寸的多种离子物种的溶液会在表面附近分层，形成按离子价态-尺寸比排序的层状结构。

Abstract: We study the effect of asymmetry in solvent and ionic size on the equilibrium properties of multivalent ionic solutions near a charged surface. For a single ionic species in solution, we derive a generalized Grahame equation at the charged surface. For general size ratio between the ions and the solvent, we obtain analytical results for the concentration profiles as a function of the distance from the surface. For weak surface charge and small ion-to-solvent size ratio, the profile follows the classical Poisson-Boltzmann equation in dilute solution conditions. However, for high surface charge and large ionic size, the concentration profile saturates near the surface, leading to distinctive dependencies of the solution properties on the surface charge density and size asymmetry. Furthermore, the crossover between dilute and saturated regimes depends on the surface charge and ionic size asymmetry. We suggest that a solution containing multiple ionic species of different valencies and sizes stratifies close to the surface in the saturation regime. This leads to the formation of layers that are ordered according to the ions' valency-to-size ratio.

### [237] [Unidirectional flow from continuous broken symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27474)
*Aaron Winn,Justine Parmentier,Eleni Katifori,Martin Brandenbourger*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究将凝聚态物理中的非互易输运（non-reciprocal transport）概念扩展到生物和人工系统中的流体输运，以淋巴系统为例，揭示分布式瓣膜作为连续破缺对称性（continuous broken symmetries）如何通过时空激发（spatiotemporal excitations）实现单向流体输运。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局部破缺对称性（locally broken symmetries）在各领域中被用于定向输运物质、粒子和信息。本研究旨在探索这一概念如何超越凝聚态物理，应用于生物系统和人工系统中的流体输运，特别是淋巴血管系统的单向流体输运机制。

Method: 研究以哺乳动物淋巴血管系统为实例，构建了收集淋巴管（collecting lymphatic）的人工模型。通过实验和理论分析，研究了由时空激发产生的单向输运的丰富动力学特性，考察了收缩波长、方向性和脉动性对流速的控制作用。

Result: 研究发现分布式瓣膜（distributed leaflets）作为连续破缺对称性，能够实现稳健且可扩展的输运，适用于任何波形和外部压力梯度。实验和理论均表明，收缩波长、方向性和脉动性控制着流速。反直觉地发现，某些波形在逆流传播时能最大化输运效率。

Conclusion: 该研究推进了对生物系统及其他领域中单向流体输运的理解，揭示了将非线性（nonlinearities）与时空激发耦合如何能够跨领域调控此类输运过程，为流体输运机制提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Locally broken symmetries are used across fields to transport matter, particles and information in preferential directions. Beyond local mechanisms, spatially distributed nonlinearities in crystalline media have enabled non-reciprocal transport, a rectification mechanism that operates continuously across scales and frequencies. Here, we show that this concept applies beyond condensed matter, to fluid transport in living organisms and artificial systems. We take the example of the lymphatic vascular system, which transports interstitial fluid in mammals, and demonstrate that distributed leaflets act as continuous broken symmetries. We build an artificial model of a collecting lymphatic and investigate the naturally richer dynamics of unidirectional transport that arises from spatiotemporal excitations. We observe robust and scalable transport for any waveshape and external pressure gradients. We show experimentally and theoretically that the contraction wavelength, directionality, and pulsatility control the flow rate. In particular, we counterintuitively find waveshapes that maximize transport when propagating against the direction of the flow. Overall, our findings advance the understanding of unidirectional fluid transport in living systems and beyond, and reveal how coupling nonlinearities with spatiotemporal excitations can tune such transport across fields.

### [238] [Cratering by the oblique impact of a spinning projectile](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27746)
*Douglas Daniel de Carvalho,Erick de Moraes Franklin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过离散元方法（DEM）计算，探究了固体弹丸以不同入射角撞击颗粒床时，弹丸自旋和堆积分数对撞击坑形成动力学的影响。研究发现弹丸可能反弹、部分或完全埋入，且埋入后可能水平迁移；堆积分数增强反弹，自旋方向影响动力学行为；撞击坑形态呈现多种形状，与弹丸行为相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用离散元方法（Discrete Element Method, DEM）进行计算模拟，系统改变弹丸自旋的大小和方向、撞击速度、颗粒床堆积分数以及入射角等参数，以研究这些因素对撞击动力学的影响。

Result: 研究发现：在给定撞击速度下，小角度入射时弹丸可能反弹，大角度时可能完全或部分埋入，且埋入弹丸有时能水平迁移较大距离；增加堆积分数会增强反弹；初始自旋的方向和取向会诱导反弹、埋入或横向偏离。撞击坑形态随参数变化呈现圆形、椭圆形、水滴状、蝌蚪状及过渡形状，与弹丸行为密切相关。

Conclusion: 研究提出了组织和分类观测动力学的图表，为理解自然界中发现的撞击坑不同形状以及撞击物质的最终命运提供了新的见解。结果表明弹丸自旋和颗粒床堆积分数是影响撞击坑形成动力学和形态的关键因素。

Abstract: We investigate the roles of spin and packing fraction on the dynamics of cratering when a solid projectile impacts a granular bed at different incident angles. For that, we carried out DEM (discrete element method) computations in which we varied the magnitude and direction of the projectile spin, the impact velocity, the bed packing fraction, and the incident angle. For a given incident velocity, we found that the projectile can rebound for small angles, or be completely or partially buried for larger angles, and that when buried it can sometimes migrate large horizontal distances depending on the incident angle. We also found that increasing the packing fraction strengthens rebounds, and that the initial spin, depending on its direction and orientation, induces rebound, burying, or transverse deviations. The crater morphology also changes with the varying parameters, acquiring circular, elliptical, goutte-like, tadpole-like, and transitional shapes, correlating well with the projectile behavior. Finally, we propose diagrams organizing and classifying the dynamics observed. Our results shed new light on the different shapes of craters found in nature and the fate of the impacting material.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该综述主要涵盖两种多链方法：原始链网络模型（primitive chain network model）强调实空间力平衡，而多链滑移弹簧模型（multi-chain slip-spring model）则源自明确定义的自由能泛函。这些方法在三维空间中显式解析多个链之间的力平衡和拓扑耦合。

Conclusion: 多链粗粒化模拟方法为缠结聚合物动力学提供了超越传统平均场管模型的更全面框架，能够更好地处理空间关联、涨落和复杂拓扑重排问题，并在多种聚合物体系中展现出广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: This review describes the development and applications of multi-chain coarse-grained simulations for entangled polymer dynamics. The mean-field tube model has long served as the standard paradigm for describing the many-body entanglement problem as the motion of a single chain in a static field; it faces intrinsic limitations when addressing spatial correlations, fluctuations, and complex topological rearrangements. To overcome these limitations, "multi-chain" approaches -- specifically the primitive chain network and multi-chain slip-spring models -- were developed. These simulations explicitly resolve the force balance and topological coupling between multiple chains in three-dimensional space. This review covers the primitive chain network model, which emphasizes real-space force balance, and the multi-chain slip-spring model, which is derived from a well-defined free-energy functional. Linear and nonlinear rheology predictions are discussed, along with molecular mechanisms such as constraint release and stretch/orientation-induced reductions in friction. Extensions to branched polymers, wall-slip phenomena, and network polymers are also mentioned.

Motivation: 气体气泡通过高多孔传输层（highly porous transport layers, PTLs）的输运是质子交换膜水电解槽等电化学装置中的关键过程，需要理解气泡在复杂多孔网络中的迁移行为。

Method: 研究采用模型系统，结合分析建模（analytical modeling）、三维颜色梯度晶格玻尔兹曼模拟（three-dimensional color-gradient lattice Boltzmann simulations）和X射线成像（X-ray radiography），研究单个、成对和多个气泡在毛细管中的运动。

Result: 对于单个气泡，推导了区分通过与堵塞的临界邦德数（critical Bond number）解析表达式；对于气泡对，发现了额外的堵塞与解堵路径，包括液膜压力驱动的流体力学解堵（hydrodynamic unclogging）和聚并诱导的堵塞与解堵（coalescence-induced clogging and unclogging）。

Conclusion: 通过将结果映射为约束比（confinement ratio）和邦德数的函数，定义了控制气泡通过的不同动力学区域；在高多孔镍泡沫中的气泡链实验证实了预测的堵塞与解堵机制。

Abstract: Gas bubble transport through highly porous transport layers (PTLs) is a key process in electrochemical devices such as proton exchange membrane water electrolyzers, where bubbles generated at catalyst surfaces must migrate through complex porous networks. To understand this process, we focus on model systems, namely the motion of single, paired and multiple bubbles in capillaries and study these by combining analytical modeling, three-dimensional color-gradient lattice Boltzmann simulations, and X-ray radiography. For single bubbles, we derive an analytical expression for the critical Bond number separating passage from clogging and show that, in the low deformation regime, it accurately predicts this transition in circular capillaries. Extending the study to bubble pairs, we uncover additional clogging and unclogging pathways, including hydrodynamic unclogging driven by pressure buildup in the interbubble film, and coalescence-induced clogging and unclogging. By mapping our results as functions of confinement ratio and Bond number, we define distinct dynamical regimes that control bubble passage. Experiments on bubble chains rising through highly porous nickel foams confirm the predicted clogging and unclogging mechanisms.

</details>


### [243] [Phase Boundaries of Bulk 2D Rhombi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28541)
*Gerardo Odriozola,Péter Gurin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过副本交换蒙特卡洛模拟研究了二维硬菱形系统的相图，发现菱形形状从近方形到针状变化时，系统展现出丰富的相行为，包括各向同性流体、向列相、菱形流体、六角流体及多种空间填充结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维硬菱形系统的相图，探索从近方形到针状不同形状菱形在密度变化时的相行为演化规律，特别是关注周期性与非周期性空间填充结构的形成条件。

Method: 采用副本交换蒙特卡洛模拟（replica exchange Monte Carlo simulations）方法，系统研究不同角度（从近90度到接近0度）的硬菱形在二维空间中的相行为。

Result: 当角度接近90度时，系统随密度增加依次呈现各向同性流体、菱形流体、转子相和柱状空间填充结构；角度接近0度时，相行为类似针状极限；在约60度时，非周期性空间填充结构占据主导地位。

Conclusion: 二维硬菱形系统的相图高度依赖于菱形形状，从近方形到针状的连续变化中，系统展现出从周期性到非周期性结构的丰富相变序列，包括六角流体等中间相的形成。

Abstract: We conducted replica exchange Monte Carlo simulations to investigate the phase diagram of identical hard rhombi systems in two dimensions. The rhombi shape varies from nearly square-like, as their minor angle a approaches 90 degrees, to needle-like, as it approaches 0 degrees. For angles near 90 degrees, we observe an isotropic fluid, a rhombatic fluid, a rotator phase, and a columnar space-filling structure with increasing density. Conversely, as a approaches 0 degrees, the results resemble the needle limit. Even for angles as small as a = 20 degrees, we still obtain isotropic, nematic, and rhombatic fluids before reaching a rhombic solid, but the nematic phase gains importance with decreasing a. At a approximately 60 degrees, aperiodic space-filling structures with long-range six-fold orientational symmetry dominate over periodic candidates such as the rhombic and rhombille. This aperiodic solid undergoes a melting process leading to a phase with quasi-long-range six-fold orientational symmetry, a hexatic fluid, before reaching the isotropic phase.

### [244] [Rounded hard squares confined in a circle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28609)
*Zhongtian Yuan,Yao Li*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过蒙特卡洛模拟揭示了圆形约束下圆角硬方块（rounded-corner hard-squares）的熵驱动结构相变：低圆度时形成具有四重拓扑缺陷的十字形畴结构，高圆度时出现六畴分区结构，包含六个+1/4缺陷和一个中心-1/2缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受限条件下的堆积（packing under confinement）通过熵效应产生丰富有序结构，是凝聚态物理、生物物理和材料科学的基本问题。然而，约束对各项异性硬粒子（anisotropic hard particles）的影响，特别是拓扑缺陷结构（topological defect structures）的出现机制仍不清楚。

Method: 采用NPT系综的蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations in the NPT ensemble），研究圆形约束对不同圆度（roundness）的圆角硬方块（rounded-corner hard-squares）有序结构的影响。

Result: 低圆度时系统形成具有四重序（tetratic order）的整合十字形畴（cross-shaped domain），包含四个+1/4向错（+1/4 disclinations）和柱状位移（column shifts）。圆度增加时发现新的分区结构（partition structure），粒子自组装成六个畴，由六个+1/4向错和一个中心-1/2向错（-1/2 disclination）分隔。

Conclusion: 约束几何与胶体形状（colloid shape）之间的相互作用能够驱动熵主导的结构相变（entropy governed structural transitions），为拓扑超材料（topological metamaterials）设计提供了新见解。

Abstract: Packing under confinement could generate rich ordered structures through entropic effects, which is a fundamental problem in condensed matter, biophysics and material science. The influence of confinement to the anisotropic hard particles--particularly regarding the emergence of topological defect structures--remains poorly understood. Recent studies have shown that granular rods confined within circular boundaries can cluster into square like super-particles, forming four disclinations. In this study, we employ Monte Carlo simulations in the NPT ensemble to investigate how circular confinement influences the ordered structures of rounded-corner hard-squares with varying roundness. At low roundness, the system forms an integrated cross-shaped domain with tetratic order and four +1/4 disclinations in the corners, along with some column shifts. As roundness increases, we found a new partition structure, where particles self-assemble into six domains separated by six +1/4 disclinations and a central -1/2 disclination. Our findings reveal that the interplay between confinement geometry and colloid shape can drive entropy governed structural transitions, offering new insights for the design of topological metamaterials.

</details>


### [245] [Active Growth Layer Induced by Micromechanical Feedback Shapes Proliferating Cell Collectives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28630)
*Fidel Álvarez Murphy,Ignacio Medina,Néstor Sepúlveda,Gustavo Düring*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究证明仅通过微观力学反馈即可形成活跃生长层，无需生化调控。通过基于粒子的增殖细胞模型，发现压缩应力局部抑制生长，产生由力学长度尺度控制的生长区域，并观察到由纯力学反馈驱动的指状不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 增殖细胞集体常在边界附近形成活跃生长层，调控扩张和形态，见于细菌生物膜、上皮组织和肿瘤球体等系统。虽然这些生长层被归因于多种机制，但其微观起源在许多情况下仍不明确。

Method: 引入基于粒子的非运动性增殖细胞模型，其中生长受压缩应力局部抑制，将分裂与力学相互作用耦合，无需生化调控即可产生活跃生长层。通过粗粒化模型得到无调整参数的连续介质描述。

Result: 涌现的力学长度尺度设定增殖区域范围，控制系统的跨尺度行为，调控生长动力学、形态并组织内部应力和速度场。当菌落扩张到被动环境时，观察到并表征了由纯力学反馈驱动的指状不稳定性（fingering instabilities）。

Conclusion: 微观力学反馈本身提供了生长层涌现的最小机制，为现有方法提供了微观基础。进一步建立了与营养耗竭模型的对应关系，为在最小微观框架内研究扩张前沿的统计特性提供了途径。

Abstract: Proliferating cell collectives often develop an active growth layer near their boundary that regulates expansion and morphology, as observed in systems ranging from bacterial biofilms to epithelial tissues and tumor spheroids. While such layers have been attributed to diverse mechanisms, their microscopic origin remains unclear in many situations. Here, we show that micromechanical feedback alone provides a minimal mechanism for their emergence. We introduce a particle-based model of non-motile proliferating cells in which growth is locally inhibited by compressive stress, coupling division to mechanical interactions and generating an active growth layer without biochemical regulation. An emergent mechanical length scale sets the extent of the proliferative region and controls the system's behavior across scales, governing growth dynamics, morphology and organizing internal stress and velocity fields. Coarse-graining the model yields a continuum description with no adjustable parameters, providing a microscopic foundation for existing approaches. When the colony expands into a passive environment, we observe and characterize fingering instabilities driven purely by mechanical feedback. We further establish a correspondence with nutrient-depletion models, providing a route to study the statistical properties of expanding fronts within a minimal microscopic framework.

### [246] [Phenol release from pNIPAM hydrogels: Scaling Molecular Dynamics simulations with Dynamical Density Functional Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28659)
*H. A. Pérez-Ramírez,A. Moncho-Jordá,G. Odriozola*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究采用分子动力学模拟和Bennett接受比方法，计算了苯酚、甲烷和5-氟尿嘧啶在不同pNIPAM浓度水溶液中的转移自由能，并分析了其与聚合物浓度的线性关系及温度依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解小分子在pNIPAM水凝胶中的转移自由能变化，这对于药物释放系统设计至关重要。特别关注温度对转移自由能的影响，以及聚合物浓度与转移自由能之间的依赖关系。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）结合Bennett接受比方法（Bennett's acceptance ratio method），计算了苯酚、甲烷和5-氟尿嘧啶在纯水和不同聚合物体积分数（φ_p）的pNIPAM水溶液中的转移自由能（ΔG_trans）。

Result: 苯酚和5-氟尿嘧啶在所有温度下均吸附于pNIPAM表面，转移自由能为负值；而甲烷的转移自由能在pNIPAM低临界溶液温度（T_c）以下为正，以上为负。所有分子的转移自由能与pNIPAM浓度呈线性关系，直至高聚合物密度。

Abstract: We employed molecular dynamics simulations (MD) and Bennett's acceptance ratio method to compute the free energy of transfer (Delta G_trans) of phenol, methane, and 5-fluorouracil (5-FU) between bulk water and water-pNIPAM mixtures with different polymer volume fractions (phi_p). To this end, we first calculate the solvation free energies in both media to obtain Delta G_trans. Phenol and 5-FU (a drug used in cancer treatment) adsorb onto the pNIPAM surface and exhibit negative values of Delta G_trans irrespective of temperature, both above and below the lower critical solution temperature (T_c) of pNIPAM. In contrast, methane changes the sign of Delta G_trans, being positive below and negative above T_c. In all cases, and in contrast with some theoretical predictions, Delta G_trans shows a linear dependence on pNIPAM concentration up to high polymer densities. We also compute the diffusion coefficient (D) of phenol in water-pNIPAM mixtures as a function of phi_p in the dilute limit. Both Delta G_trans and D as functions of phi_p are key inputs to estimate the release halftime of hollow pNIPAM microgels using dynamic density functional theory (DDFT). Our scaling approach reproduces the experimental value of 2200 s for microgels of 50 micrometer radius without a cavity, at phi_p approximately 0.83 and 315 K.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多组分凝胶系统因其优异的力学性能在过去十年备受关注，但其中如顺序凝胶化（sequential gelation）等机制主要在化学不可逆聚合物和蛋白质凝胶中研究，而在物理可逆胶体系统中探索较少。

Method: 采用介观尺度模拟技术（mesoscale simulation techniques）对双组分胶体系统进行建模，该系统组分间的种间（interspecies）和种内（intraspecies）静电相互作用可独立调控。

Result: 研究表明，仅通过时间控制和种间相互作用的调控，即可构建显著不同的网络结构：从双网络（double networks）到混合及核壳复合结构（core-shell composite structures），这些结构具有不同的粗糙度和异质性特征。

Conclusion: 这些发现为多组分胶体系统的进一步探索提供了有力依据，展示了通过简单调控参数即可实现多样化网络结构设计的潜力。

Abstract: Multicomponent gel systems have garnered much interest due to their compelling mechanical properties in the past decade. Yet, some mechanisms associated with multicomponent gels, such as sequential gelation, have been explored primarily in the context of chemical nonreversible polymeric and protein gels than in physical reversible colloidal ones. In this study, we use mesoscale simulation techniques to model the sequential gelation of two-component colloidal systems whose components' interspecies and intraspecies electrostatic interactions can be modified independently. We show that by simply leveraging temporal control and interspecies interactions, we can construct markedly different networks; from double networks to mixed and core-shell composite structures of varying coarseness and heterogeneity natures. These findings present a compelling case for further exploration of multicomponent colloidal systems.

### [248] [Symmetry analysis and exact solutions of multi-layer quasi-geostrophic problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26959)
*Serhii D. Koval,Alex Bihlo,Roman O. Popovych*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究对多层准地转（multi-layer quasi-geostrophic）模型进行了扩展对称性分析，首次正确描述了该模型的守恒律和哈密顿结构，通过李对称约化获得了包含多种经典线性方程的不变子模型，并构造了广泛的精确解族，包括重新发现的斜压罗斯贝波和相干涡旋结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多层准地转模型由任意数量的耦合正压涡度方程组成，是描述地球物理流体动力学的重要框架。先前研究未能正确描述该模型的守恒律和哈密顿结构，需要对其进行系统的对称性分析以揭示其数学结构和物理特性。

Method: 采用原创方法计算了模型的最大李不变代数（maximal Lie invariance algebra）和完整点对称伪群（complete point-symmetry pseudogroup）。通过分类李不变代数的一维和二维子代数，详尽研究了余维一、二、三的李约化（Lie reductions）。

Result: 在原始非线性模型的不变子模型中获得了包括亥姆霍兹（Helmholtz）、修正亥姆霍兹、拉普拉斯（Laplace）、克莱因-戈登（Klein-Gordon）、惠特克（Whittaker）、贝塞尔（Bessel）和线性化本杰明-博纳-马霍尼（Benjamin-Bona-Mahony）方程在内的解耦线性方程组。这些系统的积分显著依赖于模型垂直耦合矩阵的谱特性。

Conclusion: 研究构造了广泛的精确解族，包括重新发现的定常和传播斜压罗斯贝波（baroclinic Rossby waves）、相干斜压涡旋（coherent baroclinic eddies）、热涡（hetons）和局域偶极涡旋（localized dipolar vortices）的表示。使用三层海洋模型的真实地球物理数据验证了所得解的物理相关性。

Abstract: We carry out an extended symmetry analysis of the multi-layer quasi-geostrophic problem. This model is given by a system of an arbitrary number of coupled barotropic vorticity equations. Conservation laws and a Hamiltonian structure for the general case of the model are correctly described for the first time. Using original methods, we compute the maximal Lie invariance algebra and the complete point-symmetry pseudogroup of the model. After classifying one- and two-dimensional subalgebras of the Lie invariance algebra, we exhaustively study codimension-one, -two and -three Lie reductions. Notably, among invariant submodels of the original nonlinear model, we obtain uncoupled systems of well-known linear equations, including the Helmholtz, modified Helmholtz, Laplace, Klein-Gordon, Whittaker, Bessel and linearized Benjamin-Bona-Mahony equations. Integration of these systems significantly depends on spectral properties of the model's vertical coupling matrix, which we also revisit in detail. As a result, we construct wide families of exact solutions, including rediscovered representations of stationary and travelling baroclinic Rossby waves, coherent baroclinic eddies, hetons and localized dipolar vortices. We illustrate the physical relevance of obtained solutions using real-world geophysical data for a three-layer ocean model.

</details>


### [249] [Semiclassical shape resonances for magnetic Stark Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27196)
*Kentaro Kameoka,Naoya Yoshida*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了二维磁斯塔克哈密顿量（magnetic Stark Hamiltonians）在准经典极限下的形状共振（shape resonances），证明了共振与参考算子离散特征值的一一对应关系，并推导了共振数量的韦尔定律（Weyl law）和共振实部在势阱底部的渐近行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维磁斯塔克哈密顿量在准经典极限下的形状共振，旨在理解磁场和线性势扰动下量子系统的共振特性，特别是势阱存在时的共振行为。

Method: 采用复扭曲哈密顿量（complex distorted Hamiltonians）方法，将共振视为复特征值进行研究；通过复平移（complex translation）在紧集外定义复扭曲哈密顿量，并建立与参考算子离散特征值的对应关系。

Result: 证明了哈密顿量的形状共振与特定参考算子离散特征值之间存在一一对应关系；推导了共振数量的韦尔定律，并获得了共振实部在势阱底部附近的渐近行为。

Conclusion: 在标量势具有势阱的假设下，建立了磁斯塔克哈密顿量形状共振与参考算子特征值的对应关系，为理解此类系统的共振结构提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study shape resonances of two-dimensional magnetic Stark Hamiltonians in the semiclassical limit. The magnetic field is assumed to be constant and the scalar potential is a perturbation of a linear potential. Under the assumption that the scalar potential has potential wells, the existence of a one-to-one correspondence between shape resonances of the Hamiltonian and discrete eigenvalues of a certain reference operator is proved. This implies the Weyl law for the number of resonances and the asymptotic behavior of the real parts of resonances near the bottom of a potential well. Resonances are studied as complex eigenvalues of complex distorted Hamiltonians, which is defined by the complex translation outside a compact set.

### [250] [Quantum Hall States response to toroidal geometry deformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27319)
*Bruno Mera,José M. Mourão,João P. Nunes,Carolina Paiva*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文应用几何量子化（geometric quantization）技术研究整数和分数量子霍尔效应（quantum Hall effects）对环面几何形变的响应。通过复时间哈密顿演化（complex time Hamiltonian evolution）诱导几何变化，并利用广义相干态变换（generalized coherent state transforms）追踪Laughlin态的演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究整数和分数量子霍尔效应对环面几何形变的响应，探索几何量子化技术在拓扑物态研究中的应用。虽然平坦环面几何下的Laughlin态已有深入研究，但通过广义相干态变换的方法具有新颖性。

Method: 采用复时间哈密顿演化诱导几何变化，结合广义相干态变换追踪Laughlin态演化。研究两类形变：平坦环面形变（flat toroidal deformations）和非平坦Kähler环面形变（nonflat Kähler toroidal deformations）。后者对应Kähler度量空间中保持椭圆曲线模量τ的Mabuchi测地线。

Result: 平坦形变中使用的哈密顿量在平移生成元中是二次的且非周期。非平坦Kähler形变由环面上的全局双周期哈密顿量生成，对应的虚时间流在有限虚时间内会达到曲率奇点。通过限制于S^1不变形变，获得了环面几何和Laughlin态演化的显式解析表达式。

Conclusion: 该方法为研究非平坦Kähler形变提供了测试平台，并成功获得了从平坦几何到曲率奇点整个演化过程中环面几何和Laughlin态的显式解析描述，展示了几何量子化技术在拓扑物态几何响应研究中的有效性。

Abstract: In this paper, we apply techniques of geometric quantization to study the response of the integer and fractional quantum Hall effects to toroidal geometry deformation. The main method is that of using complex time Hamiltonian evolution to induce the geometry change and then the associated generalized coherent state transforms (gCST) to find the evolution of the Laughlin states. We consider two kinds of deformations. The first are flat toroidal deformations. Although Laughlin states for all flat toroidal geometries have been thoroughly studied before, we believe that our approach via the gCST is novel. It also serves as a testing ground to study the non-flat Kähler deformations. The Hamiltonians used in the flat deformations are quadratic in the generators of translations and therefore non periodic. The second kind of deformations involve nonflat Kähler toroidal deformations, generated by global, thus bi-periodic, Hamiltonians on the torus. The corresponding imaginary time flows are (elliptic curve modulus) $τ$-preserving Mabuchi geodesics in the space of Kähler metrics on the torus, hitting a curvature singularity in finite imaginary time. By restricting to $S^1$-invariant deformations we find explicit analytic expressions for the evolution of the toroidal geometry and of the Laughlin states all the way to the singularity.

</details>


### [251] [The Full Set of KMS-States for Abelian Kitaev Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27436)
*Danilo Polo Ojito,Emil Prodan*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究阿贝尔Kitaev模型的$C^\ast$-代数结构，特别是其顶点和面算子生成的子代数$\mathcal{C}$与准局域可观测量代数$\mathcal{A}$之间的关系，旨在通过群胚$C^\ast$-代数方法分析模型的动力学和热力学性质。

Method: 首先证明$\mathcal{C}$是$\mathcal{A}$的$C^\ast$-对角（$C^\ast$-diagonal），然后利用相关的Weyl群胚（Weyl groupoid）$\mathcal{G}_\mathcal{C}$将$\mathcal{A}$表示为群胚$C^\ast$-代数，其中动力学由群胚1-上循环（groupoid 1-cocycle）$c_H$生成，最后应用$(c_H,β)$-KMS测度的概念分析热力学态。

Result: 完整识别了模型的所有KMS态（KMS states），并证明了在$β\in [0,\infty)$范围内KMS态的唯一性；同时证明了当$β\rightarrow \infty$时极限存在，且与模型的唯一无阻挫基态（frustration-free ground state）一致。

Conclusion: 通过将阿贝尔Kitaev模型表示为群胚$C^\ast$-代数，成功建立了其代数结构与热力学性质之间的精确对应关系，为理解此类拓扑量子模型的热力学行为提供了严格的数学框架。

Abstract: We first prove that the subalgebra $\mathcal{C}$ generated by the vertex and face operators of an abelian Kitaev model is a $C^\ast$-diagonal of the UHF algebra $\mathcal{A}$ of quasilocal observables. This gives us access to the Weyl groupoid $\mathcal{G}_\mathcal{C}$ associated with the $C^\ast$-inclusion $\mathcal{C} \hookrightarrow \mathcal{A}$, which supplies a valuable presentation of $\mathcal{A}$ as a groupoid $C^\ast$-algebra where the dynamics of the model are generated by a groupoid 1-cocycle $c_H$. Making appeal to the notion of $(c_H,β)$-KMS measures for this groupoid, we identify the full set of KMS states of the model and prove its uniqueness for $β\in [0,\infty)$. Furthermore, we show that its limit at $β\rightarrow \infty$ exists and coincides with the unique frustration-free ground state of the model.

### [252] [Pseudo-magnetism in a strained discrete honeycomb lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27503)
*Xuenan Li,Michael I. Weinstein*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明了在具有蜂窝对称性的非磁性波传播介质中，缓慢变化的非均匀应变可诱导有效磁场（赝磁场），导致波包在特定变形方向下形成横向指数局域化的类平面波态，其能谱呈现近似平坦带（朗道能级）特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于在石墨烯、光子晶体等物理系统中观察到的现象：具有蜂窝对称性的非磁性波传播介质在非均匀应变下会诱导有效磁场（赝磁场）。本文旨在从理论上严格分析这种应变诱导局域化效应的机制和条件。

Method: 方法基于离散最近邻紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）描述非均匀应变蜂窝介质，推导出控制波包包络动力学的连续有效磁狄拉克哈密顿量（Dirac Hamiltonian）。针对保持"扶手椅"方向平移不变性的有界梯度单向变形，采用多尺度分析方法证明类平面波态的存在性。

Result: 结果表明，对于诱导近似垂直恒定赝磁场（朗道规范）的变形，存在沿扶手椅方向类平面波（赝周期）且横向指数局域化的时间谐波态。这些态的横向局域化由一维有效狄拉克哈密顿量的本征态决定，能谱呈现近似平坦带（朗道能级）特征，导致极高的态密度。相比之下，保持锯齿方向平移不变性的类似变形则不诱导此类局域化。

Conclusion: 研究严格证明了非均匀应变蜂窝介质中赝磁场诱导的局域化现象，揭示了变形方向对称性对局域化效应的关键影响：扶手椅方向变形可产生朗道能级态，而锯齿方向变形则无此效应。数值模拟结果进一步验证了不同变形类型的理论预测。

Abstract: Slowly varying nonuniform strains of non-magnetic wave propagating media with honeycomb symmetry induce an effective- or pseudo-magnetic field, a phenomenon observed first in graphene, and later in photonic crystals and other physical settings. Starting with a discrete nearest-neighbor tight-binding model of a non-uniformly strained honeycomb medium, we derive the continuum effective magnetic Dirac Hamiltonian governing the envelope dynamics of wave packets, which are spectrally localized near a Dirac point (conical band degeneracy) of the unperturbed honeycomb. For unidirectional deformations of bounded gradient, which preserve translation invariance along the ''armchair'' direction, we prove the existence of time-harmonic states which are plane-wave like (pseudo-periodic) along the armchair direction and exponentially localized transverse to it. We also obtain the leading order multi-scale structure of such modes for small deformation gradients. Their transverse localization are determined by the eigenstates of a one dimensional effective Dirac Hamiltonian. Our rigorous results apply to deformations which induce an approximate perpendicular constant pseudo-magnetic field (Landau gauge), and yield states with nearly flat band (Landau level) spectrum and hence very high density of states. In contrast, the analogous deformation which preserves translations in the zigzag direction induces no such localization. Corroborating numerical simulations for the different deformation types are presented.

### [253] [Homothetic Hodge$-$de Rham Theory and a Geometric Regularization of Elliptic Boundary Value Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27564)
*Fereidoun Sabetghadam*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种经典Weyl可积几何的同位扩展，通过将线性规范变换推广到以特定调和尺度不变形式为中心的仿射同位变换。该框架产生了扭曲外微积分，在紧致黎曼流形上建立了同位Hodge理论，并展示了标量同位Laplacian为椭圆边值问题提供了严格的扩散界面（体积惩罚）表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括：1）通过变量平移将仿射规范变换重新线性化；2）建立与de Rham复形的Witten变形结构等价的扭曲外微积分；3）在紧致黎曼流形上定义扭曲伴随算子和同位Laplacian，并证明同位Hodge分解定理。

Result: 结果表明：1）标量同位Laplacian为椭圆边值问题提供了严格的扩散界面（diffuse interface）或体积惩罚（volume penalization）表示；2）将Weyl尺度场建模为超曲面附近的固定分布时，低阶几何项形成惩罚层，可在单一几何方程中强制Dirichlet、Neumann或Cauchy边界条件；3）即使存在经典不相容的Cauchy数据，该公式仍能产生一致的弱解。

Conclusion: 该框架的应用包括构造椭圆场方程中点源的非奇异模型，该模型在保留正确Coulombian远场的同时消除了核心奇异性并产生有限场能。这为处理边界值问题和奇异性问题提供了新的几何工具。

Abstract: We introduce a homothetic extension of classical Weyl integrable geometry by generalizing the usual linear gauge transformations to affine homothetic transformations centered at a distinguished harmonic, scale-invariant form $α_d$. After relinearizing these affine gauge transformations via a suitable shift of variables, we obtain a twisted exterior calculus that is structurally equivalent to the Witten deformation of the de Rham complex. On this basis, we develop a corresponding homothetic Hodge theory: we define a twisted adjoint and homothetic Laplacian, and prove a homothetic Hodge decomposition theorem on compact Riemannian manifolds. In the context of partial differential equations, we show that the scalar homothetic Laplacian provides a rigorous diffuse interface (volume penalization) representation of elliptic boundary value problems. Modeling the Weyl scale field as a fixed distribution localized near a hypersurface, the resulting lower order geometric terms form a penalty layer that enforces Dirichlet, Neumann, or Cauchy data within a single geometric equation. This formulation yields consistent weak solutions even in the presence of classically incompatible Cauchy data. As an application, we construct a nonsingular model for point sources in elliptic field equations, which preserves the correct Coulombian far field while removing the core singularity and yielding finite field energy.
