Abstract: We consider wave propagation through a 1D periodic network of slowly time-modulated interfaces. Each interface is modelled by time-dependent spring-mass jump conditions, where mass and rigidity interface parameters are modulated in time. Low-frequency homogenisation yields a leading-order model described by an effective time-dependent wave equation, i.e.\ a wave equation with effective mass density and Young's modulus which are homogeneous in space but depend on time. This means that time-dependent bulk effective properties can be created by an array where only interfaces are modulated in time. The occurrence of k-gaps in case of a periodic modulation is also analysed.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We consider a Dirichlet waveguide in $\mathbb{R}^n$ ($n = 2,3$) with an attached cavity. We show that if the cavity admits a small gap, then the original embedded eigenvalues turn into resonances. The main question we address is how the size of the gap affects the resonant properties, in particular the imaginary part of the resonant pole. For example, in the case of a two dimensional waveguide with a gap of size $\varepsilon$, we show that the leading order term of the resonance behaves as $\mathcal O (\varepsilon^2)$. In the three-dimensional case, if the aperture is defined by a rectangular opening with volume proportional to $\varepsilon^2$, the resonant component behaves as $\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^4)$. ### [257] [A symmetry formula for correlation functions in the superintegrable chiral Potts spin chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27930)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数学证明方法，针对链长L和哈密顿量与单点平移算符（one-site translation operator）的同时本征矢，推导关联函数的精确对称公式。然后将三态链的情况推广到任意N和所有平移本征扇区（translation eigensector）。

Result: 证明了对于所有链长L和同时本征矢，关联函数满足$\langle Z_0^r Z_R^{\dagger r}\rangle^*=\langle Z_0^r Z_{L-R}^{\dagger r}\rangle$（其中$1\leqslant r\leqslant N-1$）。特别地，当L为偶数时，中点关联$\langle Z_0^r Z_{L/2}^{\dagger r}\rangle$为实数。

Conclusion: 该研究成功证明了周期边界条件下N态超可积手性Potts自旋链两点关联函数的精确对称公式，完全解决了Fabricius和McCoy的猜想，并将三态链的结果推广到任意N和所有平移本征扇区。

Abstract: We prove an exact finite-volume symmetry formula for two-point functions in the periodic $N$-state superintegrable chiral Potts spin chain. We show that, for every chain length $L$ and every simultaneous eigenvector of the Hamiltonian and the one-site translation operator, the correlations satisfy $\langle Z_0^r Z_R^{\dagger r}\rangle^*=\langle Z_0^r Z_{L-R}^{\dagger r}\rangle$ for $1\leqslant r\leqslant N-1$. Hence, whenever $L$ is even, the midpoint correlation $\langle Z_0^r Z_{L/2}^{\dagger r}\rangle$ is real. Then we generalise the three-state chain case to arbitrary $N$ and to every translation eigensector. This resolves a conjecture of Fabricius and McCoy.

### [258] [A Damage-Driven Model for Duchenne Muscular Dystrophy: Early-Stage Dynamics and Invasion Thresholds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28147)

Abstract: We introduce a spatially extended mathematical model for Duchenne muscular dystrophy based on a damage-driven paradigm, in which immune recruitment is triggered by tissue injury. We establish the global well-posedness of the system and investigate the early-stage dynamics through linearization around the healthy equilibrium. Our analysis shows that diffusion does not induce Turing instabilities, so that spatial heterogeneity cannot arise from diffusion-driven mechanisms. Instead, disease progression occurs through invasion processes. We derive explicit conditions for the onset of invasion, interpreted as an effective damage reproduction threshold and characterize the minimal propagation speed of pathological fronts, showing that the dynamics is governed by a pulled-front mechanism. Numerical simulations support the analytical results and confirm the transition between decay and invasion. These results provide a mathematical framework for early-stage disease progression and indicate that spatial patterns arise from the expansion of localized damage rather than from intrinsic pattern-forming mechanisms.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究将非厄米随机矩阵对称类中的三种通用局域体态统计扩展到了三种通用局域边缘统计。本研究旨在通过解析和数值方法深入理解这些局域统计特性，特别是复间隔比和最近邻间距分布在不同对称类中的行为。

Method: 研究分为两部分：第一部分解析研究A类（复Ginibre）在有限矩阵尺寸N下的复间隔比，引入条件点过程简化现有表达式；第二部分数值比较三类对称类（A、AI†、AII†）的复间隔比、其矩以及最近邻间距分布，并与二维泊松过程进行对比。

Result: 研究发现：1）在A类中，早期引入的不可控近似在大N极限下收敛良好；2）对于椭圆Ginibre系综，提出了参数依赖的N=3推测，可插值到高斯酉系综；3）不同边缘普适类的排斥程度可通过有效二维库仑气体模型理解；4）复间隔比在边缘处不能完全展开局域统计；5）三类对称类在体态和边缘的小参数最近邻间距分布均符合立方排斥规律。

Conclusion: 该研究系统分析了非厄米随机矩阵三类对称类的局域统计特性，通过解析推导和数值模拟揭示了复间隔比和最近邻间距分布在体态和边缘的行为差异，为理解非厄米系统的统计特性提供了重要见解。

Abstract: The conjectured three generic local bulk statistics amongst all non-Hermitian random matrix symmetry classes have recently been extended to three generic local edge statistics. We study analytically and numerically complex spacing ratios and nearest-neighbour (NN) spacing distributions that characterise such local statistics. We choose the three simplest representatives of these universality classes, given by the Gaussian ensembles of complex Ginibre, complex symmetric and complex self-dual matrices, denoted by class A, AI$^†$ and AII$^†$. In the first part, we analytically study the complex spacing ratio in class A, at finite matrix size $N$. Introducing a conditional point process, we simplify existing expressions and show why an uncontrolled approximation introduced earlier converges well in the large-$N$ limit in the bulk. When specifying to the elliptic Ginibre ensemble, we present a parameter-dependent $N=3$ surmise for the complex spacing ratio, interpolating to that of the Gaussian unitary ensemble (GUE), where such a surmise is very accurate. In the second numerical part, we compare complex spacing ratios, its moments, and NN spacing distributions for all three ensembles with that of uncorrelated points, the two-dimensional (2D) Poisson process, both in the bulk and at the edge. The varying degree of repulsion within these different edge universality classes can be well understood in terms of an effective 2D Coulomb gas description, at different values of inverse temperature $β$. We find indications that the complex spacing ratio does not fully unfold the local statistics at the edge. Finally we verify that for small argument, in all three symmetry classes the NN spacing distributions in the bulk and at the edge are consistent with the universal cubic repulsion.

</details>


### [261] [Geometry of the Ising persistence problem and the universal Bonnet-Manin Painlevé VI distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28632)
*Ivan Dornic,Robert Conte*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了非马尔可夫随机过程的完全持续概率分布，揭示了其由可积sech核的Fredholm Pfaffian结构控制，并发现该分布由Painlevé VI方程支配。持续指数在几何上被解释为相关Bonnet曲面的渐近平均曲率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于相互作用自旋系统及相关系统中的首达问题（first-passage questions）。本文旨在确定非马尔可夫随机过程的完全持续概率分布，该问题在统计物理中具有重要理论意义。

Method: 方法基于可积sech核$K_{\mathrm{sech}}=1/(2 π\cosh[(x-y)/2])$的精确Fredholm Pfaffian结构。在平稳标度区，持续概率被分解为可积sech核的偶数和奇数Fredholm行列式，这些行列式由二阶非线性常微分方程的全局解控制。

Result: 结果表明持续概率分布由Painlevé VI方程支配，该方程源于可积sech核的Fredholm Pfaffian结构。Derrida、Hakim和Pasquier最初获得的普适持续指数（universal persistence exponent）被恢复为渐近可观测量，并在几何上被解释为相关Bonnet曲面的渐近平均曲率。

Conclusion: 持续概率分布由Painlevé VI系统控制，该系统具有直接的几何解释：相关解与浸入$\mathbb R^3$中的Bonnet曲面单参数族的平均曲率一致。折叠变换（folding transformation）在这些曲面之间挑选出具有Manin系数$[0,0,0,0]$的Painlevé VI方程，该方程特别支配对称伊辛情况下的普适持续分布。

Abstract: We determine the full persistence probability distribution for a non-Markovian stochastic process, motivated by first-passage questions arising in interacting spin systems and allied systems. We show that this distribution is governed by a distinguished Painlevé VI system arising from an exact Fredholm Pfaffian structure associated with the integrable sech kernel, $K_{\mathrm{sech}}=1/(2 π\cosh[(x-y)/2])$. The universal persistence exponent originally obtained by Derrida, Hakim and Pasquier is recovered as an asymptotic observable and acquires a natural geometric interpretation. In the stationary scaling regime, the persistence probability admits an exact Pfaffian decomposition into even and odd Fredholm determinants of the integrable \emph{sech} kernel. These determinants are controlled by a unique global solution of a second-order nonlinear ordinary differential equation, which is identified as a particular Painlevé VI equation. The corresponding Painlevé VI connection problem determines the persistence exponent as a limiting value at infinity.
  We further show that the Painlevé VI system governing persistence admits a direct geometric interpretation: the relevant solution coincides with the mean curvature of a one-parameter family of Bonnet surfaces immersed in $\mathbb R^3$. A folding transformation between such surfaces singles out the Painlevé VI equation with Manin coefficients $[0,0,0,0]$, which in particular governs the universal persistence distribution in the symmetric Ising case. In this framework, the persistence exponent is identified with the asymptotic mean curvature of the associated surface.

</details>


### [262] [Invariant measures of randomized quantum trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28664)
*Tristan Benoist,Sascha Lill,Cornelia Vogel*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了当探针可观测量选择被随机化时量子轨迹（quantum trajectories）的性质，证明了非奇异随机化确保量子轨迹纯化并存在唯一不变概率测度，同时研究了该测度的正则性并引入了量子通道（quantum channels）的乘性本原性（multiplicative primitivity）新概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子轨迹（quantum trajectories）作为建模量子系统受重复间接测量的马尔可夫链，其稳态机制取决于探针可观测量的选择。本文旨在探索当探针可观测量选择被随机化时量子轨迹的性质，研究随机化如何影响量子轨迹的规律性。

Method: 研究通过引入探针可观测量选择的随机化来正则化量子轨迹，证明了非奇异随机化确保量子轨迹纯化并存在唯一不变概率测度。同时引入了量子通道（quantum channels）的乘性本原性（multiplicative primitivity）新概念，该概念强于本原性但弱于正改进性（positivity improving）。

Result: 研究结果表明非奇异随机化确保量子轨迹纯化并接受唯一不变概率测度。通过引入乘性本原性概念，进一步研究了该不变测度的正则性。最后计算了典型量子通道的不变测度，并通过多个示例探讨了假设的局限性。

Conclusion: 探针可观测量选择的随机化能够正则化量子轨迹，非奇异随机化确保量子轨迹纯化并存在唯一不变概率测度。引入的乘性本原性概念为研究量子通道的遍历性（ergodicity）提供了新工具，并通过示例展示了理论假设的适用范围。

Abstract: Quantum trajectories are Markov chains modeling quantum systems subjected to repeated indirect measurements. Their stationary regime depends on what observables are measured on the probes used to indirectly measure the system. In this article we explore the properties of quantum trajectories when the choice of probe observable is randomized. The randomization induces some regularization of the quantum trajectories. We show that non-singular randomization ensures that quantum trajectories purify and therefore accept a unique invariant probability measure. We furthermore study the regularity of that invariant measure. In that endeavour, we introduce a new notion of ergodicity for quantum channels, which we call multiplicative primitivity. It is a priory stronger than primitivity but weaker than positivity improving. Finally, we compute some invariant measures for canonical quantum channels and explore the limits of our assumptions with several examples.

*Mehrab Mahdian,Ferenc Ender,Tamas Pardy*

TL;DR: 该研究开发了Electrospinning-Data.org平台，一个FAIR原则对齐的数据聚合基础设施，用于整理分散的静电纺丝实验数据，创建结构化、可重用且包含失败实验的科学记录，以支持数据驱动研究。

Method: 研究引入了Electrospinning-Data.org平台，采用FAIR原则对齐的数据聚合基础设施，围绕统一的过程-结构-性能（process-structure-property）数据模型组织分散的实验数据。该模型通过受控词汇表（controlled vocabulary）在一致的机器可读模式（machine-readable schema）中连接实验输入、环境条件和纳米纤维形态。采用结合自动验证与专家评审的两阶段审核流程（two-stage moderation pipeline）确保数据质量和长期互操作性。

Result: 平台创建了结构化、包含失败实验的数据集（failure-inclusive corpus），为数据驱动研究提供了框架。这支持预测建模、目标形态的逆向设计（inverse design），以及系统映射不稳定性区域（instability regimes），这些原本需要大量试错实验才能实现。

Conclusion: Electrospinning-Data.org平台通过整合分散的静电纺丝实验数据，解决了该领域数据碎片化和报告不一致的问题，为数据驱动的静电纺丝研究提供了基础设施，有望减少试错实验需求并促进可重复性研究。

Abstract: Electrospinning is a versatile nanofabrication technique whose outcomes emerge from a complex, high-dimensional interplay between solution properties, processing parameters, and environmental conditions. Optimizing this parameter space for targeted fiber morphology is inherently challenging, often driving extensive trial-and-error experimentation and generating vast experimental data across laboratories worldwide. Yet this knowledge remains fragmented and underutilized due to inconsistent reporting and a pervasive bias toward successful outcomes, limiting reproducibility and hindering data-driven research. Here we introduce Electrospinning-Data.org, a FAIR-aligned data aggregation infrastructure that organizes dispersed electrospinning experiments into structured, reusable, and failure-aware scientific records. The platform is built around a unified process-structure-property data model linking experimental inputs, environmental conditions, and nanofiber morphology, annotated through a controlled vocabulary, within a consistent, machine-readable schema. A two-stage moderation pipeline combining automated validation with expert review supports data quality and long-term interoperability. The resulting structured, failure-inclusive corpus provides a framework for data-driven research, including predictive modelling, inverse design of target morphologies, and systematic mapping of instability regimes that would otherwise require extensive trial-and-error experimentation.

Result: 伪费米子方法能够高效且高精度地推断均匀电子气的能量，完全避免了费米子符号问题。在强量子简并区域（33个自旋极化电子，密度参数r_s=0.5），该方法与精确CPIMC结果的相对偏差仅为0.6%。特别地，该方法填补了CPIMC和RPIMC都无法准确模拟的空白区域（1≤r_s≤2，约化温度θ=0.0625）。

Abstract: For strongly quantum-degenerate systems at finite temperatures, the fermion sign problem remains the major obstacle to first-principles simulations. In this work, we apply the recently proposed pseudo-fermion method - designed to overcome the sign problem - to strongly quantum-degenerate uniform electron gases. We find that the pseudo-fermion method can efficiently and highly accurately infer the energy of the uniform electron gas while being free from the fermion sign problem. For example, in the strongly quantum-degenerate regime where RPIMC fails (33 spin-polarized electrons at the density parameter $r_s = 0.5$), the relative deviation between the pseudo-fermion method and the exact CPIMC result is only 0.6%. In particular, the pseudo-fermion method bridges the gap where neither CPIMC nor RPIMC can accurately simulate the regime $1 \le r_s \le 2$ at the reduced temperature $θ= 0.0625$. This work demonstrates that the pseudo-fermion method opens a new pathway for studying strongly quantum-degenerate systems in a sign-problem-free manner.

Starting from SMILES representations for monomers, ADEPT automates the construction of atomistic models and the evaluation of their properties using molecular dynamics simulations and density functional theory calculations. The simulation data are combined with curated experimental data and group contribution theory estimates to construct a unified dataset of approximately 62,000 polymer property values spanning 28 properties. Using this dataset, inter-property correlations are analyzed, and multi-task learning strategies are evaluated for joint property prediction.   <summary>Details</summary>

Here we demonstrate controlled suppression of nuclear-bath-induced decoherence in photoexcited triplet spins of pentacene co-crystallized in high-purity naphthalene single crystals. By hyperpolarizing the proton spin bath through triplet dynamic nuclear polarization (triplet-DNP), magnetic noise generated by the nuclear spins is suppressed, leading to an extension of the electron spin transverse coherence time. Experimentally, we observe a 25\% enhancement of the spin-echo decay time with $60\%$ polarization of the proton spin bath. The measured scaling of the spin-echo decay time ($T_2$) with nuclear polarization quantitatively follows the predicted dependence derived from the polarization-controlled nuclear second moment. Both the enhancement and the absolute value of the coherence time are quantitatively reproduced by cluster correlation expansion (CCE) simulations. These results establish nuclear spin hyperpolarization as a general and actively tunable approach to engineering coherence in molecular qubits. This work provides a broadly applicable design framework for high-coherence molecular and solid-state spin systems.

*Michele Ceriotti,David E. Manolopoulos,Thomas E. Markland,Mariana Rossi*

Method: 采用路径积分方法（path integral methods）作为核心框架，结合基础理论阐述和最新模拟技术介绍，构建自包含的教学体系。

Result: 本书提供了完整的路径积分方法教学资源，系统性地介绍了该方法在原子过程建模中的应用，涵盖了从基础理论到前沿模拟技术的全面内容。

Abstract: This book provides an introduction to path integral methods and their application to modeling atomistic processes. ### [269] [Hunting for quantum advantage in electronic structure calculations is a highly non-trivial task](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28648)
*Örs Legeza,Andor Menczer,Miklós Antal Werner,Sotiris S. Xantheas,Frank Neese,Martin Ganahl,Cole Brower,Samuel Rodriguez Bernabeu,Jeff Hammond,John Gunnels*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过混合精度自旋适应从头算密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）方法，在经典GPU硬件上实现了对铁硫簇分子体系（Fe₄S₄和Fe₅S₁₂H₄⁵⁻）的高精度基态能量计算，为量子优势（quantum advantage）的验证提供了必要的经典基准数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子计算与经典硬件模拟的快速发展使得识别真正展现量子优势（quantum advantage）的实际问题成为严峻挑战。在量子化学中，强关联（多参考）电子结构计算常被认为是此类问题，因为基于平均场理论（mean-field theory）的标准方法难以处理。因此，为竞争性发展方向提供最先进的经典算法基准数据至关重要。

Method: 采用混合精度自旋适应从头算密度矩阵重整化群（Density Matrix Renormalization Group, DMRG）电子结构计算方法，与ORCA程序包接口，并利用NVIDIA Blackwell图形处理单元（GPU）平台。对Fe₄S₄分子簇在CAS(54,36)模型空间进行计算，并对Fe₅S₁₂H₄⁵⁻分子体系进行基于CAS-SCF的轨道优化，达到前所未有的CAS(89,102)规模。

Result: 获得了Fe₄S₄分子簇在CAS(54,36)模型空间的高精度基态能量和最先进的性能结果。进一步突破了极限，对包含25个开壳层轨道的Fe₅S₁₂H₄⁵⁻分子体系实现了CAS(89,102)规模的轨道优化，其活性空间尺寸达到331个电子在451个轨道。

Conclusion: DMRG基准数据应作为报告量子优势时的经典参考标准。此外，应充分考虑经典硬件的全面利用，因为即使最先进的DMRG实现在利用GPU技术优势方面仍处于不成熟阶段。

Abstract: In light of major developments over the past decades in both quantum computing and simulations on classical hardware, it is a serious challenge to identify a real-world problem where quantum advantage is expected to appear. In quantum chemistry, electronic structure calculations of strongly correlated, i.e. multi-reference problems, are often argued to fall into such category because of their intractability with standard methods based on mean-field theory. Therefore, providing state-of-the-art benchmark data by classical algorithms is necessary to make a decisive conclusion when such competing development directions are compared. We report cutting-edge performance results together with high accuracy ground state energy for the Fe$_4$S$_4$ molecular cluster on a CAS(54,36) model space, a problem that has been included quite recently among the list of systems in the {\it Quantum Advantage Tracker} webpage maintained by IBM and RIKEN. Pushing the limits even further, we also present CAS-SCF based orbital optimizations for unprecedented CAS sizes of up to 89 electrons in 102 orbitals [CAS(89,102)] for the Fe$_5$S$_{12}$H$_4^{5-}$ molecular system comprising twenty five open shell orbitals in its sextet ground state and an active spaces size of 331 electrons in 451 orbitals. We have achieved our results via mixed-precision spin-adapted \textit{ab initio} Density Matrix Renormalization Group (DMRG) electronic structure calculations interfaced with the ORCA program package and utilizing the NVIDIA Blackwell graphics processing unit (GPU) platform. We argue that DMRG benchmark data should be taken as a classical reference when quantum advantage is reported. In addition, full exploitation of classical hardware should also be considered since even the most advanced DMRG implementations are still in a premature stage regarding utilization of all the benefits of GPU technology.

</details>

### [270] [When can fitness epistasis be ignored in a polygenic trait at equilibrium?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27255)
*Archana Devi,Kavita Jain*

Main category: q-bio.PE

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了多基因性状（polygenic trait）中，在稳定化选择（stabilizing selection）和表型上位性（epistasis）作用下，等位基因频率（allele frequency）的分布行为。研究发现，虽然上位性相互作用对表型量的影响可能不明显，但会显著影响等位基因频率分布。此外，等位基因效应大小（effect size）决定其频率分布是单峰（unimodal）还是双峰（bimodal）模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管许多表型性状由大量遗传变异决定，但多基因性状中等位基因频率的行为尚未被完全理解。当所关注的定量性状（quantitative trait）受到上位性选择（epistatic selection）时，问题尤其具有挑战性，因为一个位点的等位基因频率会受到其他位点的影响。

Method: 研究考虑了一个随机交配（panmictic）、二倍体（diploid）的有限种群，在稳定化选择和对称突变（symmetric mutations）作用下进化，且种群处于连锁平衡（linkage equilibrium）状态。在稳态下，使用扩散理论（diffusion theory）计算等位基因频率的边缘分布（marginal distribution）。

Result: 研究发现存在某些参数区间，其中为了准确描述频率分布，不能忽略适应度上位性（fitness epistasis）。然而，即使忽略上位性相互作用，表型最优值的平均偏差（mean deviation）和基因方差（genic variance）也能被很好地捕捉。此外，一个位点的等位基因频率分布在其效应大小低于阈值时为单峰，否则为双峰，这是确定性结果（deterministic results）的随机类比。

Conclusion: 虽然上位性的存在可能在表型量中不明显，但它能强烈影响等位基因频率分布。等位基因频率分布的模式（单峰或双峰）由其效应大小是否超过阈值决定。分析结果通过蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）和朗之万方程（Langevin equation）的数值积分得到了验证。

Abstract: Although many phenotypic traits are determined by a large number of genetic variants, the behavior of allele frequencies in a polygenic trait is not completely understood. The problem is especially challenging when the quantitative trait of interest is under epistatic selection as the allele frequency at a locus is affected by those at other loci. Here, we consider a panmictic, diploid finite population evolving under stabilizing selection and symmetric mutations when the population is in linkage equilibrium. In the stationary state, using a diffusion theory, we calculate the marginal distribution of allele frequency, and find parameter regimes where fitness epistasis can not be ignored for an accurate description of the frequency distribution. For such parameters, the mean deviation in the phenotypic optimum and genic variance are, however, found to be well captured even when epistatic interactions are neglected. Thus, while the presence of epistasis may not be evident in phenotypic quantities, it can strongly affect the allele frequency distribution.We also find that the allele frequency distribution at a locus is unimodal if its effect size is below a threshold effect and bimodal otherwise; these results are the stochastic analog of the deterministic ones where the stable allele frequency becomes bistable when the effect size exceeds a threshold. Our analytical results are verified against Monte Carlo simulations and numerical integration of a Langevin equation.

</details>

### [271] [Persistence diagrams of random matrices via Morse theory: universality and a new spectral diagnostic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27903)
*Matthew Loftus*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 该论文证明对称矩阵M的二次型在单位球面上的子水平集过滤的持久图（persistence diagram）由M的特征值解析确定，并将随机矩阵理论（RMT）的普适性转移到持久图普适性，建立了持久熵作为优于传统谱诊断工具的新指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立对称矩阵二次型在单位球面上的拓扑特征与其谱特性之间的解析联系，并将随机矩阵理论的普适性概念扩展到持久同伦（persistent homology）领域，为谱分析提供新的拓扑诊断工具。

Method: 通过莫尔斯理论（Morse theory）分析二次型f(x)=x^TMx在单位球面S^{n-1}上的子水平集过滤（sublevel set filtration），证明持久图由矩阵特征值完全确定。利用高斯正交系综（Gaussian Orthogonal Ensemble, GOE）等随机矩阵系综进行数值验证和统计分析。

Result: 持久图包含n-1个有限条带（finite bars），第k个条带位于同调维度k-1，长度等于第k个特征值间距s_k=λ_{k+1}-λ_k。对于GOE矩阵，推导出闭合形式的持久熵（persistence entropy）PE=log(8n/π)-1，并发现持久统计量的变异系数以n^{-0.6}衰减。不同随机矩阵系综（GOE、GUE、Wishart）产生不同的普适持久图。

Conclusion: 持久熵在区分GOE与GUE矩阵方面优于标准水平间距比⟨r⟩（AUC 0.978 vs 0.952），并能检测Rosenzweig-Porter模型中的全局谱扰动，而⟨r⟩对此不敏感。这些结果确立了持久熵作为捕获现有RMT工具互补信息的新谱诊断指标。

Abstract: We prove that the persistence diagram of the sublevel set filtration of the quadratic form f(x) = x^T M x restricted to the unit sphere S^{n-1} is analytically determined by the eigenvalues of the symmetric matrix M. By Morse theory, the diagram has exactly n-1 finite bars, with the k-th bar living in homological dimension k-1 and having length equal to the k-th eigenvalue spacing s_k = λ_{k+1} - λ_k. This identification transfers random matrix theory (RMT) universality to persistence diagram universality: for matrices drawn from the Gaussian Orthogonal Ensemble (GOE), we derive the closed-form persistence entropy PE = log(8n/π) - 1, and verify numerically that the coefficient of variation of persistence statistics decays as n^{-0.6}. Different random matrix ensembles (GOE, GUE, Wishart) produce distinct universal persistence diagrams, providing topological fingerprints of RMT universality classes. As a practical consequence, we show that persistence entropy outperforms the standard level spacing ratio \langle r \rangle for discriminating GOE from GUE matrices (AUC 0.978 vs. 0.952 at n = 100, non-overlapping bootstrap 95% CIs), and detects global spectral perturbations in the Rosenzweig-Porter model to which \langle r \rangle is blind. These results establish persistence entropy as a new spectral diagnostic that captures complementary information to existing RMT tools.

</details>

### [272] [Contrastive learning in tunable dynamical systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26969)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将监督对比学习理论从平衡态或稳态物理系统推广到任意动力学系统，特别是那些由耦合常微分方程描述的系统，以解决在时间反演对称性破缺条件下训练可扩展物理模型的问题。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）理论分析显示时间反演对称性破缺时梯度下降的可扩展性限制；2）提出概率近似正确学习过程，该过程由局部对比学习规则和可扩展监督协议组成；3）采用近似局部监督与误差信号前向传播相结合的训练方法。

Result: 研究结果表明：1）当物理动力学破坏时间反演对称性时，基于期望行为的成本函数梯度下降无法通过可扩展过程实现；2）概率近似正确学习过程能够成功训练多个受生物和机器学习启发的可调物理动力学模型。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将监督对比学习扩展到任意动力学系统，提出了解决时间反演对称性破缺条件下训练可扩展性问题的概率近似正确学习框架，为生物和机器学习中的物理模型训练提供了新方法。

Abstract: We generalize the theory of supervised contrastive learning, previously applied to physical systems at equilibrium or steady state, to systems following any dynamics described by coupled ordinary differential equations. We show that if physical dynamics break time reversal symmetry, gradient descent on a cost function embodying the desired behavior cannot be achieved with a scalable process, even in principle. We therefore introduce Probably Approximately Right (PAR) learning processes, composed of a local contrastive learning rule and a scalable supervision protocol. We show that approximate, local supervision with forward propagation of the error signal can be used to successfully train several tunable models of physical dynamics inspired by examples in biological and machine learning.

### [273] [Skin-Anderson localization transitions in disordered hybrid-nonreciprocal systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27069)
*C. Wang,X. R. Wang,Hechen Ren*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文报告了在混合非互易系统中发现的皮肤-安德森局域化转变，揭示了非厄米趋肤效应与安德森局域化之间的相互作用导致的新型相变现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安德森局域化（Anderson localization）转变是一种普遍的波现象，表现为无序诱导的从扩展态到局域态的量子相变；而非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect）是非厄米系统的普遍特征，导致体态在边界局域。本研究旨在探索这两种现象在混合非互易系统中的相互作用。

Method: 研究聚焦于在混合非互易系统中，该系统在不同空间方向上同时表现出互易性和非互易性。通过分析无序强度变化对系统状态的影响，揭示了两种不同的相变过程。

Result: 在弱无序区域，系统呈现边界扩展态（boundary-extended states），即在互易维度扩展而在非互易维度边界局域。随着无序增强，这些状态在临界无序强度处转变为边界局域态（boundary-localized states）。该临界点展现出与厄米安德森转变相似的普适特性，包括在数值误差内相同的临界指数。当无序超过更高临界阈值时，发生第二次转变，边界局域态转变为体局域态，从而消除非厄米趋肤效应。

Conclusion: 皮肤-安德森局域化转变（skin-Anderson localization transition）建立了一个新的框架，通过统一安德森转变物理与非厄米拓扑学，实现了对状态局域化的控制。

Abstract: Anderson (localization) transition is a universal wave phenomenon characterized by a disorder-induced quantum phase transition from extended to localized states, whereas the non-Hermitian skin effect is a generic feature of non-Hermitian systems that causes bulk states to localize at the boundaries. Here, we report an unexpected skin-Anderson localization transition arising from the interplay between these two phenomena in hybrid-nonreciprocal systems that exhibit both reciprocity and nonreciprocity in different spatial directions. In the weak-disorder regime, the states are boundary-extended, meaning they are extended in reciprocal spatial dimensions but localized at the boundaries in nonreciprocal dimensions due to the non-Hermitian skin effect. As disorder increases, these boundary-extended states transition to boundary-localized states at a critical disorder strength. Remarkably, the corresponding critical points exhibit universal characteristics akin to those of the Anderson transition in its Hermitian counterpart, including identical critical exponents within numerical errors. When disorder exceeds a higher critical threshold, a second transition occurs in which boundary-localized states become bulk-localized, thereby eliminating the non-Hermitian skin effect. Thus, the skin-Anderson localization transition establishes a new framework for controlling state localization by unifying the physics of Anderson transitions with non-Hermitian topology.

</details>


### [274] [Magnetic doping-induced second-order and first-order topological phase transition inthe photonic alloy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27924)
*Xianbin Wu,Tiantao Qu,Xiaoxuan Shi,Lei Zhang,Jun Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究在二维光子合金中实现了从二阶拓扑相到一阶拓扑相的可控相变，通过调节磁性掺杂浓度，在单个系统中灵活切换局域角态与手性边缘态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然周期性系统中不同拓扑相之间的转变已被证实，但在无序平台中这种转变的存在性仍是一个开放问题。本研究旨在探索二维光子合金中二阶拓扑相与一阶拓扑相之间的可控相变。

Method: 通过调节磁性掺杂浓度实现拓扑控制，具体方法是在具有C3旋转对称性的交替磁化蜂窝晶格中，将永磁体随机附着到非磁化钇铁石榴石棒上。通过改变掺杂浓度来调控系统拓扑性质。

Result: 零掺杂时观察到高阶角态，具有平庸陈数（Chern number）和非零体极化（bulk polarization）1/3。随着掺杂增加，角态逐渐与体态融合，体传输带隙闭合后重新打开，系统转变为具有非平庸陈数-1的一阶拓扑相，出现手性边缘态（chiral edge state）。

Conclusion: 该相变是可逆的，为在单个光子系统中灵活切换局域角态与离域手性边缘态提供了一个高度可调且实验简单的平台。

Abstract: The bulk-edge correspondence principle, a cornerstone of topological physics, ensures that first-order topological systems host robust chiral edge states in two dimension. This was later extended to higher-order phases, where second-order topological insulators exhibit localized, topologically protected corner states. While the transition between these distinct phases has been demonstrated in periodic systems, its existence in disordered platforms remains an open question. Here, we demonstrate a controllable topological phase transition between a second-order topological phase and a first-order topological phase in a two-dimensional photonic alloy. By tuning the magnetic doping concentration - implemented by attaching permanent magnets randomly to nonmagnetized yttrium iron garnet rods in an alternately magnetized honeycomb lattice with C3 rotational symmetry - we flexibly control the system's topology. At zero doping, we observe higher-order corner states, confirmed by a trivial Chern number and non-zero bulk polarizations of 1/3. As doping concentration increases, these corner states progressively merge with the bulk states, culminating in the closure of the bulk transmission gap. After the bulk transmission gap reopens with further increased doping, the system transitions to a first-order topological phase, characterized by a nontrivial Chern number of -1 and the emergence of a chiral edge state. This transition is reversible, providing a highly tunable and experimentally simple platform for flexibly switching between localized corner states and delocalized chiral edge states within a single photonic system.

</details>


### [275] [Exact Skin Critical Phase and Configurable Fractal Wavefunctions via Imaginary Gauge Phase Imprint in Non-Hermitian Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28153)
*Ji-Long Dong,Shi-Liang Zhu,Dan-Wei Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种称为"虚规范相位印记（imaginary gauge phase imprint）"的通用框架，用于在任意维度的非厄米晶格中精确设计波函数。该方法揭示了一种新的皮肤临界相（skin critical phase, SCP），其特征是宏观多重分形分布和拓扑相关的边界模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成复杂状态如多重分形临界态（multifractal critical states）在经典和量子物理中一直是一个突出挑战。需要开发新的方法来精确设计非厄米系统中的波函数。

Method: 提出了虚规范相位印记（imaginary gauge phase imprint）的通用框架，允许在任意维度的非厄米晶格中工程化精确波函数。该方法用于在一维和二维系统中揭示新的皮肤临界相（skin critical phase, SCP）。

Result: 发现了一种新的皮肤临界相（SCP），其特征是宏观多重分形分布，所有临界本征态共享相同的轮廓，并在周期边界条件下积累在特定的体界面。该方法还成功在更高维度中印记了可配置波函数，包括非分形晶格中的Sierpinski地毯和Koch雪花轮廓的复杂分形态，以及非Moire晶格中的Moire态。

Conclusion: 该工作不仅为分形现象和临界相提供了新的见解，还为工程化非厄米系统中的波操纵提供了严格的范式。皮肤临界相表现出与传统临界相不同的弹道动力学行为，而非扩散行为。

Abstract: The generation of complex states like multifractal critical states has been an outstanding challenge in both classical and quantum physics. Here we propose a general framework, termed the imaginary gauge phase imprint, allowing to engineer rigorous wavefunctions in any-dimensional non-Hermitian lattices. Using this method, we uncover a novel phase with exact critical wavefunctions in one (and two) dimension, dubbed the skin critical phase (SCP). Unlike conventional critical phases with overall uniform density distributions and non-Hermitian skin effect with eigenstate accumulation at open boundaries, the SCP is marked by a macroscopically multifractal distribution with all critical eigenstates sharing an identical profile and always accumulating at specific bulk interfaces under periodic boundary condition, which become topology-dependent boundary or interface skin modes under open boundary condition. We also show the ballistic dynamics in the SCP, in contrast to the diffusive behaviour in conventional critical phases. Moreover, we validate our method by imprinting configurable wavefunctions in higher dimensions, including complex fractal states with Sierpinski-carpet and Koch-snowflake profiles in non-fractal lattices and Moire states in non-Moire lattices. Our work not only offers fresh insights into fractal phenomena and critical phases, but also provides a rigorous paradigm for wave manipulations in engineered non-Hermitian systems.

</details>


### [276] [Will a time-varying complex system be stable?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28464)
*Francesco Ferraro,Christian Grilletta,Amos Maritan,Samir Suweis,Sandro Azaele*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究将经典的复杂性-稳定性理论（complexity-stability theory）推广到具有时变相互作用的动态系统，发现时间变异性（temporal variability）能够系统性提升系统稳定性，使复杂系统即使在其瞬时雅可比矩阵（instantaneous Jacobian）预测不稳定的情况下仍能保持稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: May的理论预测随机组装的动态系统在复杂性超过临界阈值时会变得不稳定，但经验观察到的复杂系统却表现出显著稳定性。传统复杂性-稳定性关系通常假设固定相互作用，而真实系统往往处于内在时变状态，需要理解这种时变性如何影响稳定性。

Method: 将一般非自治动力学（non-autonomous dynamics）在参考运行状态附近线性化，并将所得参数建模为随机过程（stochastic processes），这是将静态随机相互作用扩展到时变相互作用的最小扩展。通过推导精确的稳定性边界，将复杂性-稳定性理论推广到动态变化系统。

Result: 研究发现时间变异性允许系统在其瞬时雅可比矩阵预测不稳定的情况下仍能保持稳定。在非线性神经网络模型中理论精确适用，在广义Lotka-Volterra方程中数值发现时变相互作用系统性推迟了副本对称性破缺（replica-symmetry breaking）的发生。

Conclusion: 时间变异性系统性改善稳定性，展示了一种使复杂系统能够违反经典复杂性-稳定性边界的通用机制。该研究为理解经验观察到的复杂系统稳定性提供了理论框架，超越了传统静态相互作用假设的限制。

Abstract: Randomly-assembled dynamical systems are theoretically predicted to be unstable upon crossing a critical threshold of complexity, as first shown by May. Yet, empirical complex systems exhibit remarkable stability, indicating the presence of additional mechanisms playing a stabilizing role. The relation between complexity and stability is typically assessed by assuming fixed interactions, whereas real systems often evolve in intrinsically time-dependent states. To understand how this affects stability, we linearize a general non-autonomous dynamics around a reference operating state and model the resulting parameters as stochastic processes, which represent the minimal extension of static random interactions to time-varying ones. We derive exact stability bounds that generalize complexity-stability theory to dynamically varying systems. Notably, we find that temporal variability allows systems to remain stable even when their instantaneous Jacobian would predict instability. We compare our results against a non-linear neural network model, where our theory applies exactly, and the generalized Lotka-Volterra equations, where we numerically find that time-varying interactions systematically postpone the onset of replica-symmetry breaking. Overall, our results indicate that temporal variability systematically improves stability, demonstrating a general mechanism by which complex systems can violate classical complexity-stability bounds.

</details>


### [277] [Uncovering the Microscopic Mechanism of Slow Dynamics in Quasiperiodic Many-Body Localized Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28721)
*Bernard Faulend,Hrvoje Buljan,Antonio Štrkalj*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了一维准周期多体局域化（MBL）系统中的数熵和准粒子宽度，揭示了与随机系统不同的结构化慢动力学特征，并建立了基于量子振幅调制的解析模型来解释这些现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索准周期多体局域化系统中的慢动力学行为，这类现象先前主要在随机系统中被详细研究。研究者希望理解准周期系统与随机系统在动力学特征上的差异及其背后的物理机制。

Method: 研究方法包括分析一维准周期多体局域化系统中的数熵（number entropy）和准粒子宽度（quasiparticle width）演化。研究者识别了单粒子跃迁的拉比振荡振幅调制作为慢增长机制，并基于此机制建立了能够解释所有可及时间尺度动力学的解析模型。

Result: 研究发现准周期系统表现出比随机系统更结构化的可观测量增长模式。即使在深度多体局域化区域，量子振幅调制和相关的拍频现象仍能驱动慢动力学，且该机制不随粒子间距增加而减弱。建立的解析模型成功解释了观测到的动力学行为。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明量子振幅调制是多体量子系统中慢动力学的普适机制，该机制源于链中不同位置单粒子跃迁过程的相互作用。研究结果支持多体局域化相在热力学极限下的稳定性。

Abstract: We study the number entropy and quasiparticle width in one-dimensional quasiperiodic many-body localized (MBL) systems and observe slow dynamics that have previously been investigated in detail only in random systems. In contrast, quasiperiodic systems exhibit more structured growth of both observables. We identify the modulation of the Rabi oscillation amplitude of single-particle hoppings as the mechanism underlying the slow growth even deep in the MBL regime. This quantum amplitude modulation and associated beats arise from the interaction between single-particle hopping processes at different positions in the chain. Interestingly, this mechanism is not weakened by increasing the distance between particles and is generic to many-body quantum systems. We develop an analytical model based on the aforementioned mechanism that explains the observed dynamics at all accessible timescales and provides a microscopic picture of the slow dynamics in the MBL regime. Our results are consistent with the stability of the MBL phase in the thermodynamic limit.

</details>

Method: 引入MoltenFlow框架，结合性质组织的潜在表示（property-organized latent representations）、流匹配生成先验（flow-matching generative priors）和基于梯度的引导（gradient-based guidance）。

We introduce MoltenFlow, a modular framework that combines property-organized latent representations with flow-matching generative priors and gradient-based guidance. This formulation supports both conditioned generation and local optimization within a single latent-space framework. We show that guided latent flows enable efficient multi-objective molecular optimization under fixed oracle budgets with controllable trade-offs, while a learned flow prior improves unconditional generation quality.

### [279] [Hierarchy-Guided Topology Latent Flow for Molecular Graph Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27113)
*Urvi Awasthi,Alexander Arjun Lobo,Leonid Zhukov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HLTF（Hierarchy-Guided Latent Topology Flow）提出了一种分层引导的潜在拓扑流方法，通过规划器-执行器模型生成具有三维坐标的键合图，显著提高了药物分子生成的化学有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维分子生成面临离散键合拓扑的挑战：局部键合误差会导致全局失效（价态违规、断开连接、不合理环结构），特别是在具有长程约束的药物分子中。现有无条件三维生成器通常先强调坐标再推断键合或依赖后处理，导致拓扑可行性控制较弱。

Method: 提出Hierarchy-Guided Latent Topology Flow（HLTF），采用规划器-执行器模型生成具有三维坐标的键合图。该方法使用潜在多尺度规划提供全局上下文，并通过约束感知采样器抑制拓扑驱动的失效。

Result: 在QM9数据集上，HLTF达到98.8%的原子稳定性和92.9%的有效且唯一性，将PoseBusters有效性提升至94.0%（比最强基线提高0.9%）。在GEOM-DRUGS数据集上，无需后处理获得85.5%/85.0%的有效性/有效-唯一-新颖性，经过标准化弛豫后达到92.2%/91.2%，与最佳后处理基线相差仅0.9个百分点。显式拓扑生成还减少了通过RDKit净化但无法通过更严格检查的"假有效"样本。

Conclusion: HLTF通过显式生成键合拓扑并采用分层引导的潜在规划，有效解决了三维分子生成中的拓扑可行性问题，显著提高了化学有效性，特别是在药物分子生成任务中表现出色。

Abstract: Generating chemically valid 3D molecules is hindered by discrete bond topology: small local bond errors can cause global failures (valence violations, disconnections, implausible rings), especially for drug-like molecules with long-range constraints. Many unconditional 3D generators emphasize coordinates and then infer bonds or rely on post-processing, leaving topology feasibility weakly controlled. We propose Hierarchy-Guided Latent Topology Flow (HLTF), a planner-executor model that generates bond graphs with 3D coordinates, using a latent multi-scale plan for global context and a constraint-aware sampler to suppress topology-driven failures. On QM9, HLTF achieves 98.8% atom stability and 92.9% valid-and-unique, improving PoseBusters validity to 94.0% (+0.9 over the strongest reported baseline). On GEOM-DRUGS, HLTF attains 85.5%/85.0% validity/valid-unique-novel without post-processing and 92.2%/91.2% after standardized relaxation, within 0.9 points of the best post-processed baseline. Explicit topology generation also reduces "false-valid" samples that pass RDKit sanitization but fail stricter checks.

### [280] [On the critical fugacity of the hard-core model on regular bipartite graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27144)
*Daniel Hadas,Ron Peled*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文证明了在有限正则二分图上，当逸度（fugacity）超过由图扩展参数确定的阈值时，硬核模型（hard-core model）存在长程有序（long-range order）。结果适用于d维超立方图及固定边长的d维离散环面，并利用反射正性（reflection positivity）将结论推广到$\mathbb{Z}^{d}$格点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究硬核模型在有限正则二分图上的长程有序现象，旨在确定临界逸度（critical fugacity）的渐近行为。特别关注高维情况下临界逸度的精确形式，验证长期以来关于$\mathbb{Z}^{d}$格点临界逸度为$d^{-1+o(1)}$的猜想。

Method: 基于图的扩展参数（expansion parameters）建立逸度阈值条件，证明硬核模型在有限正则二分图上的长程有序。运用反射正性（reflection positivity）方法将有限图的结果转移到无限格点$\mathbb{Z}^{d}$上。

Result: 对于d维超立方图和固定边长的d维离散环面，当逸度满足$λ\geΩ(\frac{\log d}{d})$时存在长程有序。在$\mathbb{Z}^{d}$格点上验证了临界逸度具有$d^{-1+o(1)}$的渐近形式，证实了长期以来的理论预期。

Conclusion: 该研究成功建立了硬核模型在有限正则二分图上的长程有序条件，并将结果推广到$\mathbb{Z}^{d}$格点，为高维硬核模型的相变行为提供了严格的理论证明，解决了临界逸度渐近形式的重要问题。

Abstract: We establish long-range order for the hard-core model on a finite, regular bipartite graph above a threshold fugacity given in terms of expansion parameters of the graph. The result applies to the $d$-dimensional hypercube graph and, more generally, to $d$-dimensional discrete tori of fixed side length, proving long-range order at fugacities $λ\geΩ(\frac{\log d}{d})$. Furthermore, we use reflection positivity to transfer the result to the lattice $\mathbb{Z}^{d}$, verifying the long-standing belief that its critical fugacity is of the form $d^{-1+o(1)}$ as $d\to\infty$.

</details>


### [281] [Marked GUE-corners process in doubly periodic dimer models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27906)
*Tomas Berggren,Nedialko Bradinoff*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了周期性加权的Aztec diamond二聚体模型在其转折点附近的渐近行为，发现其涨落经$\sqrt{N}$缩放后可由标记的GUE-corners过程描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究周期性加权的Aztec diamond二聚体模型（periodically weighted Aztec diamond dimer models）在转折点（turning points）附近的渐近行为，旨在理解这类模型在极限情况下的统计特性。

Method: 采用双重围道积分表示（double-contour integral representation）方法，在更高亏格黎曼曲面（higher-genus Riemann surface）上分析逆Kasteleyn矩阵（inverse Kasteleyn matrix），该方法特别适合进行渐近分析。

Result: 当$N\rightarrow\infty$时，模型在转折点附近的涨落经$\sqrt{N}$缩放后，渐近地由标记的GUE-corners过程（marked GUE-corners process）描述。该极限点过程通过对GUE-corners过程的每个粒子独立分配伯努利标记（Bernoulli mark）来构造。

Conclusion: 周期性加权Aztec diamond二聚体模型在转折点附近的渐近涨落可由标记的GUE-corners过程刻画，其中伯努利参数反映了模型在极限中的周期性特征。

Abstract: We study a family of periodically weighted Aztec diamond dimer models near their turning points. We establish that, asymptotically, as $N\rightarrow\infty$, their fluctuations there, scaled by $\sqrt{N}$, are described by a marked GUE-corners process. This limiting point process is constructed by assigning a Bernoulli mark independently to each particle in a realization of the GUE-corners process. The Bernoulli parameters associated with the random marks reflect the periodicity of the model in the limit. To prove this result we use a double-contour integral representation of the inverse Kasteleyn matrix on a higher-genus Riemann surface, which is well-suited for asymptotic analysis.

</details>


### [282] [Boundary four-point connectivities of conformal loop ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28161)
*Gefei Cai*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文推导了共形环系综（CLE）在κ∈(4,8)时的边界四点格林函数，特别针对κ=6和κ=16/3的情况，建立了临界伯努利渗流和FK-Ising模型中边界四点连通性的精确公式，验证了Gori-Viti的猜想，并识别了FK-Ising模型中的对数奇异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数学推导方法，首先推导出CLE在κ∈(4,8)时的边界四点格林函数（boundary four-point Green's functions），然后将结果特化到κ=6和κ=16/3的情况，分别对应临界伯努利渗流和FK-Ising模型。该方法还扩展应用于CLE的一体（one-bulk）和两边界（two-boundary）连通性。

Abstract: We derive the boundary four-point Green's functions for conformal loop ensembles (CLE) with $κ\in(4,8)$. Specializing to $κ=6$ and $κ=16/3$, we establish the exact formulas for the boundary four-point connectivities in critical Bernoulli percolation and the FK-Ising model conjectured by Gori-Viti (2017, 2018). In particular, we identify a logarithmic singularity in the critical FK-Ising model. Our approach also applies to the one-bulk and two-boundary connectivities of CLE, thereby extending the factorization formula of Beliaev-Izyurov (2012) to all $κ\in(4,8)$.

### [283] [The Supercritical Loop O(1) and Random Current models: Uniqueness and Mixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28520)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 证明了超立方晶格$\Z^d$上任意维度d≥2的超临界伊辛模型对应的loop O(1)和随机电流模型具有吉布斯测度（Gibbs measures）的唯一性和指数比率弱混合性（exponential ratio weak mixing）。

Conclusion: 结果可推广到q-流模型（q-flow models），并自然应用于$\Z/q\mathbb{Z}$-规范理论（gauge theories）的梯度测度（gradient measures）研究。

Abstract: Much recent rigorous study of the classical ferromagnetic Ising model has been powered by its graphical representations, such as the random current and loop O(1) model (high temperature expansion). The main technical innovation is to establish unique crossing events for conditional random-cluster measures by a delicate exploration coupling of Pisztora's coarse-graining method across scales. The results generalise to $q$-flow models and have natural applications for gradient measures of $\Z/q\mathbb{Z}$-gauge theories.

### [284] [The spectrum of the stochastic Bessel operator at high temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27602)
*Laure Dumaz,Hugo Magaldi*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了在高温极限下，β-Laguerre 系综的随机贝塞尔算符的缩放特征值点过程收敛于一个非平凡极限点过程，该过程由耦合扩散族描述，并利用扩散表征建立了最大特征值的大偏差渐近。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ramírez 和 Rider (2009) 已证明 β-Laguerre 系综的硬边（hard edge）在高维极限下收敛于随机贝塞尔算符（stochastic Bessel operator）的谱底。本文旨在研究该算符在高温极限（β→0）下的特征值点过程的极限行为。

Method: 采用随机分析工具，证明在高温极限下缩放特征值点过程收敛于非平凡极限点过程。该极限过程由耦合扩散族描述，并利用扩散表征来建立大偏差渐近结果。

Result: 证明了缩放特征值点过程收敛于一个非平凡极限点过程，该过程不同于泊松点过程，因其与硬边存在相互作用。建立了最大特征值的精确大偏差渐近，并对特定参数范围，将该极限过程与有限 n 的 β-Laguerre 系综联系起来。

Conclusion: 在高温极限下，随机贝塞尔算符的特征值点过程收敛于由耦合扩散描述的极限过程，该过程与硬边相互作用。作为分析副产品，提出了关于带常数漂移的反射布朗运动击中仿射线概率的显式积分公式猜想。

Abstract: Ramírez and Rider (2009) established that the hard edge of the spectrum of the $β$-Laguerre ensemble converges, in the high-dimensional limit, to the bottom of the spectrum of the stochastic Bessel operator. Using stochastic analysis tools, we prove that, in the high-temperature limit ($β\to 0$), the rescaled eigenvalue point process of this operator converges to a non-trivial limiting point process. This limit is characterized by a family of coupled diffusions and differs from a Poisson point process due to its interaction with the hard edge. Exploiting this diffusion characterization, we establish exact large deviation asymptotics for the largest eigenvalues. Furthermore, for an explicit range of the parameters, we relate this limiting process to the finite-$n$ $β$-Laguerre ensemble, conjecturing an exact distributional match with the infinite sum of its independent exponential gaps. As a byproduct of our analysis, we also formulate a conjecture regarding an explicit integral formula for the probability that a reflected Brownian motion with a constant drift hits an affine line, generalizing a formula of Salminen and Yor (2011).

### [285] [Hyperbolic Cluster States for Fault-Tolerant Measurement-Based Quantum Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27004)
*Ahmed Adel Mahmoud,Gabrielle Tournaire,Sven Bachmann,Steven Rayan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了双曲簇态（hyperbolic cluster state），这是三维簇态在负曲率几何中的推广，通过周期双曲晶格的叶状化构造。研究表明，在电路级去极化噪声模型下，双曲簇态具有与欧几里得RHG簇态相当的容错阈值，同时在热力学极限下支持恒定编码率，显著降低了量子比特开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于测量的量子计算（MBQC）中的容错资源态主要研究欧几里得晶格上的构造，特别是Raussendorf-Harrington-Goyal（RHG）构造。本研究旨在探索负曲率几何中的簇态，以改进量子比特开销并扩展容错量子计算的几何资源。

Method: 通过周期双曲晶格（periodic hyperbolic lattices）的叶状化（foliation）构造双曲簇态，并在电路级去极化噪声模型（circuit-level depolarizing noise model）下进行大规模数值模拟。通过内存实验（memory experiments）评估逻辑错误率和解码性能。

Result: 双曲簇态展现出与欧几里得RHG簇态相当的容错阈值（fault-tolerance threshold），同时在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下支持恒定编码率（constant encoding rate）。相对于传统簇态构造，这显著降低了量子比特开销（qubit overhead）。

Conclusion: 双曲几何为可扩展的容错MBQC提供了强大且实验相关的资源，并为在量子信息处理中利用负曲率（negative curvature）开辟了新途径。这些发现确立了双曲簇态在容错量子计算中的重要价值。

Abstract: Fault-tolerant measurement-based quantum computing (MBQC) provides a compelling framework for fault-tolerant quantum computation, in which quantum information is processed through single-qubit measurements on a three-dimensional entangled resource known as cluster state. To date, this resource has been predominantly studied on Euclidean lattices, most notably in the Raussendorf-Harrington-Goyal (RHG) construction, which underlies topological fault tolerance in MBQC. In this work, we introduce the hyperbolic cluster state, a generalization of the three-dimensional cluster state to negatively curved geometries, obtained via the foliation of periodic hyperbolic lattices. We present an explicit construction of hyperbolic cluster states and investigate their fault-tolerant properties under a realistic circuit-level depolarizing noise model. Using large-scale numerical simulations, we perform memory experiments to characterize their logical error rates and decoding performance. Our results demonstrate that hyperbolic cluster states exhibit a fault-tolerance threshold comparable to that of the Euclidean RHG cluster state, while simultaneously supporting a constant encoding rate in the thermodynamic limit. This represents a substantial improvement in qubit overhead relative to conventional cluster-state constructions. These findings establish hyperbolic geometry as a powerful and experimentally relevant resource for scalable, fault-tolerant MBQC and open new avenues for leveraging negative curvature in quantum information processing.

</details>

Result: 微扰能量级数被证明为Gevrey-1型且仅在穿过Stokes线后Borel可和（Borel summable）。瞬子算子提供了微扰系数与非微扰扇区之间的显式算符桥梁，重整化能量通过涉及该算符的期望值比值表示为跨级数（trans-series）。具体计算了前七个能级（n=0,...,6）到耦合常数g的六阶，得到的精确有理系数完全复现了经典的Bender-Wu结果。

Abstract: In this work, we study the resurgence program in holomorphic quantum mechanics. As a specific problem, we investigate the resurgence in the quartic anharmonic oscillator within holomorphic quantum mechanics, using the Bargmann representation of bosonic operators. In this framework, the perturbative energy series is shown to be Gevrey-1 and Borel summable only after continuation across the Stokes line. The instanton operator, realized as a coherent-state displacement in the Segal--Bargmann space, provides an explicit operatorial bridge between perturbative coefficients and non-perturbative sectors. Alien derivative relations generate the full resurgence triangle characteristic of the Bender--Wu model, and the resummed energy is expressed as a trans-series via a ratio of expectation values involving this instanton operator. As a concrete demonstration, we compute the first seven energy levels ($n=0,\dots,6$) up to sixth order in the coupling $g$; the resulting exact rational coefficients reproduce the classic Bender--Wu results, confirming the consistency and power of the holomorphic resurgence approach.

### [288] [Complementarity Beyond Definite Causal Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27780)
*Mohd Asad Siddiqui,Md Qutubuddin,Tabish Qureshi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在量子开关（quantum switch）等因果顺序相干叠加情形下，波粒二象性（wave-particle duality）如何被修正。研究发现不存在能同时捕捉路径可区分性、空间相干性和因果顺序相干性的普适线性互补关系，揭示了空间资源与因果资源的基本分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析量子开关框架下的因果顺序相干叠加，研究考察了路径可区分性（path distinguishability）、空间相干性（spatial coherence）与因果顺序相干性之间的关系。引入了因果相干性（causal coherence）作为量化替代因果顺序间干涉的操作可测量。

Result: 不存在能同时捕捉所有三个量的普适线性互补关系，揭示了空间资源与因果资源的基本分离。虽然追踪顺序量子比特（order qubit）可在约化量子-探测器态层面恢复标准对偶关系，但因果顺序相干性在该层面不可访问。研究构建了空间对偶饱和而因果相干性最大的显式过程。

Conclusion: 互补性从根本上由因果结构塑造，无法仅通过约化量子态层面完全捕捉。研究建立了基于因果自由度不相容测量的状态依赖熵表述，该表述源于普适不确定性原理，提供了规范的操作有意义描述。

Abstract: Wave--particle duality is a cornerstone of quantum mechanics, traditionally formulated under definite causal order. We investigate how complementarity is modified when the temporal order of operations is coherently superposed, as in the quantum switch. We show that no universal linear additive complementarity relation exists that simultaneously captures path distinguishability, spatial coherence, and coherence between causal orders. This reveals a fundamental separation between spatial and causal resources, which reside on different subsystems and are therefore not jointly constrained by a single quantum state. While tracing out the order qubit recovers the standard duality relation at the level of the reduced quanton--detector state, coherence between causal orders is not accessible at the level of the reduced description. To capture this contribution, we introduce \emph{causal coherence}, defined as the coherence of the order qubit, which quantifies interference between alternative causal orders and is operationally measurable; we construct explicit processes in which spatial duality is saturated while causal coherence is maximal. We further show that complementarity admits a state-dependent entropic formulation based on incompatible measurements on the causal degree of freedom; unlike generic state-dependent relations, this formulation arises from a universal uncertainty principle and provides a canonical operationally meaningful description. These results establish that complementarity is fundamentally shaped by causal structure and cannot, in general, be fully captured at the level of reduced quantum states alone.

Method: 研究方法采用量子场论（QFT）框架，并运用量子时间概率（QTP）方法，直接从QFT推导出一类用于到达时间可观测量（time-of-arrival observables）的正算子值测度（POVM）。

Abstract: We study the time-of-arrival problem for relativistic particles constrained to move on a ring, formulating the problem entirely within Quantum Field Theory (QFT). In contrast to its counterpart for motion in a line, the circle topology implies that particles may encounter the detector multiple times before detection, making a field-theoretic treatment of the measurement interaction essential. We employ the Quantum Temporal Probabilities (QTP) method to derive a class of Positive-Operator-Valued Measures (POVMs) for time-of-arrival observables directly from QFT. We analyze the resulting detection probabilities in both semiclassical and fully quantum regimes, identifying the relevant timescales and their dependence on the field-theoretic parameters. For ensembles of particles, the detection signal is a periodic function, providing a realization of a quantum clock whose operation reflects the local spacetime structure. We also extend the formalism to rotating rings and show that rotation induces additional noise in detection probabilities, interpretable as a manifestation of the rotational Unruh effect. Finally, we investigate multi-time measurements and demonstrate the emergence of non-classical temporal correlations due to entanglement.

Abstract: The time-energy uncertainty relation is often invoked as a heuristic explanation for virtual particles in interacting quantum field theories. In this work, we use a model in which virtual excitations associated with subcycle modes of a free scalar field can be converted with unit efficiency into real excitations of an idealized rapidly-switched harmonic-oscillator Unruh-DeWitt detector coupled to the conjugate field. Defining the time uncertainty as the effective duration of the detector-field interaction, we show that a time-energy uncertainty relation is satisfied in the deep subcycle regime. Our results provide concrete operational meaning to the textbook heuristic picture of virtual particles in quantum field theory in terms of the time-energy uncertainty principle.

Abstract: We develop a quantum description of the resonant interaction between electromagnetic (EM) and gravitational waves (GW). Within this framework, we identify multiple photon-graviton scattering channels, including photon up- and down-conversion and photon creation. In the semiclassical limit of the trilinear interaction where GW acts as a classical pump and the EM field is in a vacuum, spontaneous parametric photon amplification and two-mode squeezing occur. ### [292] [Discriminating idempotent quantum channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28582)
*Satvik Singh,Bjarne Bergh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了幂等量子通道（idempotent quantum channels）的二元区分问题。当两个通道共享一个共同的全秩不变态时，图像包含条件完全决定了渐近行为：条件成立时，通道散度族简化为闭式单字母表达式，无需正则化，所有误差指数可显式计算且无自适应优势；条件不成立时，非对称指数变为无穷大，意味着完美渐近区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究幂等量子通道的二元区分问题，旨在解决一般通道中重要的开放问题——强逆性质（strong converse property）。当两个通道共享共同的全秩不变态时，探索其渐近行为的完全确定条件。

Method: 采用图像包含条件（image inclusion condition）来分析幂等量子通道的渐近行为。对于GNS对称通道（GNS-symmetric channels），研究大量自迭代的区分率收敛到相应幂等外围投影（idempotent peripheral projections）的指数速度。对于不共享共同不变态的情况，提供正则化夹心Rényi cb-散度（regularized sandwiched Rényi cb-divergence）的单字母逆界。

Result: 当图像包含条件成立时，通道散度族简化为闭式单字母表达式，无需正则化，所有误差指数（Stein/Chernoff/强逆指数）可显式计算且无自适应优势，从而为该通道族建立了强逆性质。当条件不成立时，非对称指数变为无穷大，意味着完美渐近区分。对于GNS对称通道，大量自迭代的区分率以指数速度收敛到相应幂等外围投影的区分率。

Conclusion: 对于共享共同全秩不变态的幂等量子通道，简单的图像包含条件完全决定了二元区分的渐近行为，为解决一般通道的强逆性质这一重要开放问题提供了关键进展。该结果为量子通道区分理论建立了新的解析框架和计算方法。

Abstract: We study binary discrimination of idempotent quantum channels. When the two channels share a common full-rank invariant state, we show that a simple image inclusion condition completely determines the asymptotic behavior: when it holds, a broad family of channel divergences collapse to a closed-form, single-letter expression, regularization is unnecessary, and all error exponents (Stein/Chernoff/strong-converse) are explicitly computable with no adaptive advantage. Crucially, this yields the strong converse property for this channel family, which is an important open problem for general channels. When the inclusion fails, asymmetric exponents become infinite, implying perfect asymptotic discrimination. We apply the results to GNS-symmetric channels, showing discrimination rates for large number of self iterations converge exponentially fast to those of the corresponding idempotent peripheral projections. If the two channels do not share a common invariant state, we provide a single-letter converse bound on the regularized sandwiched Rényi cb-divergence, which suffices to establish a strong converse upper bound on the Stein exponents.

### [293] [Genuine and Non-Genuine Quantum Non-Marketability: A Unified Information-Theoretic Review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28277)

Motivation: 理解开放量子动力学的特征是否真正具有量子本质是该领域的核心挑战。尽管量子动力学的非马尔可夫行为已在不同场景中被广泛研究，但对于哪些动力学性质反映真正的量子特征、哪些源于经典或非真正量子来源，学界仍缺乏共识。

Method: 综述分析了多种框架，包括基于状态可区分性（state-distinguishability-based）、基于通道（channel-based，如"CP-可分性"）以及过程张量（process-tensor）方法。对于每种框架，概述了其物理动机和区分真正量子非马尔可夫性与实际或表观记忆效应的标准。

Result: 综述提供了基于信息回流及其起源来表征量子非马尔可夫性的最新发展详细信息，调查了各种方法如何分离经典和量子贡献，并定义了揭示真正量子非马尔可夫性的操作任务。进一步比较了不同方法的优势和局限性。

Conclusion: 该综述旨在澄清基于其本质的量子非马尔可夫过程的概念和操作方面，为未来关于量子非马尔可夫性及其在推进量子信息科学和技术中作用的研究奠定基础。

Abstract: Understanding whether the features of open quantum dynamics are genuinely quantum remains a central challenge in quantum dynamics. Even though the non-Markovian behavior of quantum dynamics has been widely investigated across different settings, there is still no consensus on which properties of a dynamics reflect genuine quantum features and which arise from classical or non-genuine quantum sources. In this review, we provide detailed information on recent developments in characterizing quantum non-Markovianity based on information backflow and the nature of its origin. We also present a survey on how various approaches separate classical and quantum contributions, as well as how they define operational tasks that reveal genuine quantum non-Markovianity. We analyze several frameworks, including state-distinguishability -based, channel-based (``CP-divisibility''), and process-tensor methods. For each framework, we outline the underlying physical motivation, the criteria proposed to distinguish genuine quantum non-Markovianity from practical or apparent memory effects. We further compare different approaches and their strengths and limitations. The review aims to clarify the conceptual and operational aspects of quantum non-Markovian processes based on their nature and to provide a foundation for future research on quantum non-Markovianity and its role in advancing quantum information science and technology.

</details>


### [294] [Quantized Dissipation from the Inverse-Square Anomaly in a Non-Hermitian Klein-Gordon Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28525)
*Mansour Haghighat,Ali Nouri*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究构建了一个精确可解的相对论模型，通过纯虚数、尺度不变的标量势将反常反平方相互作用嵌入非厄米克莱因-戈登场论中，将"落向中心"不稳定性转化为具有几何间隔的复能量离散谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为反常尺度行为（scale anomaly）、边界条件诱导的非厄米性（boundary-condition-induced non-Hermiticity）以及相对论开放量子系统中的量子化耗散（quantized dissipation）提供一个最小解析框架。

Method: 方法是通过纯虚数、尺度不变的标量势将反常反平方相互作用（anomalous inverse-square interaction）嵌入非厄米克莱因-戈登场论（non-Hermitian Klein-Gordon field theory），并对奇点处施加严格出射边界条件（strictly outgoing boundary condition），将其解释为不可逆吸收。

Result: 结果是将"落向中心"不稳定性（fall-to-the-center instability）转化为具有对数周期性（log-periodic）的复能量离散谱，衰变率呈现由反常标度指数决定的普适几何间隔，且对微观短距离正则化不敏感。

Conclusion: 该模型定义了一个控制耗散动力学的涌现运动学能量尺度（emergent kinematic energy scale），为研究尺度反常、边界条件诱导的非厄米性以及相对论开放量子系统中的量子化耗散提供了最小解析框架。

Abstract: We construct an exactly solvable relativistic model that embeds the anomalous inverse-square interaction into a non-Hermitian Klein-Gordon field theory through a purely imaginary, scale-invariant scalar potential. The stationary field equation reduces to an inverse-square Schrodinger-type problem with a quadratic spectral parameter. Imposing a strictly outgoing boundary condition at the singularity-interpreted as irreversible absorption-selects a unique physical realization and converts the fall-to-the-center instability into a discrete, log-periodic spectrum of complex energies. The resulting decay rates exhibit universal geometric spacing, determined solely by the anomalous scaling exponent and insensitive to microscopic short-distance regularization. This structure defines an emergent kinematic energy scale that controls dissipative dynamics and provides a minimal analytic framework for studying scale anomaly, boundary-condition-induced non-Hermiticity, and quantized dissipation in relativistic open quantum systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: QRHD在算符形式和路径积分形式（path integral formalism）下进行表述，通过动能项中的位置相关度规（position-dependent metric）引入几何结构，并推导了相应的量子运动方程。

Abstract: We propose Quantum Riemannian Hamiltonian Descent (QRHD), a quantum algorithm for continuous optimization on Riemannian manifolds that extends Quantum Hamiltonian Descent (QHD) by incorporating geometric structure of the parameter space via a position-dependent metric in the kinetic term. We formulate QRHD at both operator and path integral formalisms and derive the corresponding quantum equations of motion, showing that quantum corrections appear in the action integral but they are suppressed at late times by the time-dependent dissipation factor. This implies that convergence near optimal points is controlled by the classical potential while quantum effects influence early-time dynamics. A quantum circuit implementation based on time-dependent Hamiltonian simulation is also discussed and the query complexity is estimated.

Abstract: Measurements can be used to monitor the evolution of quantum systems and can give rise to quantized return statistics. An analog scaling relation was previously found for random-time monitoring, indicating that weak and random-time monitoring have similar effects. We discuss how weak monitoring via ancilla coupling is linked to the unitary evolution, and how this connection can be controlled by a convergent perturbation theory.

Result: 推导出的亥姆霍兹方程包含两个几何势能项：与外曲率成正比的各向同性贡献，以及来自第二基本形式无迹部分的各向异性算子。这些线性曲率势能区分凸凹界面，并预测当材料介电常数比等于黄金比例平方时各向异性项消失。

Abstract: Surface plasmon polaritons propagating along curved metal-dielectric interfaces experience geometry-induced modifications absent on flat surfaces. In this work, we derive a covariant, effective two-dimensional wave equation for the transverse magnetic surface plasmon mode on weakly curved smooth interfaces. By perturbatively expanding Maxwell's equations with curvature-adapted boundary conditions, we find a Helmholtz equation with two geometric potential terms that enter at first order in the extrinsic curvature: an isotropic contribution proportional to the extrinsic curvature, and an anisotropic operator arising from the traceless part of the second fundamental form. These linear-in-curvature potentials distinguish convex from concave interfaces, in contrast to the quadratic potentials known from symmetrically confined systems such as dielectric waveguides. We show that our equation reproduces established results for spherical and cylindrical interfaces. We furthermore predict that the anisotropic contribution vanishes when the ratio of the material permittivities equals the square of the golden ratio. As an application, we demonstrate sign-dependent cooperative frequency shifts as well as a curvature-driven redistribution of superradiant and subradiant decay rates for a ring of quantum emitters on a curved metallic spheroid interacting through the surface plasmons.

Abstract: Quantum-enhanced Markov chain Monte Carlo, a hybrid quantum-classical algorithm in which configurations are proposed by a quantum proposer and accepted or rejected by a classical algorithm, has been introduced as a possible method for robust quantum speedup. ### [302] [The local characterization of global tensor network eigenstates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28349)
*José Garre Rubio,András Molnár,Norbert Schuch,Frank Verstraete*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究建立了矩阵乘积态（MPS）或矩阵乘积算符作为局域算符精确本征矢的充要条件，通过局域方程刻画了包括哈密顿量疤痕态、驱动系统轨迹、Lindblad稳态等广泛问题的解空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在确定矩阵乘积态（Matrix Product States, MPS）或矩阵乘积算符（Matrix Product Operators）何时能成为局域算符（如哈密顿量）的精确本征矢。这涵盖了多种物理场景，包括哈密顿量的精确本征态（如疤痕态）、驱动量子系统的精确MPS轨迹、局域Lindblad算符的稳态等。

Method: 核心方法是建立一个局域、固定尺寸的方程，描述单个算符项如何作用于张量块。该方程提供了MPS或矩阵乘积算符成为局域算符精确本征矢的充要条件，从而能够完整刻画解空间。

Result: 关键结果表明，一个局域、固定尺寸的方程足以表征所有前述问题的完整解空间。该局域表征方法可用于解析和数值识别解，并通过恢复XXZ模型的量子群对称性（quantum group symmetries）展示了其有效性。

Conclusion: 该局域表征方法为广泛物理问题提供了统一的框架，能够完整刻画矩阵乘积态作为局域算符精确本征矢的解空间。研究还讨论了该方法在MPS数值算法中的应用，以及向二维投影纠缠对态（projected entangled pair states, PEPS）的推广。

Abstract: We study the conditions under which Matrix Product States (MPS) or Matrix Product Operators are exact eigenvectors of an extensive local operator, such as a Hamiltonian. By suitably choosing the local operator, this covers a wide range of settings: Exact eigenstates of Hamiltonians, including scar states, exact MPS trajectories for driven quantum systems, steady states of local Lindbladians, generalized symmetries of either Hamiltonians or density matrices, and many more. Our key result is that that a local, fixed-size equation -- namely, how a single term in the operator acts on a block of tensors -- provides a necessary and sufficient condition for exact solutions. This allows to characterize the full space of solutions in all of the aforementioned problems, and to identify them both analytically and numerically. We elaborate on the concrete application of this characterization to all of the aforementioned settings, and in particular exemplify the power of our local characterization by using it to recover the quantum group symmetries of the XXZ model. We also discuss applications to numerical algorithms with MPS and the generalization of our results to 2D, i.e., projected entangled pair states (PEPS).

</details>


### [303] [Emergent-Coupling-Based Ansatz Evaluated on a Superconducting Quantum Processor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28486)
*Alina Joch,Kevin Lively,Benedikt Fauseweh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文实验评估了基于涌现耦合的变分拟设（ECBA），这是一种针对无序系统的物理启发性变分拟设。在超导量子处理器上实现了对无序海森堡链模型的基准测试，在30量子比特系统中实现了96.47%的相对能量精度，相比常用硬件高效拟设具有显著优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变分量子本征求解器（variational quantum eigensolver）的性能关键取决于拟设（ansatz）的选择。本文旨在实验评估一种针对无序系统的物理启发性变分拟设——基于涌现耦合的拟设（emergent-coupling-based ansatz, ECBA）。

Method: ECBA基于重整化（半）群（renormalization (semi-)group）方法确定主导的有效耦合，产生浅层电路以捕捉本质的长程纠缠结构同时平衡局域关联。在超导量子处理器上实现ECBA，对无序海森堡链模型（disordered Heisenberg chain models）进行基准测试，使用经典预优化参数和误差缓解技术（error mitigation techniques）。

Result: 在高达30量子比特的系统中，最大系统实现了96.47%的实验相对能量精度。ECBA可以高效地嵌入到具有二维方晶格连接性（two-dimensional square-lattice connectivity）的硬件上。与常用硬件高效拟设（hardware efficient ansätze）相比，ECBA在相似门数下实现了显著更高的精度。

Conclusion: 基于涌现耦合的拟设为无序系统提供了一种物理启发的有效变分拟设，能够在浅层电路中捕捉关键量子特征，并在实际量子硬件上实现高精度计算，相比传统硬件高效拟设具有性能优势。

Abstract: The performance of the variational quantum eigensolver depends critically on the choice of ansatz. In this work, we experimentally evaluate the emergent-coupling-based ansatz (ECBA), a physically motivated variational ansatz for disordered systems. The ECBA is based on a renormalization (semi-)group approach to determine the dominant effective couplings, resulting in shallow circuits that capture the essential long-range entanglement structure while balancing local correlations. We implement the ECBA on superconducting quantum processors and benchmark it on disordered Heisenberg chain models. Using classically pre-optimized parameters and error mitigation techniques, we study systems of up to 30 qubits and observe an experimental relative energy accuracy of 96.47% for the largest system. Furthermore, we find that the ECBA can be efficiently embedded on hardware with two-dimensional square-lattice connectivity. We compare to commonly used hardware efficient ansätze and observe that the ECBA achieves significantly higher accuracy at a similar gate count.

</details>


### [304] [Probing excited-state quantum phase transitions with trapped cold ions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28509)
*Marek Kuchař,Michal Macek*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出在单离子阱系统中实现激发态量子相变（ESQPTs）量子临界性的具体实验方案，定义了ESQPT见证可观测量，并研究了其临界标度行为和不同驱动速率下的状态演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在实验实现激发态量子相变（excited-state quantum phase transitions, ESQPTs）的量子临界性，特别是在单离子阱这一简单且稳健的系统中。通过识别扩展拉比模型（Extended Rabi Model, ERM）特定激发态类别，为ESQPTs的实验观测提供理论基础。

Method: 方法包括：识别ERM哈密顿量在（反）Jaynes-Cummings超辐射相中两个临界ESQPT能量之间的特定激发态类别；定义多个ESQPT见证可观测量；通过线性改变量子比特-声子耦合强度来驱动系统穿越量子临界点，研究不同有限速率下的临界标度行为和状态演化；将ERM理论控制参数映射到离子阱实验参数，并基于现有先进实验装置进行模拟。

Result: 研究确定了ERM特定激发态类别及其在ESQPT临界能量之间的分布，定义了有效的ESQPT见证可观测量并分析了其临界标度行为。通过驱动系统穿越量子临界点，观察到不同速率下的状态演化差异，并提供了理论参数到实验参数的映射，模拟结果考虑了幺正演化及相关开放系统修正。

Conclusion: 该研究为在单离子阱系统中实验观测激发态量子相变（ESQPTs）提供了具体可行的协议，通过定义见证可观测量和参数映射，为量子临界性的实验研究开辟了新途径，特别适用于现有先进离子阱实验装置。

Abstract: We propose concrete protocols to realize quantum criticality due to excited-state quantum phase transitions (ESQPTs) experimentally in presumably the simplest and most resilient system involving a single trapped ion oscillating in a radio-frequency Paul trap. We identify a specific class of excited states of the Extended Rabi Model (ERM) Hamiltonian, which occur between two critical ESQPT energies of the model in its (anti)Jaynes-Cummings superradiant phase. Properties of these states motivate the definition of several ESQPT witness observables. We study their critical scaling behaviors as well as various distinct state evolutions by driving the system across the quantum criticalities by changing the qubit-phonon coupling strength linearly in time at different finite rates. A mapping of the theoretical control parameters of the ERM to the experimental parameters of a trapped ion setup is provided, and simulations are performed for values referencing existing state-of-the-art setups, addressing both unitary state evolutions as well as relevant open-system corrections.

</details>
